Si-Phian 	(19)
	Koan3 I
[1]	Bo5 kiaN5 phaiN2-lang5 e5 ke3-bou5,  Bo5 khia7 choe7-jin5 e5 lou7,  Bo5 che7 bu2-ban7 e5 lang5 e5 ui7, chit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
2)	I sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lut8-hoat;  Mi5-jit8 sam3-su--e5, ia7 si7 I e5 lut8-hoat;
3)	I beh chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7 chai ti7 khoe-piN,  Chiau3-si5 kiat ke2-chi2,  I e5 hioh8 ia7 boe7 ta--khi3;  I sou2 choe3--e5 it-chin7 heng-thong.
4)	PhaiN2-lang5 m7-si7 an2-ni;  Si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chhou-khng hou7 hong chhe-soaN3.
5)	Sou2-i2 ti7 sim2-phoaN3, phaiN2-lang5 khia7-boe7-tiau5;  Choe7-jin5 ti7 gi7-lang5 e5 hoe7-tiong, iah8 si7 an2-ni.
6)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chai gi7-lang5 e5 lou7,  Na7-si7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 lou7 oe7 biat8-bo5.

[2]	Liat8-pang5 siaN2-su7 soan-hoa,  Cheng3 peh-siN3 siaN2-su7 ke3-bou5 khang-khang e5 su7?
2)	Se3-chiuN7 e5 kun-ong5 khia7--khi2-lai5,  Chiang2 koan5-peng3--e5 saN-kap gi7-lun7,  Beh ti2-tek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ia7 ti2-tek8 I e5 siu7 boah-iu5--e5.
3)	Kong2, Lan2 tioh8 chhoah-tng7 in e5 khun2-pak8,  Hiat-kak8 in e5 soh.
4)	Che7 ti7 thiN-teng2--e5 beh chhio3,  Chu2 beh biau2-si7 in.
5)	Hit-si5 I beh ti7 I e5 siu7-khi3-tiong lai5 tui3 i kong2,  Ti7 I e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 lai5 hou7 in kiaN.
6)	Chu2 kong2, Goa2 i2-keng siat-lip8 Goa2 e5 ong5,  Ti7 Sek-an, Goa2 e5 seng3-soaN.
7)	Goa2 beh thoan5 seng3-chi2,  Ia5-ho5-hoa bat ka7 goa2 kong2,  Li2 si7 Goa2 e5 kiaN2,  Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 siN li2.
8)	Li2 kiu5 Goa2, Goa2 chiu7 chiong liat8-pang hou7 li2 choe3 ki-giap8;  Chiong toe7 e5 kek8-thau5 hou7 li2 choe3 san2-giap8.
9)	Li2 beh eng7 thih-koaiN2 phah-phoa3 in;  Beh kong3-chhui3 in chhin-chhiuN7 sio-hui5 lang5 e5 hui5-khi3.
10)	TaN lin2 liat8-ong5 tioh8 u7 ti3-hui7;  Lin2 se3-chiuN7 e5 sim2-phoaN3-koaN tioh8 siu7 keng2-kai3.
11)	Tioh8 eng7 keng3-ui3 lai5 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Tioh8 eng7 kiaN-hiaN5 lai5 hoaN-hi2.
12)	Tioh8 eng7 chhui3 chim Seng3 KiaN2, kiaN-liau2 I siu7-khi3, lin2 chiu7 biat8-bo5 ti7 lou7-tiong.  In-ui7 I e5 siu7-khi3 beh kin2-kin2 hoat-chhut.  Hoan7-na7 oa2-kho3 I--e5, long2 si7 u7 hok-khi3 e5 lang5.

[3]	Tai7-pit8 siam2-pi7 i e5 kiaN2 Ap-sa-liong5 e5 si5, lai5 choe3 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 chiah--nih choe7!  Choe7-choe7 lang5 khi2--lai5 kong-kek goa2.
2)	Choe7-choe7 lang5 gi7-lun7 goa2 kong2,  I bo5 thang tit-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 chin2-kiu3. [Se3-lah8
3)	Chong2-si7, Ia5-ho5-hoa, Li2 si7 goa2 si3-ui5 e5 tin5-pai5;  Si7 goa2 e5 eng5-kng; koh si7 hou7 goa2 e5 thau5 kiah8-koaiN5--e5.
4)	Goa2 eng7 goa2 e5 siaN kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  I tui3 I e5 seng3-soaN in3 goa2. [Se3-lah8
5)	Goa2 to2--teh, goa2 khun3;  Goa2 cheng-sin5, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa long2 po2-hou7 goa2.
6)	Sui-jian5 chheng-ban7 lang5 khi2--lai5, ui5-lui5 kong-kek goa2,  Goa2 iah8 bo5 kiaN.
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 khi2--lai5;  Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 chin2-kiu3 goa2,  In-ui7 Li2 sian3 goa2 it-chhe3 tui3-tek8 e5 chhui3-phoe2,  Phah-chih8 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhui3-khi2.
8)	Chin2-kiu3 siok8-ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Goan7 Li2 su3-hok Li2 e5 peh-siN3. [Se3-lah8

[4]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; eng7 si hian5 e5 gak8-khi3.
1)	Hian2-beng5 goa2 e5 gi7 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 kiu5-kio3 e5 si5, kiu5 Li2 in3 goa2.  Goa2 ti7 khun3-khou2 e5 tiong-kan, Li2 bat hou7 goa2 khoan-khoah.  TaN kiu5 Li2 lin5-bin2 goa2, lai5 thiaN goa2 e5 ki5-to2.
2)	Lin2 chiah e5 siong7-teng2-lang5 ah, chiong goa2 e5 eng5-kng pian3-choe3 leng5-jiok8, beh kau3 ti7-si5?  Lin2 i3-ai3 khang-hu, chhiau-chhe7 bo5 iaN2-chiah, beh kau3 ti7-si5? [Se3-lah8
3)	Lin2 tioh8 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng hun-piat keng3-khian5 e5 lang5 choe3 I ka-ki7 e5.  Goa2 kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I beh thiaN goa2.
4)	Lin2 tioh8 kiaN-hiaN5, m7-thang hoan7-choe7;  Ti7 bin5-chhng5--nih, sim tioh8 sam3-su, iah8 tioh8 siok-cheng7. [Se3-lah8
5)	Tioh8 hian3 gi7 e5 che3,  Iah8 tioh8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
6)	Choe7-choe7 lang5 kong2, Chi7-chui7 oe7 chi2-si7 goan2 sim2-mih8 ho2--chhu3?  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 bin7 e5 kng lai5 chio3 goan2.
7)	Li2 hou7 goa2 sim-lai7 u7 hoaN-hi2,  IaN5-ke3 lang5 tit-tioh8 choe7-choe7 gou7-kak kap sin-chiu2 e5 si5.
8)	Goa2 beh an-jian5 to2--teh khun3,  In-ui7 chi2-u7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Li2 hou7 goa2 an-un2 khia7-khi2.

[5]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; eng7 pun5 e5 gak8-khi3.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 oe7.  Kam3-chhat goa2 e5 sim-su.
2)	Goa2 e5 Ong5, goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah,  Kiu5 Li2 aN3-loh8 thiaN goa2 kiu5-kio3 e5 siaN:  In-ui7 goa2 ng3 Li2 ki5-to2.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, cha2-khi2-si5 Li2 oe7 thiaN goa2 e5 siaN;  Cha2-khi2-si5 goa2 beh tui3 Li2 pai5-liat8 goa2 e5 sim-i3, soa3 beh liau5-bang7.
4)	In-ui7 Li2 m7-si7 hoaN-hi2 choe7-ok e5 Siong7-te3;  PhaiN2--e5 boe7-tit-thang kap Li2 tang5 khia7-khi2.
5)	Kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 boe7-oe7 khia7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  Choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5 long2 si7 Li2 sou2 oan3-hun7.
6)	Kong2 peh8-chhat8--e5, Li2 beh biat8 in;  Ai3 thai5 lang5 kap kan-kui2--e5, long2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 iam3-ouN3.
7)	Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 beh pin5 Li2 hong-seng7 e5 chu5-ai3 jip8 Li2 e5 chhu3;  Goa2 beh chun5 keng3-ui3 Li2 e5 sim, ng3 Li2 e5 seng3-tian7 lai5 keng3-pai3.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 in-ui7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8, pin5 Li2 e5 kong-gi7 chhoa7 goa2;  Hou7 Li2 e5 lou7 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 cheng3-tit8.
9)	In-ui7 in e5 chhui3 bo5 lau2-sit8;  In e5 sim ok-tok8 moa2-moa2;  In e5 na5-au5 si7 khui-khui e5 bong7;  In eng7 chih8 thiam2-mi7 lang5.
10)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 teng7 in e5 choe7;  Hou7 in tui3 ka-ki7 e5 ke3-bou5 poah8-to2.  In e5 choe7-koa3 chin-choe7, goan7 Li2 chiong in koaN2-chhut;  In-ui7 in poe7-poan7 Li2.
11)	KiN3-na7 oa2-kho3 Li2--e5, goan7 in hoaN-hi2;  Goan7 in eng2-eng2 hoaN-hi2 chhut-siaN; in-ui7 Li2 pi3-iu7 in.  Koh goan7 hiah e5 thiaN3-sioh Li2 e5 mia5 e5 lang5, long2 tiam3-ti7 Li2 lai5 hoaN-hi2.
12)	In-ui7 Li2 beh su3-hok hou7 gi7-lang5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 beh eng7 un-hui7, chhin-chhiuN7 tin5-pai5, si3-bin7 ui5--i.

[6]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; eng7 si-hian5 e5 gak8-khi3; tiau7, eng7 te7 poeh.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, m7-thang ti7 Li2 e5 siu7-khi3-tiong chek-pi7 goa2,  Iah8 m7-thang ti7 Li2 toa7 siu7-khi3-tiong khian3-chek goa2.	
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 kho2-lin5 goa2, in-ui7 goa2 soe-lam2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 i-ti7 goa2, in-ui7 goa2 e5 kut-thau5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.
3)	Goa2 e5 sim toa7-toa7 kiaN-hiaN5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 beh kau3 ti7-si5 chiah kiu3 goa2?
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 oat8-to3-tng2 kiu3 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7;  Ui7-tioh8 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 lai5 kiu3 goa2.
5)	In-ui7 si2-bo5 e5 tiong-kan, bo5 ki3-liam7 Li2;  Im-hu2 e5 tiong-kan, chi7-chui7 kam2-sia7 Li2?
6)	Goa2 in-ui7 haiN-haiN-chhan lai5 ia3-sian7;  Goa2 tak8-mi5 lau5 bak8-sai2, im goa2 e5 bin5-chhng5,  Sip-thau3 goa2 e5 jiok8-a2.
7)	Goa2 in-ui7 iu-bun7, bak8-chiu phah-phaiN2;  Koh in-ui7 goa2 it-chhe3 e5 tui3-tek8, lai5 bak8-chiu hoe.
8)	Lin2 it-chhe3 choe3 phaiN2 e5 lang5, tioh8 li7-khui goa2;  In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3 goa2 thi5-khau3 e5 siaN.
9)	Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 thiaN goa2 e5 khun2-kiu5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chiap-lap8 goa2 e5 ki5-to2.
10)	Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 long2 beh kian3-siau3, toa7-toa7 kiaN-hiaN5;  In beh the3 to3-tng2, hut-jian5 kian3-siau3.

[7]	Tai7-pit8 chi2 Pian7-nga2-bin2 lang5 Kou2-sit8 e5 oe7, ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiuN3-koa; tiau7, eng7 Si-kai-un.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2;  Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 it-chhe3 tui-koaN2 goa2 e5 lang5, kiu3 goa2 chhut-lai5.
2)	KiaN-liau2 i chhin-chhiuN7 sai, thiah-lih8 goa2;  Thiah kau3 chhui3-chhui3, bo5 chin2-kiu3 goa2--e5.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 na7 kiaN5 chit-e5;  Na7 u7 choe7-ok ti7 goa2 e5 chhiu2;
4)	Goa2 na7 eng7 phaiN2 po3 hit e5 kap goa2 ho5-ho2 e5 lang5;  (Ki5-sit8 lian5 hit e5 bo5 ian5-kou3 kap goa2 choe3 tui3-tek8 e5 lang5, goa2 iah8 u7 kiu3 i;)
5)	Chiu7 chhut-chai7 tui3-tek8 tui-jip goa2, kau3 jip-tioh8;  Chiong goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 tah8 ti7 thou5-kha,  Chiong goa2 e5 eng5-kng he7 ti7 thou5-hun2. [Se3-lah8
6)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 ti7 Li2 e5 siu7-khi3-tiong khi2--lai5,  Peh--khi2-lai5 khia7, ti2-tng goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3,  Kiu5 Li2 ui7-tioh8 goa2 lai5 chhiN2, chiau3 Li2 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 lai5 sim2-phoaN3.
7)	Goan7 liat8-pang e5 hoe7 ui5 Li2;  Goan7 Li2 to3-tng2 ti7 koaiN5-ui7 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa sim2-phoaN3 cheng3 peh-siN3;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 phoaN3-toan3 goa2, chiau3 goa2 e5 gi7 kap goa2 sim-lai7 e5 cheng3-tit8.
9)	Goan7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 phaiN2 kau3 chia soah, gi7-lang5 Li2 hou7 i khia7-chai7;  In-ui7 kong-gi7 e5 Siong7-te3 kam3-chhat lang5 e5 sim-tng5.
10)	Goa2 e5 tin5-pai5 chai7-ti7 Siong7-te3,  I chin2-kiu3 sim-lai7 cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5.
11)	Siong7-te3 si7 kong-gi7 e5 sim2-phoaN3-si;  Iah8 si7 jit8-jit8 hoat-chhut siu7-khi3 e5 Siong7-te3.
12)	Lang5 na7 m7 hoan2-hoe2, I beh boa5 I e5 to;  I u7 tiuN I e5 keng, pi7-pan7 pian7-pian7.
13)	I pi7-pan7 oe7 hou7 lang5 si2 e5 ke-si,  I sou2 sia7 e5 chiN3 si7 he2 chiN3.
14)	Li2 khoaN3, phaiN2 lang5 tou5-bou5 kan-ok,  Hoai5-in7 tok8-hai7, siN-chhut hu-ke2.
15)	I khui khut, kut8 hou7 i chhim;  Keng2-jian5 poah8-loh8 ti7 i sou2 khui e5 ham7-khiN.
16)	I e5 tok8-hai7 beh to3-tng2 kau3 i e5 thau5-khak;  I e5 kiong5-po7 beh loh8 ti7 i e5 thau5-khak-teng2.
17)	Goa2 beh chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 kong-gi7 kam2-sia7 I;  Koh o-lo2 chi3-koaiN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5.

[8]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN, eng7 Ka-tek8 e5 gak8-khi3;
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Chu2 ah,  Li2 e5 mia5 ti7 choan5-toe7 kau3 chiah koaiN5-toa7!  Li2 chiong Li2 e5 eng5-kng pai5-siat ti7 thiN--nih.
2)	Li2 in-ui7 Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 e5 ian5-kou3, tui3 eN-a2 kap chiah8-leng--e5 e5 chhui3, kian3-lip8 leng5-lek8;  Beh hou7 tui3-tek8 kap po3-oan--e5 cheng7-cheng7.
3)	Goa2 khoaN3 Li2 e5 thiN, Li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 cho7--e5,  Kap Li2 sou2 pai5-liat8 e5 geh8 kap chhiN;
4)	Se3-kan lang5 si7 sim2-mih8, Li2 siau3-liam7 i?  Lang5 e5 kiaN2 si7 sim2-mih8, Li2 koan3-kou3--i?
5)	Li2 hou7 i pi2 thiN-sai3 li5-a2 khah-su,  Koh siuN2-su3 i eng5-kng chun-kui3 choe3 bian2-liu5.
6)	Li2 siat-lip8 i koan2-li2 Li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 cho7--e5,  He7 ban7-mih8 ti7 i e5 kha-e7;
7)	Chiu7-si7 it-chhe3 e5 iuN5 kap gu5, SoaN-ia2 e5 chau2-siu3;
8)	ThiN-tiong e5 chiau2, hai2-lai7 e5 hi5,  Kap kiN3-na7 keng-ke3 hai2--nih e5 lou7 e5, long2 he7 ti7 i e5 kha-e7.
9)	Ia5-ho5-hoa, goan2 e5 Chu2 ah,  Li2 e5 mia5 ti7 choan5-toe7 kau3 hiah koaiN5-toa7!

[9]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN, tiau7, eng7 Bou7-lah8-pian7.
1)	Goa2 beh choan5-sim kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Goa2 beh po3-iong5 Li2 it-chhe3 ki5-biau7 e5 sou2-choe3.
2)	Goa2 beh chai7-ti7 Li2 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8;  Chi3-koaiN5--e5 ah, goa2 beh o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5.
3)	Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 oat8-tng2-sin the3--khi3 e5 si5,  Chiu7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 poah8-to2 biat8-bo5.
4)	Li2 i2-keng thoe3 goa2 sin-oan, thoe3 goa2 pian7-beng5;  Li2 che7 ti7 po2-cho7, chiau3 kong-gi7 sim2-phoaN3.
5)	Li2 u7 chek-pi7 liat8-pang, Li2 u7 biat8-bo5 phaiN2-lang5,  Li2 u7 chhat-biat8 in e5 mia5 kau3 eng2-oan2.
6)	Tui3-tek8 kau3 kiat-kiok8, siu7 hong-hoe3 kau3 eng2-oan2;  Li2 hui2-hoai7 in e5 siaN5;  Lian5 in e5 ki3-liam7 iah8 bo5--khi3.
7)	Tok8-tok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa che7-ui7 kau3 eng2-oan2;  I i2-keng ui7 sim2-phoaN3, an-ti3 I e5 po2-cho7.
8)	I beh chiau3 kong-gi7 sim2-phoaN3 se3-kai3,  Chiau3 cheng3-tit8 phoaN3-toan3 cheng3 peh-siN3.
9)	Ia5-ho5-hoa koh beh choe3 siu7 ap-pek e5 lang5 e5 koaiN5-tai5,  Ti7 hoan7-lan7 e5 si5 e5 koaiN5-tai5.  
10)	Bat Li2 e5 mia5 e5 lang5 beh oa2-kho3 Li2;  In-ui7, Ia5-ho5-hoa, Li2 be7-bat khi3-sak chhe7 Li2 e5 lang5.
11)	Tioh8 o-lo2 khia7-khi2 Sek-an e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Chiong I sou2 kiaN5--e5 po3-iong5 ti7 cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan.
12)	In-ui7 hit e5 cha-pan7 beng7-an3--e5 ki3-tit in;  Bo5 boe7 ki3-tit khun3-khou2 lang5 e5 ai-kiu5.
13)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 lin5-bin2 goa2;  Li2 si7 tui3 si2-mng5 kiu3 goa2 khi2--lai5--e5,  Tioh8 kam3-chhat hiah e5 oan3-hun7 goa2 e5 lang5 sou2 hou7 goa2 tu2-tioh8 e5 khou2-lan7.
14)	Thang hou7 goa2 kong2-khi2 Li2 it-chhe3 e5 ho2 mia5-siaN;  Goa2 beh ti7 Sek-an siaN5 e5 mng5,  Ui7-tioh8 Li2 e5 kiu3-un lai5 hoaN-hi2.
15)	Liat8-pang ham7-loh8 ti7 in sou2 khui e5 ham7-khiN;  In e5 kha tiN5 ti7 in am3-chiN7 siat e5 lo5-bang7.
16)	Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng hian2-beng5 ka-ki7, I i2-keng kiaN5 sim2-phoaN3;  PhaiN2 lang5 hou7 ka-ki7 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5 tiN5--tioh8. [Hi-kai-un. Se3-lah8
17)	PhaiN2-lang5 beh kui ti7 im-hu2,  Boe7 ki3--tit Siong7-te3 e5 liat8-pang iah8 beh an2-ni.
18)	In-ui7 song3-hiong-lang5 tek-khak bo5 eng2-oan2 hou7 Siong7-te3 boe7 ki3-tit,  Khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 e5 ng3-bang7, tek-khak boe7 eng2-eng2 bo5--khi3.
19)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 khi2--lai5, m7-thang iong5-un2 lang5 khah-iaN5;  Goan7 liat8-pang ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 siu7 sim2-phoaN3.
20)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 in kiaN-hiaN5;  Goan7 liat8-pang chai ka-ki7 put-ko3 si7 lang5 na7-tiaN7. [Se3-lah8

[10]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 siaN2-su7 hng7-hng7 teh khia7?  Ti7 hoan7-lan7 e5 si5, Li2 siaN2-su7 tiam3-bat8?
2)	PhaiN2-lang5 ti7 kiau-ngou7 e5 tiong-kan, tui-jip khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 chin kin2-kip,  Goan7 in ham7-loh8 ti7 ka-ki7 sou2 siat e5 ke3-bou5.
3)	PhaiN2-lang5 khoa-khau2 i e5 sim sou2 ai3,  Tham--sim--e5 khi3-sak Ia5-ho5-hoa, koh bu2-ban7 I.
4)	PhaiN2-lang5 bin7 tai3 kiau-ngou7, kong2, I bo5-beh kiu3-kham3;  I sou2 siuN7--e5 long2 liah8-choe3 bo5 Siong7-te3.
5)	KiN3-na7 i sou2 kiaN5--e5 siong5-siong5 un2-tang3;  Li2 e5 sim2-phoaN3 poaN5-ke3 i e5 gan2-kai3;  Lun7-kau3 i it-chhe3 e5 tui3-tek8, i long2 biau2-si7 in.
6)	I sim-lai7 kong2, Goa2 tek-khak boe7 io5-choah,  Tai7-tai7 boe7 tu2-tioh8 chai-lan7.
7)	I e5 chhui3 moa2-moa2 chiu3-me7, kan-cha3, khi-ap;  I e5 chih8-e7 ok-tok8, hu-ke2.
8)	I ti7 hiuN-chhng bai5-hok8 e5 sou2-chai7 che7-teh;  I ti7 un2-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7 hai7-si2 bo5 choe7 e5 lang5,  I e5 bak8-chiu am3-chiN7 tit8-tit8 siong3 bo5 i-oa2 e5 lang5.
9)	I bai5-hok8 ti7 am3-chiN7 e5 sou2-chai7,  chhin-chhiuN7 sai bih ti7 i e5 hiat8;  I bai5-hok8 beh liah8 song3-hiong lang5;  Eng7 bang7 ui5 song3-hiong lang5, lai5 liah8--tioh8 i.
10)	I khut-sin phak--teh,  Bo5 i-oa2 e5 lang5 chiu7 to2 ti7 i jiau2-ge5--e5 e7-bin7.
11)	I sim-lai7 kong2, Siong7-te3 boe7-ki3-tit;  Ng I e5 bin7; eng2-oan2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3.
12)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 khi2--lai5;  Siong7-te3 ah, kiah8-khi2 Li2 e5 chhiu2;  M7-thang boe7 ki3-tit song3-hiong-lang5.
13)	PhaiN2-lang5 siaN2-su7 biau2-si7 Siong7-te3,  Sim-lai7 kong2, Li2 bo5 beh kun-kiu3?
14)	Li2 i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3; in-ui7 ok-tok8 oan3-tou3, Li2 long2 kam3-chhat, beh eng7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 po3-eng3;  Bo5 i-oa2 e5 lang5, chiong pun2-sin kau-tai3 Li2;  Li2 si7 pang-chan7 bo5 pe7 e5 kiaN2--e5.
15)	Goan7 Li2 phah-chih8 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhiu2-kut;  Lun7-kau3 ok-lang5, goan7 Li2 kun-kiu3 i e5 phaiN2 kau3 thiat-ti2.
16)	Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 ong5, tui3 eng2-oan2 kau3 eng2-oan2;  Liat8-pang-lang5 tui3 I e5 toe7 long2 biat8-bo5.
17)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, khiam-pi e5 lang5 e5 sim-goan7, Li2 i2-keng thiaN-kiN3;  Li2 beh pi7-pan7 in e5 sim, Li2 beh aN3 hi7-khang lai5 thiaN.
18)	Beh thoe3 bo5 pe7 e5 kiaN2, i2-kip8 siu7 ap-pek e5 lang5, sin-oan.  Hou7 se3-kan-lang5 bo5 koh hang2-hoah lang5.

[11]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Goa2 si7 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Lin2 siaN2-su7 tui3 goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 kong2,  Li2 tioh8 chhin-chhiuN7 chiau2, pe--khi3 lin2 e5 soaN.
2)	KhoaN3 ah, phaiN2-lang5 tiuN keng,  An in e5 chiN3 ti7 keng-hian5,  Beh am3-chiN7 sia7 sim-lai7 cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5.
3)	Toe7-ki na7 to2-hoai7,  Gi7-lang5 iau2 oe7 choe3 sim2-mih8?
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 I e5 seng3-tian7,  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 po2-cho7 ti7 thiN--nih;  I e5 bak8-chiu teh khoaN3,  I e5 bak8-chiu kam3-chhat se3-kan-lang5.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa chhi3-giam7 gi7-lang5,  Tok8-tok8 phaiN2-lang5 kap ai3 kiong5-po7--e5, I e5 sim oan3-hun7 i.
6)	I beh chiong lo5-bang7 pha ti7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 sin-chiuN7;  U7 he2-iam7, jiu5-ng5, kap jiat8-jiat8 e5 hong, choe3 in poe-tiong e5 hun7-giah8.
7)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 kong-gi7;  I hoaN-hi2 kong-gi7,  Cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5 beh kiN3-tioh8 I e5 bin7.

[12]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, eng7 te7 poeh.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 chin2-kiu3;  In-ui7 khian5-seng5 e5 lang5 choat8--lah; se3-kan-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, tiong-sin3 e5 lang5 bo5--lah.
2)	Lang5-lang5 kap chhu3-piN kong2 peh8-chhat8;  Eng7 thiam2-mi7 e5 chhui3-tun5, kap nng7-iuN7 e5 sim lai5 kong2-oe7.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa beh koah-tng7 thiam2-mi7 e5 chhui3-tun5,  I2-kip8 kong2 toa7-oe7 e5 chih8.
4)	In bat kong2, Goan2 beh eng7 chih8 lai5 khah-iaN5;  Goan2 e5 chhui3-tun5 si7 goan2 e5;  chi7-chui7 oe7 choe3 goan2 e5 chu2 ah?
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, In-ui7 khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 e5 oan-ong2, kap song3-hiong lang5 e5 thou2-khui3,  Goa2 taN beh khi2--lai5, an-ti3 i ti7 i sou2 chhiat-chhiat him-bou7 un2-tang3 e5 sou2-chai7.
6)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 si7 sun5-choan5 chheng-khi3 e5 oe7;  Chhin-chhiuN7 gun5 ti7 thou5 e5 lou5 thoan3-lian7,  Thoan3-ke3 chhit-pai2.
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 beh po2-hou7 in,  Beh pi3-iu7 in, eng2-oan2 thoat-li7 chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5.
8)	Put-tiong3-iong7 lang5 ko-seng ti7 se3-kan-lang5 e5 tiong-kan,  Chiu7 phaiN2-lang5 tak8 sou2-chai7 teh kiaN5-iu5.

[13]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 boe7-ki3-tit goa2, beh joa7-ku2 ah? kau3 eng2-oan2 mah?  Li2 ng bin7 m7 khoaN3 goa2, beh joa7-ku2 ah?
2)	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 siuN7-lai5 siuN7-khi3, goa2 e5 sim thong-jit8 iu-khou2, beh kau3 joa7-ku2 ah?  Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 ko-seng iaN5-ke3 goa2 beh kau3 joa7-ku2 ah?
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 khoaN3-kou3 goa2, thiaN goa2;  Hou7 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu kng-beng5; kiaN-liau2 goa2 khun3 kau3 si2;
4)	KiaN-liau2 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 kong2, Goa2 khah-iaN5 i;  KiaN-liau2 goa2 e5 kiu5-siu5 ti7 goa2 io5-choah e5 si5 lai5 hoaN-hi2.
5)	Chong2-si7 goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3;  Goa2 e5 sim in-ui7 Li2 e5 chin2-kiu3 lai5 khoai3-lok8.
6)	Goa2 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  In-ui7 I eng7 toa7-un khoan2-thai7 goa2.

[14]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Gong7-lang5 sim-lai7 kong2, Bo5 u7 Siong7-te3.  In than3 sia5-ok, kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7;  Bo5 chit8-lang5 kiaN5-ho2.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 thiN aN3-loh8 khoaN3 se3-kan-lang5,  Beh khoaN3 u7 beng5-li2--e5, U7 chhe7-kiu5 Siong7-te3--e5 a2-bo5.
3)	In long2 oai-chhoah8, it-khai3 pian3-choe3 u3-oe3;  Bo5 lang5 kiaN5-ho2, lian5 chit8-e5 iah8 bo5.
4)	Choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5 kiam2 long2 boe7 hiau2-tit mah?  In thun-chiah8 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8 piaN2,  Iah8 bo5 kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
5)	In ti7-hia toa7-toa7 kiaN-hiaN5;  In-ui7 Siong7-te3 ti7 gi7-lang5 e5 chok8-lui7-tiong.
6)	Lin2 hou7 song3-hiong lang5 e5 ke3-bou5 piN3-choe3 kian3-siau3,  Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 i to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7.
7)	Goan7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chin2-kiu3 tui3 Sek-an chhut!  Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu3 I siu7-liah8 e5 peh-siN3 to3-tng2-lai5,  Hit-si5 Nga2-kok beh khoai3-lok8, I2-sek-liat8 beh hoaN-hi2.

[15]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, chi7-chui7 oe7 kia3-kha ti7 Li2 e5 pou3-piN5?  Chi7-chui7 oe7 khia7-khi2 ti7 Li2 e5 Seng3-soaN?
2)	Chiu7-si7 sou2 kiaN5 cheng3-tit8, sou2-choe3 kong-gi7,  Sim-lai7 kong2 seng5-sit8 e5 lang5.
3)	I bo5 eng7 chih8 ka-bu5 lang5,  Bo5 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 peng5-iu2,  Lang5 hui2-pong3 chhu3-piN, i bo5 si3-koe3 iau5.
4)	I e5 bak8-chiu khoaN3-khin hui2-lui7,  Chun-tiong7 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5.  I chiu3-choa7, sui-bong2 ka-ki7 khek-khui, iah8 bo5 pian3-oaN7.
5)	I gun5 chioh lang5 bo5 ui7-tioh8 li7-sek;  Bo5 siu7 pou3-lou7 lai5 hai7 bo5 choe7--e5;  KiaN5 chit-ho7 su7 e5 lang5 eng2-eng2 bo5 io5-choah.

[16]	Tai7-pit8 kim e5 si.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 po2-hou7 goa2; in-ui7 goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2.
2)	Goa2 e5 leng5 ah, li2 bat tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Chu2,  Li2 i2-goa7, goa2 bo5 hok-khi3.
3)	Lun7-kau3 toe7-chiuN7 seng3 e5 peh-siN3,  In si7 kek-ki5 ho2, si7 goa2 sou2 chhim-chhim hoaN-hi2 e5.
4)	Eng7 pat8 e5 sin5 thoe3-oaN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, in e5 iu-khou2 beh na2 ke-thiN;  In hian3 tian7-huih e5 che3, goa2 bo5 beh hian3;  Goa2 e5 chhui3-tun5 iah8 m7 the5-khi2 in e5 mia5.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 e5 san2-giap8, kap goa2 poe-tiong e5 hun7-giah8;  Goa2 sou2 eng3-tit--e5, Li2 ka7 goa2 kou3-siu2.
6)	Sou2 niu5 hou7 goa2 e5 toe7, si7 ti7 chin sui2 e5 sou2-chai7;  Goa2 e5 san2-giap8 sit8-chai7 chin ho2.
7)	Goa2 beh o-lo2 hit e5 ka3-si7 goa2 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Mi5--si5 goa2 e5 sim-tng5 iah8 chi2-tiam2 goa2.
8)	Goa2 siong5-siong5 keng3-hong7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  In-ui7 I ti7 goa2 e5 chiaN3-peng5, goa2 chiu7 bo5 io5-choah.
9)	In-ui7 an2-ni goa2 e5 sim hoaN-hi2, goa2 e5 sin5 khoai3-lok8;  Goa2 e5 jiok8-sin iah8 beh an-jian5 khia7-khi2.
10)	In-ui7 Li2 bo5 chiong goa2 e5 leng5-hun5 pang3-he7 ti7 im-kan;  Iah8 bo5 hou7 Li2 e5 seng3--e5 tu2-tioh8 hiu2-noa7.
11)	Li2 beh chiong oah8-mia7 e5 lou7 chi2-si7 goa2;  Ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 u7 moa2-chiok e5 hoaN-hi2;  Ti7 Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 u7 eng2-oan2 e5 khoai3-lok8.

[17]	Tai7-pit8 e5 ki5-to2.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 thiaN kong-gi7, liu5-sim thiaN goa2 e5 kiu5-kio3;  Goa2 e5 ki5-to2 m7-si7 tui3 kan-cha3 e5 chhui3-tun5 chhut; kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang lai5 thiaN.
2)	Goan7 goa2 e5 phoaN3-su5 tui3 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 hoat-chhut,  Goan7 Li2 e5 bak8-chiu kam3-chhat cheng3-tit8.
3)	Li2 i2-keng chhi3-giam7 goa2 e5 sim,  Li2 ti7 mi5--si5 kam3-chhat goa2;  Li2 thoan3-lian7 goa2, bo5 chhe7--tioh8 sim2-mih8;  Goa2 lip8-chi3, hou7 goa2 e5 chhui3 bo5 u7 ke3-sit.
4)	Lun7-kau3 lang5 e5 kiaN5-choe3, goa2 than3 Li2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7,  Ka-ki7 kin2-siu2, bo5 kiaN5 kiong5-ok lang5 e5 lou7.
5)	Goa2 e5 kha tiaN7-tiaN7 kiaN5 Li2 e5 lou7, Goa2 e5 kha be7-bat tah8-chhu7.
6)	Siong7-te3 ah, lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 bat kiu5-kio3 Li2, in-ui7 Li2 beh in3 goa2;  Kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 oe7.
7)	Kiu5 Li2 hian2-beng5 Li2 koh-iuN7 e5 jin5-chu5, Li2 si7 eng7 chiaN3-chhiu2 kiu3 oa2-kho3 Li2 e5 lang5,  Thoat-li7 hiah e5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek in--e5.
8)	Kiu5 Li2 po2-hou7 goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 po2-hou7 bak8-chiu-jin5,  Chiong goa2 kham3-bat8 ti7 Li2 e5 sit8-e7.
9)	Hou7 goa2 thoat-li7 hiah e5 chhiuN2-kiap goa2 e5 phaiN2-lang5,  Chiu7-si7 ui5-khun3 goa2, beh hai7 goa2 siN3-mia7 e5 tui3-tek8.
10)	In hou7 ka-ki7 e5 iu5 pau-bat8;  In e5 chhui3 kong2 kiau-ngou7 e5 oe7.
11)	In hian7-chai7 ui5-khun3 goan2 e5 kha-pou7;  In chu3-bak8 beh chhia-to2 goan2 ti7 toe7--nih.
12)	In chhin-chhiuN7 sai siau3-siuN7 beh ka7 mih8;  Koh chhin-chhiuN7 beng2 e5 sai-a2-thun5 bih ti7 am3-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7.
13)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 khi2--lai5, ti2-tng tui3-tek8;  Chiong i taN2-to2;  Eng7 Li2 e5 to kiu3 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 thoat-li7 phaiN2-lang5.
14)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, eng7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 se3-kan-lang5;  Thoat-li7 hiah e5 ti7 kim-seng u7 hok-hun7 e5 se3-kan-lang5.  Li2 chiong Li2 e5 chai5-po2 chhiong-moa2 in e5 pak-tou2;  In u7 kiaN2-ji5 kau3 sim-moa2 i3-chiok;  chiong ki5-u5 e5 chai5-but8 lau5 hou7 in e5 eN-a2.
15)	Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 beh ti7 gi7 e5 tiong-kan khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 e5 bin7;  Goa2 khun3-chhiN2 e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 e5 heng5-iong5, chiu7 sim-moa2 i3-chiok.

[18]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.  Tng Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu3 i thoat-li7 it-chhe3 e5 tui3-tek8, kap So3-lo5 e5 chhiu2 e5 jit8, i tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa liam7 chit e5 si e5 oe7; kong2,
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 khui3-lat8 ah, goa2 thiaN3 Li2.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 e5 soaN-giam5, goa2 e5 soaN-che7, goa2 e5 Kiu3-chu2;  Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 e5 chioh8-poaN5, goa2 beh oa2-kho3 I;  I si7 goa2 e5 tin5-pai5, si7 kiu3 goa2 e5 kak, si7 goa2 e5 koaiN5-tai5.
3)	Goa2 beh kiu5-kio3 eng-kai o-lo2 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Goa2 chiu7 tit-tioh8 kiu3 thoat-li7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8.
4)	Si2-bo5 e5 soh tiN5 goa2, Hui2-lui7 e5 toa7-chui2 hou7 goa2 kiaN.
5)	Im-kan e5 soh ui5-khun3 goa2, Si2-bo5 e5 lo5-bang7 lim5-kau3 goa2.
6)	Goa2 ti7 khou2-lan7-tiong ki5-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Tui3 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 kiu5-kio3;  I tui3 I e5 tian7-lai7 thiaN goa2 e5 siaN,  Goa2 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 kiu5--e5 jip8 ti7 I e5 hi7-khang.
7)	In-ui7 I siu7-khi3, toe7 chiu7 io5 koh choah;  SoaN e5 toe7-ki iah8 tin2-tang7 io5-choah.
8)	Tui3 I e5 phiN7-khang chheng3-chhut ian,  Tui3 I e5 chhui3-lai7 hoat-chhut he2,  Thou5-thoaN3 tui3 an2-ni toh8.
9)	I hou7 thiN sui5-loh8 ke7, pun2-sin lim5-kau3,  I e5 kha-e7 ou-am3-am3.
10)	I khia5 ki-lou7-peng teh pe;  I eng7 hong e5 sit8 kin2-kin2 pe.
11)	I eng7 ou-am3 choe3 bih-sin e5 sou2-chai7, choe3 tiuN3-pang5 lai5 ui5 I;  Chiu7-si7 chui2 e5 ou-am3, khong-tiong e5 bat8-hun5.
12)	In-ui7 I thau5-cheng5 e5 kng, chiu7 I e5 bat8-hun5 kiaN5 ke3-khi3,  U7 phauh8 kap toh8 e5 thou5-thoaN3.
13)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 thiN--nih khi2 lui5,  Chi3-koaiN5--e5 chhut I e5 siaN;  U7 phauh8 kap toh8 e5 thou5-thoaN3.
14)	I sia7-chhut I e5 chiN3, hou7 tui3-tek8 si3-soaN3;  Hoat-chhut choe7-choe7 sih-na3, hou7 in jiau2-loan7.
15)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 chek-pi7 chit8-e7 hoat,  Li2 e5 phiN7-khang e5 khi3 chit8-e7 chhut,  Chui2-toe2 chiu7 chhut-hian7,  Toa7-toe7 e5 kun-ki iah8 lou7-hian7.
16)	I tui3 teng2-bin7 chhun-chhiu2 khiu2 goa2,  Khan goa2 chhut toa7-chui2 e5 tiong-kan.
17)	I kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa2 beng2 e5 tui3-tek8,  I2-kip8 hiah e5 oan3-hun7 goa2 e5 lang5;  In-ui7 in pi2 goa2 khah-kiong5.
18)	Goa2 tu2-tioh8 chai-lan7 e5 jit8, in lai5 kong-kek goa2;  chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 sou2 oa2-kho3--e5.
19)	I iah8 chhoa7 goa2 kau3 khui-khoah e5 sou2-chai7,  I kiu3 goa2, in-ui7 I hoaN-hi2 goa2.
20)	Ia5-ho5-hoa chiau3 goa2 e5 gi7 po3-tap goa2;  Chiau3 goa2 chhiu2 e5 chheng-khi3 po3-siuN2 goa2.
21)	In-ui7 goa2 chun-siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 to7-lou7,  Be7-bat choe3-phaiN2, li7-khui goa2 e5 Siong7-te3.
22)	I e5 hoat-lut8 long2 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  I e5 le2-gi5, goa2 be7-bat khi3-sak.
23)	Goa2 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 choe3 oan5-choan5,  Goa2 iah8 po2-siu2 ka-ki7, li7-khui goa2 e5 choe7-ok.
24)	Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa po3-siuN2 goa2, si7 chiau3 goa2 e5 gi7;  Iah8 si7 chiau3 goa2 ti7 I e5 bak8-chiu cheng5, goa2 chhiu2 e5 chheng-khi3.
25)	Chu5-ai3 e5 lang5, Li2 eng7 chu5-ai3 khoan2-thai7 i;  Oan5-choan5 e5 lang5, Li2 eng7 oan5-choan5 khoan2-thai7 i;
26)	Chheng-khi3 e5 lang5, Li2 eng7 chheng-khi3 khoan2-thai7 i;  Koai7-phiah e5 lang5, Li2 eng7 oan-khiau khoan2-thai7 i.
27)	In-ui7 khun3-khou2 e5 peh-siN3, Li2 beh kiu3 i;  Chu7-ko e5 bak8-chiu, Li2 beh hou7 i he5--loh8-khi3.
28)	In-ui7 Li2 beh tiam2-toh8 goa2 e5 teng;  Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh chio3-kng goa2 e5 am3.
29)	In-ui7 goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2, chhiong-jip8 kun-tui7,  Oa2-kho3 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 thiau3-ke3 chhiuN5.
30)	Lun7-kau3 Siong7-te3, I e5 lou7 si7 oan5-choan5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 si7 ke3 thoan3-lian7--e5;  KiN3-na7 oa2-kho3 I--e5, I chiu7 choe3 in e5 tin5-pai5.
31)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-goa7, chi7-chui7 si7 Siong7-te3?  Goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 i2-goa7, chi7-chui7 si7 chioh8-poaN5?
32)	Chiu7-si7 hit e5 eng7 khui3-lat8 ha5 goa2 e5 io,  Hou7 goa2 e5 lou7 oan5-choan5 e5 Siong7-te3.
33)	I hou7 goa2 e5 kha chhin-chhiuN7 lok8-bu2 e5 kha,  Koh an-ti3 goa2 ti7 goa2 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7.
34)	I ka3-si7 goa2 e5 chhiu2 gau5 kau-chian3,  Ti3-kau3 goa2 e5 chhiu2-kut oe7 khui tang5 e5 keng.
35)	Li2 eng7 Li2 kiu3-un e5 tin5-pai5 hou7 goa2;  Li2 eng7 chiaN3-chhiu2 hu5-chhi5 goa2;  Li2 e5 un-ho5 hou7 goa2 choe3 toa7.
36)	Li2 hou7 goa2 sou2 tah8 e5 toe7 khui-khoah;  Goa2 e5 kha be7-bat tah8-chhu7.
37)	Goa2 beh tui goa2 e5 tui3-tek8, iah8 beh jip--tioh8 in;  In iau2-be7 biat8-bo5 e5 tai7-seng, goa2 bo5 beh to3-tng2.
38)	Goa2 beh phah in thiam2-thiam2, ti3-kau3 in boe7 khi2-lai5;  In beh to2 ti7 goa2 e5 kha-e7.
39)	In-ui7 Li2 bat eng7 khui3-lat8 ha5 goa2 e5 io, hou7 goa2 gau5 kau-chian3;  Li2 hou7 hiah e5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek goa2--e5, long2 hang5-hok8 ti7 goa2 e5 e7-bin7.
40)	Li2 iah8 hou7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 oat8-tng2-sin to5-chau2;  Hou7 goa2 oe7 chau5-biat8 hiah e5 oan3-hun7 goa2 e5 lang5.
41)	In kiu5-kio3, iah8 bo5 lang5 kiu3 in;  Chiu7 kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I iah8 bo5 in3.
42)	Goa2 tui5 in kau3 chhui3-chhui3, chhin-chhiuN7 hong chhe e5 thou5-hun2;  PiaN3-chhut in, chhin-chhiuN7 koe-lou7 e5 thou5-be5.
43)	Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 peh-siN3 e5 saN-chiN;  Li2 siat-lip8 goa2 choe3 liat8-pang e5 thau5;  Goa2 pun2-jian5 m7-bat e5 peh-siN3 beh hok8-sai7 goa2;
44)	In chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 goa2 e5 mia5 chiu7 beh sun7-than3 goa2; IN7-pang e5 lang5 beh tau5-hang5 goa2.
45)	IN7-pang lang5 beh soe-the3,  KiaN-hiaN5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, chhut in e5 iaN5-che7.
46)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 oah8--e5, goan7 goa2 e5 chioh8-poaN5 tit-tioh8 o-lo2;  Goan7 kiu3 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 tit-tioh8 seng-koaiN5.
47)	Chit e5 Siong7-te3 chiu7-si7 hit e5 ka7 goa2 sin-oan,  Hou7 cheng3 peh-siN3 hang5-hok8 ti7 goa2 e5 e7-bin7--e5.
48)	I kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8,  Li2 chiong goa2 ku2-khi2 khah koaiN5 hiah e5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek goa2 e5;  Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 kiong5-po7 e5 lang5.
49)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, in-ui7 an2-ni goa2 beh ti7 liat8-pang-tiong kam2-sia7 Li2;  ChhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5.
50)	Ia5-ho5-hoa siuN2-su3 kek8-toa7 e5 kiu3-un, hou7 I sou2 siat-lip8 e5 ong5;  Si-chhut chu5-ai3 hou7 I siu7-boah-iu5 e5,  Chiu7-si7 hou7 Tai7-pit8 kap i e5 hou7-e3, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.

[19]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Chiah e5 thiN kong2-khi2 Siong7-te3 e5 eng5-kng,  Kiong-chhong po3-iong5 I e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5.
2)	Chit-jit8 tui3 hit-jit8 hoat-chhut gian5-gu2,  Chit-mi5 tui3 hit-mi5 thoan5-chhut chai-bat.
3)	Bo5 gian5 bo5 gu2;  In e5 siaN bo5 thang thiaN-kiN3.
4)	In e5 chun2-chin5 pian3 ti7 thiN-e7,  In e5 gian5-gu2 kau3 ti7 toe7-kek8.  Siong7-te3 ti7 in tiong-kan ui7-tioh8 jit8-thau5 an-ti3 tiuN3-pang5.
5)	Jit8-thau5 chhin-chhiuN7 sin-kiaN2-sai3 chhut i e5 pang5,  Iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 beng2-iong2 e5 lang5 hoaN-hi2 chau2 i e5 lou7.
6)	I tui3 thiN e5 chit-peng5 chhut,  Seh8 kau3 thiN e5 hit-peng5;  Bo5 chit8-hang7-mih8 khng3-bat8, bo5 tit-tioh8 i e5 jiat8-khi3.
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lut8-hoat chiau5-chng5, oe7 hou7 lang5 e5 sim-sin5 oah8--khi2-lai5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 kan-cheng3 khak-sit8, oe7 hou7 gong7-lang5 u7 ti3-hui7.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 ka3-si7 cheng3-tit8, oe7 hou7 lang5 e5 sim hoaN-hi2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 chheng-kiat, oe7 hou7 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu kng-beng5.
9)	Keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 to7-li2 si7 chheng-khi3, eng2-oan2 chun5-chai7;  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 phoaN3-toan3 chin-sit8, it-khai3 si7 kong-gi7.
10)	Pi2 kim, pi2 choe7-choe7 ho2 kim, khah thang him-bou7;  Pi2 bit8, pi2 phang-pang5 tih--loh8-lai5 e5 bit8 khah-tiN.
11)	Koh Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 tui3 chiah-e5 siu7 keng2-kai3;  Siu2 chiah-e5 u7 toa7 siuN2-su3.
12)	Chi7-chui7 oe7 chai i e5 sit-chho3 ah?  Kiu5 Li2 tu5--khi3 goa2 am3-chiN7 e5 ke3-sit.
13)	Kiu5 Li2 chou2-chi2 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, bo5 kou3-i3 hoan7-choe7;  M7-chun2 hit e5 choe7-ok koan2-hat goa2;  Goa2 chiu7 oan5-choan5, bian2 hoan7 toa7-choe7.
14)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 chioh8-poaN5, kiu3-siok8 goa2 e5 Chu2 ah;  Goan7 goa2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2--e5, sim sou2 siuN7--e5, ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 chiap-lap8.

[20]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8 thiaN li2;  Goan7 Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5 an-ti3 li2 ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7;
2)	Tui3 seng3-sou2 pang-chan7 li2,  Tui3 Sek-an hu5-chhi5 li2.
3)	Ki3-liam7 li2 it-chhe3 sou2 hian3--e5,  Chiap-lap8 li2 e5 sio-che3. [Se3-lah8
4)	Chiau3 li2 e5 sim sou2-ai3-e5 hou7 li2,  ChiaN5 li2 it-chhe3 e5 ke3-ek8.
5)	Goan2 beh in-ui7 Li2 e5 kiu3-un lai5 chhiuN3-koa;  Goan2 beh hong7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5 lai5 khia7-ki5.  Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiaN5 li2 it-chhe3 sou2 kiu5--e5.
6)	TaN goa2 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu3 I siu7-boah-iu5--e5,  Beh tui3 I seng3 e5 thiN thiaN--i;  Eng7 i chiaN3-chhiu2 e5 khui3-lat8 kiu3 i.
7)	U7 lang5 oa2-kho3 chhia, u7 lang5 oa2-kho3 be2;  Tok8-tok8 goan2 beh kong2-khi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5.
8)	In phak-loh8 poah8-to2;  Goan2 chiu7 khi2--lai5 khia7 chai7-chai7.
9)	Kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa chin2-kiu3; Goan2 kiu5-kio3 e5 si5, goan7 Ong5 thiaN goan2.

[21]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, ong5 beh in-ui7 Li2 e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 hoaN-hi2.  In-ui7 Li2 e5 chin2-kiu3, i e5 khoai3-lok8 chaiN2-iuN7 e5 toa7!
2)	I e5 sim sou2-ai3--e5, Li2 i2-keng hou7 i;  I e5 chhui3 sou2 kiu5--e5, Li2 bo5 m7 un2 i. [Se3-lah8
3)	In-ui7 Li2 eng7 toa7 hok-khi3 ngia5-chih i,  Eng7 ho2-kim e5 bian2-liu5 ti3 ti7 i e5 thau5-khak.

5)	I in-ui7 Li2 e5 chin2-kiu3, u7 toa7 eng5-kng;  Li2 koh chiong chun-kui3 ui-giam5 he7 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7.
6)	Li2 hou7 i u7 toa7 hok-khi3, kau3 ti7 eng2-oan2;  Koh hou7 i ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8.
7)	In-ui7 ong5 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Ti7 Chi3-koaiN5--e5 e5 chu5-ai3 bo5 ti3-kau3 io5-choah.
8)	Li2 e5 chhiu2 beh chhe7-tioh8 Li2 it-chhe3 e5 tui3-tek8;  Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 beh chhe7-tioh8 hiah e5 oan3-hun7 Li2 e5 lang5.
9)	Li2 siu7-khi3 e5 si5, beh hou7 in chhin-chhiuN7 iam7-jiat8 e5 he2-lou5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ti7 I e5 toa7 siu7-khi3-tiong thun--in,  He2 beh ka7 in sio-lio--khi3.
10)	Li2 beh tui3 se3-chiuN7 chau5-biat8 in e5 kiaN2-sun;  Tui3 lang5 e5 tiong-kan chau5-biat8 in e5 hou7-e3.
11)	In-ui7 in u7 i3-su3 beh hai7 Li2;  In siat ke3-bou5, chong2-si7 boe7 chiaN5.
12)	Li2 beh hou7 in oat8-tng2-sin chau2,  Li2 beh khui keng, sia7 in e5 bin7.
13)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goan7 Li2 tui3 Li2 e5 khui3-lat8 seng-koaiN5;  An2-ni goan2 beh gim5-si o-lo2 Li2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5.

[22]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, eng7 "Cha2-khi2 si5 e5 lok8-bu2".
1)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, siaN2-su7 pang3-li7 goa2?  SiaN2-su7 li7-khui hng7-hng7, bo5 kiu3 goa2; m7-thiaN goa2 au5-kio3 e5 oe7?
2)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 jit8--si5 kiu5-kio3, Li2 bo5 thiaN goa2;  Mi5--si5 kiu5-kio3, goa2 iah8 bo5 cheng7-cheng7.
3)	Chong2-si7 Li2 si7 seng3,  Li2 si7 eng7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 o-lo2 choe3 cho7-ui7--e5.
4)	Goan2 e5 liat8-chou2 oa2-kho3 Li2,  In oa2-kho3 Li2, Li2 chiu7 chin2-kiu3 in.
5)	In ai-kiu5 Li2, chiu7 tit-tioh8 chin2-kiu3;  In oa2-kho3 Li2 chiu7 put-ti3 kian3-siau3.
6)	Chong2-si7 goa2 si7 thang5-thoa7, m7-si7 lang5;  Hou7 lang5 ki-chhi3, hou7 peh-siN3 khoaN3-khin.
7)	Hoan7-na7 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 e5, long2 thi2-chhio3 goa2;  In ngiauh-chhui3 io5-thau5, kong2,
8)	Tioh8 chiong pun2-sin kau-tai3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I thang kiu3--i;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ki3-jian5 hoaN-hi2 i, I thang kiu3--i.
9)	Chong2-si7 Li2 si7 hou7 goa2 chhut lau7-bu2 e5 thai--e5,  Goa2 ti7 lau7-bu2 e5 heng-cheng5, Li2 hou7 goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2.
10)	Goa2 tui3 thai--nih chhut, chiu7 kau-tai3 Li2;  Tui3 goa2 chhut lau7-bu2 e5 pak-tou2, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3.
11)	M7-thang li7-khui goa2 hng7-hng7; in-ui7 hoan7-lan7 pek-kun7,  Bo5 u7 pang-chan7 goa2 e5.
12)	U7 choe7-choe7 gu5-kang2 ui5-lui5 goa2;  Pa-san iong2 e5 gu5 si3-bin7 ui5-khun3 goa2.
13)	In ng3 goa2 khui-chhui3,  Chhin-chhiuN7 teh peh-thiah, teh toa7-siaN hau2 e5 sai.
14)	Goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 chui2 piaN3-chhut,  Goa2 e5 kut long2 thut8-lun5;  Goa2 e5 sim chhin-chhiuN7 lah8,  Siau-iuN5 ti7 pak-lai7.
15)	Goa2 e5 cheng-lek8 kou-ta5, chhin-chhiuN7 hau7-phiaN-phe3;  Goa2 e5 chih8 liam5 ti7 goa2 e5 chiuN7-kiuN;  Li2 he7 goa2 ti7 si2-toe7 e5 thou5-hun2.
16)	Kau2 e5 lui7 ui5 goa2;  PhaiN2-tong2 pau-ui5 goa2;  In chhak8 goa2 e5 chhiu2, goa2 e5 kha.
17)	Goa2 e5 kut-thau5, goa2 long2 oe7 sng3-tit;  In teh khoaN3 goa2, teh siong3 goa2.
18)	In pun goa2 e5 saN,  Liam-khau goa2 e5 i-hok8.
19)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang li7-khui goa2 hng7-hng7;  Goa2 e5 khui3-lat8 ah, kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 lai5 pang-chan7 goa2.
20)	Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 thoat-li7 to-kiam3;  Kiu3 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 thoat-li7 kau2 e5 lui7 e5 se3-lek8.
21)	Kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 sai e5 chhui3;  Li2 i2-keng thiaN goa2, hou7 goa2 thoat-li7 ia2-gu5 e5 kak.
22)	Goa2 beh po3-iong5 Li2 e5 mia5 ti7 goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7;  Goa2 beh o-lo2 Li2 ti7 hoe7-tiong.
23)	Lin2 kiaN-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5, tioh8 o-lo2 I;  Nga2-kok e5 hou7-e3, long2 tioh8 eng5-kng I.  I2-sek-liat8 e5 hou7-e3, long2 tioh8 keng3-ui3 I.
24)	In-ui7 I bo5 khoaN3-khin, iah8 bo5 iam3-chian7, khun3-khou2 lang5 e5 khun3-khou2;  Iah8 bo5 tui3 i ng-bin7;  I kiu5-kio3 I e5 si5, I chiu7 thiaN i.
25)	Goa2 ti7 toa7 chu7-hoe7 e5 tiong-kan sou2 o-lo2--e5, si7 tui3 li2 lai5;  Goa2 beh ti7 kiaN-ui3 I e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, sia7 goa2 e5 goan7.
26)	Khiam-pi e5 lang5 beh tit-tioh8 chiah8-pa2;  Chhe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5 beh o-lo2 I;  Goan7 lin2 e5 sim oah8 kau3 eng2-oan2.
27)	Toe7 e5 kek8-thau5 long2 beh siau3-liam7, lai5 kui-sun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Liat8-pang e5 ban7-chok8 long2 beh keng3-pai3 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
28)	In-ui7 kok si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5;  I si7 ban7-kok e5 chu2-chaiN2.
29)	Toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 ho2-han3 e5 lang5 beh lim chiah8 lai5 keng3-pai3;  KiN3-na7 kui-thou2 e5 lang5, boe7-oe7 po2-choan5 siN3-mia7--e5, long2 beh phak-pai3 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5.
30)	U7 hou7-e3 beh hok8-sai7 I;  Chu2 e5 tai7-chi3 beh thoan5 ti7 au7-tai7.
31)	In beh lai5, iah8 beh thoan5 I e5 kong-gi7,  Hou7 tit-beh chhut-si3 e5 peh-siN3 chai chit e5 su7 si7 I choe3--e5.

[23]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 e5 bok8-chia2, goa2 bo5 khiam3-kheh.

[24]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.

[25]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 e5 sim-sin5 giong2-bong7 Li2.
2)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 peng5-sou3 oa2-kho3 Li2, m7-thang hou7 goa2 kian3-siau3.  M7-thang hou7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 in-ui7 iaN5 goa2 lai5 khoa-khau2.

7)	Kiu5 Li2 m7-thang ki3-liam7 goa2 siau3-lian5 e5 che7-koa3, kap goa2 e5 ke3-sit;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3, in-ui7 Li2 e5 un-hui7 ki3-liam7 goa2.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 ho2 koh cheng3-tit8;  Sou2-i2 I beh chi2-si7 choe7-jin5 kiaN5 chiaN3-lou7.
9)	I beh eng7 kong-peng5 in2-chhoa7 khiam-sun3 e5 lang5,  I beh eng7 I e5 to7-lou7 ka3-si7 khiam-sun3 e5 lang5.
10)	KiN3-na7 siu2 I e5 iok, kap I e5 kan-cheng3 e5 lang5,  Ia5-ho5-hoa khoan2-thai7 in long2 si7 eng7 chu5-ai3 seng5-sit8.
11)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 e5 choe7 chin tang7;  Kiu5 Li2 in-ui7 Li2 e5 mia5 sia3-bian2 goa2.
12)	Sim2-mih8 lang5 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa?  Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chi2-si7 i sou2 tioh8 keng2 e5 lou7.
13)	I e5 sim-sin5 beh tit-tioh8 an-hioh;  I e5 hou7-e3 beh seng5-chiap thou2-toe7.
14)	Ia5-ho5-hoa kap keng3-ui3 I e5 lang5 chhin-bit8;  Koh beh chiong I e5 iok chi2-si7 in.
15)	Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu siong5-siong5 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  In-ui7 I beh hou7 goa2 e5 kha thoat-li7 lo5-bang7.
16)	Kiu5 Li2 oat8-tng2 ng3 goa2, kho2-lin5 goa2;  In-ui7 goa2 si7 kou-toaN koh khun3-khou2.
17)	Goa2 e5 sim-lai7 e5 iu-khou2 chin choe7,  Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 ti7 goa2 long2-chong2 e5 hoan7-lan7.
18)	Kiu5 Li2 khoaN3 goa2 e5 kan-lan5 kap goa2 e5 lo5-khou2;  Sia3-bian2 goa2 it-chhe3 e5 choe7.
19)	Kiu5 Li2 khoaN3 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8, in-ui7 in chin choe7;  In oan3-hun7 goa2 chin ok-tok8.
20)	Kiu5 Li2 po2-hou7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7, chin2-kiu3 goa2;  Hou7 goa2 bo5 kian3-siau3, in-ui7 goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2.
21)	Goan7 sun5-choan5 cheng3-tit8 po2-hou7 goa2,  In-ui7 goa2 theng3-hau7 Li2.
22)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kiu3-siok8 I2-sek-liat8,  Thoat-li7 i it-chhe3 e5 kan-khou2.

[26]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 ka7 goa2 phoaN3-toan3; in-ui7 goa2 u7 chiau3 goa2 e5 sun5-choan5 lai5 kiaN5;  Goa2 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 io5-choah.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 kam3-chhat goa2, chhi3-giam7 goa2;  Thoan3-lian7 goa2 e5 sim-tng5.
3)	In-ui7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 siong5-siong5 ti7 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5;  Goa2 iah8 u7 chiau3 Li2 e5 chin-li2 kiaN5.
4)	Goa2 be7-bat kap hong-ham3 e5 lang5 saN-kap che7;  Iah8 bo5 kap ke2-choe3 e5 lang5 choe3-tin7.
5)	Goa2 oan3-hun7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 hoe7;  Bo5 beh kap ok-tok8 e5 lang5 tang5 che7.
6)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 beh soe2 chhiu2 piau2-beng5 goa2 e5 bo5 choe7,  Chiah lai5 seh8 Li2 e5 che3-toaN5;
7)	Thang hou7 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 kam2-sia7 e5 siaN,  Koh thang kong2-khi2 Li2 it-chhe3 ki5-biau7 e5 sou2-choe3.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 thiaN3-sioh Li2 sou2 toa3 e5 chhu3;  I2-kip8 Li2 eng5-kng sou2 ti7-teh e5 sou2-chai7.
9)	M7-thang chiong goa2 e5 leng5-hun5 kap choe7-jin5 choe3 chit8-e7 siu-sip8--khi3;  M7-thang chiong goa2 e5 oah8-mia7 kap thai5-lang5--e5 choe3 chit8-e7 siu-sip8--khi3.
10)	In e5 chhiu2-tiong u7 kan-ok;  In e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 moa2-moa2 pou3-lou7.
11)	Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 beh chiau3 goa2 e5 sun5-choan5 lai5 kiaN5;  Kiu5 Li2 kiu3-siok8 goa2, lin5-bin2 goa2.
12)	Goa2 e5 kha khia7 ti7 piN5-thaN2 e5 sou2-chai7,  Ti7 cheng3-hoe7-tiong, goa2 beh o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[27]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 e5 kng, si7 goa2 e5 chin2-kiu3; goa2 beh kiaN chi7-chui7?  Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 oah8-mia7 e5 khui3-lat8; goa2 beh kiaN chi7-chui7?	
2)	Hiah e5 choe3 phaiN2 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 goa2 e5 kiu5-siu5, goa2 e5 tui3-tek8, lai5 kong-kek goa2, beh chiah8 goa2 e5 bah,  Hit-si5 in chiu7 tioh8-tak poah8-to2.
3)	Sui-jian5 u7 kun-peng chat-iaN5, beh kong-kek goa2,  Goa2 e5 sim iah8 bo5 kiaN-hiaN5;  Sui-jian5 heng-khi2 to-peng kong-kek goa2,  Goa2 iu5-goan5 chu7-chai7.
4)	U7 chit8 hang7 su7 goa2 bat tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu5, goa2 iu5-goan5 ti3-i3 ai3 tit-tioh8;  Chiu7-si7 chit8-si3-lang5 khia7-khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3,  KhoaN3 I e5 eng5-kng, siau3-liam7 I e5 tian7.
5)	In-ui7 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8, I beh am3-chiN7 po2-hou7 goa2 ti7 I e5 tiuN3-ui5 lai7;  Chiong goa2 khng3 ti7 I pou3-piN5 kham3-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7;  Ku2-khi2 goa2 ti7 chioh8-poaN5-teng2.
6)	TaN goa2 e5 thau5-khak tit-tioh8 kiah8-khi2, khah-koaiN5 ti7 goa2 si3-bin7 e5 tui3-tek8;  Goa2 beh ti7 I e5 pou3-piN5 hian3 hoaN-hi2 e5 che3;  Goa2 beh gim5-si, iah8 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 chhut-siaN kiu5-kio3 e5 si5, kiu5 Li2 thiaN;  Koh kiu5 Li2 lin5-bin2 goa2, in3 goa2.
8)	Li2 bat kong2, Lin2 tioh8 him-bou7 kiN3 Goa2 e5 bin7; hit-si5 goa2 e5 sim tui3 Li2 kong2,  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 beh him-bou7 kiN3 Li2 e5 bin7.
9)	M7-thang tui3 goa2 ng Li2 e5 bin7;  M7-thang siu7-khi3 lai5 koaN2 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8;  Li2 peng5-sou3 si7 choe3 goa2 e5 pang-chan7;  Kiu3 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, m7-thang pang3-sak goa2, iah8 m7-thang li7-khui goa2.
10)	In-ui7 pe7-bu2 li7-khui goa2, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh siu-liu5 goa2.
11)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 to7-lou7 chi2-si7 goa2;  In-ui7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 e5 ian5-kou3, chhoa7 goa2 ti7 piN5-thaN2 e5 lou7.
12)	M7-thang chiong goa2 kau hou7 tui3-tek8, chiaN5 in e5 sim-goan7;  In-ui7 lam7-sam2 kan-cheng3 e5 lang5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek goa2, in iah8 thou3-chhut hiong-ok e5 oe7.
13)	Goa2 na7 m7-sin3 ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7 tit-tioh8 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 un-hui7,  Chiu7 tek-khak choat8-bang7.
14)	Tioh8 theng3-hau7 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Tioh8 iong2-chong3, li2 e5 sim tioh8 kian-kou3;  Sit8-chai7 tioh8 theng3-hau7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[28]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 beh kiu5-kio3 Li2;  Goa2 e5 chioh8-poaN5 ah, m7-thang bo5 beh thiaN goa2.  Na7 Li2 tui3 goa2 cheng7-cheng7,  Goa2 chiu7 chhin-chhiuN7 jip8 bong7 e5 lang5 chit8-iuN7.
2)	Goa2 kiu5-kio3 Li2, ng3 Li2 e5 chi3-seng3-sou2 kiah8 chhiu2 e5 si5, kiu5 Li2 thiaN goa2 khun2-kiu5 e5 siaN.
3)	M7-thang chiong goa2 kap phaiN2-lang5, i2-kip8 chok-giat8 e5 lang5, choe3 chit8-e7 tu5--khi3.  In kap chhu3-piN kong2 ho5-peng5 e5 oe7, chong2-si7 in e5 sim kan-hiam2.
4)	Goan7 Li2 chiau3 in sou2 choe3--e5, ia7 chiau3 in sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2-tai7, khoan2-thai7 in;  Goan7 Li2 chiau3 in e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5, khoan2-thai7 in;  Chiong in sou2 eng-kai tu2-tioh8-e5 po3-eng3 in.
5)	In ki3-jian5 bo5 liu5-sim ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kiaN5--e5,  I2-kip8 I e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5;  I chiu7 beh hui2-hoai7 in, bo5 beh kian3-lip8 in.
6)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 eng-kai o-lo2--e5,  In-ui7 I thiaN goa2 khun2-kiu5 e5 siaN.
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 e5 khui3-lat8, iah8 si7 goa2 e5 tin5-pai5.  Goa2 e5 sim oa2-kho3 I, goa2 chiu7 tit-tioh8 pang-chan7.  Sou2-i2 goa2 e5 sim toa7 hoaN-hi2;  Goa2 beh eng7 goa2 e5 si-koa o-lo2 I.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 I e5 peh-siN3 e5 khui3-lat8;  Ia7 si7 I siu7 boah-iu5--e5 tit-kiu3 e5 oe7-sou2.
9)	Kiu5 Li2 chin2-kiu3 Li2 e5 peh-siN3, su3-hok Li2 e5 san2-giap8,  IuN2-chhi7 in, hu5-chhi5 in, kau3 ti7 eng2-oan2.

[29]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Toa7 koan5-leng5--e5 e5 kiaN2 ah, lin2 tioh8 chiong eng5-kng khui3-lat8 kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
2)	Tioh8 chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 sou2 eng-kai tit-tioh8 e5 eng5-kng kui hou7 I.  Eng7 seng3-kiat e5 chng-thaN7 keng3-pai3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN ti7 chui2-bin7;  Eng5-kng e5 Siong7-te3 khi2 lui5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 choe7-choe7 chui2 e5 teng2-bin7.
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN u7 toa7 khui3-lat8;  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN moa2-moa2 ui-giam5.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN phah-chih8 pek-hiuN-chhiu7;  Ia5-ho5-hoa phah-chhui3 Li7-pa-lun3 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7.
6)	I iah8 hou7 i tio5-thiau3 chhin-chhiuN7 gu5-a2;  Hou7 Li7-pa-lun3 kap Se-lian5 tio5-thiau3 chhin-chhiuN7 ia2-gu5 e5 kiaN2.
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN hou7 he2-iam7 pun-chhe.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN tin2-tang7 khong3-ia2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa tin2-tang7 Ka-te-su e5 khong3-ia2.
9)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN hou7 lok8-bu2 kiaN-tioh8, lai5 siN-kiaN2;  Iah8 hou7 chhiu7-na5 e5 chhiu7-hioh8 lak kng-kng;  KiN3-na7 ti7 tian7-lai7--e5 long2 kong2, Eng5-kng.
10)	Toa7-chui2 hoan3-lam7 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa che7-teh choe3 ong5,  Ia5-ho5-hoa che7-teh choe3 ong5, tit8 kau3 eng2-oan2.
11)	Ia5-ho5-hoa beh siuN2-su3 khui3-lat8 hou7 I e5 peh-siN3;  Ia5-ho5-hoa beh eng7 peng5-an su3-hok I e5 peh-siN3.

[30]	 Chit e5 si si7 hian3 kiong-tian7 e5 koa; Tai7-pit8 choe3--e5.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 beh chun-tiong7 Li2 choe3 chi3-koaiN5, in-ui7 Li2 bat the5-poat8 goa2,  Bo5 hou7 goa2 e5 kiu5-siu5 tui3 goa2 khoa-khau2.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah,  Goa2 bat kiu5-kio3 Li2, Li2 chiu7 i-ho2 goa2.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 bat kiu3 goa2 e5 leng5-hun5 tui3 im-kan khi2--lai5.  Li2 hou7 goa2 oah8-teh, bian2-ti3 jip8 bong7.
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa seng3 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 I,  Ki3-liam7 I e5 seng3 mia5 lai5 kam2-sia7 I.
5)	In-ui7 I e5 siu7-khi3 put-ko3 bak8-nih-ku2;  I e5 un-tian2 si7 it-seng e5 ku2;  Kui-mi5 sui-jian5 u7 thi5-khau3,  Cha2-khi2 si5 chiu7 u7 hoaN-hi2.
6)	Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 ti7 heng-thong e5 si5 chiu7 kong2,  Goa2 eng2 boe7 io5-choah.
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 bat si-un, hou7 goa2 e5 soaN khia7-chai7 kian-kou3,  Li2 ng Li2 e5 bin7, goa2 chiu7 peh-pak.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 kiu5-kio3 Li2;  Goa2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu5 un, kong2,
9)	Goa2 lau5-huih, goa2 jip8 bong7, u7 siaN2 li7-ek?  Tin5-ai kiam2 oe7 o-lo2 Li2?  kiam2 oe7 po3-iong5 Li2 e5 chin-sit8 mah?
10)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 thiaN goa2, lin5-bin2 goa2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 pang-chan7 goa2.
11)	Li2 i2-keng chiong goa2 e5 thi5-khau3 pian3-choe3 thiau3-bu2;  Li2 chiong goa2 e5 moa5-saN thng3--khi3, eng7 hoaN-hi2 ka7 goa2 ha5;
12)	Thang hou7 goa2 e5 sim-sin5 chhiuN3-koa, o-lo2 Li2, iah8 bo5 cheng7-cheng7. Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 beh kam2-sia7 Li2, kau3 eng2-oan2.

[31]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2, kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 eng2-eng2 bo5 kian3-siau3;  Chiau3 Li2 e5 kong-gi7 chin2-kiu3 goa2.
2)	Kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2, kin2-kin2 lai5 kiu3 goa2;  Choe3 goa2 kian-kou3 e5 chioh8-poaN5, choe3 chin2-kiu3 goa2 e5 oe7-sou2.
3)	In-ui7 Li2 si7 goa2 e5 soaN-giam5, goa2 e5 soaN-che7.  Sou2-i2 kiu5 Li2 in-ui7 Li2 e5 mia5 lai5 in2-chhoa7 goa2, chi2-tiam2 goa2.
4)	Lang5 am3-chiN7 tiuN lo5-bang7 beh bang7 goa2, kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7;  In-ui7 Li2 si7 goa2 e5 oe7-sou2.
5)	Goa2 chiong goa2 e5 leng5-hun5 kau ti7 Li2 e5 chhiu2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa chin-sit8 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 u7 kiu3-siok8 goa2.
6)	Goa2 oan3-hun7 hiah e5 sin3-hong7 hu-ke2 e5 lang5;  Tok8-tok8 goa2 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
7)	Goa2 in-ui7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 beh hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8;  In-ui7 Li2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 e5 kan-khou2,  Chai goa2 sim-sin5 e5 kan-lan5.
8)	Li2 be7-bat chiong goa2 kau ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2;  Li2 hou7 goa2 e5 kha khia7 ti7 khui-khoah e5 sou2-chai7.
9)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 ti7 hoan7-lan7 tiong, kiu5 Li2 lin5-bin2 goa2;  Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu in-ui7 iu-bun7 phah-phaiN2,  goa2 e5 sim-sin5, goa2 e5 sin-the2, iah8 si7 an2-ni.
10)	Goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 in-ui7 iu-khou2 lai5 siau-bo5;  Goa2 e5 ni5-he3 ui7-tioh8 thou2-khui3 iah8 an2-ni;  Goa2 e5 khui3-lat8 in-ui7 goa2 e5 choe7-ok lai5 soe-lam2;  Goa2 e5 kut-thau5 iah8 kou-ta5.
11)	Goa2 in-ui7 goa2 it-chhe3 e5 tui3-tek8 chiaN5-choe3 leng5-jiok8;  Ti7 goa2 e5 chhu3-piN-tau koh-khah siong-tiong7; hiah e5 bat goa2 e5 lang5 long2 kiaN goa2;  Ti7 goa7-bin7 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 e5 lang5 chau2-siam2 li7-khui goa2.
12)	Goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 si2-lang5 hou7 lang5 boe7 ki3-tit, bo5 lang5 siau3-liam7;  Goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 phoa3-chhui3 e5 khi2-ku7.
13)	In-ui7 goa2 thiaN-kiN3 choe7-choe7 lang5 e5 hui2-pong3,  Si3-ui5 long2 si7 kiaN-hiaN5;  In saN-kap chham-siong5 kong-kek goa2 e5 si5,  Chiu7 ke3-bou5 beh hai7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7.
14)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 iu5-goan5 oa2-kho3 Li2;  Goa2 kong2, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3.
15)	Goa2 e5 cho-gu7 ti7 Li2 e5 chhiu2;  Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2, i2-kip8 khun2-pek goa2 e5 lang5.
16)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 Li2 e5 bin7 chio3-kng Li2 e5 lou5-pok8;  Chiau3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 chin2-kiu3 goa2.
17)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 bo5 kian3-siau3; in-ui7 goa2 u7 kiu5-kio3 Li2.  Kiu5 Li2 hou7 phaiN2-lang5 kian3-siau3, hou7 in ti7 im-kan cheng7 chauh-chauh.
18)	Goan7 Li2 hou7 hiah e5 peh8-chhat8 e5 chhui3 pian3 e2-kau2;  Chiu7-si7 kiau-ngou7 khoaN3-khin, lam7-sam2 bu2-ban7 gi7-lang5--e5.
19)	Keng3-ui3 Li2 e5 lang5, Li2 ui7-tioh8 in sou2 chek-chu7 e5 un-hui7,  Ui7-tioh8 oa2-kho3 Li2 e5 lang5, ti7 se3-kan-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, sou2 si-heng5 e5 un-hui7, chaiN2-iuN7 hiah toa7!
20)	Li2 beh chiong in khng3 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 un2-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7; bian2-ti3 tu2-tioh8 lang5 e5 ke3-bou5;  Li2 beh am3-chiN7 po2-siu2 in ti7 tiuN3-ui5-lai7, bian2 siu7 chhui3-chih8 e5 cheng-pian7.
21)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 eng-kai o-lo2--e5,  In-ui7 I ti7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5 tui3 goa2 si-chhut I ki5-biau7 e5 chu5-ai3.
22)	Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 bat tioh8-kip kong2, Tui3 Li2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, goa2 siu7 keh-tng7;  Chong2-si7 goa2 kiu5-kio3 Li2 e5 si5, Li2 iu5-goan5 thiaN goa2 khun2-kiu5 e5 siaN.
23)	Ia5-ho5-hoa seng3 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 long2 tioh8 thiaN3 I;  Ia5-ho5-hoa po2-siu2 seng5-sit8 e5 lang5,  Tang7-tang7 po3-eng3 kiaN5 kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5.
24)	KiN3-na7 ng3-bang7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5,  Lin2 tioh8 chong3-taN2, lin2 e5 sim tioh8 kian-kou3.

[32]	Tai7-pit8 e5 ka3-si7 e5 si.
1)	Ke3-sit tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2, choe7-koa3 tit-tioh8 jia-kham3--e5, che lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 sng3 i choe3 u7 choe7,  I e5 sim bo5 kan-cha3--e5, che lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
3)	Goa2 cheng7-cheng7 e5 si5, goa2 e5 kut-thau5 kou-ta5;  In-ui7 goa2 thong-jit8 toa7-siaN hau2.
4)	In-ui7 mi5-jit8 Li2 e5 chhiu2 tang7-tang7 chhih8 goa2;  Goa2 e5 cheng-ek8 piN3 chhin-chhiuN7 he7-thiN e5 ta-so3. [Se3-lah8
5)	Goa2 tui3 Li2 pai5-liat8 goa2 e5 choe7-koa3, bo5 un2-moa5 goa2 e5 choe7-ok;  Goa2 kong2, Goa2 beh tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa seng5-jin7 goa2 e5 ke3-sit;  Li2 chiu7 sia3-bian2 goa2 hoan7-hoat e5 choe7. [Se3-lah8
6)	In-ui7 an2-ni, kiN3-na7 khian5-seng5 e5 lang5, ti7 thang chhe7--tioh8 Li2 e5 si5, tioh8 ki5-to2 Li2.  Toa7-chui2 hoan3-lam7 e5 si5, tek-khak boe7 kau3 i hia.
7)	Li2 si7 goa2 siam2-bih e5 sou2-chai7;  Li2 beh pi3-iu7 goa2 thoat-li7 kan-khou2;  Li2 beh eng7 tit-kiu3 e5 koa si3-bin7 ui5 goa2. [Se3-lah8
8)	Goa2 beh ka3-si7 li2, chi2-si7 li2 eng-kai kiaN5 e5 lou7;  Goa2 beh chu3-bak8 khoaN3 li2, lai5 khoan3-kai3 li2.
9)	M7-thang chhin-chhiuN7 be2, lo5, in bo5 ti3-sek;  Tioh8 eng7 be2-ka-kiuN be2-lek8-soh iok-sok--in,  Na7 bo5, in chiu7 m7 oa2-kun7 li2.
10)	PhaiN2-lang5 siu7 choe7-choe7 khou2-lan7;  tok8-tok8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5 beh u7 chu5-ai3 si3-bin7 ui5 i.
11)	Lin2 gi7-lang5 ah, tioh8 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8;  Sim cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5 ah, lin2 tioh8 chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.

[33]	Lin2 gi7-lang5 ah, tioh8 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 hoaN-hi2;  Cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5 e5 o-lo2 si7 hap8-gi5.
2)	Lin2 tioh8 toaN5-khim5 kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Eng7 chap8-tiau5 hian5 e5 sek o-lo2 I.
3)	Tioh8 tui3 I chhiuN3 sin e5 koa,  ToaN5 kau3 chin ho2, siaN-im hiang2-liang7.
4)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 gian5-gu2 cheng3-tit8;  Hoan7 I sou2 choe3--e5, it-chin7 si7 seng5-sit8.
5)	I hoaN-hi2 gi7-li2 kap kong-peng5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chu5-ai3 moa2-moa2 ti7 toe7-chiuN7.
6)	Chiah e5 thiN tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lai5 cho7,  ThiN--nih e5 ban7-lui7 tui3 I e5 chhui3 e5 khi3 lai5 chiaN5.
7)	I chu7-chip8 hai2-chui2 chhin-chhiuN7 kui-tui,  Siu-khng3 chhim-ian ti7 khou3-pang5.
8)	Choan5-toe7 tioh8 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Hoan7-na7 khia7-khi2 ti7 se3-chiuN7--e5, long2 tioh8 kiaN I.
9)	In-ui7 I kong2-chhut chiu7 u7;  I beng7-leng7 chiu7 khia7-chai7.
10)	Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 liat8-pang e5 ke3-ek8 kui ti7 khang-khang;  Hou7 cheng3 peh-siN3 sou2 siuN7--e5, bo5 kong-hau7.
11)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 ke3-ek8 eng2-oan2 khia7-chai7,  I e5 sim sou2 siuN7--e5 kau3 ban7 se3-tai7.
12)	Jin7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 i e5 Siong7-te3--e5, hit kok u7 hok-khi3;  I keng2-soan2 choe3 I e5 san2-giap8--e5, hit e5 peh-siN3 u7 hok-khi3.
13)	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 thiN teh khoaN3;  I kam3-chhat long2-chong2 e5 se3-kan lang5.
14)	I tui3 I khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 ng3 goa7-bin7,  KhoaN3 toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3.
15)	I si7 cho7-chiaN5 in cheng3-lang5 e5 sim--e5,  Liu5-sim ti7 in it-chhe3 e5 sou2-choe3--e5.
16)	Kun-ong5 boe7-oe7 in-ui7 peng choe7 tit-tioh8 kiu3;  Beng2-lang5 boe7-oe7 in-ui7 khui3-lat8 toa7 tit-tioh8 kiu3-chhut.
17)	Oa2-kho3 be2 tit-tioh8 kiu3, si7 bo5 chhai2-kang;  Boe7-oe7 eng7 i e5 toa7 lat8 lai5 kiu3 lang5.
18)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bak8-chiu khoaN3 keng3-ui3 I e5 lang5,  KhoaN3 ng3-bang7 I e5 chu5-ai3 e5 lang5;
19)	Beh kiu3 in e5 siN3-mia7 thoat-li7 si2-bo5,  Po2-chun5 in e5 oah8-mia7 ti7 ki-hng e5 si5.
20)	Goan2 e5 sim-sin5 peng5-sou3 theng3-hau7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  I si7 choe3 goan2 e5 pang-chan7, choe3 goan2 e5 tin5-pai5.
21)	Goan2 e5 sim beh oa2-kho3 I lai5 hoaN-hi2,  In-ui7 goan2 peng5-sou3 oa2-kho3 I e5 seng3-mia5.
22)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goan7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 lim5-kau3 goan2,  Chiau3 goan2 sou2 ng3-bang7 Li2 e5.

[34]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si; chiu7-si7 i ti7 A-pi3-bi2-lek8 e5 bin7-cheng5 ke2 hong-tian, siu7 koaN2--chhut-khi3 e5 si5 sou2 choe3--e5.
1)	Goa2 beh si5-si5 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  O-lo2 I e5 oe7 beh siong5-siong5 ti7 goa2 e5 chhui3.
2)	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 beh in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 khoa-khau2;  Khiam-pi e5 lang5 thiaN-kiN3, iah8 beh hoaN-hi2.
3)	Lin2 kap goa2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 toa7,  SaN-kap chun I e5 mia5 choe3 koaiN5.
4)	Goa2 bat kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I chiu7 in3 goa2;  Kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa2 it-chhe3 thang kiaN e5 su7.
5)	In kiah8-thau5 khoaN3 I, chiu7 tit-tioh8 kng-beng5;  In e5 bin7 eng2 boe7 kian3-siau3.
6)	Chit e5 khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 kiu5-kio3, Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3;  Kiu3 i thoat-li7 i it-chhe3 e5 hoan7-lan7.
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 ti7 keng3-ui3 I e5 lang5 e5 si3-ui5 chat-iaN5,  Lai5 chin2-kiu3 in.
8)	Lin2 tioh8 chhi3-khoaN3, chiu7 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 ho2;  Oa2-kho3 I e5 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
9)	Ia5-ho5-hoa seng3 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 keng3-ui3 I;  In-ui7 keng3-ui3 I e5 lang5 bo5 khiam3-kheh chit8-hang7.
10)	Sai-a2-thun5 u7 khiam3-kheh, u7 iau;  Tok8-tok8 chhe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5 bo5 khiam3 sim2-mih8 hang7 e5 ho2.
11)	Soe3-kiaN2 ah, lin2 tioh8 lai5 thiaN goa2,  Goa2 beh chiong keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 to7-li2 ka3-si7 lin2.
12)	Sim2-mih8 lang5 ai3 oah8-mia7,  Him-bou7 he3-siu7, beh tit-tioh8 hok-khi3?
13)	Chiu7 tioh8 kim3 li2 e5 chih8 bo5 kong2 phaiN2-oe7;  Li2 e5 chhui3-tun5 bo5 kong2 kan-cha3 e5 oe7.
14)	Tioh8 li7-khui phaiN2, kiaN5 ho2;  Chhe7 ho5-peng5, lai5 tui-jip--i.
15)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bak8-chiu khoaN3 gi7-lang5;  I e5 hi7-khang thiaN in e5 ki5-to2.
16)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7 ng3 kiaN5-phaiN2 e5 lang5,  Beh tui3 se3-kan tu5-biat8 in e5 mia5-ji7.
17)	Gi7-lang5 kiu5-kio3, Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3,  Chiu7 kiu3 in thoat-li7 it-chhe3 e5 hoan7-lan7.
18)	Ia5-ho5-hoa oa2-kun7 siong-sim e5 lang5,  Chin2-kiu3 leng5-seng3 thong3-hoe2 e5 lang5.
19)	Gi7-lang5 u7 choe7-choe7 khou2-lan7,  Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu3 i long2 thoat-li7.
20)	Po2-choan5 i long2-chong2 e5 kut;  Chit8-ki iah8 bo5 phah-chih8.
21)	Choe7-ok beh hai7-si2 phaiN2-lang5;  Oan3-hun7 gi7-lang5--e5 beh siu7 teng7-choe7.
22)	Ia5-ho5-hoa kiu3-siok8 I e5 lou5-pok8 e5 sin5-hun5;  Hoan7-na7 oa2-kho3 I--e5, bo5 chit8-e5 siu7 teng7-choe7.

[35]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kap goa2 saN-chiN-e5, kiu5 Li2 kap in saN-chiN;  Kap goa2 kau-chian3--e5, kiu5 Li2 kap in kau-chian3.
2)	Theh8 toa7-soe3 e5 tin5-pai5,  Khi2-lai5 pang-chan7 goa2.
3)	Thiu-chhut chhiuN, chou2-chi2 hiah e5 tui-koaN2 goa2--e5;  Tui3 goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 kong2, Goa2 si7 chin2-kiu3 li2--e5.
4)	Goan7 hiah e5 siau3-siuN7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 siu7 kian3-siau3 leng5-jiok8;  Goan7 hiah e5 ke3-bou5 hai7 goa2 e5 lang5 oat8-to3-tng2 lau3-khui3.
5)	Goan7 in chhin-chhiuN7 hong chhe e5 chhou-khng;  U7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 teh koaN2 in.
6)	Goan7 in e5 lou7 am3 koh kut8,  U7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 teh koaN2 in.
7)	In-ui7 in bo5 in-toaN ui7 goa2 am3-siat lo5-bang7 ti7 khiN-lai7,  Bo5 in-toaN kut8 ham7-khiN beh hai7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7.
8)	Goan7 ti7 i bo5 phah-sng3 e5 si5, chai-e7 kau3 i e5 sin-chiuN7;  Goan7 i am3-siat e5 lo5-bang7 tiN5-tioh8 i ka-ki7;  Goan7 i poah8-loh8 hi2 lai7-bin7, siu7 hai7.
9)	Chiu7 goa2 e5 sim beh ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 khoai3-lok8;  Ti7 I e5 kiu3-un lai5 hoaN-hi2.
10)	Goa2 e5 kut-thau5 long2 beh kong2,  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, chi7-chui7 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 Li2?  Li2 chin2-kiu3 khun3-khou2 e5 lang5, thoat-li7 hiah e5 pi2 i khah-kiong5--e5;  Chin2-kiu3 khun3-khou2 kap song3-hiong e5 lang5 thoat-li7 hiah e5 chhiuN2-toat8 i--e5.
11)	Hiong-ok e5 kan-cheng3--e5 khi2-lai5;  Goa2 sou2 m7-chai e5 su7, in chha5-mng7 goa2.
12)	In tui3-ti7 goa2 eng7 phaiN2 po3 ho2:  Hou7 goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 kou-toaN.
13)	Lun7-kau3 goa2, tng in phoa3-piN7 e5 si5, goa2 chiu7 chheng7 moa5-saN,  Eng7 kim3-chiah8 khek-khou2 goa2 e5 sim-sin5;  Goa2 sou2 kiu5--e5, long2 kui ti7 ka-ki7 e5 sim-hoai5.
14)	Goa2 an2-ni kiaN5, chhin-chhiuN7 i si7 goa2 e5 peng5-iu2, goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7;  Goa2 khut-loh8 seng-khu pi-ai, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 ui7-tioh8 lau7-bu2 ai-siong.
15)	Goa2 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7, in chiu7 hoaN-hi2, saN-kap chu7-chip8;  Goa2 sou2 m7 saN-bat e5 ha7-teng2-lang5 chu7-chip8 kong-kek goa2;  In khiu2-lak8 goa2 bo5 soah.
16)	In chhin-chhiuN7 hi3-hiauh, pian2-chiah8 e5 bo5 he7-loh8 lang5,  Tui3 goa2 ka7 chhui3-khi2-kun.
17)	Chu2 ah, Li2 tiaN7-tiaN7 teh khoaN3, beh kau3 joa7-ku2?  Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 thoat-li7 in e5 chan5-hai7,  Kiu3 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 thoat-li7 beng2 e5 sai-a2-thun5.
18)	Goa2 ti7 toa7 chu7-hoe7 e5 tiong-kan beh kam2-sia7 Li2;  Ti7 cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan beh o-lo2 Li2.
19)	Kiu5 Li2 boh8-tit iong5-un2 hiah e5 bo5 li2-iu5 tui3-tek8 goa2-e5, tui3 goa2 khoa-khau2;  Boh8-tit iong5-un2 hiah e5 bo5 in-toaN oan3-hun7 goa2-e5 gin5--goa2.
20)	In-ui7 in bo5 kong2 ho5-peng5 e5 oe7;  Chiu7-si7 ke3-bou5 khui2-khiat e5 oe7; hai7 toe7-chiuN7 an-hun7 e5 lang5.
21)	In toa7-toa7 khui-chhui3 kong-kek goa2;  Kong2, Houh--chai7!  Houh--chai7!  Goan2 e5 bak8-chiu i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3 lah.
22)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3; kiu5 Li2 m7-thang cheng7-cheng7;  Chu2 ah, m7-thang li7-khui goa2.
23)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 e5 Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 cheng-sin5, khi2--lai5;  PhoaN3-koat goa2 e5 su7, pan7-li2 goa2 e5 an3.
24)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 kong-gi7 phoaN3-toan3 goa2;  Boh8-tit iong5-un2 in tui3 goa2 khoa-khau2.
25)	Boh8-tit iong5-un2 in sim-lai7 kong2,  Houh--chai7, chiau3 goan2 e5 sim-goan7 lah;  Boh8-tit iong5-un2 in kong2, Goan2 i2-keng ka7 i thun--loh8-khi3 lah.
26)	Goan7 hiah e5 hoaN-hi2 goa2 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7--e5, long2 kian3-siau3 lau3-khui3;  Goan7 hiah e5 tui3 goa2 ka-ki7 chun-toa7--e5, siu7 kian3-siau3 lak-lian2.
27)	Goan7 hiah e5 ai3 goa2 tit-tioh8 sin-oan e5 lang5, chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN khoai3-lok8;  Goan7 in siong5-siong5 kong2, Tioh8 chun Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 toa7.  In-ui7 I hoaN-hi2 I e5 lou5-pok8 peng5-an.
28)	Goa2 e5 chih8 beh kong2-khi2 Li2 e5 gi7,  Thong-jit8 o-lo2 Li2.

[36]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau-hou7 Gak-koaN.
1)	PhaiN2-lang5 e5 choe7-koa3, u7 oe7 ti7 goa2 e5 sim kong2,  I e5 bak8-chiu-tiong bo5 kiaN Siong7-te3.
2)	In-ui7 ti7 i e5 bak8-chiu-lai7 i ka-ki7 thiam2-mi7,  Phah-sng3 i e5 choe7-ok eng2 boe7 lou7-hian7, boe7 siu7 oan3-hun7.
3)	I chhui3-lai7 e5 oe7, long2 si7 choe7-ok kap kan-cha3;  I kap ti3-hui7 ho2 e5 sou2-kiaN5 i2-keng toan7-choat8.
4)	I ti7 bin5-chhng5 tou5-bou5 choe7-ok,  I tiaN7-tioh8 i3-su3 khia7 ti7 m7-ho2 e5 lou7;  I bo5 oan3-hun7 phaiN2-tai7.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 si7 ti7 thiN--nih;  Li2 e5 sin3-sit8 kau3 ti7 kiong-chhong.
6)	Li2 e5 gi7 chhin-chhiuN7 kek8-koaiN5 e5 soaN;  Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chhim-ian.  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, lang5 kap cheng-siN, Li2 long2 po2-hou7 in.
7)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 chaiN2-iuN7 hiah po2-poe3 ah!  Se3-kan-lang5 bih ti7 Li2 sit8-kou2 e5 ti3-im3-e7.
8)	In beh in-ui7 Li2 e5 chhu3 e5 ho2-mih8, tit-tioh8 pa2-chiok;  Li2 iah8 beh hou7 in lim Li2 khoai3-lok8 e5 ho5-chui2.
9)	In-ui7 oah8-mia7 e5 goan5-thau5, chai7 ti7 Li2 hia;  Ti7 Li2 e5 kng, goan2 beh khoaN3-kiN3 kng.
10)	Goan7 Li2 siong5-siong5 si chu5-ai3 hou7 bat Li2 e5 lang5;  Siong5-siong5 eng7 Li2 e5 kong-gi7 si hou7 sim-lai7 cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5.
11)	M7-thang iong5-un2 kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 e5 kha thun2-tah8 goa2,  M7-thang iong5-un2 hiong-ok e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2 koaN2-tiok8 goa2.
12)	Ti7-hia choe3 phaiN2 e5 lang5 i2-keng to2--loh8-khi3;  I siu7 chhia-to2, boe7-oe7 koh khi2-lai5.

[37]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	M7-thang in-ui7 choe3 phaiN2 e5 lang5, sim-lai7 put-peng5;  Iah8 m7-thang oan3-tou3 kiaN5 put-gi7 e5 lang5.
2)	In-ui7 in chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2 khoai3-khoai3 koah;  Koh chhin-chhiuN7 chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhai3 lau2--khi3.
3)	Tioh8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 kiaN5 ho2,  Tiam3 ti7 chit e5 thou2-toe7, eng7 seng5-sit8 choe3 bi2-niu5.
4)	Tioh8 liah8 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 hoaN-hi2,  I beh chiong li2 e5 sim sou2 kiu5--e5 hou7 li2.
5)	Tioh8 chiong li2 e5 tai7-chi3 kau-tai3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Koh oa2-kho3 I, I beh hou7 i chiaN5.
6)	I beh hou7 li2 e5 gi7 hoat-chhut chhin-chhiuN7 kng;  Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3, chhin-chhiuN7 tiong-tau3 e5 kng.
7)	Tioh8 cheng7-cheng7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, khoan-sim theng3-hau7 I;  M7-thang in-ui7 hit-ho7 su7-su7 heng-thong-e5,  Kap hit-ho7 phaiN2 ke3-bou5 tit-tioh8 chiaN5--e5, lai5 put-peng5.
8)	Tioh8 soah siu7-khi3, li7-khui toa7 siu7-khi3;  M7-thang put-peng5, kiaN-liau2 oe7 choe3 phaiN2.
9)	In-ui7 kiaN5-phaiN2 e5 lang5 beh siu7 chau5-biat8;  Tok8-tok8 theng3-hau7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5, in beh seng5-chiap thou2-toe7.
10)	In-ui7 koh tiap-a2-ku2, phaiN2-lang5 beh bo5--khi3;  Li2 na7 siong5-se3 chha5 i e5 sou2-chai7, i iah8 bo5--khi3;
11)	Tok8-tok8 khiam-pi e5 lang5 beh seng5-chiap thou2-toe7;  In-ui7 peng5-an hong-seng7 toa7-tim5 hoaN-hi2.
12)	PhaiN2-lang5 siat ke3-bou5 beh hai7 gi7-lang5,  Koh ng3 i ka7 chhui3-khi2-kun.
13)	Chu2 beh chhio3 i,  In-ui7 khoaN3-kiN3 i e5 jit8-chi2 beh kau3.
14)	PhaiN2-lang5 puih8-to khui-keng, beh taN2-to2 khun3-khou2 song3-hiong e5 lang5;  Beh thai5-si2 kiaN5-choe3 cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5.
15)	In e5 to beh chhi3-jip8 ka-ki7 e5 sim,  In e5 keng beh siu7 at-chih8.
16)	Gi7-lang5 sou2-u7-e5 chio2-chio2,  IaN5-ke3 choe7-choe7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 pu3-u7.
17)	In-ui7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhiu2 beh siu7 at-chih8;  Tok8-tok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa hu5-chhi5 gi7 e5 lang5.
18)	Ia5-ho5-hoa chai oan5-choan5 e5 lang5 e5 si5-jit8;  In e5 san2-giap8 beh eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
19)	In ti7 hoan7-lan7 e5 si5 put-ti3 kian3-siau3;  Ti7 ki-hng e5 jit8 beh tit-tioh8 pa2-chiok.
20)	Chong2-si7 phaiN2-lang5 beh biat8-bo5,  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tui3-tek8 beh chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2-pou e5 bou7-seng7;  In beh siau-bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 he2-hun e5 siau-bo5.
21)	PhaiN2-lang5 ka7 lang5 chioh, ia7 bo5 heng5;  Na7-si7 gi7-lang5 kiaN5 lin5-bin2, sia2-si3 lang5.
22)	Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok e5 lang5, in beh seng5-chiap thou2-toe7;  Hou7 I chiu3-chou2 e5 lang5 beh siu7 biat8-bo5.
23)	Gi7-lang5 e5 kha-pou7 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 an-ti3;  Koh I hoaN-hi2 i e5 lou7.
24)	I sui-bong2 poah8-to2, iah8 bo5 kau3 kui-sin siak--loh8-khi3;  In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 I e5 chhiu2 hu5 i.
25)	Goa2 cheng5 siau3-lian5, taN ni5 lau7;  Chong2-si7 be7-bat khoaN3-kiN3 gi7-lang5 siu7 pang3-sak,  Iah8 i e5 hou7-e3 choe3 khit-chiah8.
26)	I thong-jit8 lin5-bin2 lang5, chioh lang5,  I e5 hou7-e3 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.
27)	Li2 tioh8 li7-khui phaiN2, kiaN5 ho2,  Chiah thang eng2-oan2 khia7-khi2.
28)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoaN-hi2 kong-peng5,  Bo5 pang3-sak I seng3 e5 peh-siN3;  In eng2-oan2 siu7 po2-hou7,  Tok8-tok8 phaiN2-lang5 e5 hou7-e3 beh siu7 chau5-biat8.
29)	Gi7-lang5 beh seng5-chiap thou2-toe7,  Eng2-oan2 tiam3 ti7-hia.
30)	Gi7-lang5 e5 chhui3 kong2 ti3-hui7,  I e5 chih8 tam5-lun7 kong-peng5.
31)	I e5 Siong7-te3 e5 lut8-hoat ti7 i e5 sim-lai7;  I e5 kha long2 boe7 tah8-thut8.
32)	PhaiN2-lang5 thau-khoaN3 gi7-lang5,  Siau3-siuN7 thai5--i.
33)	Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 pang3-sak i ti7 phaiN2 lang5 e5 chhiu2;  Tng sim2-phoaN3 e5 si5, iah8 bo5 teng7 i e5 choe7.
34)	Li2 tioh8 theng3-hau7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chun-siu2 I e5 to7-lou7;  I chiu7 ko-seng li2, hou7 li2 seng5-chiap thou2-toe7;  PhaiN2-lang5 siu7 chau5-biat8 e5 si5, li2 beh khoaN3-kiN3.
35)	Goa2 bat khoaN3-kiN3 phaiN2-lang5 u7 toa7 se3-lek8,  Koh hoat-tat8 chhin-chhiuN7 am7 e5 chhiu7 ti7 i e5 pun2 thou2-toe7.
36)	U7 lang5 tui3 hia keng-ke3, khoaN3 ah, i bo5--khi3 lah;  Goa2 iah8 chhe7 i, chhe7 boe7 tioh8.
37)	Li2 tioh8 siong5-se3 khoaN3 hit e5 oan5-choan5 e5 lang5, khoaN3 hit e5 cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5,  In-ui7 ho5-peng5 e5 lang5 u7 ho2 e5 kiat-kiok8.
38)	Lun7-kau3 hoan7-hoat e5 lang5, beh choe3-chit8-e7 biat8-bo5;  PhaiN2-lang5 e5 kiat-kiok8 beh siu7 chau5-biat8.
39)	Chong2-si7 gi7-lang5 tit-tioh8 kiu3, si7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Tng hoan7-lan7 e5 si5, I choe3 in e5 iaN5-che7.
40)	Ia5-ho5-hoa pang-chan7 in, chin2-kiu3 in;  I chin2-kiu3 in thoat-li7 phaiN2-lang5, lai5 khan-kiu3 in;  In-ui7 in oa2-kho3 I.

[38]	Tai7-pit8 e5 ki3-liam7 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang ti7 siu7-khi3-tiong chek-pi7 goa2;  M7-thang ti7 toa7 siu7-khi3-tiong keng2-kai3 goa2.
2)	In-ui7 Li2 e5 chiN3 sia7 goa2 e5 seng-khu,  Li2 e5 chhiu2 tang7-tang7 chhih8 goa2.
3)	In-ui7 Li2 e5 siu7-khi3, goa2 e5 bah bo5 chit8-ui7 oan5-choan5;  In-ui7 goa2 e5 choe7-koa3, goa2 e5 kut iah8 bo5 peng5-an.
4)	Goa2 e5 choe7-ok poaN5-ke3 goa2 e5 thau5-khak,  Chhin-chhiuN7 tang7-taN3 hou7 goa2 taN-boe7-khi2.
5)	In-ui7 goa2 e5 gu5-gong7,  Goa2 e5 siong noa7, koh chhau3.
6)	Goa2 thang3-thiaN3 koh khiau-ku,  Thong-jit8 ai-siong.
7)	In-ui7 goa2 moa2-io si7 he2;  Goa2 e5 bah bo5 chit8-ui7 oan5-choan5.
8)	Goa2 siu7 phah-siong, chin bo5 lat8;  In-ui7 goa2 e5 sim put-an, chiu7 toa7 ai-chhan.
9)	Chu2 ah, goa2 e5 sim-goan7 long2 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5,  Goa2 e5 thou2-khui3 bo5 tui3 Li2 un2-moa5.
10)	Goa2 e5 sim phok8-phok8-chheng2, goa2 e5 lat8 soe-bi5;  Lian5 goa2 bak8-chiu-tiong e5 kng iah8 li7-khui goa2.
11)	ThiaN3 goa2 e5 lang5 kap goa2 e5 peng5-iu2, in-ui7 goa2 e5 phaiN2 cheng3-thau5, long2 siam2 ti7 piN-a2;  Goa2 e5 chhin-chhek iah8 hng7-hng7 teh khia7.
12)	Hiah e5 siau3-siuN7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7--e5 siat lo5-bang7;  SiuN7 beh hai7 goa2 e5, kong2-chhut ok-tok8 e5 oe7;  Thong-jit8 siuN7 khui2-khiat e5 ke3-bou5.
13)	Chong2-si7 goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau3-hi7-lang5--e5 bo5 thiaN-kiN3,  Chhin-chhiuN7 e2-kau2--e5, bo5 khui chhui3.
14)	Goa2 iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 e5 lang5,  Chhui3 bo5 in3-tap--e5.
15)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 theng3-hau7 Li2;  Chu2, Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 beh thiaN goa2.
16)	In-ui7 goa2 bat kong2, KiaN-liau2 in tui3 goa2 khoa-khau2;  Goa2 e5 kha tah8-thut8 e5 si5, in tui3 goa2 ka-ki7 chun-toa7.
17)	In-ui7 goa2 hiam2-hiam2 poah8-to2,  Goa2 e5 iu-bun7 siong5-siong5 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
18)	In-ui7 goa2 beh jin7 goa2 e5 choe7-ok;  Koh ui7-tioh8 goa2 e5 choe7 lai5 iu-bun7.
19)	Chong2-si7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 ia7 oah8-tang7, iah8 iong2-beng2;  Bo5 li2-iu5 oan3-hun7 goa2 e5, ke-thiN na2-choe7.
20)	Eng7 phaiN2 po3 ho2--e5, kap goa2 choe3 tui3-thau5;  In-ui7 goa2 si7 tui-jip ho2.
21)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, m7-thang pang3-sak goa2;  Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, m7-thang li7-khui goa2 hng7-hng7.
22)	Chu2 ah, Chin2-kiu3 goa2 e5,  Kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 pang-chan7 goa2.

[39]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN, Ia5-tou7-tun3.
1)	Goa2 bat kong2, Goa2 beh kin2-sin7 goa2 e5 lou7,  Bian2-tit eng7 goa2 e5 chih8 hoan7-choe7;  PhaiN2-lang5 ti7 goa2 bin7-cheng5 e5 si5, Goa2 beh iok-sok goa2 e5 chhui3 chhin-chhiuN7 be2-ka7-kiuN.
2)	Goa2 cheng7-cheng7 bo5 siaN, lian5 ho2-oe7 iah8 bo5 kong2-chhut chhui3;  Goa2 e5 iu-bun7 chiu7 gia5--khi2-lai5.
3)	Goa2 e5 sim ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 jiat8-jiat8;  Goa2 cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 e5 si5, he2 chiu7 toh8--khi2-lai5;  Goa2 chiu7 eng7 chih8 lai5 kong2:
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 chai pun2-sin e5 kiat-kiok8,  Kap goa2 ni5-he3 e5 siau3-giah8 joa7-choe7;  Hou7 goa2 chai loan2-jiok8 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7.
5)	Li2 hou7 goa2 e5 jit8-chi2 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8-pa-chiuN2,  Goa2 it-seng e5 ni5-he2, ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chhin-chhiuN7 bo5;  Tak8-lang5 khia7-chai7 e5 si5, chin-chiaN3 long2 si7 khang-khang. [Se3-lah8
6)	Se3-kan-lang5 kiaN5-choe3 sit8-chai7 chhin-chhiuN7 iaN2;  In bo5-eng5 chhih-chhih, chin-chiaN3 bo5 chhai2-kang;  I sou2 chek-chu7--e5, m7-chai chiong-lai5 chi7-chui7 tit--khi3.
7)	Chu2 ah, goa2 taN theng3-hau7 sim2-mih8?  Goa2 e5 ng3-bang7 chai7-ti7 Li2.
8)	Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa2 it-chhe3 e5 ke3-sit;  M7-thang hou7 goa2 siu7 gong7-lang5 e5 leng5-jiok8.
9)	Goa2 cheng7-cheng7 bo5 khui-chhui3;  In-ui7 si7 Li2 choe3 e5.
10)	Li2 sou2 kang3 e5 chek-hoat8 kiu5 Li2 ka7 goa2 tu5--khi3;  In-ui7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 e5 tok-chek, goa2 chiu7 siau-biat8.
11)	Li2 in-ui7 lang5 e5 choe7-ok, keng2-kai3 i e5 si5,  Hou7 i sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5 siau-biat8, chhin-chhiuN7 tioh8 chiu3-thang5;  Se3-kan lang5 chin-chiaN3 si7 khang-khang. [Se3-lah8
12)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 thiaN goa2 e5 ki5-to2, aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 kiu5-kio3,  Goa2 lau5 bak8-sai2, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang bo5 chhut siaN;  In-ui7 goa2 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 si7 chhut-goa7-lang5,  Si7 kia3-kha--e5, chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 e5 liat8-chou2 chit8-poaN-iuN7.
13)	Kiu5 Li2 khoan-iong5 goa2, hou7 goa2 iau2-be7 khi3 lai5 kui ti7 bo5 e5 tai7-seng,  Thang tit-tioh8 song2-khoai3.

[40]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Goa2 bat thun-lun2 theng3-hau7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  I aN3-loh8 ng3 goa2, thiaN goa2 e5 kiu5-kio3.
2)	I tui3 thang kiaN e5 ham7-khiN, tui3 thou5-be5 tiong, khan goa2 khi2-lai5;  Hou7 goa2 e5 kha khia7 ti7 chioh8-poaN5-teng2, hou7 goa2 e5 kha-pou7 chai7-ngou2.
3)	I hou7 goa2 e5 chhui3 chhiuN3 sin e5 koa, chiu7-si7 o-lo2 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3--e5;  Choe7-choe7 lang5 beh khoaN3-kiN3 lai5 kiaN-ui3,  Iah8 beh oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
4)	Tok8-tok8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, bo5 chhap hiah e5 kiau-ngou7, i2-kip8 phian-ng3 hu-ke2 e5 lang5,  Chit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 ki5-su7,  I2-kip8 Li2 tui3 goan2 sou2 chun5 e5 liam7-thau5 chin-choe7;  Boe7-oe7 tui3 Li2 pai5-liat8;  Goa2 na7 beh the5-khi2 lai5 kong2,  Hit e5 siau3-giah8 sng3-boe7-liau2.
6)	Che3-su7 kap le2-mih8 Li2 bo5 hoaN-hi2;  Li2 u7 khui goa2 e5 hi7-khang;  Sio-che3 kap siok8-choe7-che3, Li2 bo5 ai3-tih8:
7)	Hit-si5 goa2 kong2, Li2 khoaN3, Goa2 lai5 lah;  Goa2 e5 su7 i2-keng ki3 ti7 chheh--nih.
8)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 e5 chi2-i3 goa2 hoaN-hi2 than3;  Li2 e5 lut8-hoat ti7 goa2 e5 sim-lai7.
9)	Goa2 ti7 toa7 chu7-hoe7 e5 tiong-kan, soan-thoan5 kong-gi7 e5 ho2 siau-sit;  Goa2 bo5 beh theng5-chi2 goa2 e5 chhui3-tun5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, che si7 Li2 sou2 chai e5.
10)	Goa2 be7-bat chiong Li2 e5 kong-gi7 kham3-bat8 ti7 goa2 e5 sim-lai7;  Goa2 i2-keng pai5-liat8 Li2 e5 sin3-sit8, kap Li2 e5 kiu3-un.  Goa2 tui3 toa7 chu7-hoe7 be7-bat un2-khng3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 kap seng5-sit8.
11)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang tui3 goa2 theng5-chi2 Li2 e5 chu5-pi;  Goan7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 kap seng5-sit8 siong5-siong5 po2-hou7 goa2.
12)	In-ui7 u7 boe7-sng3-tit e5 chai-e7 ui5-khun3 goa2;  Goa2 e5 choe7-ok jip-tioh8 goa2, hou7 goa2 boe7-oe7 kiah8-bak8;  Chiah e5 choe7-ok pi2 goa2 e5 thau5-mng5 khah-choe7; goa2 e5 sim soa3 li7-khui goa2.
13)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 hoaN-hi2 chin2-kiu3 goa2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 pang-chan7 goa2.
14)	Goan7 hiah e5 siau3-siuN7 beh hai7 goa2 siN3-mia7--e5 choe3 chit8-e7 kian3-siau3, lau3-khui3;  Goan7 hiah e5 hoaN-hi2 goa2 siu7 ham7-hai7--e5, oat8-to3-tng2 siu7 leng5-jiok8.
15)	Goan7 hiah e5 tui3 goa2 kong2, Houh--chai7, Houh--chai7 e5, In-ui7 kian3-siau3 lai5 pai7-bo5.
16)	Goan7 it-chhe3 chhe7 Li2 e5, in-ui7 Li2 lai5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8;  Goan7 hiah e5 him-bou7 Li2 kiu3-un--e5 siong5-siong5 kong2,  Tioh8 chun Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 toa7.
17)	Chong2-si7 goa2 si7 khun3-khou2 song3-hiong--e5,  Chu2 iau2-ku2 siau3-liam7 goa2;  Li2 si7 pang-chan7 goa2--e5, chin2-kiu3 goa2--e5;  Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang ian5-chhian5.

[41]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Koan3-kou3 song3-hiong lang5 e5, u7 hok-khi3;  Tng hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh kiu3 i.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa beh po2-choan5 i, hou7 i oah8--teh, i beh ti7 toe7-chiuN7 hiong2-hok;  Kiu5 Li2 m7-thang chiong i kau hou7 tui3-tek8, lai5 chiau3 in sou2 ai3.
3)	I to2 chai7-chhng5, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hu5-chhi5 i;  I phoa3-piN7 e5 si5,  Li2 beh liau7-li2 i e5 phe7-phou.
4)	Goa2 bat kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 lin5-bin2 goa2;  I-ho2 goa2 e5 sim-sin5, in-ui7 goa2 u7 teh-choe7 ti7 Li2.
5)	Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 eng7 phaiN2-oe7 gi7-lun7 goa2, kong2,  I ti7-si5 oe7 si2, i e5 mia5 ti7-si5 oe7 biat8-bo5?
6)	I na7 lai5 khoaN3 goa2, chiu7 kong2 bo5-iaN2 oe7;  I e5 sim chek-chu7 kan-ok,  Chhut-khi3 goa7-khau2, chiu7 si3-koe3 kong2.
7)	It-chhe3 oan3-hun7 goa2 e5 lang5 chi-bu2 chi7-chu7 gi7-lun7 goa2;  In siat ke3-bou5 beh hai7 goa2;
8)	In kong2, U7 koai3-piN7 tiau5 ti7 i e5 seng-khu;  I i2-keng to2-chhng5, eng2 boe7 koh khi2--lai5.
9)	Lian5 goa2 ti-ki2 e5 peng5-iu2, goa2 sou2 oa2-kho3, chiah8 goa2 e5 piaN2--e5,  Kiah8-khi2 kha-au7-tiN that goa2.
10)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 lin5-bin2 goa2,  Hou7 goa2 khi2-lai5 thang po3-eng3 in.
11)	In-ui7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 boe7 tit-tioh8 tui3 goa2 khoa-khau2 khah-iaN5;  Goa2 tui3 an2-ni chiu7 chai Li2 hoaN-hi2 goa2.
12)	Lun7-kau3 goa2, Li2 in-ui7 goa2 e5 sun5-choan5 chiu7 hu5-chhi5 goa2,  Hou7 goa2 eng2-oan2 khia7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
13)	Tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3,  Tui3 eng2-oan2 kau3 eng2-oan2,  A-beng7, koh A-beng7.

	Koan3 II
[42]	Kho2-lah8 hou7-e3 ka3-si7 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 e5 sim chhiat-chhiat him-bou7 Li2,  Chhin-chhiuN7 lok8 chhiat-chhiat him-bou7 khoe-chui2.
2)	Goa2 e5 sim chhui3-ta, him-bou7 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 oah8 e5 Siong7-te3;  Goa2 siaN2-si5 oe7 kau3 Siong7-te3 bin7-cheng5, lai5 kiN3 I ah?
3)	Goa2 mi5-jit8 eng7 goa2 e5 bak8-sai2 chun2 png7 chiah8,  In tui3 goa2 kong2 bo5 soah, Li2 e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 toh-loh8?
4)	Goa2 cha2-cheng5 kap cheng3-lang5 choe3-tin7 khi3, chhoa7 in kau3 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3;  Eng7 hoaN-hi2 o-lo2 e5 siaN, tai7-ke siu2 choeh;  Goa2 tui-liam7 chiah e5 su7, goa2 e5 sim kek8-ki5 pi-siong.
5)	Goa2 e5 sim ah, li2 siaN2-su7 ut-chut?  SiaN2-su7 ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 tioh8-kip?  Li2 tioh8 ng3-bang7 Siong7-te3,  In-ui7 I e5 bin7 ng3 goa2, lai5 chin2-kiu3 goa2; sou2-i2 goa2 iau2-ku2 beh o-lo2 I.
6)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 e5 sim ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 ut-chut;  Sou2-i2 goa2 tui3 Iok-tan3 e5 toe7 kap Hek-bun5,  Iah8 tui3 Bi2-sat e5 soaN ki3-liam7 Li2.
7)	Li2 e5 phok8-pou3 chhut-siaN, chiu7 chhim-ian kap chhim-ian saN kio3 in3;  Li2 e5 pho-long7, Li2 e5 toa7-eng2, long2 im-bat8 goa2.
8)	Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa jit8--si5 beh si-chhut I e5 chu5-ai3;  Mi5--si5 I hou7 goa2 chhiuN3-koa,  Lai5 kiu5 siuN2-su3 goa2 oah8-mia7 e5 Siong7-te3.
9)	Goa2 beh tui3 Siong7-te3, goa2 e5 chioh8-poaN5, kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 boe7-ki3-tit goa2?  Goa2 siaN2-su7 in-ui7 tui3-tek8 e5 ap-pek, iu-bun7 lai5 kiaN5 ah?
10)	Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 ki-chhi3 goa2, chhin-chhiuN7 phah-chhui3 goa2 e5 kut-thau5;  In tui3 goa2 kong2 bo5 soah, Li2 e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 toh-loh8?
11)	Goa2 e5 sim ah, li2 siaN2-su7 ut-chut?  SiaN2-su7 ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 tioh8-kip?  Li2 tioh8 ng3-bang7 Siong7-te3; in-ui7 goa2 iau2-ku2 beh o-lo2 I;  I si7 goa2 e5 bin7 e5 eng5-kng, iah8 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3.

[43]	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 ka7 goa2 phoaN3-toan3; tui3 bo5 khian5-seng5 e5 kok, pian7-beng5 goa2 e5 an3.  Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 kan-cha3 put-gi7 e5 lang5.
2)	In-ui7 Li2 si7 hou7 goa2 u7 khui3-lat8 e5 Siong7-te3; siaN2-su7 pang3-sak goa2?  Goa2 siaN2-su7 in-ui7 tui3-tek8 e5 ap-pek, siong5-siong5 iu-bun7 lai5 kiaN5 ah?
3)	Kiu5 Li2 hoat-chhut Li2 e5 kng kap Li2 e5 chin-sit8, hou7 i chhoa7 goa2;  Toa3 goa2 kau3 Li2 e5 seng3-soaN, kau3 Li2 e5 hoe7-bou7.
4)	Goa2 chiu7 beh kau3 Siong7-te3 e5 che3-toaN5, kau3 goa2 kek8 hoaN-hi2 e5 Siong7-te3 hia;  Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 beh toaN5 khim5 lai5 o-lo2 Li2.
5)	Goa2 e5 sim ah, li2 siaN2-su7 ut-chut?  SiaN2-su7 ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 tioh8-kip?  Li2 tioh8 ng3-bang7 Siong7-te3;  In-ui7 goa2 iau2-ku2 beh o-lo2 I;  I si7 goa2 e5 bin7 e5 eng5-kng, iah8 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3.

[44]	Kho2-lah8 hou7-e3 ka3-si7 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 ti7 kou2-cha2, goan2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 si5, sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7, goan2 chhin-hi7 thiaN-kiN3,  Goan2 e5 liat8-chou2 iah8 u7 tui3 goan2 kong2-khi2.
2)	Li2 bat eng7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 koaN2 liat8-pang, lai5 chai-poe5 goan2 e5 liat8-chou2,  Li2 khou2-chhou2 hiah e5 chok8, lai5 hou7 in hoat-tat8.
3)	In-ui7 in m7-si7 tui3 in e5 to-kiam3 lai5 tit-tioh8 thou2-toe7;  Iah8 m7-si7 in e5 chhiu2 kiu3 in;  Chiu7-si7 Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2, Li2 e5 chhiu2-kut, Li2 e5 bin7 e5 kng kiu3 in;  In-ui7 Li2 hoaN-hi2 in.
4)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Ong5;  Kiu5 Li2 chhut leng7, chin2-kiu3 Nga2-kok.
5)	Goan2 oa2-kho3 Li2, beh chhia-to2 goan2 e5 tui3-tek8;  Goan2 oa2-kho3 Li2 e5 mia5, beh thun2-tah8 hiah e5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek goan2 e5 lang5.
6)	In-ui7 goa2 bo5 beh oa2-kho3 goa2 e5 keng,  Goa2 e5 to iah8 boe7 kiu3 goa2.
7)	Tok8-tok8 Li2 bat kiu3 goan2 thoat-li7 tui3-tek8,  Hou7 oan3-hun7 goan2 e5 lang5 kian3-siau3.
8)	Goan2 thong-jit8 in-ui7 Siong7-te3 lai5 khoa-khau2,  Goan2 beh o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5 kau3 eng2-oan2. [Se3-lah8
9)	Chong2-si7 hian7-kim Li2 pang3-sak goan2, hou7 goan2 siu7 leng5-jiok8;  Bo5 kap goan2 e5 kun-peng saN-kap chhut-khi3.
10)	Li2 hou7 goan2 ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 bin7-cheng5 oat8-tng2-sin chau2;  Hiah e5 oan3-hun7 goan2 e5 lang5, chhut-chai7 in lai5 chhiuN2-theh8.
11)	Li2 hou7 goan2 chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5 choe3 lang5 e5 chiah8-mih8;  Hou7 goan2 siN3-soaN3 ti7 liat8-pang tiong.
12)	Li2 boe7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3, iah8 bo5 than3-chiN5,  sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 ke3-chiN5, ia7 bo5 ke-thiN Li2 e5 ho2-giah8.
13)	Li2 hou7 goan2 siu7 keh-piah kok e5 leng5-jiok8;  Siu7 si3-ui5 e5 lang5 thi2-chhio3 ki-chhi3.
14)	Li2 hou7 goan2 ti7 liat8-pang-tiong choe3 oe7-piN3;  Hou7 cheng3 peh-siN3 tui3 goan2 io5-thau5.
15)	Goa2 e5 leng5-jiok8 thong-jit8 ti7 goa2 e5 thau5-cheng5;  Goa2 e5 bin7 e5 kian3-siau3 jia-kham3 goa2;
16)	Si7 in-ui7 hit e5 loe2-me7, hui2-pong3 e5 lang5 e5 siaN,  Koh in-ui7 tui3-tek8 kap po3-oan e5 lang5 e5 ian5-kou3.
17)	Chiah-e5 long2 lim5-kau3 goan2, goan2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Li2.  Iah8 bo5 ke2-iaN2 siu2 Li2 e5 iok.
18)	Goan2 e5 sim bo5 poe7 Li2;  Goan2 e5 kha-pou7 bo5 phian-li7 Li2 e5 lou7.
19)	Li2 keng2-jian5 ti7 soaN-kau2 e5 sou2-chai7 teh-siong goan2,  Eng7 si2 e5 im3-ng2 jia-kham3 goan2.
20)	Siat-su2 goan2 boe7-ki3-tit goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5,  A2-si7 ng3 pat8 e5 sin5 kiah8-khi2 chhiu2;
21)	Siong7-te3 kiam2 bo5 kam3-chhat chit e5 su7 mah?  In-ui7 I chai lang5 sim-lai7 e5 un2-bat8.
22)	Goan2 in-ui7 Li2 e5 ian5-kou3, thong-jit8 siu7 thai5;  KhoaN3 choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 beh thai5 e5 iuN5.
23)	Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 cheng-sin5, siaN2-su7 teh khun3?  Kiu5 Li2 khi2--lai5, m7-thang eng2-oan2 khi3-sak goan2.
24)	Li2 siaN2-su7 ng Li2 e5 bin7?  SiaN2-su7 boe7-ki3-tit goan2 sou2 siu7 e5 khou2-lan7 kap ap-che3?
25)	In-ui7 goan2 e5 siN3-mia7 phak ti7 thou5-hun2;  Goan2 e5 pak-tou2 liam5 ti7 toe7-bin7.
26)	Kiu5 Li2 khi2-lai5 pang-chan7 goan2,  Tai3-liam7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 kiu3-siok8 goan2.

[45]	Kho2-lah8 hou7-e3 ka3-si7 e5 si, koh si7 ai3-bou7 e5 koa; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, si7 eng7 "Pek-hap8-hoe".
1)	Goa2 e5 sim chheng3-chhut ho2 e5 oe7;  Goa2 kong2-khi2 goa2 ui7-tioh8 ong5 sou2 choe3--e5;  Goa2 e5 chih8 si7 bin2-chiat8 e5 lang5 e5 pit.
