2)	Li2 pi2 se3-kan lang5 khah ho2-khoaN3,  Ti7 li2 e5 chhui3 moa2-moa2 u7 un-hui7,  Sou2-i2 Siong7-te3 su3-hok li2, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.
3)	Toa7 koan5-leng5--e5 ah, li2 tioh8 pe7 kiam3 ti7 io--nih,  Hian2-chhut li2 e5 eng5-kng kap ui-giam5.
4)	Koh ti7 ui-giam5 e5 tiong-kan, ui7-tioh8 chin-li2, khiam-pi, kong-gi7,  Li2 che7-chhia chin3-cheng5 khi3, bo5 m7 tek-seng3;  Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 beh choe3 thang kiaN e5 su7, hou7 li2 khoaN3.
5)	Li2 e5 chiN3-bah chin lai7, Sia7-tioh8 ong5 e5 tui3-tek8 e5 sim,  Liat8-pang to2 ti7 li2 e5 e7-bin7.
6)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 e5 po2-cho7 si7 eng2-eng2 oan2-oan2 e5,  Li2 e5 kok e5 koan5-peng3 si7 cheng3-tit8 e5 koan5-peng3.
7)	Li2 hoaN-hi2 kong-gi7, oan3-hun7 put-hoat,  Sou2-i2 Siong7-te3, li2 e5 Siong7-te3, eng7 hoaN-hi2 e5 iu5 boah li2,  IaN5-ke3 li2 chiah e5 tang5-phoaN7.
8)	Li2 e5 i-chiuN5 long2 u7 but8-ioh8, tim5-hiuN, jiok8-kui3 e5 phang;  Tui3 chhiuN7-ge5 e5 ong5-kiong, u7 si-hian5 e5 gak8-khi3 hou7 li2 hoaN-hi2.
9)	U7 ong5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ti7 li2 chun-kui3 hu7-lu2 e5 tiong-kan;  Ong5-hou7 eng7 Go5-hui e5 kim chng-thaN7, khia7 ti7 li2 e5 chiaN3-peng5.
10)	Cha-bou2-gin2-a2 ah, li2 tioh8 thiaN, tioh8 khoaN3, tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang;  M7-thang ki3-tit li2 e5 peh-siN3, kap li2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke;
11)	Ong5 chiu7 beh him-bou7 li2 e5 sui2;  In-ui7 i si7 li2 e5 chu2, li2 tioh8 pai3 i.
12)	Chhui-lo5 e5 peh-siN3 beh lai5 sang3 le2-mih8,  Peh-siN3 tiong e5 ho2-giah8 lang5 beh tui3 li2 kiu5 un.
13)	Ong5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ti7 ong5-kiong-lai7, kek8-ki5 eng5-hoa5;  I e5 i-hok8 si7 eng7 kim-soaN3 siu3--e5.
14)	I beh chheng7 siu3-hoe e5 i-hok8, siu7 chhoa7 kau3 ong5 e5 bin7-cheng5;  Choe3-phoaN7 kun-sui5 i e5 chai7-sek-lu2 iah8 beh siu7 chhoa7 kau3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5;
15)	In beh hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8 siu7 in2-chhoa7;  In beh chin3-jip8 ong5-kiong.
16)	Li2 e5 kiaN2-sun beh soa3-chiap li2 e5 liat8-chou2;  Li2 beh siat-lip8 in ti7 choan5-toe7 choe3-ong5.
17)	Goa2 beh hou7 li2 e5 mia5 ban7-tai7 hou7 lang5 ki3-liam7;  Sou2-i2 ban7 peh-siN3 beh eng2-eng2 oan2-oan2 kam2-sia7 li2.

[46]	Kho2-lah8 hou7-e3 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, si7 eng7 lu2-im.
1)	Siong7-te3 si7 goan2 to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7 kap khui3-lat8.  Iah8 si7 hoan7-lan7-tiong kip8-si5 e5 pang-chan7.
2)	Sou2-i2 toe7 sui-jian5 pian3-chhian,  SoaN sui-jian5 io5-tang7 kau3 hai2-tiong,
3)	Ki5-tiong e5 chui2 sui-jian5 hoa7-hoa7-hau2 gia5-eng2,  SoaN sui-jian5 in-ui7 hai2-tiong3 io5-choah, goan2 iah8 bo5 kiaN. [Se3-lah8
4)	U7 chit8 tiau5 ho5, i e5 khui-chhe hou7 Siong7-te3 e5 siaN5 hoaN-hi2;  chiu7-si7 Chi3-koaiN5--e5 sou2 khia7-khi2 seng3 e5 sou2-chai7.
5)	Siong7-te3 ti7 hit tiong-kan, siaN5 tek-khak boe7 io5-tang7;  ThiN-phu2-kng, Siong7-te3 beh pang-chan7 i.
6)	IN7-pang hoa7-hoa7-hau2, liat8-kok io5-tang7;  Siong7-te3 chhut I e5 siaN, toe7 chiu7 siau-iuN5.
7)	Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap goan2 ti7--teh,  Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 choe3 goan2 e5 koaiN5-tai5. [Se3-lah8
8)	Lai5 ah, lai5 khoaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sou2-choe3,  KhoaN3 I hou7 toe7 hong-hoe3 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7.
9)	I hou7 kau-chian3 soah, kau3 ti7 toe7-kek8;  I at-chih8 keng, cham7-tng7 chhiuN;  Chiong chian3-chhia sio ti7 he2-tiong.
10)	Lin2 tioh8 tiaN7-tiaN7, tioh8 chai Goa2 si7 Siong7-te3;  Goa2 beh ti7 liat8-pang-tiong choe3 koaiN5-toa7, siu7 chun choe3 toa7, Ti7 pian3 toe7-chiuN7 iah8 choe3 koaiN5-toa7.
11)	Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap goan2 ti7-teh;  Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 choe3 goan2 e5 koaiN5-tai5.

[47]	Kho2-lah8 hou7-e3 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Lin2 cheng3 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 long2 tioh8 tah-chhiu2;  Tioh8 eng7 tek-seng3 e5 siaN, toa7-siaN o-lo2 Siong7-te3.
2)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chi3-koaiN5--e5, thang kiaN--e5,  I si7 toa7 kun-ong5, koan2-li2 choan5-toe7.
3)	I beh hou7 ban7 peh-siN3 hang5-hok8 ti7 goan2 e5 e7-bin7;  Iah8 beh hou7 liat8-pang ti7 goan2 e5 kha-e7.
4)	I ka7 goan2 keng2 goan2 e5 san2-giap8,  Chiu7-si7 I sou2 thiaN3 e5 Nga2-kok e5 eng5-kng. [Se3-lah8
5)	Siong7-te3 chiuN7-khi3, u7 hoah e5 siaN te3--I,  Ia5-ho5-hoa chiuN7-khi3, u7 ho7-thau5 e5 siaN te3--I.
6)	Lin2 tioh8 chhiuN3-koa, o-lo2 Siong7-te3, tioh8 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2;  ChhiuN3-koa o-lo2 lan2 e5 Ong5, tioh8 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2;
7)	In-ui7 Siong7-te3 si7 choan5-toe7 e5 Ong5,  Tioh8 eng7 ti3-hui7 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 I.
8)	Siong7-te3 choe3 ong5 ti7-li2 ban7-kok;  Siong7-te3 che7 ti7 I seng3 e5 po2-cho7.
9)	Liat8-pang e5 kui3-chok8 chu7-chip8,  Beh choe3 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 peh-siN3;  In-ui7 se3-kai3 e5 tin5-pai5 si7 siok8 ti7 Siong7-te3;  I si7 kek8-koaiN5.

[48]	Kho2-lah8 hou7-e3 e5 si-koa.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa chi3 toa7, eng-kai toa7-toa7 tit-tioh8 o-lo2;  Chiu7-si7 ti7 lan2 Siong7-te3 e5 siaN5, ti7 I seng3 e5 soaN.
2)	Sek-an soaN, toa7 kun-ong5 e5 siaN5, ti7 pak-bin7,  KoaiN5-toa7 koh ho2-khoaN3,  Hou7 choan5-toe7 sou2 hoaN-hi2.
3)	Siong7-te3 ti7 i e5 keng-tian7-lai7 ka-ki7 hian2-beng5 choe3 koaiN5-tai5.
4)	KhoaN3 ah, liat8-ong5 chu7-chip8,  In saN-kap tui3-chia keng-ke3.
5)	In khoaN3-kiN3 chiu7 gong5-ngiah8;  KiaN-hiaN5 kin2-kin2 chau2.
6)	In ti7-hia ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah,  Thang3-thiaN3 chhin-chhiuN7 siN-kiaN2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5.
7)	Li2 eng7 tang-hong,  Phah-phoa3 Tha-si e5 chun5.
8)	Goan2 ti7 ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN5-tiong, chiu7-si7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 siaN5-tiong,  Sou2 khoaN3-kiN3-e5 tu2-tu2 chiau3 goan2 sou2 thiaN-kiN3;  Siong7-te3 beh hou7 chit e5 siaN5 kian-kou3 kau3 eng2-oan2. [Se3-lah8
9)	Siong7-te3 ah, goan2 ti7 Li2 e5 tian7-lai7,  Siau3-liam7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3.
10)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 sou2 siu7 e5 o-lo2,  Tu2-tu2 kap Li2 e5 mia5 saN-hap8, kau3 ti7 toe7-kek8.  Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 moa2-moa2 kong-gi7.
11)	In-ui7 Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3,  Sek-an soaN tioh8 hoaN-hi2,  Iu5-tai7 e5 siaN5 tioh8 khoai3-lok8.
12)	Lin2 tioh8 seh8 Sek-an, si3-ui5 kiaN5 i,  Sng3 i e5 siaN5-lau5,
13)	Siong5-se3 khoaN3 i e5 siaN5-chhiuN5,  Seng2-chhat i e5 ong5-kiong,  Beh hou7 lin2 soan-thoan5 ti7 au7-tai7.
14)	In-ui7 chit e5 Siong7-te3 eng2-eng2 oan2-oan2 choe3 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3;  I beh chhoa7 lan2 kau3 ti7 si2 e5 si5.

[49]	Kho2-lah8 hou7-e3 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN;
1)	Cheng3 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 long2 tioh8 thiaN chit-e5,  Se3-chiuN7 long2-chong2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, lin2 tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang;
2)	Bo5-lun7 ha7-teng2 siong7-teng2,  Ho2-giah8 song3-hiong, long2 tioh8 an2-ni.
3)	Goa2 e5 chhui3 beh kong2 ti3-hui7,  Goa2 e5 sim sou2 siuN7 si7 thong-tat8.
4)	Goa2 beh aN3 hi7-khang thiaN phi3-ju7,  Goa2 beh eng7 khim5 koe2-beng5 goa2 e5 o3-biau7.
5)	Kan-ok te3 goa2 e5 kha-au7-tiN si3-bin7 ui5 goa2,  Ti7 chit-ho7 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8 goa2 mih-sai2 kiaN?
6)	Hiah e5 oa2-kho3 in e5 se3-lek8,  Khoa-khau2 in e5 pu3-u7 e5 lang5,
7)	Bo5 chit8-e5 u7 hoat-tou7 thang siok8-hoe5 ka-ki7 e5 hiaN-ti7,  Iah8 boe7-oe7 thoe3 i chiong siok8-hoe5 e5 ke3-chiN5 hou7 Siong7-te3;
8)	(In-ui7 siok8-hoe5 in e5 siN3-mia7 e5 ke3-chiN5 chin kui3,  Chi2-u7 eng2-oan2 pang3-soah;)
9)	Hou7 i tng5-tng5 oah8--teh,  Bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 hiu2-hoai7;
10)	In-ui7 i khoaN3-kiN3 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 si2,  Gu5-gong7 e5 lang5, kap chhin-chhiuN7 cheng-siN hit-khoan2 e5 lang5, iah8 choe3-chit8-e7 biat8-bo5;  Lau5 in e5 chiN5-chai5 hou7 pat8-lang5.
11)	In sim-lai7 siuN7 in e5 chhu3 beh eng2-eng2 ti7-teh,  In khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 beh kau3 ban7-tai7;  In eng7 ka-ki7 e5 mia5 lai5 mia5 ka-ki7 e5 toe7.
12)	Chong2-si7 lang5 tiam3 ti7 chun-kui3 e5 tiong-kan, boe7 ku2-tng5;  Chhin-chhiuN7 oe7 si2 e5 cheng-siN.
13)	In kiaN5 chit e5 lou7, si7 in e5 gong7;  Chong2-si7 in i2-au7 e5 lang5 iau2-ku2 liah8 in e5 oe7 choe3 tioh8. [Se3-lah8
14)	In chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-kun5, tiaN7-tioh8 tioh8 loh8 im-kan;  Si2-bo5 beh choe3 in e5 bok8-chia2;  Kau3 cha2-khi2 si5, cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5 beh koan2-hat in;  In e5 sui2 beh hou7 im-kan biat8--khi3,  Ti3-kau3 bo5 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7.
15)	Tok8-tok8 Siong7-te3 beh siok8-hoe5 goa2 e5 leng5-hun5, thoat-li7 im-kan e5 koan5-peng3;  In-ui7 I beh chiap-lap8 goa2. [Se3-lah8
16)	Lang5 hoat-chai5, ka-teng5 ke-thiN eng5-kng,  Li2 m7-bian2 in-ui7 an2-ni lai5 kiaN;
17)	In-ui7 i si2, bo5 chit8-hang7 oe7 toa3 khi3,  I e5 eng5-kng boe7-oe7 te3 i khi3.
18)	I chai7-siN sui-jian5 ka-ki7 khoa-khau2 u7 hok-khi3,  (Li2 na7 gau5 chiau3-kou3 ka-ki7, lang5 beh o-lo2 li2),
19)	Na7-si7 i beh kui kau3 i lek8-tai7 e5 chou2-kong hia,  In eng2-oan2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 kng.
20)	Lang5 tiam3 ti7 chun-kui3 e5 tiong-kan, iah8 bo5 chhiN2-gou7,  Si7 chhin-chhiuN7 oe7 si2 e5 cheng-siN.

[50]	A-sat e5 si.
1)	Choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 kong2-chhut oe7, lai5 tiau3 thiN-e7;  Tui3 jit8-chhut kau3 jit8-loh8 e5 sou2-chai7.
2)	Tui3 chiau5-chng5 sui2 e5 Sek-an,  Siong7-te3 u7 hoat-chhut kng.
3)	Goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh lai5, koat-toan3 bo5 cheng7-cheng7;  U7 he2 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 teh sio,  U7 hong ti7 I e5 si3-ui5 chin thau3.
4)	I beh kio3 teng2-bin7 e5 thiN kap toe7;  Ui7-tioh8 beh sim2-phoaN3 I e5 peh-siN3;
5)	Kong2, Tioh8 chio-chip8 Goa2 seng3 e5 peh-siN3 lai5 Goa2 chia,  Chiu7-si7 hiah-e5 eng7 che3-su7 kap Goa2 lip8-iok e5 lang5.
6)	Chiah e5 thiN beh hian2-beng5 I e5 kong-gi7;  In-ui7 Siong7-te3 pun2-sin si7 choe3 sim2-phoaN3--e5. [Se3-lah8
7)	Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 thiaN, Goa2 beh kong2;  I2-sek-liat8 ah, Goa2 beh keng2-kai3 li2;  Goa2 si7 Siong7-te3, li2 e5 Siong7-te3.
8)	Goa2 bo5 in-ui7 li2 e5 che3-su7 chek-pi7 li2;  Li2 e5 sio-che3 siong5-siong5 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
9)	Goa2 bo5 tui3 li2 e5 chhu3 chhu2 kang e5 gu5,  Iah8 bo5 tui3 li2 e5 tiau5 chhu2 kang e5 soaN-iuN5.
10)	In-ui7 chhiu7-na5-lai7 e5 pah-siu3,  Chheng-soaN e5 cheng-siN, long2 si7 Goa2 e5.
11)	SoaN-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, Goa2 long2 chai;  Khong3-ia2 e5 chau2-siu3 iah8 long2 siok8 ti7 Goa2.
12)	Goa2 na7 iau, bo5 beh ka7 li2 kong2;  In-ui7 se3-kai3 kap ki5-tiong sou2 chhiong-moa2 e5, long2 si7 Goa2 e5.
13)	Goa2 kiam2 beh chiah8 gu5-kang2 e5 bah,  A2-si7 lim soaN-iuN5-kang2 e5 huih mah?
14)	Li2 tioh8 eng7 kam2-sia7 choe3 che3, hian3 hou7 Siong7-te3;  Koh tioh8 tui3 Chi3-koaiN5--e5, sia7 li2 e5 goan7;
15)	Ti7 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8 tioh8 kiu5-kio3 Goa2;  Goa2 beh kiu3 li2, li2 iah8 beh eng5-kng Goa2.
16)	Na7-si7 Siong7-te3 tui3 phaiN2-lang5 kong2,  Li2 thai2-tho2 kaN2 thoan5 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7,  Chhui3 kong2-khi2 Goa2 e5 iok ah?
17)	Ki5-sit8 li2 iam3-chian7 ka3-si7,  Chiong Goa2 e5 oe7 hiat ti7 li2 e5 ka-chiah-au7.
18)	Li2 khoaN3-kiN3 chhat8, chiu7 kap i tang5-sim;  Koh kap kiaN5 kan-im5 e5 lang5 saN-kap u7 hun7.
19)	Li2 hou7 li2 e5 chhui3 siong5-siong5 kong2 phaiN2-oe7,  Li2 e5 chih8 cho7-chok kan-cha3.
20)	Li2 che7-teh hui2-pong3 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7;  Bu5-loa7 li2 e5 tang5-pau.
21)	Li2 kiaN5 chiah e5 su7, Goa2 cheng7-cheng7 bo5 kong2;  Li2 phah-sng3 Goa2 tu2-tu2 kap li2 chit8-iuN7.  Ki5-sit8 Goa2 beh chek-pi7 li2; chiong chiah e5 su7 pai5 ti7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5.
22)	Lin2 boe7-ki3-tit Siong7-te3 e5 lang5, tioh8 siuN7 chit e5 su7,  Bian2-ti3 Goa2 chiong lin2 thiah-chhui3, bo5 lang5 chin2-kiu3.
23)	KiN3-na7 eng7 kam2-sia7 hian3 choe3 che3-e5, chiu7-si7 eng5-kng Goa2;  Kin2-sin7 kiaN5 e5 lang5,  Goa2 beh hou7 i khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-te3 e5 kiu3-un.

[51]	Tai7-pit8 kap Poat8-si7-pa tang5-pang5 i2-au7, sian-ti Na2-tan lai5 kiN3 i, i choe3 chit e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, chiau3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 lin5-bin2 goa2;  Chiau3 Li2 hong-seng7 e5 chu5-pi chhat-siau goa2 e5 ke3-sit;
2)	Chiong goa2 e5 choe7-ok it-chin7 soe2-tu5,  Iah8 soe2-chheng goa2, kau3 bo5 choe7.
3)	In-ui7 goa2 ka-ki7 chai goa2 e5 ke3-sit;  Goa2 e5 choe7 siong5-siong5 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
4)	Goa2 sou2 hoan7-tioh8--e5, chiu7-si7 tek-choe7 Li2 na7-tiaN7,  Ti7 Li2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 kiaN5 chit-ho7 phaiN2;  Ti3-kau3 Li2 kong2-oe7 e5 si5, hian2-beng5 choe3-gi7;  PhoaN3-toan3 e5 si5, hian2-beng5 kong-to7.
5)	Goa2 si7 ti7 choe7-ok-tiong siN--e5,  Ti7 choe7 e5 tiong-kan, goa2 e5 lau7-bu2 hoai5-in7 goa2.
6)	Li2 sou2 ai3--e5 si7 sim-lai7 seng5-sit8;  Ti7 goa2 e5 pak-lai7, Li2 beh hou7 goa2 tit-tioh8 ti3-hui7.
7)	Kiu5 Li2 eng7 giu5-chhek-chhau2 soe2 goa2, goa2 chiu7 chheng-khi3;  Kiu5 Li2 soe2 goa2, goa2 chiu7 pi2 seh khah-peh8.
8)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 tit-tioh8 thiaN-kiN3 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8 e5 siaN;  Hou7 Li2 sou2 at-chih8 e5 kut thang hoaN-hi2.
9)	Kiu5 Li2 ng Li2 e5 bin7, bo5 khoaN3 goa2 e5 choe7,  Chhat-siau goa2 it-chhe3 e5 choe7-ok.
10)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 ka7 goa2 chhong3-cho7 chheng-khi3 e5 sim,  Hou7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 u7 oaN7-sin cheng3-tit8 e5 sin5.
11)	M7-thang koaN2 goa2, hou7 goa2 li7-khui Li2 e5 bin7;  M7-thang tui3 goa2 siu-hoe5 Li2 seng3 e5 sin5.
12)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 iu5-goan5 tit-tioh8 Li2 kiu3-un e5 khoai3-lok8;  SiuN2-su3 goa2 u7 chu7-iu5 e5 sin5, lai5 hu5-chhi5 goa2.
13)	Goa2 chiu7 chiong Li2 e5 to7-lou7 chi2-si7 u7 ke3-sit e5 lang5;  U7 choe7 e5 lang5 chiu7 beh kui-sun7 Li2.
14)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 si7 kiu3 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3,  Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 thai5-lang5 e5 choe7;  Goa2 e5 chih8 beh toa7-siaN gim5-si o-lo2 Li2 e5 gi7.
15)	Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 khui goa2 e5 chhui3-tun5;  Goa2 e5 chhui3 chiu7 beh po3-iong5 Li2 e5 ho2 mia5-siaN.
16)	In-ui7 Li2 bo5 ai3 che3-mih8; na7 ai3, goa2 chiu7 beh hian3;  Sio-che3 Li2 iah8 bo5 hoaN-hi2.
17)	Siong7-te3 sou2 ai3 e5 che3, chiu7-si7 iu-siong e5 sin5;  Siong7-te3 ah, iu-siong thong3-hoe2 e5 sim, Li2 bo5 beh khoaN3-khin i.
18)	Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 ho2 i3-su3, ho2 khoan2-thai7 Sek-an;  Khi2-cho7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5.
19)	Hit-si5 Li2 beh hoaN-hi2 gi7 e5 che3, kap sio-che3, i2-kip8 ka-nng5-chiah cheng-siN e5 sio-che3;  Hit-si5 lang5 beh chiong kang e5 gu5 hian3 ti7 Li2 e5 toaN5.

[52]	I2-tong lang5 To-ek lai5 po3 So3-lo5 kong2, Tai7-pit8 kau3 A-hi-bi2-lek8 e5 ke.  Hit-si5 Tai7-pit8 choe3 chit e5 ka3-si7 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Iong2-beng2 e5 lang5 ah, li2 siaN2-su7 ui7-tioh8 choe3-phaiN2 lai5 khoa-khau2?  Siong7-te3 e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
2)	Li2 e5 chih8 tou5-bou5 sia5-ok;  Chhin-chhiuN7 lai7 e5 thi3-thau5-to, kiaN5 kan-cha3.
3)	Li2 ai3 phaiN2 iaN5-ke3 ai3 ho2;  Ai3 peh8-chhat8 iaN5-ke3 ai3 kong2 gi7-li2. [Se3-lah8
4)	Khui2-khiat e5 chih8 ah,  Li2 ai3 kong2 it-chhe3 thun-chiah8 e5 oe7.
5)	Siong7-te3 iah8 beh hui2-hoai7 li2, kau3 eng2-oan2,  I beh liah8 li2, tui3 li2 e5 pou3-piN5-tiong khiu2--chhut-lai5;  Tui3 oah8 lang5 e5 toe7, chiong li2 puih8 chhut lai5. [Se3-lah8
6)	Gi7-lang5 beh khoaN3-kiN3 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5,  Iah8 beh chhio3 i, kong2,
7)	KhoaN3 ah, che chiu7-si7 hit-ho7 bo5 liah8 Siong7-te3 choe3 i e5 khui3-lat8 e5 lang5;  Si7 oa2-kho3 i e5 chiN5-chai5 e5 choe7,  Ti7 sia5-ok ka-ki7 khia7-chai7.
8)	Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 Siong7-te3 chhu3-lai7 chhiN-chhui3 e5 kaN-na2-chhiu7;  Goa2 eng2-eng2 oan2-oan2 oa2-kho3 Siong7-te3 e5 chu5-ai3.
9)	In-ui7 Li2 kiaN5 che, goa2 beh kam2-sia7 Li2 kau3 eng2-oan2;  Goa2 iah8 beh ti7 Li2 seng3 e5 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5 ng3-bang7 Li2 e5 mia5; in-ui7 i e5 mia5 si7 ho2.

[53]	Tai7-pit8 ka3-si7 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, si7 eng7 Ba5-hap-lah8.
1)	Gong7-lang5 sim-lai7 kong2, Bo5 u7 Siong7-te3.  In than3 sia5-ok, kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 choe7;  Bo5 chit8-lang5 kiaN5 ho2.
2)	Siong7-te3 tui3 thiN aN3-loh8 khoaN3 se3-kan-lang5,  Beh khoaN3 u7 beng5-li2 e5 lang5,  U7 chhe7-kiu5 Siong7-te3 e5 lang5 a2-bo5.
3)	In tak8-lang5 long2 the3-au7, it-khai3 pian3-choe3 u3-oe3;  Bo5 lang5 kiaN5 ho2, lian5 chit8-e5 iah8 bo5.
4)	Choe3 phaiN2 e5 lang5 kiam2 boe7 hiau2-tit mah?  In thun-chiah8 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8-piaN2.  Iah8 bo5 kiu5-kio3 Siong7-te3.
5)	In ti7 bo5 thang kiaN-hiaN5 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7 toa7-toa7 kiaN-hiaN5;  In-ui7 siong7-te3 chiong hit-e5 an-iaN5 kong-kek li2 e5 lang5 e5 kut-thau5 phah-soaN3;  Li2 hou7 in kian3-siau3, in-ui7 Siong7-te3 khi3-sak in.
6)	Goan7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chin2-kiu3 tui3 Sek-an chhut;  Siong7-te3 kiu3 I siu7-liah8 e5 peh-siN3 to3-tng2--lai5,  Hit-si5 Nga2-kok beh khoai3-lok8, I2-sek-liat8 beh hoaN-hi2.

[54]	Se-hut lang5 lai5 tui3 So3-lo5 kong2, Tai7-pit8 kiam2-m7-si7 bih ti7 goan2 hia mah?  Hit-si5 Tai7-pit8 choe3 chit e5 ka3-si7 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; eng7 si-hian5 e5 gak8-khi3.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 mia5 kiu3 goa2;  Eng7 Li2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5 thoe3 goa2 sin-oan.
2)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 thiaN goa2 e5 ki5-to2;  AN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.
3)	In-ui7 goa7-lang5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek goa2,  Kiong5-ok e5 lang5 siau3-siuN7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7;  In bo5 keng3-hong7 Siong7-te3 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5. [Se3-lah8
4)	Siong7-te3 si7 pang-chan7 goa2 e5,  Chu2 si7 hu5-chhi5 goa2 e5 oah8-mia7 e5.
5)	I beh chiong goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2 po3-eng3 in;  Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 seng5-sit8 biat8-bo5 in.
6)	Goa2 beh chiong kam-sim e5 che3-su7 hian3 hou7 Li2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 beh kam2-sia7 o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5; in-ui7 Li2 e5 mia5 si7 ho2.
7)	I kiu3 goa2 chhut it-chhe3 e5 hoan7-lan7;  Goa2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 tu2-tioh8 po3-eng3.

[55]	Tai7-pit8 ka3-si7 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; eng7 si-hian5 e5 gak8-khi3. 
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 ki5-to2;  M7-thang tiam3-bat8, m7 thiaN goa2 e5 khun2-kiu5.
2)	Kiu5 Li2 aN3-loh8 thiaN goa2, in3 goa2;  Goa2 pi-siong bo5 peng5-an, haiN-haiN-chhan;
3)	Long2 si7 in-ui7 tui3-tek8 e5 siaN, phaiN2-lang5 e5 che3-ap;  In-ui7 in chiong choe7-koa3 chhia hou7 goa2, eng7 siu7-khi3 pek goa2.
4)	Goa2 e5 sim ti7 goa2 lai7-bin7 chin khou2-thang3;  Si2-bo5 e5 kiaN-hiaN5 kau3 ti7 goa2.
5)	KiaN-hiaN5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah kau3 ti7 goa2,  KiaN-hiaN5 im-bat8 goa2.
6)	Goa2 chiu7 kong2, Goan7 goa2 tit-tioh8 sit8, chhin-chhiuN7 kap,  Goa2 chiu7 pe--khi3, tit-tioh8 an-jian5 khia7-khi2.
7)	Goa2 beh pe--khi3 hng7-hng7,  Hioh ti7 khong3-ia2. [Se3-lah8
8)	Goa2 beh kin2-kin2 chau2 kau3 siam2-pi7 e5 sou2-chai7,  Thoat-li7 kong5-hong po3-thau5.
9)	Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 thun-biat8 in, pun-khui in e5 chih8;  In-ui7 goa2 ti7 siaN5-lai7 bat khoaN3-kiN3 kiong5-po7 kap saN-chiN e5 su7.
10)	In mi5-jit8 kiaN5-seh8 ti7 siaN5-chhiuN5-teng2;  Ti7 siaN5-lai7 u7 hu-ke2 ok-tok8.
11)	Sia5-ok ti7 hit lai7-bin7;  Ap-che3 kan-cha3 bo5 li7-khui i e5 koe-lou7.
12)	In-ui7 hui2-pong3 goa2--e5, m7-si7 tui3-tek8;  Siat-su2 si7, chiu7 iau2 oe7 lun2--tit;  Chu7-ko kong-kek goa2--e5, m7-si7 oan3-hun7 goa2 e5 lang5;  Siat-su2 si7, chiu7 oe7 bih lai5 siam2 i.
13)	Bo5 phah-sng3 si7 li2, tou si7 goa2 peng5-poe3 e5 lang5,  Goa2 e5 tang5-phoaN7, goa2 ti-ki2 e5 peng5-iu2.
14)	Lan2 peng5-sou3 saN-kap tam5-lun7 chin chhin-bit8, Lan2 kap cheng3-lang5 saN-kap kiaN5 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3.
15)	Goan7 si2-bo5 hut-jian5 kau3 ti7 in,  Hou7 in oah8-oah8 loh8 im-kan;  In-ui7 sia5-ok ti7 in khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, ti7 in e5 tiong-kan.
16)	Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 beh kiu5-kio3 Siong7-te3;  Ia5-ho5-hoa beh kiu3 goa2.
17)	E5-hng, cha2-khi2, jit8-tau3, goa2 beh ai-siong thou2-khui3;  I iah8 beh thiaN goa2 e5 siaN.
18)	I kiu3-siok8 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7, thoat-li7 kong-kek goa2 e5 lang5; hou7 goa2 tit-tioh8 peng5-an;  In-ui7 hoan2-tui3 goa2 e5 lang5 choe7.
19)	Tui3 kou2-cha2 siong5-siong5 ti7-teh e5 Siong7-te3,  Beh thiaN-kiN3, iah8 beh po3-eng3 in; [Se3-lah8	
	Chiu7-si7 hiah e5 bo5 koe2-piN3, bo5 keng3-ui3 Siong7-te3 e5 lang5.
20)	I chhun-chhiu2 kong-kek kap i saN-ho5 e5 lang5;  I i2-keng poe7 i e5 iok.
21)	I e5 chhui3 kut8-tiah8, chhin-chhiuN7 lin-iu5;  I e5 sim khng3 kau-chian3;  I e5 oe7 jiu5-loan2, khah-iaN5 ko-iu5,  Ki5-sit8 si7 chhut-siu3 e5 to.
22)	Tioh8 chiong li2 e5 taN3, sia3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  I beh hu5-chhi5 li2, I eng2-eng2 bo5 hou7 gi7-lang5 io5-choah.
23)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 beh hou7 in ham7-loh8 ti7 biat8-bo5 e5 khiN;  Thai5-si2 lang5 kiaN5 kan-cha3 e5, boe7 oah8 kau3 tiong-lian5;  Tok8-tok8 goa2 beh oa2-kho3 Li2.

[56]	Hui-li7-su7 lang5 ti7 Ka-tek8 liah8-tioh8 Tai7-pit8, hit-si5 i choe3 chit e5 kim e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, si7 eng7 "hng7-hng7 bo5 siaN e5 kap"
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kho2-lin5 goa2, in-ui7 lang5 beh thun-chiah8 goa2;  Thong-jit8 kong-kek, ap-che3 goa2.
2)	Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 thong-jit8 beh thun-chiah8 goa2,  In-ui7 khi2 kiau-ngou7 kong-kek goa2 e5 lang5 chin choe7.
3)	Goa2 ti7 kiaN-hiaN5 e5 si5,  Goa2 beh oa2-kho3 Li2.
4)	Goa2 kho3 Siong7-te3, goa2 beh o-lo2 I e5 oe7;  Goa2 i2-keng oa2-kho3 Siong7-te3, goa2 chiu7 bo5 kiaN.  Siok8 ti7 hiat-khi3--e5 beh siaN2 hoat-tit goa2 ta-oa5?
5)	In thong-jit8 koe2-chhoah8 goa2 e5 oe7;  In tui3 goa2 sou2-siuN7--e5, long2 si7 beh hai7 goa2.
6)	In chu7-chip8, bai5-hok8, teh siong3 goa2 e5 kha-pou7,  Chhin-chhiuN7 tng-tan2 beh hai7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7.
7)	In choe3-phaiN2 kiam2 oe7 to5-thoat mah?  Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 ti7 siu7-khi3-tiong, hou7 cheng3 peh-siN3 tui7-loh8.
8)	Goa2 e5 liu5-lok8, Li2 long2 ki3-siau3;  Kiu5 Li2 chiong goa2 e5 bak8-sai2 siu ti7 Li2 e5 phe5-long5;  Che kiam2 bo5 long2 ki3 ti7 Li2 e5 chheh mah?
9)	Goa2 kiu5-kio3 e5 jit8, goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 long2 beh oat8-tng2-sin the3--khi3;  Siong7-te3 ui7 goa2, che si7 goa2 sou2 chai.
10)	Goa2 kho3 Siong7-te3, goa2 beh o-lo2 I e5 oe7;  Goa2 kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, goa2 beh o-lo2 I e5 oe7.
11)	Goa2 i2-keng oa2-kho3 Siong7-te3, goa2 chiu7 bo5 kiaN;  Lang5 beh siaN2 hoat-tit goa2 ta-oa5?
12)	Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 tui3 Li2 sou2 he7 e5 goan7 ti7 goa2 e5 sin-chiuN7;  Goa2 beh eng7 sia7-un e5 che3 hian3 hou7 Li2.
13)	In-ui7 Li2 kiu3 goa2 e5 oah8-mia7 thoat-li7 si2-bo5;  Li2 kiam2-m7-si7 po2-hou7 goa2 e5 kha bo5 poah8-to2 mah?  Hou7 goa2 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, kiaN5 ti7 oah8-mia7 e5 kng tiong mah?

[57]	Tai7-pit8 siam2-pi7 So3-lo5, bih ti7 tong7-lai7; hit-si5 i choe3 chit e5 kim e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, si7 eng7 "Boh8-tit hui2-hoai7--e5".
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kho2-lin5 goa2, kho2-lin5 goa2;  Goa2 e5 sin beh tau5-hioh ti7 Li2;  Goa2 beh tau5-hioh ti7 Li2 sit8-kou2 e5 ti3-im3-e7,  Theng3-hau7 chiah e5 chai-e7 keng-ke3.
2)	Goa2 beh kiu5-kio3 Chi3-koaiN5 e5 Siong7-te3;  Chiu7-si7 ka7 goa2 chhiaN5-ti5 tak8-hang7 su7 e5 Siong7-te3.
3)	Tng hit e5 beh thun-chiah8 goa2 e5 lang5 hui2-pong3 goa2 e5 si5,  Siong7-te3 beh si-un, tui3 thiN kiu3 goa2; [Se3-lah8  Iah8 beh hoat-chhut I e5 chu5-ai3, kap I e5 seng5-sit8.
4)	Goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 ti7 sai e5 tiong-kan;  Goa2 to2 ti7 chhin-chhiuN7 he2 toh8 e5 se3-kan lang5 e5 tiong-kan;  In e5 chhui3-khi2 si7 chhiuN si7 chiN3,  In e5 chih8 si7 lai7-to.
5)	Siong7-te3 ah, goan7 Li2 koaiN5-toa7 poaN5-ke3 chiah e5 thiN,  Goan7 Li2 e5 eng5-kng poaN5-ke3 choan5-toe7.
6)	In ka7 goa2 e5 kha-pou7 siat lo5-bang7,  Ap-che3 goa2 e5 sim-sin5;  In ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 khui ham7-khiN,  Ka-ki7 hoan2-tng2 poah8-loh8 hit lai7-bin7. [Se3-lah8
7)	Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 e5 sim chu7-chai7, goa2 e5 sim chu7-chai7;  Goa2 beh gim5-si, goa2 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2.
8)	Goa2 e5 sin5 ah, li2 tioh8 cheng-sin5 khi2-lai5;  Khim5 ah, sek ah, lin2 tioh8 cheng-sin5 khi2-lai5;  Goa2 pun2-sin beh chin cha2 cheng-sin5 khi2-lai5.
9)	Chu2 ah, Goa2 beh ti7 ban7 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan kam2-sia7 Li2;  Ti7 liat8-pang e5 tiong-kan chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2.
10)	In-ui7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 toa7 kau3 tu2-thiN,  Li2 e5 seng5-sit8 kau3 kiong-chhong.
11)	Siong7-te3 ah, goan7 Li2 koaiN5-toa7 poaN5-ke3 chiah e5 thiN;  Goan7 Li2 e5 eng5-kng poaN5-ke3 choan5-toe7.

[58]	Tai7-pit8 kim e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, si7 eng7 "Boh8--tit hui2-hoai7".
1)	Se3-kan lang5 ah, lin2 cheng7-cheng7 kiam2 chin-chiaN3 kong2 kong-gi7 mah?  Lin2 kiam2 chiau3 seng5-sit8 kiaN5 sim2-phoaN3 mah?	
2)	M7-si7, lin2 si7 sim-lai7 choe3 phaiN2;  Lin2 ti7 toe7-chiuN7, eng7 lin2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 e5 kiong5-po7, chhin3 hou7 lang5.
3)	PhaiN2-lang5 chit8-e7 chhut bu2-thai, chiu7 kap Siong7-te3 chhiN-sou;  Chit8-e7 li7-khui lau7-bu2 e5 pak-tou2, chiu7 kiaN5 chha-lou7, kong2 peh8-chhat8 oe7.
4)	In e5 tok8 chhin-chhiuN7 choa5 e5 tok8,  In chhin-chhiuN7 chhau3-hi7-lang5 e5 tok8-choa5 that-bat8 hi7-khang;
5)	M7-thiaN khu-choa5 e5 lang5 e5 siaN,  Sui-bong2 gau5 ui7-hu5 liam7-chiu3--e5, in iah8 m7-thiaN.
6)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 phah-chih8 in chhui3-lai7 e5 khi2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 phah-chih8 sai-a2-thun5 e5 toa7 ki chhui3-khi2.
7)	Goan7 in siau-biat8 chhin-chhiuN7 kin2-kin2 lau5 e5 chui2;  In e5 chiN3 pi2 beh sia7 e5 si5, goan7 in e5 chiN3 chhin-chhiuN7 phah-chih8.
8)	Goan7 in chhin-chhiuN7 lou5-le5, siau-iuN5--khi3;  Koh chhin-chhiuN7 hu5-jin5-lang5 ka-lauh8 bo5 kiN3-tioh8 thiN-jit8 e5 thai.
9)	Lin2 eng7 chhi3-a2 hiaN5 he2, tiaN2 iau2-be7 jiat8,  I beh eng7 kng2-le5-hong, chiong chhiN--e5 kap toh8--e5, choe3 chit8-e7 sau3--khi3.
10)	Gi7-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 po3-eng3 e5 su7, chiu7 hoaN-hi2;  I beh ti7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 huih soe2 i e5 kha.
11)	Lang5 chiu7 beh kong2, Gi7-lang5 chin-chiaN3 u7 ho2-po3;  Ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 ko2-jian5 u7 Siong7-te3 teh phoaN3-toan3.

[59]	So3-lo5 chhe lang5 khi3 bai5-hok8 Tai7-pit8 e5 chhu3, beh thai5--i;  hit-si5 Tai7-pit8 choe3 chit e5 kim e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, eng7 "Boh8-tit hui2-hoai7".
1)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8;  An-ti3 goa2 ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7, tit-tioh8 thoat-li7 hiah-e5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek goa2 e5 lang5.
2)	Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5,  Koh kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 ai3 thai5-si2 lang5 e5 lang5.
3)	In-ui7 in bai5-hok8 beh hai7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7;  U7 beng2-lang5 chu7-chip8 lai5 kong-kek goa2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, che m7-si7 in-ui7 goa2 e5 ke3-sit, iah8 m7-si7 in-ui7 goa2 e5 choe7-koa3.
4)	Goa2 sui-jian5 bo5 ke3-sit, in chau2 lai5, pi7-pan7 beh hai7 goa2;  Kiu5 Li2 cheng-sin5 khi2-lai5 pang-chan7 goa2, lai5 kam3-chhat.
5)	Ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 ah,  Kiu5 Li2 khi2--lai5, pan7-li2 ban7-kok; m7-thang lin5-bin2 kiN3-na7 kiaN5 kan-cha3 e5 phaiN2-lang5. [Se3-lah8
6)	In e5-hng-si5 to3--lai5, au5-kio3 chhin-chhiuN7 kau2;  Ti7 siaN5--nih si3-koe3 kiaN5.
7)	In e5 chhui3 thou3-chhut phaiN2-oe7,  Chhui3-tun5 u7 to.  In-ui7 in kong2, Chi7-chui7 thiaN-kiN3?
8)	Na7-si7 Li2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chhio3 in,  Li2 beh chhin3-chhio3 liat8-pang.
9)	Goa2 e5 khui3-lat8 ah, goa2 beh ng3-bang7 Li2;  In-ui7 Siong7-te3 si7 goa2 e5 koaiN5-tai5.
10)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh eng7 chu5-ai3 ngia5-chih goa2;  Siong7-te3 beh hou7 goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 siu7 po3-eng3.
11)	Boh8-tit chau5-biat8 in, kiaN-kiN3 goa2 e5 peh-siN3 boe7-ki3-tit;  Chu2 ah, goan2 e5 tin5-pai5 ah,  Kiu5 Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 khui3-lat8, hou7 in si3-soaN3, koh kang3-ke7.
12)	In-ui7 in chhui3 e5 choe7-koa3 kap chhui3-tun5 e5 oe7,  I2-kip8 in sou2 kong2 e5 chiu3-me7 kap peh8-chhat8,  Goan7 in ti7 kiau-ngou7 e5 tiong-kan siu7 liah8-tioh8.
13)	Kiu5 Li2 siu7-khi3 chau5-biat8 in, chau5-biat8 in, kau3 long2 bo5--khi3;  Hou7 in chai Siong7-te3 ti7 Nga2-kok e5 tiong-kan chiang2-koan5,  Kau3 ti7 toe7-kek8. [Se3-lah8
14)	In e5-hng-si5 to3--lai5, au5-kio3 chhin-chhiuN7 kau2;  Ti7 siaN5--nih si3-koe3 kiaN5.
15)	In beh chau2-lai5 chau2-khi3 chhe7 chiah8-mih8;  Na7 bo5 tit-tioh8 pa2, chiu7 thong-mi5 theng3-hau7.
16)	Na7-si7 goa2 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2 e5 khui3-lat8,  Cha2-khi2-si5 beh toa7-siaN o-lo2 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3;  In-ui7 Li2 bat choe3 goa2 e5 koaiN5-tai5,  Ti7 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8, choe3 goa2 to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7.
17)	Goa2 e5 khui3-lat8 ah, goa2 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2;  In-ui7 Siong7-te3 si7 goa2 e5 koaiN5-tai5, si7 goa2 chu5-ai3 e5 Siong7-te3.

[60]	Tai7-pit8 ti7 nng7-tiau5 khoe e5 A-lan5, i2-kip8 So2-pa e5 A-lan5, kau-chian3 e5 si5, Iok-ap to3-lai5 ti7 Iam5-kok, thai5-si2 I2-tong lang5 chit8-ban7 nng7-chheng, hit-si5 Tai7-pit8 choe3 chit e5 kim e5 si, hou7 lang5 hak8-sip8; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, eng7 "Choe3 kan-cheng3 e5 pek-hap8-hoe".
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 bat khi3-sak goan2, pho3-hoai7 goan2;  Li2 bat siu7-khi3 goan2, kiu5 Li2 hou7 goan2 koh heng-khi2.
2)	Li2 hou7 toe7 tin2-tang7, iah8 hou7 i pang-lih8;  Goan7 Li2 i-ho2 i e5 lih8-hun5; in-ui7 toe7 io5-tang7.
3)	Li2 hou7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 tu2-tioh8 kan-lan5;  Li2 hou7 goan2 lim hit e5 hou7 lang5 tian-lai5 to2-khi3 e5 chiu2.
4)	Li2 eng7 ki5 siuN2-su3 keng3-ui3 Li2 e5 lang5,  Thang ui7 chin-li2 kiah8--khi2-lai5 iat8. [Se3-lah8
5)	Kiu5 Li2 thiaN goan2, eng7 chiaN3-chhiu2 khan-kiu3 goan2,  Thang hou7 Li2 sou2 thiaN3 e5 lang5 tit-tioh8 kiu3.
6)	Siong7-te3 i2-keng ki2 I e5 seng3-kiat lai5 kong2, Goa2 beh tai7-iat8,  Goa2 beh pun-khui Si7-kiam3, niu5 Sou-kat e5 soaN-kok.
7)	Ki-liat8 si7 Goa2-e5, Ma2-na2-se iah8 si7 Goa2-e5;  I2-hoat-lian5 si7 Goa2 e5 thau5-khoe;  Iu5-tai7 si7 Goa2 e5 koan5-peng3.
8)	Mou5-ap beh choe3 Goa2 e5 ek8-phun5;  Goa2 beh hiat Goa2 e5 oe5 ti7 I2-tong;  Hui-li7-su7 toe7 ah, li2 in-ui7 Goa2 lai5 toa7-siaN hoah.
9)	Chi7-chui7 oe7 chhoa7 goa2 jip8 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5?  Chi7-chui7 chhoa7 goa2 jip8 I2-tong e5 toe7?
10)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 kiam2 m7-si7 khi3-sak goan2 mah?  Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 bo5 kap goan2 e5 kun-peng saN-kap chhut-khi3.
11)	Kiu5 Li2 pang-chan7 goan2 kong-kek tui3-tek8;  In-ui7 lang5 e5 chin2-kiu3 si7 khang-khang.
12)	Goan2 oa2-kho3 Siong7-te3, choe3-chiaN5 toa7 tai7-chi3;  In-ui7 thun2-tah8 goan2 e5 tui3-tek8--e5, chiu7-si7 I.

[61]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; eng7 si-hian5 e5 gak8-khi3.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 thiaN goa2 e5 kiu5-kio3;  AN3-loh8 thiaN goa2 e5 ki5-to2.
2)	Goa2 e5 sim sit-chi3 e5 si5, chiu7 beh tui3 toe7-kek8 kiu5-kio3 Li2;  Kiu5 Li2 chhoa7 goa2 kau3 hit-e5 pi2 goa2 khah-koaiN5 e5 chioh8-poaN5.
3)	In-ui7 Li2 bat choe3 goa2 to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7.  Choe3 goa2 kian-kou3 e5 tai5, lai5 thoat-li7 tui3-tek8.
4)	Goa2 beh eng2-oan2 toa3 ti7 Li2 e5 pou3-piN5;  Goa2 beh bih ti7 Li2 sit8-e7 un2-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7. [Se3-lah8
5)	Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 sou2 he7 e5 goan7, Li2 u7 thiaN-kiN3;  Li2 u7 chiong san2-giap8 siuN2-su3 keng3-ui3 Li2 e5 mia5 e5 lang5.
6)	Li2 beh ke-thiN ong5 e5 he3-siu7;  I e5 ni5-he3 beh kau3 tai7-tai7.
7)	I beh eng2-oan2 che7-ui7 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5;  Goan7 Li2 pi7-pan7 chu5-ai3 kap seng5-sit8 lai5 po2-hou7 i.
8)	An2-ni goa2 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5, kau3 eng2-oan2;  Thang jit8-jit8 sia7 goa2 e5 goan7.

[62]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, chiau3 Ia5-tou7-tun3 e5 choe3-hoat; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Goa2 e5 sim cheng7-cheng7, choan-bu7 theng3-hau7 Siong7-te3,  Goa2 e5 chin2-kiu3 si7 tui3 I lai5.
2)	Tok8-tok8 I si7 goa2 e5 chioh8-poaN5, chin2-kiu3 goa2-e5;  I si7 goa2 e5 koaiN5-tai5, goa2 boe7 toa7 io5-tang7.
3)	Lin2 tai7-ke kong-kek lang5,  Chiong i hui2-hoai7,  Chhin-chhiuN7 hui2-hoai7 khi-chhia5 e5 chhiuN5, beh to2 e5 piah, beh kau3 ti7-si5 ah?
4)	In saN-kap ke3-bou5 choan-bu7 beh tui3 i chun-kui3 e5 ui7 ka7 i chhia--loh8-khi3,  In hoaN-hi2 peh8-chhat8;  In chhui3 chiok-hok, sim chiu3-chou2. [Se3-lah8
5)	Goa2 e5 sin5 ah, li2 tioh8 cheng7-cheng7, choan-bu7 theng3-hau7 Siong7-te3;  In-ui7 goa2 e5 ng3-bang7 si7 tui3 I lai5.
6)	Tok8-tok8 I si7 goa2 e5 chioh8-poaN5, si7 chin2-kiu3 goa2 e5;  I si7 goa2 e5 koaiN5-tai5, goa2 boe7 io5-tang7.
7)	Goa2 e5 chin2-kiu3, goa2 e5 eng5-kng, chai7-ti7 Siong7-te3;  Goa2 e5 khui3-lat8 e5 chioh8-poaN5, goa2 e5 siam2-pi7 e5 sou2-chai7, iah8 chai7-ti7 Siong7-te3.
8)	Lin2 cheng3 peh-siN3, tioh8 si5-si5 oa2-kho3 I;  Ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 piaN3-chhut lin2 e5 sim;  Siong7-te3 si7 lan2 to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7. [Se3-lah8
9)	Pi-bi5 e5 lang5 chin-chiaN3 si7 khang-hu, chun-kui3 e5 lang5 ia7 si7 hu-ke2;  He7 ti7 thian-pheng5-oaN2, tek-khak phu5--khi2-lai5,  In it-khai3 pi2 hou-khip e5 khi3 khah-khin.
10)	M7-thang oa2-kho3 po7-giok8;  M7-thang in-ui7 chhiuN2-theh8 lai5 kiau-ngou7;  Na7 chai5-po2 ke-thiN, m7-thang chu3-i3 ti7-hia.
11)	Siong7-te3 kong2 chit8-pai2,  Goa2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 nng7-hang7;  Chiu7-si7 koan5-leng5 siok8 ti7 Siong7-te3.
12)	Chu2 ah, chu5-ai3 iah8 si7 siok8 ti7 Li2;  In-ui7 Li2 chiau3 tak8-lang5 e5 sou2-kiaN5 lai5 po3-eng3 i.

[63]	Tai7-pit8 ti7 Iu5-tai7 khong3-ia2 e5 si5 choe3 chit siu2 si.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3; goa2 than3-cha2 beh chhe7 Li2.  Ti7 khong3-han7, khun3-khou2, bo5 chui2 e5 toe7,  Goa2 e5 sim chhui3-ta siau3-liam7 Li2,  goa2 e5 jiok8-the2 chhiat-chhiat him-bou7 Li2.
2)	Goa2 bat an2-ni ti7 seng3-sou2 tiau5-kiN3 Li2,  Ui7-tioh8 ai3 khoaN3 Li2 e5 koan5-leng5 kap Li2 e5 eng5-kng.
3)	In-ui7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 pi2 siN3-mia7 khah-ho2,  Goa2 e5 chhui3-tun5 beh o-lo2 Li2.
4)	Goa2 iau2-oah8 e5 si5, beh an2-ni o-lo2 Li2;  Goa2 beh hong7 Li2 e5 mia5, kiah8-khi2 goa2 e5 chhiu2.
5)	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 beh pa2-chiok chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8 kut-chhe2 iu5-ji7;  Goa2 iah8 beh eng7 hoaN-hi2 e5 chhui3-tun5 o-lo2 Li2;
6)	Chiu7-si7 goa2 to2 ti7 bin5-chhng5 ki3-liam7 Li2,  Ti7 mi5-kan tak8-kiN siau3-liam7 Li2 e5 si5.
7)	In-ui7 Li2 bat pang-chan7 goa2,  Goa2 tiam3 ti7 Li2 sit8-kou2 e5 ti3-im3-e7 beh hoaN-hi2 chhut-siaN.
8)	Goa2 e5 sim te3 Li2 tiau5-tiau5;  Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 hu5-chhi5 goa2.
9)	Tok8-tok8 hiah e5 siau3-siuN7 beh biat8 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5,  I beh ham7-loh8 ti7 toe7-e7 chhim e5 sou2-chai7.
10)	In beh hou7 to-kiam3 thai5;  In beh hou7 soaN-kau2 chiah8.
11)	Chong2-si7 ong5 beh in-ui7 Siong7-te3 lai5 hoaN-hi2;  Hoan7-na7 ki2 I lai5 chiu3-choa7--e5 teh-beh khoa-khau2;  In-ui7 peh8-chhat8 lang5 e5 chhui3 beh siu7 that-bat8.

[64]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 ai-siong e5 si5, kiu5 Li2 thiaN goa2 e5 siaN;  Kiu5 Li2 po2-hou7 goa2 e5 oah8-mia7 bian2 kiaN tui3-tek8.
2)	Kiu5 Li2 chiong goa2 khng3-bat8, hou7 goa2 thoat-li7 choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5 am3-chiN7 e5 ke3-bou5,  Kap kiaN5 put-gi7 e5 lang5 e5 jiau2-loan7.
3)	In boa5 in e5 chih8 chhin-chhiuN7 to;  In pi2-chun2 in e5 chiN3, chiu7-si7 ok-tok8 e5 oe7.
4)	Beh ti7 am3-chiN7 e5 sou2-chai7 sia7 oan5-choan5 e5 lang5;  In hut-jian5 sia7-tioh8 i, iah8 m7-kiaN.
5)	In saN bian2-le7 siat phaiN2 ke3-bou5;  In chham-siong5 am3-chiN7 tiuN lo5-bang7;  Kong2, Chi7-chui7 oe7 khoaN3-kiN3 in?
6)	In tou5-bou5 phaiN2-tai7, kong2, Goan2 chin7-lat8 tou5-bou5 i2-keng u7 tu2-ho2 e5 ke3-bou5;  In tak8-lang5 e5 liam7-thau5 kap sim-su put-chi2 chhim.
7)	Chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 beh eng7 chiN3 sia7 in;  In hut-jian5 tioh8-siong.
8)	In beh tioh8-tak, in e5 chih8 oe7 hai7 in pun2-sin;  Hoan7-na7 khoaN3-kiN3 in e5 , long2 beh io5-thau5.
9)	Cheng3-lang5 long2 beh kiaN-hiaN5,  Beh po3-iong5 Siong7-te3 sou2 choe3--e5,  Koh siong5-se3 siuN7 I e5 sou2-kiaN5.
10)	Gi7-lang5 beh in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 hoaN-hi2, iah8 beh oa2-kho3 I;  Hoan7-na7 sim cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5, long2 beh khoa-khau2.

[65]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si-koa, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, ti7 Sek-an u7 lang5 o-lo2 teh theng3-hau7 Li2;  Iah8 beh tui3 Li2 sia7 sou2 he7 e5 goan7.
2)	ThiaN lang5 ki5-to2 e5 Chu2 ah,  KiN3 u7 hiat-khi3-e5 long2 beh chiu7-kun7 Li2.
3)	Choe7-ok khah-iaN5 goa2;  Lun7-kau3 goan2 e5 ke3-sit, Li2 long2 beh sia3-bian2.
4)	Li2 sou2 keng2-soan2, hou7 i chhin-kun7 Li2,  Tiam3 ti7 Li2 e5 iN7-lai7--e5, chit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3;  Goan2 beh in-ui7 Li2 e5 chhu3, Li2 e5 seng3-tian7 e5 hok-khi3,  Lai5 sim-moa2 i3-chiok.
5)	Kiu3 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah,  Li2 beh eng7 ui-giam5, peng2 kong-gi7 lai5 in3 goan2;  Li2 si7 toe7-kek8 kap hai2-bin7 hng7-hng7 e5 lang5,  Long2-chong2 sou2 oa2-kho3--e5.
6)	I i2-keng eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 ha5-io;  Chiu7 eng7 I e5 khui3-lat8 an-tiaN7 chiah e5 soaN.
7)	Chiah e5 hai2 hoa7-hoa7-hau2, kap ki5-tiong hai2-eng2 hoa7-hoa7-hau2,  I2-kip8 ban7 peh-siN3 e5 soan-hoa, I hou7 in peng5-cheng7.
8)	Khia7-khi2 toe7-kek8 e5 lang5 in-ui7 Li2 e5 sin5-jiah lai5 kiaN-hiaN5;  Jit8-chhut jit8-loh8 e5 sou2-chai7, Li2 hou7 in long2 hoaN-hi2.
9)	Li2 koan3-kou3 thou2-toe7, loh8 hou7 koan3-ak i, hou7 i chin-pui5;  Siong7-te3 e5 ho5, i e5 chui2 moa2-moa2;  Li2 an2-ni pi7-pan7 thou2-toe7, chiu7-si7 thoe3 lang5 pi7-pan7 gou7-kak.
10)	Li2 koan3-ak chhan5-hng5, moa2 i e5 kau, siu piN5 i e5 leng5;  Loh8 ho2 e5 hou7-chui2, hou7 thou2-toe7 nng2-nng2;  Ki5-tiong sou2 hoat-siN--e5 tit-tioh8 Li2 su3-hok.
11)	Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 un-tian2 choe3 ni5-tang e5 bian2-liu5,  Li2 e5 lou7-keng3 long2 u7 iu5 teh tih.
12)	Tih ti7 khong3-ia2 e5 chhau2-pou;  SoaN-thau5 eng7 hoaN-hi2 choe3-toa3 lai5 ha5.
13)	Chhau2-pou eng7 iuN5-kun5 choe3 saN lai5 chheng7;  SoaN-kok eng7 gou7-kak choe3 moa lai5 kham3;  In long2 hoaN-hi2 chhut-siaN, lai5 gim5-si.

[66]	Chit phiN si-koa, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Choan5-toe7 long2 tioh8 tui3 Siong7-te3 lai5 chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN;
2)	ChhiuN3-koa o-lo2 I e5 mia5 e5 eng5-kng;  Eng7 o-lo2 e5 oe7 lai5 hian2-beng5 I e5 eng5-kng.
3)	Tioh8 tui3 Siong7-te3 kong2, Li2 e5 sou2-choe3 kau3 hiah thang kiaN!  In-ui7 Li2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5, Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 beh hang5-hok8 Li2.
4)	Choan5-toe7 beh keng3-pai3 Li2,  Gim5-si o-lo2 Li2;  Beh gim5-si o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5. [Se3-lah8
5)	Lin2 tioh8 lai5, lai5 khoaN3 Siong7-te3 sou2-kiaN5 e5 su7,  I tui3 se3-kan-lang5 sou2-choe3--e5, put-chi2 thang kiaN.
6)	I chiong hai2 pian3-choe3 ta-toe7;  In pou7-kiaN5 ke3-ho5;  Ti7-hia goan2 in-ui7 I lai5 hoaN-hi2.
7)	I eng7 I e5 koan5 ti7-li2, tit8 kau3 eng2-oan2;  I e5 bak8-chiu kam3-chhat liat8-pang;  Poe7-gek8 e5 lang5 m7 thang chu7-ko. [Se3-lah8
8)	Ban7 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3;  Hou7 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 o-lo2 I e5 siaN.
9)	I hou7 goan2 e5 siN3-mia7 oah8-teh;  Iah8 bo5 hou7 goan2 e5 kha io5-tang7.
10)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 bat chhi3-giam7 goan2;  Thoan3-lian7 goan2 chhin-chhiuN7 thoan3-lian7 gun5 chit8-iuN7.
11)	Li2 hou7 goan2 jip8 lo5-bang7;  Eng7 tang7-taN3 he7 ti7 goan2 e5 sin-chiuN7.
12)	Li2 hou7 lang5 che7-chhia, poaN5-ke3 goan2 e5 thau5-khak;  Goan2 keng-ke3 chui2-he2.  Chong2-si7 Li2 hou7 goan2 kau3 pu3-u7 e5 sou2-chai7.
13)	Goa2 beh eng7 sio-che3 chin3-jip8 Li2 e5 chhu3;  Goa2 beh tui3 Li2 sia7 goa2 e5 goan7,
14)	Chiu7-si7 ti7 goa2 hoan7-lan7 e5 si5, goa2 e5 chhui3-tun5 sou2 kong2--e5,  Goa2 e5 chhui3 sou2 he7 e5 goan7.
15)	Goa2 beh eng7 pui5 e5 cheng-siN e5 sio-che3,  Kap kang-iuN5 e5 phang-bi7, hian3 hou7 Li2;  Koh eng7 kang e5 gu5, kang e5 soaN-iuN5, lai5 hian3. [Se3-lah8
16)	Hoan7-na7 keng3-ui3 Siong7-te3 e5 lang5, lin2 long2 tioh8 lai5 thiaN;  Goa2 beh kong2-khi2 I ui7 goa2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7.
17)	Goa2 bat eng7 goa2 e5 chhui3 kiu5-kio3 I;  Eng7 goa2 e5 chih8 o-lo2 I choe3 koaiN5.
18)	Goa2 na7 sim-lai7 chu3-tiong7 choe7-ok,  Chu2 tek-khak bo5 beh thiaN;
19)	Chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 sit8-chai7 u7 thiaN-kiN3;  I2-keng aN3-loh8 thiaN goa2 ki5-to2 e5 siaN.
20)	Siong7-te3 si7 eng-kai o-lo2--e5,  I be7-bat the-si5 goa2 e5 ki5-to2, iah8 be7-bat hou7 I e5 chu5-ai3 li7-khui goa2.

[67]	Chit phiN si-koa; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; eng7 si-hian5 e5 gak8-khi3.
1)	Goan7 Siong7-te3 lin5-bin2 goan2, su3-hok goan2;  Hou7 I e5 bin7 chio3-kng goan2; [Se3-lah8
2)	Thang hou7 se3-kai3 chai Li2 e5 to7-lou7,  Ban7-kok-tiong chai Li2 e5 kiu3-un.
3)	Siong7-te3 ah, goan7 liat8-pang o-lo2 Li2;  Goan7 liat8-pang long2 o-lo2 Li2.
4)	Goan7 ban7-kok khoai3-lok8, chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN;  In-ui7 Li2 beh chiau3 kong-to7 sim2-phoaN3 liat8-pang;  Ti7-li2 toe7-chiuN7 e5 ban7-kok. [Se3-lah8
5)	Siong7-te3 ah, goan7 liat8-pang o-lo2 Li2;  Goan7 liat8-pang long2 o-lo2 Li2.
6)	Toe7 i2-keng chhut thou2-san2,  Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3, beh su3-hok goan2.
7)	Siong7-te3 beh su3-hok goan2;  Toe7 e5 si3-kek8 long2 beh keng3-ui3 I.

[68]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si-koa; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Goan7 Siong7-te3 khi2--lai5,  hou7 I e5 tui3-tek8 si3-soaN3;  Hou7 oan3-hun7 I e5 lang5, tui3 I e5 bin7-cheng5 to5-chau2.
2)	Li2 ka7 in koaN2-soaN3, chhin-chhiuN7 ian siu7 chhe-soaN3;  PhaiN2-lang5 kiN3-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7 chiu7 siau-biat8;  Chhin-chhiuN7 lah8 kiN3-tioh8 he2 chiu7 iuN5--khi3.
3)	Chong2-si7 gi7-lang5 beh hoaN-hi2, in ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 beh khoai3-lok8;  In iah8 beh hoaN-hoaN hi2-hi2.
4)	Lin2 tioh8 tui3 Siong7-te3 gim5-si, chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 I e5 mia5;  Ui7-tioh8 hit e5 che7-chhia keng-ke3 khong3-ia2--e5, siu-cho7 toa7-lou7;  I e5 mia5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Tioh8 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 khoai3-lok8.
5)	Siong7-te3 ti7 I seng3 e5 sou2-chai7, choe3 kou-ji5 e5 pe7;  choe3 koaN2-hu7 e5 sin-oan--e5.
6)	Siong7-te3 hou7 kou-toaN e5 lang5 u7 ke;  Hou7 siu7 koaiN-kaN e5 lang5 chhut-lai5 hiong2-hok;  Tok8-tok8 poe7-gek8 e5 lang5 tiam3 ti7 ta-so3 e5 toe7.
7)	Siong7-te3 ah, cha2 Li2 kiaN5 ti7 peh-siN3 e5 thau5-cheng5,  Keng-ke3 khong3-ia2; [Se3-lah8
8)	Hit-si5 toe7 kiN3-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7 chiu7 tin2-tang7,  ThiN iah8 loh8 hou7;  Hit e5 Se-nai2 ia7 tin2-tang7, si7 kiN3-tioh8 Siong7-te3, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7.
9)	Siong7-te3--ah, Li2 loh8 toa7 hou7,  Li2 e5 san2-giap8 I2-sek-liat8 ia3-sian7 e5 si5, Li2 hou7 i kian-kou3.
10)	Li2 e5 hoe7-chiong3 tiam3 ti7 hit tiong-kan;  Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 ui7-tioh8 song3-hiong lang5 pi7-pan7 un-hui7.
11)	Chu2 chhut beng7-leng7;  Thoan5 ho2 siau-sit e5 hu7-lu2 chiaN5 toa7-tin7.
12)	Koan2-peng e5 ong5 to5-chau2 lah, to5-chau2 lah,  Tiam3 ti7 ke-lai7 e5 hu7-lu2 pun-tioh8 sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8.
13)	Lin2 to2 ti7 iuN5-tiau5-lai7 e5 si5,  Chhin-chhiuN7 kap e5 sit8 siuN peh8-gun5;  I e5 mng5 siuN ng5-kim.
14)	Choan5-leng5--e5 ti7 hit lai7-bin7 koaN2-soaN3 liat8-ong5 e5 si5,  Se3-bin7 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Sat-bun5-soaN loh8-seh.
15)	Pa-san soaN si7 Siong7-te3 e5 soaN;  Pa-san soaN si7 choe7-choe7 soaN-chiam e5 soaN.
16)	Lin2 choe7-choe7 soaN-chiam e5 soaN ah,  Lin2 siaN2-su7 gin5 Siong7-te3 sou2 ai3 khia7-khi2 e5 soaN?  Ia5-ho5-hoa beh tiam3 ti7-hia kau3 eng2-oan2.
17)	Siong7-te3 e5 chhia chheng-chheng ban7-ban7;  Chu2 ti7 hit tiong-kan, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Se-nai2, ti7 seng3 e5 sou2-chai7.
18)	Li2 i2-keng chiuN7 kau3 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7, liah8 hiah e5 siu7-liah8--e5;  Li2 ti7 lang5 e5 tiong-kan siu7 in sou2 hian3--e5, lian5 poe7-gek8 e5 lang5 iah8 hian3;  Hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 thang khia7-khi2 in tiong-kan.
19)	Chu2 si7 eng-kai o-lo2--e5, I jit8-jit8 pe7 goan2 e5 taN3;  Chiu7-si7 kiu3 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3. [Se3-lah8
20)	Siong7-te3 si7 ka7 goan2 kiaN5 tak8-iuN7 chin2-kiu3 e5 Siong7-te3;  Oe7 thoat-li7 si2-bo5, si7 chai7-ti7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
21)	Chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 beh phah-phoa3 I e5 tui3-tek8 e5 thau5-khak;  Chiu7-si7 hit e5 siong5-siong5 hoan7-choe7 e5 lang5 e5 thau5-khak.
22)	Chu2 kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 in tui3 Pa-san to3-tng2--lai5,  Tui3 chhim-ian hou7 in to3-tng2-lai5;
23)	Hou7 li2 phah-chhui3 in, li2 e5 kha tah8 ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 huih;  Li2 e5 kau2 e5 chih8 chi7--in.
24)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 e5 ong5;  Lang5 i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 teh kiaN5, kiaN5 jip8 seng3 e5 sou2-chai7.
25)	ChhiuN3-koa--e5 kiaN5 ti7 thau5-cheng5, chok-gak8--e5 te3 ti7 au7-bin7,  Io5 lin-long-kou2 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 ti7 tiong-kan.
26)	Tui3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 goan5-thau5 lai5--e5,  Ti7 tak8 e5 hoe7-tiong, tioh8 o-lo2 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 Chu2.
27)	Ti7-hia u7 koan2-hat in e5 sio2 Pian7-nga2-bin2,  U7 Iu5-tai7 e5 chok8-tiuN2 kap in kui-kun5 e5 cheng3-lang5;  U7 Se-pou3-lun5 e5 chok8-tiuN2, u7 Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5 chok8-tiuN2.
28)	Li2 e5 Siong7-te3 tiaN7-tioh8 li2 e5 khui3-lat8;  Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kian-kou3 Li2 ka7 goan2 sou2 chiaN5 e5 su7.
29)	Ui7-tioh8 Li2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 tian7,  Liat8-ong5 beh toa3 le2-mih8 hian3 hou7 Li2.
30)	Kiu5 Li2 chek-pi7 lou5-ui2-tiong e5 ia2-siu3,  Kap kui-kun5 e5 gu5-kang2, i2-kip8 liat8-pang-tiong e5 gu5-a2,  Chiong gun5 tah8 ti7 kha-e7;  Siong7-te3 koaN2-soaN3 ai3 kau-chian3 e5 peh-siN3.
31)	Toa7-koaN beh tui3 Ai-kip8 lai5;  Kou2-sit8 beh koaN2-kin2 ng3 Siong7-te3 lai5 kiah8-khi2 chhiu2.
32)	Se3-chiuN7 e5 liat8-kok ah, lin2 tioh8 tui3 Siong7-te3 chhiuN3-koa,  Goan7 lin2 gim5-si o-lo2 Chu2. [Se3-lah8
33)	Chiu7-si7 o-lo2 hit e5 che7 ti7 tui3 kou2-cha2 chiu7 u7, kek8-koaiN5 e5 thiN e5 Chu2.  I hoat-chhut I e5 siaN, chiu7-si7 kek8-toa7 e5 siaN.
34)	Lin2 tioh8 chiong koan5-leng5 kui hou7 Siong7-te3;  I e5 ui-giam5 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 teng2-bin7,  I e5 koan5-leng5 si7 ti7 kiong-chhong.
35)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 tui3 Li2 seng3 e5 sou2-chai7 chin-chiaN3 thang kiaN;  I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 si7 hit e5 chiong khui3-lat8 koan5-leng5 siuN2-su3 I e5 peh-siN3 e5,  Siong7-te3 si7 eng-kai o-lo2 e5.

[69]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7 si7 eng7 "Pek-hap8-hoe".
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2,  In-ui7 chiah e5 chui2 beh im goa2 e5 siN3-mia7.
2)	Goa2 ham7-loh8 ti7 chhim e5 thou5-be5-lai7, bo5 thang khia7-kha e5 sou2-chai7;  Goa2 kau3 chhim e5 chui2-lai7, toa7-chui2 im-bat8 goa2.
3)	Goa2 in-ui7 goa2 e5 au5-kio3 kau3 ia3-sian7, goa2 e5 na5-au5 ta--khi3;  Goa2 in-ui7 theng3-hau7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, bak8-chiu hoe.
4)	Bo5 in-toaN oan3-hun7 goa2-e5 khah choe7 goa2 e5 thau5-mng5;  Lam7-sam2 choe3 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8, beh biat8-bo5 goa2-e5, put-chi2 kiong5-beng2;  Goa2 sou2 bo5 chhiuN2 e5, goa2 ia7 tioh8 heng5.
5)	Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 e5 gu5-gong7 Li2 pun2 chai;  Goa2 e5 choe7-koa3 bo5 un2-moa5 ti7 Li2.
6)	Ban7-kun e5 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang hou7 hiah e5 theng3-hau7 Li2 e5 lang5 ui7-tioh8 goa2 lai5 kian3-siau3;  I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang hou7 hiah e5 chhe7 Li2 e5 lang5 ui7-tioh8 goa2 lai5 siu7 leng5-jiok8.
7)	In-ui7 goa2 ui7-tioh8 Li2 e5 ian5-kou3 siu7 loe2-me7,  Goa2 moa2-bin7 kian3-siau3.
8)	Goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7 khoaN3 goa2 choe3 ke3-lou7 e5 lang5,  Goa2 e5 tang5-pau khoaN3 goa2 choe3 goa7-pang-lang5.
9)	In-ui7 goa2 ui7-tioh8 Li2 e5 chhu3 sim-lai7 chhin-chhiuN7 he2 toh8;  Koh loe2-me7 Li2 e5 lang5 e5 loe2-me7 long2 kau3 ti7 goa2.
10)	Goa2 lau5 bak8-sai2, eng7 kim3-chiah8 khek-khou2 goa2 e5 sim;  Che hoan2-tng2 choe3 goa2 e5 leng5-jiok8.
11)	Goa2 eng7 moa5-pou3 choe3 i-chiuN5,  Lang5 chiu7 eng7 goa2 choe3 chhiau3-tam5.
12)	Che7 ti7 siaN5-mng5--e5 tam5-lun7 goa2;  Chiu2-han3 eng7 goa2 choe3 koa-khek.
13)	Chong2-si7 goa2 ti7 tit-tioh8 chiap-lap8 e5 si5, tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa Li2 ki5-to2;  Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 chu5-ai3 e5 hong-seng7,  Chiau3 Li2 chin2-kiu3 e5 chin-sit8 lai5 in3 goa2.
14)	Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 chhut thou5-be5, hou7 goa2 bo5 tim5--loh8-khi3;  Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 oan3-hun7 goa2 e5 lang5, hou7 goa2 chhut chhim e5 chui2.
15)	Kiu5 Li2 boh8-tit iong5-un2 toa7-chui2 im-bat8 goa2;  Boh8-tit iong5-un2 chhim-ian thun goa2;  Boh8-tit iong5-un2 ham7-khiN ham7 goa2.
16)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 in3 goa2, in-ui7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 si7 ho2;  Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 chu5-pi e5 hong-seng7 oat8--ke3-lai5 khoaN3 goa2.
17)	M7-thang ng-bin7 m7-khoaN3 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8;  In-ui7 goa2 ti7 hoan7-lan7 e5 tiong-kan, kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 lai5 in3 goa2.
18)	Kiu5 Li2 chhin-kun7 goa2 e5 leng5-hun5 lai5 kiu3-siok8 i;  Kiu5 Li2 in-ui7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 lai5 siok8-hoe5 goa2.
19)	Li2 chai goa2 sou2 siu7 e5 loe2-me7, kian3-siau3, leng5-jiok8;  Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 long2 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
20)	Loe2-me7 i2-kneg thiah-lih8 goa2 e5 sim, goa2 e5 iu-bun7 moa2-moa2;  Goa2 ng3-bang7 lang5 kho2-lin5, ia7 bo5 chit8-e5,  Ng3-bang7 lang5 an-ui3, ia7 chhe7 bo5 chit8-e5.
21)	In theh8 khou2-taN2 hou7 goa2 choe3 chiah8-mih8,  Goa2 chhui3-ta, in eng7 chhou3 hou7 goa2 lim.
22)	Goan7 in e5 ian5-toh ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 piN3-choe3 lo5-bang7,  Ti7 in peng5-an e5 si5, piN3-choe3 oah8-tauh.
23)	Goan7 in e5 bak8-chiu ou-am3 boe7 khoaN3-kiN3,  Goan7 Li2 hou7 in e5 io siong5-siong5 gi7-gi7-chhoah.
24)	Goan7 Li2 e5 thong3-hun7 piaN3 ti7 in e5 sin-chiuN7;  Hou7 Li2 liat8-liat8 e5 siu7-khi3 jip--tioh8 in.
25)	Goan7 in khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 piN3-choe3 pha-hng;  Goan7 in e5 pou3-piN5 bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.
26)	In-ui7 Li2 sou2 phah hit e5 lang5, in chiu7 khun2-pek i;  Li2 sou2 phah-siong hiah e5 lang5, in poaN-tiah8 in e5 iu-khou2.
27)	Goan7 Li2 ti7 in e5 choe7-siong7 ka choe7;  Boh8-tit iong5-un2 in u7 hun7 Li2 e5 gi7.
28)	Goan7 in tui3 oah8-mia7 e5 chheh siu7 chhat-biat8,  Bo5 ki3 ti7 gi7-lang5 e5 tiong-kan.
29)	Chong2-si7 goa2 si7 khun3-khou2 iu-siong e5 lang5;  Siong7-te3 ah, goan7 Li2 e5 kiu3-un an-ti3 goa2 ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7.
30)	Goa2 beh eng7 si-koa o-lo2 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5;  Ia7 beh eng7 kam2-sia7 chheng I choe3 toa7.
31)	Che si7 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoaN-hi2, iaN5-ke3 hian3 gu5,  A2-si7 hian3 u7-kak u7-toe5 e5 gu5-kang2.
32)	Khiam-pi e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 chiu7 hoaN-hi2;  Lin2 chhe7 Siong7-te3 e5 lang5, goan7 lin2 e5 sim oah8--khi2-lai5.
33)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN song3-hiong e5 lang5,  Bo5 khoaN3-khin ui7-tioh8 I siu7 koaiN-kaN e5 lang5.
34)	Goan7 thiN kap toe7 o-lo2 I;  Hai2 kap ki5-tiong it-chhe3 e5 tong7-but8 ia7 tioh8 o-lo2 I.
35)	In-ui7 Siong7-te3 beh kiu3 Sek-an, khi2-cho7 Iu5-tai7 e5 siaN5;  In beh khia7-khi2 ti7-hia, tit-tioh8 i choe3-giap8.
36)	I e5 lou5-pok8 e5 hou7-e3 beh soa3-chiap i,  ThiaN3 I e5 mia5 e5 lang5 beh tiam3 ti7 hit tiong-kan.

[70]	Tai7-pit8 e5 ki3-liam7 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 chin2-kiu3 goa2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 pang-chan7 goa2.
2)	Goan7 hiah e5 siau3-siuN7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5, kian3-siau3 lau3-khui3;  Goan7 hiah e5 hoaN-hi2 goa2 siu7 ham7-hai7--e5, oat8-to3-tng2 siu7 leng5-jiok8.
3)	Goan7 hiah-e5 kong2, Houh--chai7, Houh--chai7 e5,  In-ui7 kian3-siau3 lai5 oat8-to3-tng2.
4)	Goan7 it-chhe3 chhe7 Li2 e5 in-ui7 Li2 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8;  Goan7 hiah e5 him-bou7 Li2 kiu3-un7-e5 siong5-siong5 kong2,  Tioh8 chun Siong7-te3 choe3 toa7.
5)	Chong2-si7 goa2 si7 khun3-khou2 song3-hiong-e5,  Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 kau3 goa2 chia;  Li2 si7 pang-chan7 goa2 e5, chin2-kiu3 goa2 e5,  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang ian5-chhian5.

[71]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2,  Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 eng2-eng2 bo5 kian3-siau3.
2)	Chiau3 Li2 e5 kong-gi7 chin2-kiu3 goa2, hou7 goa2 thoat-li7;  AN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2, lai5 kiu3 goa2.
3)	Kiu5 Li2 choe3 goa2 thang khia7-khi2 e5 chioh8-poaN5, hou7 goa2 siong5-siong5 khi3 tiam3 hia;  Li2 i2-keng beng7-leng7 beh kiu3 goa2.  In-ui7 Li2 si7 goa2 e5 soaN-giam5, goa2 e5 soaN-che7.
4)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhiu2,  Thoat-li7 put-gi7 kap chan5-jim2 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2-thau5.
5)	In-ui7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, Li2 si7 goa2 sou2 ng3-bang7-e5;  Tui3 goa2 siau3-lian5 e5 si5 Li2 si7 goa2 sou2 oa2-kho3-e5.
6)	Goa2 tui3 thai--nih hou7 Li2 hu5-chhi5,  Hou7 goa2 chhut lau7-bu2 e5 pak-tou2 e5, si7 Li2;  Goa2 beh siong5-siong5 o-lo2 Li2.
7)	Choe7-choe7 lang5 liah8 goa2 choe3 ki5-koai3;  Chong2-si7 Li2 si7 goa2 kian-kou3 to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7.
8)	Goa2 moa2-chhui3 beh o-lo2 Li2,  Thong-jit8 beh eng5-kng Li2.
9)	Goa2 ni5-lau7 e5 si5, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang pang3-sak goa2;  Goa2 khui3-lat8 soe-lam2 e5 si5, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang li7-khui goa2.
10)	In-ui7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 gi7-lun7 goa2;  Hiah-e5 tng-tan2 beh hai7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7--e5 saN-kap chham-siong5,
11)	Kong2, Siong7-te3 i2-keng pang3-sak i;  TaN tioh8 tui-koaN2 i, liah8 i; in-ui7 bo5 kiu3 i e5.
12)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang li7-khui goa2 hng7-hng7;  Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 lai5 pang-chan7 goa2.
13)	Goan7 hiah-e5 choe3 goa2 siN3-mia7 e5 tui3-tek8 e5, siu7 kian3-siau3 biat8-bo5;  Goan7 hiah e5 ke3-bou5 hai7 goa2 e5, siu7 leng5-jiok8 lau3-khui3.
14)	Chong2-si7 goa2 beh siong5-siong5 ng3-bang7,  Goa2 beh na2-ku2 na2 o-lo2 Li2,
15)	Li2 e5 kong-gi7, i2-kip8 Li2 e5 chin2-kiu3 sng3-boe7-liau2,  Goa2 e5 chhui3 thong-jit8 beh kong2-khi2.
16)	Goa2 beh lai5 kong2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 su7;  Goa2 toaN-toaN beh kong2-khi2 Li2 e5 gi7.
17)	Siong7-te3 ah, tui3 goa2 siau3-lian5 e5 si5 Li2 u7 ka3-si7 goa2;  Kau3 hian7-kim goa2 bat po3-iong5 Li2 ki5-biau7 e5 sou2-choe3.
18)	Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 kau3 ni5-lau7; thau5-mng5-peh8 e5 si5, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang pang3-sak goa2;  Theng3-hau7 goa2 chiong Li2 e5 khui3-lat8 chi2-si7 e7-tai7,  Chiong Li2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5 chi2-si7 it-chhe3 chiong-lai5 e5 lang5.
19)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 e5 gi7 chin koaiN5;  Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 bat kiaN5 toa7 e5 su7;  Chi7-chui7 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 Li2?
20)	Li2 si7 hou7 goan2 lek8-ke3 choe7-choe7 toa7 hoan7-lan7 e5;  Li2 beh hou7 goan2 koh-chai3 oah8;  Ia7 beh kiu3 goan2 tui3 toe7 e5 chhim-ian khi2-lai5.
21)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 na2 koaiN5-toa7,  Koh to3-tng2 an-ui3 goa2.
22)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 beh toaN5-sek o-lo2 Li2,  O-lo2 Li2 e5 chin-sit8;  I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3-e5 ah,  Goa2 beh toaN5-khim5 o-lo2 Li2.
23)	Goa2 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2 e5 si5,  Goa2 e5 chhui3-tun5, i2-kip8 Li2 sou2 kiu3-siok8 goa2 e5 leng5-hun5, beh hoaN-hi2 chhut-siaN.
24)	Koh goa2 e5 chih8 kui-jit8 beh kang2-lun7 Li2 e5 gi7,  In-ui7 hiah e5 ke3-bou5 hai7 goa2 e5 lang5 i2-keng kian3-siau3 siu7 leng5-jiok8.

[72]	Sou2-lo5-bun5 e5 si.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 chiong Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 siuN2-su3 ong5,  Chiong Li2 e5 kong-gi7 siuN2-su3 ong5 e5 kiaN2.
2)	I beh chiau3 kong-gi7 sim2-phoaN3 Li2 e5 peh-siN3,  Chiau3 kong-peng5 phoaN3-toan3 Li2 hiah e5 khun3-khou2 e5 lang5.
3)	Toa7-soaN beh in-ui7 kong-gi7, hou7 peh-siN3 peng5-an,  SoaN-a2 ia7 beh an2-ni.
4)	I beh ka7 peh-siN3-tiong khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 phoaN3-toan3,  I beh kiu3 song3-hiong e5 lang5,  I beh teh-chhui3 po7-giok8 e5 lang5.
5)	Lang5 beh keng3-ui3 Li2 jit8-ku2 geh8-tng5,  Tit8-kau3 ban7 se3-tai7.
6)	I beh kang3-lim5 chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 loh8 ti7 i2-keng koah e5 chhau2,  Chhin-chhiuN7 kip8-si5 e5 hou7 lun7-tek8 thou2-toe7.
7)	Ti7 i e5 jit8-chi2 gi7-lang5 beh heng-ong7;  Toa7-toa7 peng5-an kap geh8 piN5 ku2.
8)	I beh chiang2-koan5 tui3 chit e5 hai2 kau3 hit e5 hai2,  Tui3 Toa7-ho5 kau3 toe7-kek8.
9)	Khia7-khi2 ti7 khong3-ia2-e5 beh kui7-pai3 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5;  I e5 tui3-tek8 beh chi7 thou5-hun2.
10)	Tha-si kap hai2-su7 e5 liat8-ong5 beh chin3-kong3;  Si7-pa kap Se-pa e5 ong5 beh hian3 le2-mih8.
11)	Liat8-ong5 long2 beh phak-loh8 pai3 i,  Ban7-kok long2 beh hok8-sai7 i.
12)	In-ui7 song3-hiong lang5 kiu5-kio3 e5 si5, i beh kiu3 i;  Khun3-khou2 bo5 i-oa2 e5 lang5 i ia7 beh kiu3.
13)	I beh lin5-bin2 chheng-tam7 song3-hiong e5 lang5,  I beh chin2-kiu3 song3-hiong lang5 e5 siN3-mia7.
14)	I beh kiu3-siok8 in e5 siN3-mia7 thoat-li7 ap-pek kap po7-giok8;  I beh khoaN3 in e5 huih choe3 po2-poe3.
15)	I beh oah8--teh; beh chiong Si7-pa e5 kim hou7 i,  Beh siong5-siong5 ui7 i ki5-to2,  Thong-jit8 o-lo2 i.
16)	Ti7 toe7--nih, ti7 soaN-teng2, gou7-kak tek-khak bou7-seng7,  Sou2 kiat e5 gou7-kak beh io5-tang7, chhin-chhiuN7 Li7-pa-lun3 e5 chhiu7;  SiaN5-lai7 e5 lang5 beh heng-ong7, chhin-chhiuN7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 chhau2.
17)	I e5 mia5 beh lau5 kau3 eng2-oan2;  I e5 mia5 beh liu5-thoan5 chhin-chhiuN7 jit8 e5 ku2;  Lang5 beh in-ui7 i lai5 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3;  Ban7-kok beh chheng-hou i u7 hok-khi3.
18)	Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3,  Chi2-u7 I kiaN5 ki5-iN7 e5 su7, eng-kai o-lo2 I.
19)	Goan7 I eng5-kng e5 mia5 eng2-oan2 siu7 o-lo2;  Goan7 I e5 eng5-kng chhiong-moa2 choan5-toe7.  A-beng7, koh A-beng7.
20)	Ia5-se e5 kiaN2 Tai7-pit8 e5 ki5-to2 beng5-pek8.

	Koan3 III
[73]	A-sat e5 si.
1)	Siong7-te3 sit8-chai7 ho2 khoan2-thai7 I2-sek-liat8,  Ho2 khoan2-thai7 hiah e5 sim chheng-khi3 e5 lang5.
2)	Chong2-si7 lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 e5 kha hiam2-hiam2 tah8-thut8,  Goa2 e5 kha hiam2-hiam2 chhu7--loh8-khi3.
3)	In-ui7 goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 phaiN2-lang5 kap kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 heng-ong7,  Hit-si5 goa2 chiu7 put-peng5.
4)	In-ui7 in si2 e5 si5 bo5 thang3-thiaN3,  In e5 khui3-lat8 ia7 iong2-kiaN7.
5)	In bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 pat8-lang5 lo5-khou2,  Ia7 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 pat8-lang5 siu7 chai-e7.
6)	Sou2-i2 eng7 kiau-ngou7 choe3 lian7-a2 koa3 ti7 in e5 am7-kun2,  Eng7 po7-giok8 choe3 i-chiuN5 jia in e5 seng-khu.
7)	In in-ui7 sin-the2 pui5, bak8-chiu chiu7 phong3-chhut;  In sou2 tit-tioh8-e5, iaN5-ke3 sim sou2 ai3--e5.
8)	In ki-chhi3 leng5, chiau3 phaiN2 i3-su3 kong2 che3-ap lang5 e5 oe7;  In kong2 toa7-oe7.
9)	In e5 chhui3 siat-tok8 thiN,  In e5 chih8 hou-hat choan5-toe7.
10)	Sou2-i2 i e5 peh-siN3 kui-oa2 ti7-chia,  Moa2-poe e5 chui2 in lim kau3 liau2.
11)	In kong2, Siong7-te3 thai2-tho2 oe7 chai?  Chi3-koaiN5--e5 kiam2 oe7 hiau2-tit mah?
12)	KhoaN3, chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 phaiN2-lang5;  In siong5-siong5 an-iat8, chai5-po2 na2 ke-thiN.
13)	Goa2 chheng-khi3 goa2 e5 sim sit8-chai7 khang-khang;  Goa2 bo5 choe7 lai5 soe2 chhiu2 ia7 si7 khang-khang.
14)	In-ui7 goa2 thong-jit8 tu2-tioh8 chai-e7,  Tak8 cha2-khi2 siu7 chek-pi7.
15)	Goa2 na7 kong2, Goa2 beh an2-ni kong2,  Che si7 eng7 kan-cha3 khoan2-thai7 Li2 e5 kiaN2-lui7.
16)	Goa2 teh siuN7 ai3 beng5-pek8 chit e5 li2,  KhoaN3-liau2 sit8-chai7 ui5-lan5;
17)	Kau3 goa2 jip8 Siong7-te3 seng3 e5 sou2-chai7,  Siong5-se3 siuN7 in e5 kiat-kiok8.
18)	Li2 sit8-chai7 chiong in he7 ti7 kut8-kut8 e5 toe7,  Hou7 in poah8 ti7 tim5-lun5 e5 tiong-kan.
19)	In bak8-nih-ku2 chiaN5-choe3 hiah-nih chhiN-chhin3;  In hou7 kiaN-hiaN5 biat8 kau3 liau2.
20)	Lang5 khun3 cheng-sin5 chaiN2-iuN7 khoaN3 i e5 bang7,  Chu2 ah, Li2 cheng-sin5 ia7 beh an2-ni khoaN3-khin in e5 iaN2-siong7.
21)	In-ui7 goa2 e5 sim chin sng,  Goa2 e5 chong7-hu2 chhi3-chhak8.
22)	Goa2 chit-khoan2 e5 gu5-gong7, bu5-ti;  Ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chhin-chhiuN7 cheng-siN chit8-poaN.
23)	Chong2-si7 goa2 siong5-siong5 kap Li2 ti7-teh,  Li2 khan goa2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2.
24)	Li2 beh eng7 Li2 e5 ka3-si7 in2-chhoa7 goa2,  Au7-lai5 beh chiap-lap8 goa2 jip8 ti7 eng5-kng.
25)	Li2 i2-goa7 ti7 thiN--nih goa2 u7 chi7-chui7?  Li2 i2-goa7 ti7 toe7--nih goa2 bo5 sou2 him-bou7.
26)	Goa2 e5 jiok8-the2, goa2 e5 sim-tng5, siau-bo5,  Chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 si7 goa2 sim-koaN e5 khui3-lat8, ia7 si7 goa2 e5 ki-giap8 tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.
27)	Li7-khui Li2 hng7-hng7-e5 tek-khak si2-bo5;  Hoan7-na7 pang3-sak Li2 kiaN5 kan-im5-e5, Li2 long2 biat8-bo5 in.
28)	Chong2-si7 goa2 chiu7-kun7 Siong7-te3 si7 choe3 goa2 e5 li7-ek;  Goa2 eng7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 goa2 siam2-pi7 e5 sou2-chai7,  Thang hou7 goa2 kong2-khi2 Li2 it-chhe3 e5 sou2-choe3.

[74]	A-sat ka3-si7 e5 si.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 siaN2-su7 eng2-oan2 pang3-sak goan2?  Li2 siaN2-su7 siu7-khi3 Li2 chhau2-tiuN5 e5 iuN5, chhin-chhiuN7 chhut he2-ian?
2)	Kiu5 Li2 ki3-liam7 Li2 cha2-si5 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 hoe7-chiong3,  Chiu7-si7 Li2 sou2 siok8-hoe5 choe3 Li2 e5 giap8 e5 chi-phai3 e5;  Ia7 tioh8 ki3-liam7 Li2 peng5-si5 sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 Sek-an soaN.
3)	Kiu5 Li2 kiaN5 kau3 hiah e5 ku2-ku2 pha-hng e5 toe7,  KhoaN3 tui3-tek8 ti7 seng3-sou2 it-chhe3 sou2 hui2-hoai7 e5.
4)	Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 ti7 Li2 e5 hoe7-lai7 hoa7-hoa7-hau2;  In khia7 in e5 ki5 choe3 ki3-ho7.
5)	In chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 kiah8-khi2 pou2-thau5,  Lai5 chho3 chhiu7-na5 e5 chhiu7.
6)	Seng3-sou2 e5 lai7-bin7 it-chhe3 tiau-khek-e5,  In hian7-chai7 eng7 pou2-thau5 kap thui5 it-chin7 phah-phaiN2.
7)	In pang3-he2 sio Li2 e5 seng3-sou2,  Phah la5-sam5 Li2 e5 mia5 sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, chiaN5-choe3 piN5-toe7.
8)	In sim-lai7 kong2, Lan2 tioh8 it-chin7 hui2-hoai7 in;  In ti7 pian3-toe7 chiong Siong7-te3 e5 hoe7-tng5 long2 sio-lio--khi3.
9)	Goan2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 goan2 e5 tiau7-thau5,  Bo5 koh u7 sian-ti;  Goan2 tiong-kan ia7 bo5 lang5 chai beh kau3 sim2-mih8 si5.
10)	Siong7-te3 ah, tui3-tek8 ki-chhi3 beh kau3 sim2-mih8 si5?  Kiu5-siu5 siat-tok8 Li2 e5 mia5 beh kau3 eng2-oan2 mah?
11)	Li2 ui7-ho5 kiu Li2 e5 chhiu2, chiu7-si7 Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2?  Kiu5 Li2 tui3 Li2 e5 heng-cheng5 chhun-chhut--lai5, hui2-biat8 in.
12)	Chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 tui3 cha2 i2-lai5 choe3 goa2 e5 ong5,  Ti7 toe7--nih kiaN5 chin2-kiu3.
13)	Li2 bat eng7 Li2 e5 koan5-leng5 chiong hai2 pun-khui;  Phah-phoa3 chui2-tiong toa7 tong7-but8 e5 thau5-khak.
14)	Li2 bat kong3-chhui3 gok8-hi5 e5 thau5-khak,  Chiong i hou7 khong3-ia2 e5 ia2-siu3 choe3 chiah8-mih8.
15)	Li2 bat pun-khui chui2-goan5 kap ho5;  Li2 bat hou7 tng5-lau5 e5 kang-ho5 ta--khi3.
16)	Jit8--si5 siok8 Li2, mi5--si5 ia7 siok8 Li2;  Kng kap jit8-thau5 si7 Li2 sou2 pi7-pan7--e5.
17)	Toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-han7 si7 Li2 sou2 siat-lip8;  He7-thiN kap tang-thiN si7 Li2 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8.
18)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 ki3-tit, tui3-tek8 u7 hui2-pong3,  Gong7 e5 peh-siN3 siat-tok8 Li2 e5 mia5.
19)	Li2 e5 ka-chui e5 siN3-mia7, m7-thang kau hou7 ia2-siu3;  Li2 song3-hiong lang5 e5 oah8-mia7 m7-thang eng2-oan2 boe7 ki3-tit.
20)	Kiu5 Li2 siau3-liam7 sou2 lip8 e5 iok;  In-ui7 toe7-chiuN7 ou-am3 e5 sou2-chai7 moa2-moa2 si7 kiong5-po7 e5 chau5-hiat8
21)	Siu7 ap-che3 e5 lang5, m7-thang hou7 in kian3-siau3 to3--khi3;  Khun3-khou2 song3-hiong e5 lang5 tioh8 hou7 in o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5.
22)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 khi2-lai5 ui7 ka-ki7 hun-sou3;  Tioh8 ki3--tit gong7-lang5 thong-jit8 chaiN2-iuN7 teh hui2-pong3 Li2.
23)	M7-thang boe7-ki3--tit Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 e5 siaN;  Hiah e5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek Li2 e5 lang5, in e5 han2-hoa7 siong5-siong5 chiuN7 kau3 teng2-bin7.

[75]	A-sat e5 si-koa, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, si7 eng7 "Boh8-tit hui2-hoai7--e5".
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, goan2 kam2-sia7 Li2,  Goan2 kam2-sia7 Li2, in-ui7 Li2 e5 mia5 kun7-kun7;  Lang5 po3-iong5 Li2 ki5-biau7 e5 sou2-choe3.
2)	Goa2 kau3 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 jit8-ki5,  Goa2 beh chiau3 cheng3-tit8 sim2-phoaN3.
3)	Toe7 kap toe7-chiuN7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 long2 siau-iuN5;  Goa2 chim-chiok8 khia7-chai7 toe7 e5 thiau7. [Se3-lah8
4)	Goa2 tui3 kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 kong2, Boh8-tit kiau-ngou7;  Tui3 phaiN2-lang5 kong2, Boh8-tit kiah8-khi2 li2 e5 kak;
5)	Boh8-tit koaiN5-koaiN5 kiah8-khi2 li e5 kak;  Boh8-tit ngi7 li2 e5 am7-kun2 lai5 kong2-oe7.
6)	In-ui7 m7-si7 tui3 tang, m7-si7 tui3 sai,  Iah8 m7-si7 tui3 lam5 lai5 tit-tioh8 ku2-khi2;
7)	Chi2-u7 Siong7-te3 si7 phoaN3-toan3--e5,  I hou7 chit-e5 kang3-ke7, hou7 hit-e5 seng-koaiN5.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiu2--nih u7 poe, ki5-tiong e5 chiu2 khi2 pheh8;  Poe-lai7 u7 ke3-thau3 e5 chiu2 moa2-moa2, I piaN3--chhut-lai5;  Toe7-chiuN7 e5 phaiN2-lang5 beh long2 lim chit e5 chiu2 e5 che-tai2, lim kau3 liau2-liau2.
9)	Tok8-tok8 goa2 beh po3-iong5 tit8 kau3 eng2-oan2;  Goa2 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3.
10)	PhaiN2-lang5 it-chhe3 e5 kak, Goa2 beh cham7-tng7;  Gi7-lang5 e5 kak beh tit-tioh8 ku2-khi2.

[76]	A-sat e5 si-koa, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; eng7 si-hian5 e5 gak8-khi3.
1)	Ti7 Iu5-tai7 Siong7-te3 hou7 lang5 sou2 bat;  Ti7 I2-sek-liat8 I e5 mia5 choe3 toa7.
2)	Ti7 Sat-leng2 u7 I e5 tiuN3-pang5,  Ti7 Sek-an u7 I khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7.
3)	I ti7-hia at-chih8 keng e5 chiN3,  Kap tin5-pai5, to-kiam3, i2-kip8 kau-chian3 e5 ke-si. [Se3-lah8
4)	Li2 tui3 chhiuN2-mih8 e5 soaN-che7 lai5, u7 eng5-kng kap ui-giam5.
5)	Sim iong2-kam2 e5 lang5 long2 siu7 chhiuN2-kiap; in e5 khun3 si7 tng5-tng5 khun3;  Eng-hiong5 e5 lang5, bo5 chit8-e5 oe7 chhut-chhiu2.
6)	Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 e5 chek-pi7 chit8-e7 hoat-chhut,  Chhia, be2, long2 khun3 tang7-bin5.
7)	Tok8-tok8 Li2 si7 thang kiaN--e5;  Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 chit8-e7 hoat-chhut, chi7-chui7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 khia7-oe7-tiau5 ah?
8)	Li2 tui3 thiN--nih hou7 lang5 thiaN phoaN3-toan3;  Toe7 chiu7 kiaN-hiaN5 cheng7-cheng7;
9)	Chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 khi2--lai5 sim2-phoaN3,  Beh kiu3 toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 khiam-pi e5 lang5. [Se3-lah8
10)	Lang5 e5 siu7-khi3, tek-khak hou7 Li2 tit-tioh8 o-lo2;  Ki5-u5 e5 siu7-khi3, Li2 beh kim3-chi2.
11)	Lin2 tioh8 tui3 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa he7-goan7 koh sia7-goan7;  Si3-ui5 e5 lang5 tioh8 toa3 le2-mih8 kong3-hian3 ti7 thang keng3-ui3 e5 Chu2.
12)	I beh at-chi2 kui3-chok8 e5 kiau-khi3,  I hou7 se3-chiuN7 e5 liat8-ong5 kiaN-ui3.

[77]	A-sat e5 si, chiau3 Ia5-tou7-tun3 e5 choe3-hoat; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Goa2 beh tui3 Siong7-te3 chhut-siaN kiu5-kio3;  Goa2 tui3 Siong7-te3 chhut-siaN, I beh aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2.
2)	Ti7 goa2 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8 goa2 chhe7 Chu2;  Goa2 ti7 mi5--si5 kiah8-khi2 chhiu2 bo5 theng5,  Goa2 e5 sim m7-kheng2 siu7 an-ui3.
3)	Goa2 siau3-liam7 Siong7-te3, chiu7 peh-pak;  Goa2 cheng7-cheng7 siuN7, sim-sin5 hun7--khi3. [Se3-lah8
4)	Li2 hou7 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu bo5 chit8-si5 khoeh;  Goa2 hoan5-lo2 kau3 long2 boe7 kong2-oe7.
5)	Goa2 tui-liam7 kou2-cha2 e5 jit8,  Chiu7-si7 kek8-cha2 e5 ni5.
6)	Goa2 siuN7-khi2 goa2 mi5-kan e5 si-koa,  Goa2 bong-sim ka-ki7 mng7,  Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 iah8 siong5-se3 seng2-chhat.
7)	Chu2 kiam2 beh eng2-oan2 pang3-sak mah?  Bo5 koh si-un mah?
8)	I e5 chu5-ai3 kiam2 eng2-oan2 kiong5-chin7 mah?  I e5 eng3-un2 kiam2 tai7-tia7 hoe3-bo5 mah?
9)	Siong7-te3 kiam2 boe7-ki3-tit si-un mah?  Kiam2 in-ui7 siu7-khi3 that-bat8 I e5 chu5-pi mah? [Se3-lah8
10)	Goa2 kong2, Che chiu7-si7 goa2 e5 loan2-jiok8;  Chi3-koaiN5--e5 chhun-chhut chiaN3-chhiu2 e5 ni5, goa2 beh siau3-liam7.
11)	Goa2 beh kong2-khi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sou2-kiaN5,  Siau3-liam7 I cha2-si5 e5 sin5-jiah.
12)	Goa2 beh chhun2-tok8 Li2 e5 sou2-kiaN5,  Cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 Li2 e5 sou2-choe3.
13)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 e5 lou7 si7 seng3--e5;  U7 sim2-mih8 sin5-beng5 toa7 chhin-chhiuN7 Siong7-te3?
14)	Li2 si7 kiaN5 ki5-su7 e5 Siong7-te3;  Li2 bat ti7 ban7 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan, hian2-beng5 Li2 e5 koan5-leng5.
15)	Li2 bat eng7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 siok8-hoe5 Li2 e5 peh-siN3,  Chiu7-si7 Nga2-kok kap Iok-sek e5 kiaN2-sun. [Se3-lah8
16)	Siong7-te3 ah, chiah e5 chui2 kiN3-tioh8 Li2,  Chiah e5 chui2 kiN3-tioh8 Li2, long2 kiaN-hiaN5,  Chhim-ian iah8 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.
17)	Bat8-hun5 piaN3-chhut chui2,  Kiong-chhong chhut-siaN,  Li2 e5 chiN3 si3-koe3 sia7.
18)	Ti7 kng2-le5-hong-lai7 u7 Li2 lui5 e5 siaN;  Sih-na3 e5 kng sih kau3 thong se3-kan;  Toe7 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, koh tin2-tang7.
19)	Li2 e5 to7-lou7 ti7 hai2-tiong,  Li2 e5 lou7-keng3 ti7 toa7-chui2-tiong,  Li2 e5 kha-jiah bo5 lang5 oe7 chai.
20)	Cha2 Li2 eng7 Mou5-se A-lun5 e5 chhiu2,  Chhoa7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-kun5.

[78]	A-sat ka3-si7 e5 si.
1)	Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 thiaN goa2 e5 ka3-si7,  AN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 chhui3 e5 oe7.
2)	Goa2 beh khui-chhui3 siat phi3-ju7,  Goa2 beh kong2-chhut kou2-cha2 un2-bat8 e5 oe7,
3)	Chiu7-si7 goan2 sou2 thiaN-kiN3, sou2 chai e5;  Iah8 si7 goan2 e5 chou2-kong thoan5 hou7 goan2--e5.
4)	Goan2 bo5 beh chiong chiah e5 su7 tui3 in e5 kiaN2-sun un2-moa5;  Beh chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5-siaN kap I e5 koan5-leng5, i2-kip8 I sou2 kiaN5 ki5-biau7 e5 su7,  Thoan5 hou7 au7 se3-tai7.
5)	In-ui7 I ti7 Nga2-kok lip8 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7, ti7 I2-sek-liat8 siat lut8-hoat;  Si7 I beng7-leng7 lan2 e5 chou2-kong e5, thang thoan5 hou7 in e5 kiaN2-sun.
6)	Hou7 au7-tai7, chiu7-si7 tit-beh chhut-si3 e5 kiaN2-sun chai;  In iah8 beh khi2-lai5 thoan5 hou7 in e5 kiaN2-sun;
7)	Hou7 in e5 ng3-bang7 chai7-ti7 Siong7-te3,  Bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Choan5-leng5--e5 e5 sou2 choe3,  Si7 beh chun-siu2 I e5 kai3-beng7.
8)	Bian2-tit chhin-chhiuN7 in e5 chou2-kong,  Si7 ngi7-sim poe7-gek8 e5 se3-tai7,  Si7 chun5-sim bo5 si3-chiaN3 e5 se3-tai7,  In ng3 Siong7-te3 e5 sim bo5 kian-kou3.
9)	I2-hoat-lian5 e5 kiaN2-sun kiah8 ke-si kap keng-chiN3,  Lim5-tin7 e5 jit8, oat8-tng2-sin the3-au7.
10)	In bo5 chun-siu2 Siong7-te3 e5 iok,  M7-kheng2 chiau3 I e5 lut8-hoat lai5 kiaN5.
11)	Koh boe7-ki3-tit I sou2-kiaN5-e5,  Kap I sou2 hou7 in khoaN3 ki5-biau7 e5 su7.
12)	I ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7, So2-an e5 chhan5,  Ti7 in chou2-kong e5 bak8-chiu cheng5, kiaN5 ki5-iN7 e5 su7.
13)	I pun-khui hai2, hou7 in ke3--khi3;  Koh hou7 chui2 khia7--khi2-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 thou5-tui.
14)	I jit8--si5 eng7 hun5 chhoa7--in,  Thong-mi5 eng7 he2 e5 kng chhoa7--in.
15)	I ti7 khong3-ia2 hou7 chioh8-poaN5 lih8-khui,  Hou7 in choe7-choe7 chui2 thang lim, chhin-chhiuN7 tui3 chhim-ian chhut.
16)	I hou7 chui2 tui3 chioh8-poaN5 chheng3-chhut,  Hou7 chui2 chhin-chhiuN7 kang-ho5 lau5-loh8.
17)	In iu5-goan5 tauh8-tauh8 tek-choe7 I;  Ti7 ta-so3 e5 toe7 poe7-gek8 Chi3-koaiN5--e5.
18)	In sim-lai7 chhi3 Siong7-te3,  Chiau3 in ka-ki7 sou2-ai3--e5 kiu5 chiah8-mih8.
19)	In lam7-sam2 gi7-lun7 Siong7-te3, kong2, Choan5-leng5 e5 Chu2 ti7 khong3-ia2 kiam2 oe7 pan7-toh mah?
20)	I bat phah chioh8-poaN5 hou7 chui2 chheng3-chhut,  Kang-ho5 moa2--chhut-lai5;  I ia7 oe7 siuN2-su3 bi2-niu5 mah?  I ia7 oe7 ka7 I e5 peh-siN3 pi7-pan7 bah mah?
21)	Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 siu7-khi3,  Chiu7 u7 iam7-he2 sio Nga2-kok e5 ke,  Siu7-khi3 hoat-khi2 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 chok8.
22)	In-ui7 in m7 sin3-hok8 Siong7-te3,  M7 oa2-kho3 I e5 kiu3-un.
23)	Chong2-si7 I chiu7 beng7-leng7 ti7 teng2-bin7 e5 kiong-chhong,  Koh khui thiN e5 mng5;
24)	I kang3-loh8 ma2-na2 chhin-chhiuN7 loh8 hou7, hou7 in chiah8;  Chiong thiN e5 bi2-niu5 siuN2-su3 in.
25)	Lang5 chiah8 toa7-koan5-leng5--e5 e5 chiah8-mih8;  I siuN2-su3 bi2-niu5 hou7 in pa2-chiok.
26)	I hou7 tang-hong khi2 ti7 thiN--nih;  Eng7 I e5 koan5-leng5 chhoa7 lam5-hong lai5.
27)	I kang3-loh8 bah ti7 in tiong-kan, choe7 chhin-chhiuN7 thou5-hun2,  Koh pe-chiau2 choe7 chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-soa.
28)	Loh8 ti7 in e5 iaN5-tiong,  Ti7 in khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 e5 si3-ui5.
29)	In chiu7 chiah8 kau3 pa2-pa2;  I chiau3 in sou2-ai3-e5 hou7 in.
30)	In e5 sou2-ai3, iau2-be7 pa2-ia3,  In e5 chiah8-mih8 iau2 ti7 in e5 chhui3-lai7 e5 si5,
31)	Siong7-te3 chiu7 tui3 in hoat-khi2 siu7-khi3,  Thai5-si2 in tiong-kan e5 ho2-han3 lang5,  TaN2-to2 I2-sek-liat8 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5.
32)	Sui-jian5 an2-ni, in iu5-goan5 koh hoan7-choe7;  Bo5 in-ui7 I ki5-koai3 e5 sou2-choe3 lai5 sin3 I.
33)	Sou2-i2 I hou7 in khang-khang ke3-jit8;  Hou7 in lek8-ni5 kiaN-hiaN5.
34)	I thai5 in e5 si5, in chiah lai5 kiu5 I;  Chiu7 oat8-to3-tng2 chhiat-chhiat kiu5 Siong7-te3.
35)	In iah8 tui-liam7 Siong7-te3 si7 in e5 chioh8-poaN5,  Chi3-koaiN5 e5 Choan5-leng5-e5 si7 siok8-hoe5 in--e5.
36)	Chong2-si7 in eng7 chhui3 thiam2-mi7 I,  Eng7 chih8 tui3 I kong2 peh8-chhat8.
37)	In-ui7 in bo5 kian-sim i3-hiong3 I,  Bo5 chin7-tiong siu2 I e5 iok.
38)	Chong2-si7 I u7 lin5-bin2, sia3-bian2 in e5 choe7-ok, bo5 biat8-bo5 in;  Koh tauh8-tauh8 siau I e5 siu7-khi3,  Bo5 it-chin7 hoat-chhut I e5 siu7-khi3.
39)	I siuN7-tioh8 in put-ko3 si7 hiat-khi3,  Si7 chhe-ke3--khi3 bo5 to3-tng2 e5 hong.
40)	In ti7 khong3-ia2 poe7-gek8 I,  Ti7 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7, hou7 I iu-bun7, kau3 hiah choe7 pai2 ah!
41)	In chai3-saN chhi3 Siong7-te3,  Tu2-tak I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5.
42)	In boe7-ki3-tit I e5 koan5-leng5,  Kap siok8-hoe5 in thoat-li7 tui3-tek8 e5 jit8;
43)	I chaiN2-iuN7 ti7 Ai-kip8 hian2-chhut I e5 sin5-jiah;  Ti7 So2-an chhan5, hian2-chhut ki5-su7;
44)	Chiong in e5 kang-ho5 piN3-choe3 huih,  In e5 kang2 iah8 si7 an2-ni, ti3-kau3 long2 boe7 lim--tit.
45)	I hou7 hou5-sin5 kui-tin7 kau3 in tiong-kan lai5 cham in;  Koh hou7 chhan5-kap-a2 lai5 hai7 in.
46)	Chiong in e5 thou2-san2, kau hou7 thang5-thoa7;  Chiong in lo5-khou2 lai5 tit-tioh8-e5 kau hou7 chhau2-meh.
47)	I loh8-phauh8, hui2-hoai7 in e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7,  Loh8-sng, hui2-hoai7 in e5 sng-chai5-chhiu7.
48)	Koh chiong in e5 cheng-siN kau hou7 phauh8,  Chiong in kui-kun5 e5 cheng-siN kau hou7 sih-na3.
49)	I hoat-chhut I e5 toa7 siu7-khi3,  I2-kip8 siu7-khi3, thong3-hun7, khou2-lan7,  Kui-tin7 kang3 chai-e7 e5 su3-chia2 long2 kau3 ti7 in.
50)	I ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 e5 siu7-khi3 phou-piN5 I e5 lou7;  Hou7 in e5 siN3-mia7 boe7 bian2-tit si2;  Chiong in e5 oah8-mia7 kau hou7 un-ek8.
51)	Ti7 Ai-kip8 phah-si2 it-chhe3 e5 toa7-kiaN2,  Ti7 Ham5 e5 pou3-piN5-tiong phah-si2 in e5 thau5-chiuN7-kiaN2.
52)	Chong2-si7 I chhoa7-chhut ka-ki7 e5 peh-siN3, chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5;  Ti7 khong3-ia2 chhoa7 in chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-kun5.
53)	I chhoa7 in an-un2, hou7 in bo5 kiaN-hiaN5;  Hai2 chiu7 im-si2 in e5 tui3-tek8.
54)	I koh chhoa7 in kau3 seng3-toe7 e5 kau-kai3;  Kau3 I chiaN3-chhiu2 sou2 tit-tioh8 chit e5 soaN.
55)	I ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut liat8-pang-lang5;  Eng7 soh-a2 chiong goa7-pang-lang5 e5 toe7 niu5 hou7 in choe3-giap8;  Hou7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chi-phai3 khia7-khi2 in e5 pou3-piN5.
56)	In iu5-goan5 chhi3 chi3-koaiN5 e5 Siong7-te3, lai5 poe7-gek8 I;  Bo5 siu2 I kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
57)	Sit-sin3 poe7-gek8, bo5 koh-iuN7 in e5 chou2-kong;  Pian3-khoan2 chhin-chhiuN7 keng peng2-lin3-tng2.
58)	In-ui7 in eng7 in soaN-thau5 e5 toaN5, jia2-tioh8 I e5 siu7-khi3;  Eng7 in tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7, hou7 I thong3-hun7.
59)	Siong7-te3 thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 siu7-khi3,  Toa7 iam3-ouN3 I2-sek-liat8.
60)	Sim7-chi3 khi3-sak Si7-lo5 e5 hoe7-bou7,  Chiu7-si7 I ti7 lang5 e5 tiong-kan sou2 tah e5 pou3-piN5.
61)	Koh chiong I e5 khui3-lat8, kau hou7 lang5 chhiuN2--khi3;  Chiong I e5 eng5-kng kau ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2.
62)	Iah8 chiong I e5 peh-siN3 kau hou7 to-kiam3,  Lai5 siu7-khi3 I e5 ke-giap8.
63)	In e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 hou7 he2 sio-biat8,  In e5 chai7-sek-lu2 bo5 tit-tioh8 lang5 e5 ho7-hi2.
64)	Che3-si to2 ti7 to-e7,  Chiu2-koaN2-lang5 iah8 bo5 thi5-khau3.
65)	Hit-si5 Chu2 chhin-chhiuN7 khun3 e5 lang5 cheng-sin5;  Chhin-chhiuN7 iong2-beng2 e5 lang5, lim-chiu2 teh hoah.
66)	I phah-the3 I e5 tui3-tek8;  Hou7 in eng2-eng2 siu7 leng5-jiok8.
67)	Koh I khi3-sak Iok-sek e5 pou3-piN5,  Bo5 keng2-soan2 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 chi-phai3;
68)	Chong2-si7 keng2 Iu5-tai7 e5 chi-phai3,  I sou2 i3-ai3 e5 Sek-an soaN.
69)	Koh khi2-cho7 I e5 Seng3-sou2, koaiN5 chhin-chhiuN7 thiN,  Koh chhin-chhiuN7 I kian3-lip8 eng2-eng2 ti7-teh e5 toe7.
70)	Koh keng2 I e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8,  Chhoa7 i tui3 iuN5-tiau5 lai5.
71)	Hou7 i bo5 koh te3 hiah e5 iuN5-bu2,  Beh hou7 i iuN2-chhi7 I e5 peh-siN3 Nga2-kok, kap I e5 ke-giap8 I2-sek-liat8,
72)	I chiu7 chiau3 i sim-lai7 e5 cheng3-tit8 iuN2-chhi7 in;  Koh eng7 i khiau2-biau7 e5 chhiu2 in2-chhoa7 in.

[79]	A-sat e5 si.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, goa7-pang-lang5 chin3-jip8 Li2 e5 san2-giap8,  Phah la5-sam5 Li2 e5 seng3-tian7,  Hou7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 piN3-chiaN5 thou5-tui.
2)	In chiong Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 e5 sin-si, kau hou7 khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, choe3 chiah8-mih8;  Chiong Li2 seng3 e5 peh-siN3 e5 bah, kau hou7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 ia2-siu3.
3)	Ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiu-ui5, lau5 in e5 huih chhin-chhiuN7 chui2;  Iah8 bo5 lang5 bai5-chong3 i.
4)	Goan2 hou7 goan2 keh-piah kok sou2 leng5-jiok8,  Hou7 goan2 si3-ui5 e5 lang5 leng2-chhio3 ki-chhi3.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 beh joa7-ku2, kau3 eng2-oan2 mah?  Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 beh chhin-chhiuN7 he2 toh8 mah?
6)	Goan7 Li2 chiong Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 piaN3-loh8 ti7 hiah e5 m7-bat Li2 e5 goa7-pang,  I2-kip8 hiah-e5 bo5 kiu5-kio3 Li2 e5 mia5 e5 liat8-kok.
7)	In-ui7 in thun-chiah8 Nga2-kok,  Hou7 i khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 pha-hng.
8)	Kiu5 Li2 m7-thang ki3-tit goan2 e5 chou2-kong e5 choe7, lai5 tui3 goan2 tho2;  Goan7 Li2 e5 chu5-pi kin2-kin2 lim5-kau3 goan2;  In-ui7 goan2 loh8 kau3 kek8 pi-bi5 e5 toe7-ui7.
9)	Kiu3 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 in-ui7 Li2 e5 mia5 e5 eng5-kng pang-chan7 goan2;  In-ui7 Li2 e5 mia5 e5 ian5-kou3 kiu3 goan2, sia3-bian2 goan2 e5 choe7.
10)	SiaN2-su7 ti3-kau3 goa7-pang lang5 kong2, In e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 toh-loh8?  Goan7 Li2 sin Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 lau5-huih e5 oan, hou7 goa7-pang lang5 chai,  Hou7 goan2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3.
11)	Goan7 siu5-hoan7 e5 thou2-khui3 thau3-kau3 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  Goan7 Li2, chiau3 Li2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5, po2-chun5 hiah e5 gi2-tiaN7 tioh8-si2 e5 lang5.
12)	Chu2 ah, goan7 Li2 chiong goan2 keh-piah kok sou2 leng5-jiok8 Li2 e5 leng5-jiok8,  Ke-thiN chhit-pe7, kui ti7 in e5 sin-chiuN7.
13)	An2-ni goan2 choe3 Li2 e5 peh-siN3, Li2 e5 chhau2-tiuN5 e5 iuN5-e5,  Beh kam2-sia7 Li2 kau3 eng2-oan2;  Beh o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5 kau3 ban7 se3-tai7.

[80]	A-sat e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, eng7 "Choe3 kan-cheng3 e5 peh-hap8-hoe".
1)	I2-sek-liat8 e5 bok8-chia2 ah, chhoa7 Iok-sek chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-kun5--e5, kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN;  Che7 ti7 ki-lou7-peng e5 teng2-bin7--e5, kiu5 Li2 hoat-chhut Li2 e5 kng.
2)	Ti7 I2-hoat-lian5, Pian7-nga2-bin2, Ma2-na2-se e5 bin7-cheng5, tian2-chhut Li2 e5 koan5-leng5,  Lai5 kiu3 goan2.
3)	Siong7-te3 ah, hou7 goan2 to3-tng2;  Hou7 Li2 e5 bin7 hoat-chhut kng, goan2 chiu7 tit-tioh8 kiu3.
4)	Ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah,  Li2 ng3 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 ki5-to2 hoat-chhut siu7-khi3, beh joa7-ku2 ah?
5)	Li2 eng7 bak8-sai2 choe3 chiah8-mih8, hou7 in chiah8;  Koh niu5 choe7-choe7 bak8-sai3 hou7 in lim.
6)	Li2 hou7 keh-piah-kok in-ui7 goan2 lai5 saN-chiN,  Goan2 e5 tui3-tek8 saN-kap teh chhio3.
7)	Ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3 ah, hou7 goan2 to3-tng2,  Hou7 Li2 e5 bin7 hoat-chhut kng, goan2 chiu7 tit-tioh8 kiu3.
8)	Li2 tui3 Ai-kip8 soa2 chit8-chang5 phu5-to5-chhiu7,  KoaN2-chhut liat8-pang, lai5 chai--i,
9)	Li2 ti7 i e5 thau5-cheng5 piaN3-khang thou2-toe7;  I e5 kun teng3 chhim, chiu7 siN-thoaN3 moa2-toe7.
10)	I e5 iaN2 jia-bat8 chiah e5 soaN,  I e5 ki chhin-chhiuN7 chin-ho2 e5 peh-hiuN-chhiu7.
11)	Hoat-chhut i e5 ki, chhun kau3 toa7-hai2,  I e5 tin5 thoaN3 kau3 Toa7-ho5.
12)	Li2 siaN2-su7 thiah-hui2 i e5 li5-pa,  Chhut-chai7 it-chhe3 ke3-lou7 e5 lang5 ban2--i?
13)	Chhiu7-na5-lai7 chhut-lai5 e5 soaN-ti chau-that--i,  Khong3-ia2 e5 chau2-siu3 chiah8--i.
14)	Ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 to3-tng2;  Tui3 thiN aN3-loh8 khoaN3, chiau3-kou3 chit chang5 phu5-to5-chhiu7,
15)	Po2-hou7 Li2 chiaN3-chhiu2 sou2 chai--e5,  Kap Li2 ui7 ka-ki7 sou2 kian-kou3 e5 ki.
16)	I i2-keng siu7 he2 sio, siu7 to chho3;  Ui7-tioh8 Li2 e5 bin7 e5 siu7-khi3, in chiu7 biat8-bo5.
17)	Goan7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 hoaN7 ti7 Li2 chiaN3-peng5 e5 lang5,  Chiu7-si7 Li2 ui7 ka-ki7 sou2 kian-kou3 e5 jin5-chu2.
18)	An2-ni, goan2 chiu7 bo5 to3-the3 li7-khui Li2;  Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goan2 tit-tioh8 oah8, goan2 chiu7 beh kiu5-kio3 Li2 e5 mia5.
19)	Ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, hou7 goan2 to3-tng2;  Hou7 Li2 e5 bin7 hoat-chhut kng, goan2 chiu7 tit-tioh8 kiu3.

[81]	A-sat e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; eng7 Ka-tek8 e5 tiau7.
1)	Siong7-te3 si7 goan2 e5 khui3-lat8, lin2 tioh8 toa7-siaN o-lo2 I;  Tioh8 chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, o-lo2 Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3.
2)	Tioh8 chhiuN3 si-koa, io5 lin-long-kou2;  ToaN5 ho2-thiaN e5 khim5 kap sek.
3)	Tioh8 ti7 chhoe-it chap8-gou7,  Goan2 choeh-ki5 e5 jit8, pun5 sau3-kak.
4)	In-ui7 che si7 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 lut8-le7,  Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 e5 le2-gi5.
5)	I khi3 kong-kek Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 si5,  Ti7 Iok-sek e5 tiong-kan, lip8 chit-e5 choe3 kan-cheng3;  Ti7-hia goa2 thiaN-kiN3 sou2 boe7 hiau2-tit e5 oe7.
6)	Siong7-te3 kong2, Goa2 hou7 i e5 keng-thau5 thoat-li7 tang7-taN3,  Hou7 i e5 chhiu2 pang3-loh8 kheng-a2.
7)	Li2 ti7 hoan7-lan7-tiong kiu5-kio3, Goa2 bat kiu3 li2;  Goa2 ti7 lui5 un2-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7 in3 li2;  Goa2 ti7 Bi2-li7-pa e5 chui2-piN chhi3 li2. [Se3-lah8
8)	Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, li2 tioh8 thiaN;  Goa2 beh tui3 li2 choe3 kan-cheng3;  I2-sek-liat8 ah, goan7 li2 thiaN-than3 Goa2.
9)	Ti7 li2 e5 tiong-kan m7-thang u7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3,  Goa7-pang e5 siong7-te3, li2 iah8 m7-thang kui7-pai3.
10)	Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, li2 e5 Siong7-te3,  Bat chhoa7 li2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chiuN7--lai5;  Tioh8 toa7 khui li2 e5 chhui3, Goa2 chiu7 chhiong-moa2--i.
11)	Chong2-si7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 m7-thiaN Goa2 e5 siaN;  I2-sek-liat8 choan5-jian5 m7 chhiu3-chhai2 Goa2.
12)	Goa2 chiu7 chhut-chai7 in, chiau3 in e5 sim e5 kou3-chip;  Hou7 in chiau3 in ka-ki7 e5 ke3-bou5 khi3 kiaN5.
13)	Goan7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 kheng2 thiaN Goa2;  I2-sek-liat8 kheng2 kiaN5 Goa2 e5 lou7.
14)	Goa2 chiu7 kin2-kin2 che3-ap in e5 kiu5-siu5;  Oat8-tng2 Goa2 e5 chhiu2, kong-kek in e5 tui3-tek8.
15)	Oan3-hun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5, beh lai5 tau5-hang5 I,  Chong2-si7 in e5 si5-tai7 beh ku2-tng5 ti7-teh.
16)	I iah8 beh eng7 ho2 e5 beh8 hou7 in chiah8;  Goa2 eng7 tui3 chioh8-poaN5 chhut e5 bit8, hou7 in chiah8 pa2.

[82]	A-sat e5 si.
1)	Siong7-te3 khia7 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 hoe7-tiong,  Ti7 chiah e5 siong7-te3 e5 tiong-kan teh sim2-phoaN3.
2)	Lin2 sim2-phoaN3 bo5 chiau3 kong-gi7,  Sun5 phaiN2-lang5 e5 cheng5-bian7, beh kau3 ti7-si5 ah? [Se3-lah8
3)	Lin2 tioh8 ka7 song3-hiong-lang5 kap bo5-pe7 e5 kiaN2 sin-oan;  Tioh8 ka7 khun3-khou2 kap khiam3-kheh e5 lang5 kiaN5 kong-gi7.
4)	Tioh8 chin2-kiu3 song3-hiong kap khiam3-kheh e5 lang5,  Hou7 in thoat-li7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhiu2.
5)	In m7-chai, iah8 bo5 beng5-li2;  In ti7 ou-am3-tiong kiaN5-lai5 kiaN5-khi3;  Toe7 e5 kun-ki long2 io5-tang7.
6)	Goa2 bat kong2, Lin2 si7 siong7-te3.  Lin2 long2 si7 Chi3-koaiN5--e5 e5 kiaN2;
7)	Chong2-si7 lin2 oe7 si2, kap se3-kan lang5 chit8-iuN7;  Beh to2--loh8-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 kui3-chok8 e5 chit8-e5.
8)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 khi2--lai5, sim2-phoaN3 se3-kai3;  In-ui7 Li2 beh tit-tioh8 ban7-kok choe3 ki-giap8.

[83]	A-sat e5 si-koa.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang cheng7-cheng7;  Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang bo5 khui-chhui3, iah8 m7-thang bo5 choe3-siaN;
2)	In-ui7 Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 hoa7-hoa7-jiong2;  Oan3-hun7 Li2 e5 lang5 kiah8-khi2 thau5.
3)	In eng7 kan-cha3 e5 ke3-bou5 beh hai7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3;  In saN-kap gi7-lun7, beh hai7 Li2 sou2 khng3-bat8 e5 lang5.
4)	In kong2, Lai5 ah, lan2 lai5 biat8-bo5 in, hou7 in boe7 chiaN5 kok,  Hou7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 mia5 bo5 koh hou7 lang5 ki3-liam7.
5)	In tang5-sim saN-kap chham-siong5,  SaN-kap kiat-iok beh ti2-tek8 Li2;
6)	Chiu7-si7 khia7-khi2 pou3-piN5 e5 I2-tong kap I2-sit8-ma2-li7 lang5,  Mou5-ap kap Ha7-Kah lang5,
7)	Ka-pa-lek8, A-bun5, kap A-ma2-lek8;  Hui-li7-su7, i2-kip8 Chhui-lo5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3;
8)	A-sut8 iah8 kap in lian5-hap8,  In choe3 Lo5-tek e5 kiaN2-sun e5 pang-chhiu2. [Se3-lah8
9)	Kiu5 Li2 khoan2-thai7 in, chhin-chhiuN7 cha2 khoan2-thai7 Bi2-tian5;  Chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Ki-sun7 ho5, khoan2-thai7 Se-se-lah kap Ia5-pin chit8-iuN7.
10)	In ti7 Un2-to5-jiN2 biat8-bo5,  ChiaN5-choe3 toe7-chiuN7 e5 pun3-thou5.
