11)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 in e5 leng2-siu3 chhin-chhiuN7 OU-lip8 kap Se-i-pek;  Hou7 in e5 kun-tiuN2 long2 chhin-chhiuN7 Se-pa kap Sat-bun5-na2.
12)	In kong2, Lan2 tioh8 chiong Siong7-te3 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, Chiam3 lai5 choe3 ka-ki7 e5.
13)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 in chhin-chhiuN7 kng2-le5-hong e5 tin5-ai,  Chhin-chhiuN7 hong-cheng5 e5 tiu7-sap;
14)	Chhin-chhiuN7 he2 sio chhiu7-na5,  Chhin-chhiuN7 he2-iam7 sio soaN-thau5.
15)	Kiu5 Li2 iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni eng7 Li2 e5 kong5-hong tui-koaN2 in,  Eng7 Li2 e5 toa7-hong hou7 in kiaN-hiaN5.
16)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 in moa2-bin7 kian3-siau3,  Thang lai5 ki5-kiu5 Li2 e5 mia5.
17)	Hou7 in eng2-oan2 kian3-siau3, kiaN-hiaN5;  Hou7 in lau3-khui3 biat8-bo5.
18)	Hou7 in chai chi2-u7 Li2, mia5 choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5,  Si7 choan5-toe7-chiuN7 chi3-koaiN5 e5.

[84]	Kho2-lah8 e5 hou7-e3 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; eng7 Ka-tek8 e5 gak8-khi3.
1)	Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah,  Li2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, chaiN2-iuN7 hiah thang i3-ai3.
2)	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 loan5-bou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7-iN7 kau3 hun7--khi3;  Goa2 e5 sim-tng5, goa2 e5 jiok8-the2, ng3 oah8 e5 Siong7-te3 kiu5-kio3.
3)	Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, goa2 e5 Ong5, goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah,  Chhek-chiau2-a2 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 chhe7-tioh8 chit8 e5 chhu3,  IN3-a2 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 chhe7-tioh8 pu7-kiaN2 e5 siu7;  Chiu7-si7 ti7 Li2 hiah e5 che3-toaN5 hia.
4)	Khia7-khi2 ti7 Li2 e5 chhu3 e5, hit ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3;  In beh tit8-tit8 o-lo2 Li2. [Se3-lah8
5)	I e5 lat8 chai7-ti7 Li2,  In e5 sim i3-hiong3 Sek-an e5 toa7-lou7--e5, hit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
6)	In keng-ke3 Lau5-bak8-sai2 e5 soaN-kok, hou7 i piN3-choe3 chui2-choaN5 e5 sou2-chai7;  Koh u7 chhiu-thiN e5 hou7 e5 hok-khi3 ka7 i kham3-moa2.
7)	In na2-kiaN5, khui3-lat8 na2 ke-thiN,  Tak8-lang5 kau3 Sek-an tiau5-kiN3 Siong7-te3.
8)	Ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 thiaN goa2 e5 ki5-to2;  Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang lai5 thiaN. [Se3-lah8
9)	Choe3 goan2 e5 tin5-pai5 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 tioh8 khoaN3;  KhoaN3 Li2 siu7 boah-iu5--e5 e5 bin7.
10)	Ti7 Li2 e5 tian7-iN7 toa3 chit8-jit8, khah-ho2 chit8-chheng jit8;  Leng5-khou2 ti7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3 kou3-mng5,  Khah-ho2 tiam3 ti7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 pou3-piN5,
11)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 si7 jit8-thau5, si7 tin5-pai5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa siuN2-su3 un-hui7 kap eng5-kng;  I be7-bat lau5 chit8-hang7 ho2-mih8,  Bo5 hou7 hiah e5 kiaN5 cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5.
12)	Ban7-kun e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah,  Oa2-kho3 Li2 e5 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.

[85]	Kho2-lah8 e5 hou7-e3 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 i2-keng si-un ti7 Li2 e5 toe7,  Nga2-kok siu7-liah8 e5 lang5, Li2 kiu3 i to3-lai5.
2)	Li2 sia3-bian2 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 choe7-ok,  Li2 jia-kham3 in it-chhe3 e5 choe7-koa3. [Se3-lah8
3)	Li2 siu-hoe5 Li2 it-chhe3 e5 siu7-khi3,  Soah Li2 beng2-liat8 e5 siu7-khi3.
4)	Kiu3 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 goan2 to3-tng2,  Soah Li2 ng3 goan2 e5 siu7-khi3.
5)	Li2 beh siu7-khi3 goan2 kau3 eng2-oan2 mah?  Li2 beh chiong Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 lau5 kau3 ban7-tai7 mah?
6)	Li2 kiam2 m7 koh chiong goan2 kiu3 oah8,  Hou7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 in-ui7 Li2 lai5 hoaN-hi2 mah?
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 goan2 khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3;  Koh chiong Li2 e5 kiu3-un siuN2-su3 goan2.
8)	Goa2 goan7 thiaN Choan5-leng5 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beh kong2--e5;  In-ui7 I beh tui3 I e5 peh-siN3, kap I seng3 e5 peh-siN3, kong2 peng5-an;  Chong2-si7 in m7-thang koh khi3 lam7-sam2 kiaN5.
9)	I e5 kiu3-un sit8-chai7 kun7 ti7 kiaN-ui3 I e5 lang5;  Hou7 eng5-kng tiam3 ti7 lan2 e5 keng2-lai7.
10)	Chu5-ai3 kap chin-sit8 saN tu2-tioh8;  Kong-gi7 kap peng5-an saN chim-chhui3.
11)	Chin-sit8 tui3 toe7--nih hoat-siN,  Kong-gi7 tui3 thiN khoaN3--loh8-lai5.
12)	Ia5-ho5-hoa beh siuN2-su3 ho2-mih8,  Lan2 e5 thou2-toe7 beh chhut i e5 thou2-san2.
13)	Kong-gi7 beh kiaN5 ti7 I e5 thau5-cheng5,  Hou7 I e5 kha-jiah chiaN5-choe3 lou7.

[86]	Tai7-pit8 e5 ki5-to2.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2;  In-ui7 goa2 si7 khun3-khou2 song3-hiong e5.
2)	Kiu5 Li2 po2-chun5 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7, in-ui7 goa2 si7 khian5-seng5 e5 lang5.  Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 oa2-kho3 Li2; kiu5 Li2 chin2-kiu3 i.
3)	Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 lin5-bin2 goa2;  In-ui7 goa2 thong-jit8 kiu5-kio3 Li2.
4)	Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 sim hoaN-hi2;  In-ui7 goa2 eng7 goa2 e5 sim giong2-bong7 Li2.
5)	Chu2 ah, in-ui7 Li2 si7 ho2, hoaN-hi2 sia3-bian2 lang5;  U7 hong-seng7 e5 chu5-ai3, siuN2-su3 hoan7-na7 kiu5-kio3 Li2 e5 lang5.
6)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 ki5-to2;  AN3-loh8 thiaN goa2 khun2-kiu5 e5 siaN.
7)	Ti7 goa2 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8, beh kiu5-kio3 Li2;  Li2 beh in3 goa2.
8)	Chu2 ah, chiah e5 siong7-te3 e5 tiong-kan, bo5 chit8-e5 oe7 pi2-tit Li2;  Li2 e5 sou2 choe3 iah8 bo5 thang pi2-pheng7.
9)	Chu2 ah, Li2 sou2 cho7 e5 ban7-pang long2 beh lai5 phak-pai3 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  In iah8 beh eng5-kng Li2 e5 mia5.
10)	In-ui7 Li2 choe3 toa7, koh kiaN5 ki5-biau7 e5 su7;  Chi2-u7 Li2 si7 Siong7-te3.
11)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 chiong Li2 e5 to7-lou7 chi2-si7 goa2; goa2 beh chiau3 Li2 e5 chin-li2 lai5 kiaN5;  Hou7 goa2 choan-it e5 sim keng3-ui3 Li2 e5 mia5.
12)	Chu2, goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 beh choan5-sim o-lo2 Li2;  Goa2 beh eng5-kng Li2 e5 mia5 kau3 eng2-oan2.
13)	In-ui7 Li2 tui3 goa2 hoat-chhut toa7 e5 chu5-ai3,  Li2 kiu3 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 bian2 loh8 kek8-chhim e5 im-kan.
14)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek goa2;  Koh u7 kiong5-po7 e5 tong2 siau3-siuN7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7;  In bo5 keng3-hong7 Li2 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5.
15)	Chu2 ah, Li2 si7 jin5-chu5 un-tian2 e5 Siong7-te3;  Bo5 khoai3-khoai3 siu7-khi3, koh u7 hong-seng7 e5 chu5-ai3 kap seng5-sit8.
16)	Kiu5 Li2 oat8--ke3-lai5 khoaN3 goa2, kho2-lin5 goa2;  Chiong Li2 e5 khui3-lat8 siuN2-su3 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8,  Kiu3 Li2 e5 lu2-pi7 e5 kiaN2.
17)	Kiu5 Li2 hian2-chhut un-tian2 goa2 e5 pin5-ku3,  Hou7 oan3-hun7 goa2 e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 lai5 kian3-siau3;  In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Li2 pang-chan7 goa2, an-ui3 goa2.

[87]	Kho2-lah8 e5 hou7-e3 e5 si-koa.
1)	I e5 toe7-ki chai7-ti7 seng3-soaN.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN3 Sek-an e5 mng5,  IaN5-ke3 Nga2-kok long2-chong2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7.
3)	Siong7-te3 e5 siaN5 ah,  U7 eng5-kng e5 su7, si7 chi2 li2 lai5 kong2--e5. [Se3-lah8
4)	Goa2 beh sng3 Lah8-hap-pek kap Pa-pi2-lun5 ti7 bat Goa2--e5 e5 lai7-bin7;  KhoaN3 ah, Hui-li7-su7, Chhui-lo5, Kou2-sit8,  Chit-e5 chhut-si3 ti7-hia.
5)	Lun7-kau3 Sek-an beh kong2, Chit-e5, hit-e5, chhut-si3 ti7 hit tiong-kan;  Koh Chi3-koaiN5-e5 beh chhin-sin kian-kou3--i.
6)	Tng Ia5-ho5-hoa ki3 ban7 peh-siN3 siau3-giah8 e5 si5,  I beh sng3 chit-e5 chhut-si3 ti7-hia. [Se3-lah8
7)	ChhiuN3-koa-e5, thiau3-bu2-e5, long2 beh kong2,  Goa2 e5 chui2-goan5 long2 chai7-ti7 Li2.

[88]	Kho2-lah8 hou7-e3 e5 si-koa, chiu7-si7 I2-su7-lah8 lang5 Hi-ban7 ka3-si7 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN; tiau7, eng7 Mou5-hap8-lah8 Li7-am3-ngou5.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa, kiu3 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah,  Goa2 jit8-mi5 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 kiu5-kio3.
2)	Goan7 goa2 e5 ki5-to2 kau3 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  Kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 ki5-kiu5.
3)	In-ui7 goa2 e5 sim moa2-moa2 hoan7-lan7,  Goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 kun7 ti7 im-kan.
4)	Goa2 sng3 kap loh8-hiat8 e5 lang5 tang5-liat8;  Ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 tit-tioh8 pang-chan7 e5 lang5.
5)	Goa2 siu7 hiat-kak8 ti7 si2-lang5-tiong,  Chhin-chhiuN7 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 to2 ti7 bong7-lai7;  In si7 Li2 bo5 koh ki3-tit-e5,  Tui3 Li2 e5 chhiu2 keh-tng7.
6)	Li2 he7 goa2 ti7 kek8-chhim e5 hiat8;  Ti7 ou-am3 e5 toe7-hng, ti7 chhim-ian.
7)	Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 tang7-tang7 teh goa2;  Li2 eng7 Li2 it-chhe3 e5 hai2-eng2 khou2-chhou2 khun2-pek goa2. [Se3-lah8
8)	Kap goa2 sio-bat e5 lang5 Li2 hou7 in li7-khui goa2 hng7-hng7,  Hou7 in iam3-ouN3 goa2;  Goa2 siu7 koaiN-kim3, boe7-tit chhut-lai5.
9)	Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu in-ui7 khun3-khou2 phah-phaiN2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 jit8-jit8 kiu5-kio3 Li2,  Goa2 ng3 Li2 kiah8-chhiu2.
10)	Li2 kiam2 beh kiaN5 ki5-su7 hou7 si2-lang5 khoaN3 mah?  Chong2-bo5 im-hun5 iau2 oe7 khi2-lai5 o-lo2 Li2 ah? [Se3-lah8
11)	Kiam2 oe7 ti7 bong7-lai7 kong2-khi2 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 mah?  Kiam2 oe7 ti7 biat8-bo5 e5 tiong-kan kong2-khi2 Li2 e5 sin3-sit8 mah?
12)	Ti7 ou-am3 e5 sou2-chai7, kiam2 oe7 chai Li2 e5 ki5-su7 mah?  Ti7 boe7-ki3-tit tai7-chi3 e5 toe7-hng, kiam2 oe7 chai Li2 e5 kong-gi7 mah?
13)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 u7 ki5-kiu5 Li2;  Ti7 cha2-khi2-si5 goa2 e5 ki5-to2 beh thau3 kau3 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
14)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 siaN2-su7 khi3-sak goa2?  SiaN2-su7 ng Li2 e5 bin7, m7 khoaN3 goa2?
15)	Goa2 tui3 siau3-lian5 siu7-khou2, hiam2-hiam2 si2;  Goa2 siu7-tioh8 Li2 e5 kiaN-hiaN5, ti3-kau3 sim hun-loan7.
16)	Li2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 im-bat8 goa2;  Li2 eng7 kiaN-hiaN5 tu5-biat8 goa2.
17)	Chiah-e5 thong-jit8 chhin-chhiuN7 chui2 ui5 goa2;  Chit8-choe5 lai5 ui5-khun3 goa2.
18)	Li2 chiong goa2 e5 liong5-peng5 bit8-iu2 keh-khui hng7-hng7;  Hou7 goa2 sou2 saN-bat e5 lang5 jip8 ti7 ou-am3 e5 sou2-chai7.

[89]	I2-su-lah8 lang5, I2-tham3, ka3-si7 e5 si.
1)	Goa2 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chu5-ai3 kau3 ti7 eng2-oan2.  Beh eng7 goa2 e5 chhui3 thoan5 Li2 e5 sin3-sit8 kau3 tai7-tai7.
2)	In-ui7 goa2 bat kong2, Chu5-ai3 beh siu7 kian3-lip8 kau3 eng2-oan2;  Li2 beh chiong Li2 e5 sin3-sit8 kian-kou3 ti7 thiN--nih.
3)	Goa2 kap Goa2 sou2 keng2 e5 lang5 lip8-iok,  Tui3 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 chiu3-choa7.
4)	Goa2 beh hou7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 kian-kou3 kau3 eng2-oan2,  Koh hou7 li2 e5 po2-cho7 kian3-lip8 kau3 tai7-tai7. [Se3-lah8
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, chiah e5 thiN beh o-lo2 Li2 e5 ki5-su7;  Ti7 seng3--e5 e5 hoe7-tiong, beh o-lo2 Li2 e5 sin3-sit8.
6)	Ti7 khong-tiong chi7-chui7 oe7 pi2-tit Ia5-ho5-hoa?  Toa7 koan5-leng5--e5 e5 cheng3-kiaN2-tiong, chi7-chui7 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa?
7)	I ti7 seng3--e5 e5 gi7-hoe7 tiong, si7 toa7-toa7 u7 ui-giam5 e5 Siong7-te3;  Pi2 it-chhe3 ti7 I si3-ui5 e5, koh-khah thang kiaN-ui3.
8)	Ban7-kun e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah,  Toh-loh8 chit8-e5 toa7 koan5-leng5--e5, chhin-chhiuN7 Li2 Ia5-ho5-hoa?  Li2 e5 sin3-sit8 ti7 Li2 e5 si3-ui5.
9)	Hai2-chui2 tiong3-koaiN5, Li2 koan2-hat--i;  Hai2-eng2 gia5--khi2-lai5, Li2 hou7 i piN5.
10)	Li2 phah chhui3 Lah8-hap-pek, chhin-chhiuN7 i2-keng thai5-si2 e5 lang5;  Li2 eng7 u7 khui3-lat8 e5 chhiu2 phah-soaN3 Li2 e5 tui3-tek8.
11)	ThiN siok8 Li2, toe7 iah8 siok8 Li2;  Se3-kai3 kap ki5-tiong sou2 chhiong-moa2--e5, long2 si7 Li2 sou2 kian3-lip8.
12)	Lam5-pak si7 Li2 sou2 chhong3-cho7;  Tha-pok8 kap Hek-bun5, in-ui7 Li2 e5 mia5 lai5 hoaN-hi2.
13)	Li2 u7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2,  Li2 e5 chhiu2 u7 lat8, Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 kiah8 koaiN5-koaiN5.
14)	Kong-peng5 kap gi7-li2 si7 Li2 e5 po2-cho7 e5 toe7-ki;  Chu5-ai3 kap seng5-sit8 kiaN5 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
15)	Oe7 bat hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN--e5, hit e5 peh-siN3 u7 hok-khi3;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, in ti7 Li2 e5 bin7 sou2 hoat-chhut e5 kng teh kiaN5.
16)	In jit8-jit8 in-ui7 Li2 e5 mia5 lai5 hoaN-hi2;  In-ui7 Li2 e5 kong-gi7 tit-tioh8 seng-koaiN5.
17)	In-ui7 Li2 si7 in khui3-lat8 e5 eng5-kng;  Koh in-ui7 Li2 hoaN-hi2 goan2, goan2 e5 kak beh tit-tioh8 kiah8-koaiN5.
18)	Goan2 e5 tin5-pai5 siok8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Goan2 e5 ong5 siok8 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Seng3--e5.
19)	Tng-si5 Li2 ti7 iN7-siong7-tiong hoan-hu3 Li2 seng3 e5 peh-siN3, kong2,  Goa2 eng7 pang-chan7 e5 lat8, he7 ti7 hit e5 u7 koan5-leng5--e5 e5 sin-chiuN7;  Tui3 peh-siN3-tiong keng2--e5, Goa2 ko-seng--i.
20)	Goa2 chhe7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8;  Eng7 Goa2 e5 seng3-iu5 boah--i.
21)	Goa2 e5 chhiu2 beh siong5-siong5 kap i ti7-teh,  Goa2 e5 chhiu2-kut iah8 beh kian-kou3--i.
22)	Tui3-tek8 boe7-oe7 lek8-sek i;  Hiong-ok e5 lang5 boe7-oe7 khou2-chhou2--i.
23)	Goa2 beh ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5 phah-chhui3 i e5 tui3-tek8;  Kong-kek hit e5 oan3-hun7 i e5 lang5.
24)	Chong2-si7 Goa2 e5 sin3-sit8, kap Goa2 e5 chu5-ai3, beh kap i ti7-teh;  In-ui7 Goa2 e5 mia5, i e5 kak beh tit-tioh8 kiah8-koaiN5.
25)	Goa2 beh hou7 i e5 chhiu2 chhun kau3 hai2;  ChiaN3-chhiu2 chhun kau3 chiah e5 ho5.
26)	I beh chheng-hou Goa2 kong2, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 pe7,  Si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, si7 kiu3 goa2 e5 chioh8-poaN5.
27)	Goa2 iah8 beh siat-lip8 i choe3 toa7-kiaN2,  Choe3 se3-chiuN7 te7-it koaiN5 e5 kun-ong5.
28)	Goa2 beh ui7-tioh8 i po2-chun5 Goa2 e5 chu5-ai3 kau3 eng2-oan2;  Goa2 kap i sou2 lip8 e5 iok, tek-khak bo5 pian3-oaN7.
29)	Goa2 iah8 beh po2-chun5 i e5 hou7-e3 kau3 tai7-tai7;  Hou7 i e5 po2-cho7 chhin-chhiuN7 thiN e5 ku2.
30)	Siat-su2 i e5 kiaN2-sun pang3-sak Goa2 e5 lut8-hoat;  Bo5 kiaN5 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7;
31)	Poe7-biu7 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7,  Bo5 siu2 Goa2 e5 kai3-beng7;
32)	Goa2 chiu7 beh eng7 koaiN2-a2 chek-hoat8 in e5 ke3-sit;  Eng7 piN chek-hoat8 in e5 choe7-ok.
33)	Chong2-si7 Goa2 tek-khak bo5 chiong goa2 e5 chu5-ai3 it-chin7 tui3 i siu-hoe5;  Iah8 tek-khak bo5 hou7 Goa2 e5 sin3-sit8 hoe3-bo5.
34)	Goa2 tek-khak bo5 sit Goa2 e5 iok,  Iah8 bo5 koe2-oaN7 Goa2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2--e5.
35)	Goa2 chit8-pai2 ki2 ka-ki7 e5 seng3-kiat lai5 chiu3-choa7,  Goa2 koat-toan3 bo5 tui3 Tai7-pit8 kong2 peh8-chhat8;
36)	I e5 hou7-e3 beh thoan5 kau3 eng2-oan2;  I e5 po2-cho7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5, chhin-chhiuN7 jit8 e5 ku2-tng5;
37)	Iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 geh8 e5 eng2-oan2 kian3-lip8;  Koh chhin-chhiuN7 thiN-teng2 khak-sit8 e5 kan-cheng3. [Se3-lah8
38)	Chong2-si7 Li2 u7 siu7-khi3 Li2 e5 siu7-boah-iu5--e5,  Iam3-chian7 khi3-sak i.
39)	Li2 i2-keng iam3-ouN3 kap Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 sou2 lip8 e5 iok,  Chiong i e5 bian2-liu5 chau-that ti7 toe7--nih.
40)	Li2 i2-keng thiah i it-chhe3 e5 li5-pa;  Hou7 i e5 oe7-sou2 piN3 choe3 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7.
41)	Ke3-lou7 lang5 long2 chhiuN2-theh8 i;  I chiaN5-choe3 keh-piah kok sou2 leng5-jiok8--e5.
42)	Li2 hou7 i e5 tui3-tek8 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 kiah8-koaiN5;  Hou7 i e5 kiu5-siu5 long2 hoaN-hi2.
43)	Li2 hou7 i e5 to-kiam3 to2-mi5,  Hou7 i ti7 kau-chian3 e5 si5 khia7-boe7-tiau5.
44)	Li2 hou7 i e5 eng5-hian2 bo5--khi3,  Chiong i e5 po2-cho7 chhia-to2 ti7 toe7--nih.
45)	Li2 kiam2-chio2 i chheng-lian5 e5 jit8-chi2;  Koh hou7 i moa2-moa2 kian3-siau3. [Se3-lah8
46)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 beh joa7-ku2 ka-ki7 khng3-bat8, kau3 eng2-oan2 mah?  Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 chhin-chhiuN7 he2 toh8, beh joa7-ku2 ah?
47)	Kiu5 Li2 ki3-tit goa2 e5 si5-kan, chaiN2-iuN7 hiah te2-chio2;  Li2 chhong3-cho7 it-chhe3 e5 se3-kan lang5, hou7 in kau3 hiah khang-hu ah!
48)	Sim2-mih8 lang5 oe7 tng5-tng5 oah8, bo5 kiN3-tioh8 si2,  Oe7 kiu3 i e5 leng5-hun5 thoat-li7 im-kan e5 koan5-peng3 ah? [Se3-lah8
49)	Chu2 ah, Li2 cheng5 pin5 Li2 e5 sin3-sit8, tui3 Tai7-pit8 chiu3-choa7--e5,  Hiah e5 chu5-ai3 taN ti7 toh-loh8?
50)	Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 ki3-liam7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 sou2 siu7 e5 leng5-jiok8,  Ki3-liam7 goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 chiong it-chhe3 kiong5-seng7 e5 peh-siN3 e5 leng5-jiok8 chun5 ti7 goa2 e5 sim-lai7;
51)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 eng7 chit e5 leng5-jiok8,  Chiu7-si7 leng5-jiok8 Li2 siu7 boah-iu5--e5 e5 chong-chek.
52)	Tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kau3 eng2-oan2.  A-beng7, koh A-beng7.

	Koan3 IV
[90]	Siong7-te3 e5 lang5 Mou5-se e5 ki5-to2.
1)	Chu2 ah, Li2 tak8 se3-tai7 choe3 goan2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7.
2)	Chiah e5 soaN iau2-be7 siN-chhut,  Toe7 kap se3-kai3 Li2 iau2-be7 cho7-chiaN5,  Tui3 eng2-oan2 kau3 eng2-oan2 Li2 si7 Siong7-te3.
3)	Li2 hou7 lang5 kui thou2,  Kong2, Lin2 se3-kan lang5, tioh8 oat8-to3-tng2.
4)	In-ui7 chai7 Li2 khoaN3, chit8-chheng ni5 chhin-chhiuN7 i2-keng ke3--khi3 e5 cha7-jit8;  Koh chhin-chhiuN7 mi5-kan e5 chit8-kiN.
5)	Li2 chhin-chhiuN7 eng7 toa7-chui2 ka7 in lau5--khi3; in chhin-chhiuN7 khun3 chit8-chhiN2;  Cha2-khi2-si5 in chhin-chhiuN7 hoat-siN e5 chhau2.
6)	Cha2-khi2-si5 hoat-siN bou7-seng7;  E5-hng-si5 siu7-koah chiu7 kou-ta5.
7)	In-ui7 goan2 tui3 Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 chiu7 siau-biat8,  Koh goan2 tui3 Li2 e5 hoat-seng3 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5.
8)	Li2 chiong goan2 e5 choe7-ok pai5 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5,  Chiong goan2 un2-bat8 e5 phaiN2 pai5 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7 e5 kng-beng5-tiong.
9)	Goan2 e5 jit8-chi2 long2 keng-ke3 ti7 Li2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3;  Goan2 e5 ni5-he3 ke3-liau2, chhin-chhiuN7 thou2 chit8 e5 khui3.
10)	Goan2 it-seng e5 ni5-jit8 si7 chhit-chap8 he3,  Na7 si7 iong2-chong3 thang kau3 poeh-chap8 he3,  Chong2-si7 ki5-tiong sou2 khoa-khau2--e5, put-ko3 si7 lo5-khou2 iu-chhiu5;  I kin2-kin2 ke3, goan2 chiu7 pe--khi3.
11)	Chi7-chui7 chai Li2 siu7-khi3 e5 koan5-se3,  Iah8 chiau3 Li2 eng-kai siu7 e5 keng3-ui3, chai Li2 e5 siu7-khi3 ah?
12)	Kiu5 Li2 ka3-si7 goan2, chaiN2-iuN7 sng3 ka-ki7 e5 jit8-chi2;  Hou7 goan2 tit-tioh8 ti3-hui7 e5 sim.
13)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, beh kau3 ti7-si5 nih? kiu5 Li2 to3-tng2;  Ui7-tioh8 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 lai5 hoe5-sim.
14)	Kiu5 Li2 cha2-khi2-si5 eng7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 hou7 goan2 moa2-chiok;  Hou7 goan2 chit8-si3-lang5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8.
15)	Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 khou2-chhou2 goan2 e5 jit8,  Chiau3 goan2 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 ni5, hou7 goan2 hoaN-hi2.
16)	Goan7 Li2 e5 sou2-choe3 tui3 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 hian2-hian7,  Li2 e5 eng5-kng tui3 in e5 kiaN2-sun hian2-beng5.
17)	Goan7 Chu2 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 bi2-biau7 tiam3 ti7 goan2 e5 teng2-bin7;  Goan7 Li2 kian-kou3 goan2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 e5 kang,  Goan2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 e5 kang, goan7 Li2 kian-kou3 i.

[91]	Tiam3 ti7 Chi3-koaiN5--e5 un2-bat8 e5 sou2-chai7--e5,  Hit e5 lang5 beh khia7-khi2 ti7 Choan5-leng5--e5 e5 im3-ng2.
2)	Lun7-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, goa2 beh kong2, I si7 goa2 to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7, si7 goa2 e5 soaN-che7;  Si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 sou2 oa2-kho3--e5.
3)	In-ui7 I beh kiu3 li2 thoat-li7 tng chiau2-a2 e5 lo5-bang7,  Kap tok8-hai7 e5 un-ek8.
4)	I beh eng7 I e5 sit8-kou2 aN5 li2,  Li2 beh bih ti7 I e5 sit8-e7,  I e5 seng5-sit8 si7 toa7-soe3 e5 tin5-pai5.
5)	Li2 m7-bian2 kiaN mi5-kan e5 kiaN-hiaN5,  A2-si7 jit8--si5 teh pe e5 chiN3.
6)	Iah8 bian2 kiaN ou-am3-tiong liu5-heng5 e5 un-ek8,  A2-si7 jit8 tiong-kau3 biat8-bo5 lang5 e5 tok8-cheng3.
7)	U7 chheng lang5 lek--loh8-khi3 ti7 li2 e5 sin-piN,  U7 ban7 lang5 lek--loh8-khi3 ti7 li2 e5 chiaN3-peng5,  Che iah8 boe7 oa2-kun7 li2.
8)	Put-ko3 li2 oe7 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3,  Iah8 khoaN3-kiN3 phaiN2-lang5 siu7 po3-eng3.
9)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Li2 si7 goa2 to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7;  Li2 bat eng7 Chi3-koaiN5--e5 choe3 li2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7;
10)	Chiu7 chai-hai7 boe7 kau3 ti7 li2,  Un-ek8 iah8 boe7 oa2-kun7 li2 e5 pou3-piN5.
11)	In-ui7 I beh ui7-tioh8 li2 hoan-hu3 I e5 su3-chia2,  Ti7 li2 it-chhe3 e5 lou7 po2-hou7 li2.
12)	In beh eng7 chhiu2 hu5 li2,  Bian2-tit li2 e5 kha tak-tioh8 chioh8.
13)	Li2 beh tah8 sai kap tok8-choa5,  Lap sai-a2-thun5 kap toa7-be2 choa5.
14)	In-ui7 i chin thiaN3 Goa2, Goa2 chiu7 beh kiu3 i;  In-ui7 i bat Goa2 e5 mia5, Goa2 chiu7 beh an-ti3 i ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7.
15)	I kiu5-kio3 Goa2, Goa2 chiu7 beh in3--i;  I ti7 gui5-kip e5 si5, Goa2 beh kap i ti7-teh;  Goa2 beh kiu3 i, hou7 i chun-kui3.
16)	Goa2 beh eng7 tng5 he3-siu7 hou7 i moa2-chiok,  Hou7 i khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 e5 kiu3-un.

[92]	An-hioh-jit8 e5 si-koa.
1)	Chin-ho2 ah, kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  ChhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2 Chi3-koaiN5--e5 e5 mia5;
2)	Cha2-khi2-si5 po3-iong5 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3;  E5-hng-si5 po3-iong5 Li2 e5 sin3-sit8.
3)	Eng7 chap8-tiau5-hian5 e5 gak8-khi3 kap sek;  Eng7 khim5 toaN5 chong-giam5 e5 siaN-im.
4)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 sou2-kiaN5 hou7 goa2 hoaN-hi2;  Goa2 beh in-ui7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5 lai5 khoai3-lok8.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa, Li2 e5 sou2-choe3 chaiN2-iuN7 hiah-toa7;  Li2 e5 sim-su kek8-ki5 chhim.
6)	Bu5-ti e5 lang5 boe7 hiau2-tit,  Gu5-chhun2 e5 lang5 iah8 boe7 beng5-pek8 chit-e5.
7)	PhaiN2-lang5 hoat-siN chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2,  It-chhe3 choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5 bou7-seng7 e5 si5,  ChiaN3-si7 in beh biat8-bo5 kau3 eng2-oan2;
8)	Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Li2 si7 chi3-koaiN5, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.
9)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 khoaN3, Li2 e5 tui3-tek8,  Li2 khoaN3, Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 tek-khak biat8-bo5;  It-chhe3 choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5 iah8 beh si3-soaN3.
10)	Chong2-si7 Li2 hou7 goa2 e5 kak kiah8-koaiN5, chhin-chhiuN7 ia2-gu5 e5 kak;  Goa2 si7 siu7 sin e5 iu5 boah--e5.
11)	Goa2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 tu2-tioh8 po3-eng3;  Goa2 chhin-hi7 thiaN-kiN3 hiah e5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek goa2 e5 phaiN2-lang5 siu7 heng5-hoat8.
12)	Gi7-lang5 beh heng-ong7 chhin-chhiuN7 cho2-chhiu7;  Beh tiong2-toa7 chhin-chhiuN7 Li7-pa-lun3 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7.
13)	KiN3-na7 chai ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3--e5,  Beh heng-ong7 ti7 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 iN7-lai7.
14)	In ni5-lau7 e5 si5 iu5-goan5 beh kiat ke2-chi2;  In e5 chiap moa2-moa2, sek chhiN-chhui3;
15)	Thang hian2-beng5 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 cheng3-tit8--e5,  I si7 goa2 e5 chioh8-poaN5, I long2 bo5 put-gi7.

[93]	Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 ong5, I eng7 ui-giam5 ka-ki7 chheng7;  Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 khui3-lat8 ka-ki7 chheng7, ka-ki7 ha5;  Se3-kai3 chiu7 kian-kou3 boe7 io5-tang7.
2)	Li2 e5 po2-cho7 tui3 kou2-cha2 kian3-lip8,  Li2 tui3 eng2-oan2 chiu7 u7.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, toa7-chui2 i2-keng hoat-khi2,  Toa7-chui2 i2-keng hoat-khi2 i e5 siaN;  Toa7-chui2 hoat-khi2 i e5 eng2.
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 koaiN5-ui7 u7 toa7 leng5-lek8,  IaN5-ke3 chiah e5 chui2 e5 siaN,  I2-kip8 hai2--nih e5 toa7-eng2.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 kan-cheng3 put-chi2 khak-sit8;  Seng3-kiat hap8 ti7 Li2 e5 chhu3, kau3 eng2-oan2.

[94]	Ia5-ho5-hoa sin-oan e5 Siong7-te3 ah,  Sin-oan e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 hian2-chhut kng.
2)	Sim2-phoaN3 se3-kai3 e5 Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 khi2--lai5;  Hou7 kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 siu7 eng-kai siu7 e5 po3-eng3.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, PhaiN2-lang5 beh joa7-ku2 ah?  PhaiN2-lang5 tek-seng3 tai7-iat8, beh joa7-ku2 ah?
4)	In sui5-pian7 kong2, kong2-chhut kiau-ngou7 e5 oe7;  It-chhe3 kiaN5-phaiN2 e5 lang5 long2 ka-ki7 phin2-phong2.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, in ap-che3 Li2 e5 peh-siN3;  Khou2-chhou2 Li2 e5 san2-giap8.
6)	In thai5-si2 chiu2-koaN2-lang5 kap chhut-goa7 lang5;  Koh hai7-si2 kou-ji5.
7)	In kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak bo5 teh khoaN3;  Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 tek-khak bo5 ti3-i3.
8)	Lin2 peh-siN3-tiong cheng-siN hit-khoan2 e5 lang5 tioh8 siuN7;  Gu5-gong7 e5 lang5 kau3 ti7-si5 chiah u7 ti3-hui7 ah?
9)	An-ti3 hi7-khang--e5, chong2 bo5 I bo5 thiaN-kiN3?  Chhong3-cho7 bak8-chiu--e5, chong2 bo5 I boe7 khoaN3-kiN3 mah?
10)	Kau3-tok liat8-pang e5, chiu7-si7 hou7 lang5 tit-tioh8 ti3-sek--e5,  Chong2 bo5 I boe7 hiau2 pan7-li2 lang5 mah?
11)	Ia5-ho5-hoa chai lang5 e5 sim-su,  Chai in si7 khang-khang.
12)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 sou2 kau3-tok koh eng7 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat sou2 ka3-si7--e5,  Hit e5 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
13)	Beh hou7 i ti7 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8, tit-tioh8 peng5-an,  Kau3 ti7 ui7-tioh8 phaiN2-lang5 khui ham7-khiN e5 si5.
14)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak bo5 khi3-sak I e5 peh-siN3;  Iah8 bo5 pang3-li7 I e5 san2-giap8.
15)	In-ui7 sim2-phoaN3 beh chiau3 kong-gi7,  Sim cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5 beh long2 te3 I.
16)	Chi7-chui7 beh ui7 goa2 khi2--lai5 kong-kek phaiN2-lang5?  Chi7-chui7 beh ui7 goa2 khia7--khi2-lai5 kong-kek kiaN5 choe7-ok e5 lang5?
17)	Na7 m7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa pang-chan7 goa2,  chiu7 goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 khoai3-khoai3 tiam3 ti7 leng2-cheng7 e5 tiong-kan.
18)	Goa2 kong2, Goa2 e5 kha tioh8-tak;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, hit-si5 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 hu5-chhi5 goa2.
19)	Goa2 e5 sim choe7-choe7 iu-bun7 khoa3-lu7,  Li2 e5 an-ui3 chiu7 hou7 goa2 e5 sim-sin5 khoai3-lok8.
20)	Kan-ok e5 cho7-ui7, ka2-chia3 lut8-le7, ke3-bou5 chan5-hai7,  Kiam2 oe7 kap Li2 kau-thong mah?
21)	In tai7-ke chu7-chip8, kong-kek gi7-lang5 e5 siN3-mia7;  Chiong bo5-choe7 e5 lang5 teng7 si2-choe7.
22)	Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa peng5-si5 choe3 goa2 e5 koaiN5-tai5;  Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 choe3 goa2 to5-siam2 e5 chioh8-poaN5.
23)	I hou7 in e5 choe7-ok kui ti7 in e5 sin-chiuN7;  In ti7 kiaN5-phaiN2 e5 si5, I beh chau5-biat8 in;  Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh chau5-biat8 in.

[95]	Lai5 ah, lan2 tioh8 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiuN3-koa;  Ng3 kiu3 lan2 e5 chioh8-poaN5 chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.
2)	Lan2 tioh8 kau3 I e5 bin7-cheng5 kam2-sia7 I,  Eng7 si-koa ng3 I chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.
3)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 toa7 e5 Siong7-te3,  Si7 toa7 e5 ong5, iaN5-ke3 long2-chong2 e5 siong7-te3;
4)	Toe7 chhim e5 sou2-chai7 ti7 I e5 chhiu2-tiong;  SoaN koaiN5 e5 soaN-chiam iah8 siok8 ti7 I.
5)	IuN5-hai2 siok8 ti7 I, si7 I chhong3-cho7--e5;  Ta-toe7 iah8 si7 I e5 chhiu2 cho7-chiaN5-e5.
6)	Lai5 ah, lan2 tioh8 kiok-kiong keng3-pai3;  Kui7-loh8 ti7 chhong3-cho7 lan2 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5;
7)	In-ui7 I si7 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3,  Lan2 si7 I iuN2-chhi7 e5 peh-siN3, si7 I chhiu2-e7 e5 iuN5.  Kin-a2-jit8, lin2 na7 thiaN I e5 siaN,
8)	Chiu7 m7-thang ngi7 lin2 e5 sim, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Bi2-li7-pa,  Chhin-chhiuN7 tong-jit8 ti7 khong3-ia2 e5 Ma2-sat;
9)	Hit-si5 lin2 e5 chou2-kong chhi3 Goa2,  Giam7 Goa2, koh khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 e5 sou2-choe3.
10)	Si3-chap8 ni5 ku2, Goa2 iam3-hun7 hit se3-tai7 e5 lang5,  Kong2 Chiah-e5 si7 sim be5-loan7 e5 peh-siN3,  M7-bat Goa2 e5 lou7;
11)	Sou2-i2 Goa2 ti7 siu7-khi3 e5 tiong-kan, chiu3-choa7 kong2,  In toan3-toan3 boe7-tit-thang jip8 Goa2 e5 an-hioh.

[96]	Lin2 tioh8 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiuN3 sin e5 koa,  Choan5-toe7 long2 tioh8 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiuN3-koa.
2)	Tioh8 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiuN3-koa, chiok-sia7 I e5 mia5;  Jit8-jit8 thoan5-po3 I e5 kiu3-un.
3)	Ti7 liat8-pang e5 tiong-kan kong2-khi2 I e5 eng5-kng;  Ti7 ban7 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan kong2-khi2 I ki5-biau7 e5 sou2-choe3.
4)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 toa7, eng-kai siu7 kek8-toa7 e5 o-lo2;  I ti7 cheng3 sin5-beng5 e5 teng2-bin7 eng-kai siu7 keng3-ui3.
5)	In-ui7 liat8-pang e5 siong7-te3 long2 si7 hu-ke2;  Tok8-tok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhong3-cho7 chiah e5 thiN.
6)	Ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 u7 chun-kui3 kap ui-giam5;  Ti7 I e5 seng3-sou2 u7 koan5-leng5 kap eng5-kng.
7)	Peh-siN3-tiong e5 tak8-chok8 ah, lin2 tioh8 chiong koan5-leng5 eng5-kng,  Kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
8)	Eng7 I e5 mia5 sou2 eng-kai tit-tioh8 e5 eng5-kng, kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Toa3 le2-mih8 lai5 jip8 I e5 iN7.
9)	Tioh8 eng7 seng3-kiat e5 chng-thaN7 keng3-pai3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Choan5-toe7 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.
10)	Ti7 liat8-pang-tiong tioh8 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 ong5,  Se3-kai3 kian-kou3, boe7 io5-tang7;  I beh chiau3 kong-peng5 sim2-phoaN3 ban7 peh-siN3.
11)	Goan7 thiN hoaN-hi2, toe7 khoai3-lok8;  Goan7 hai2 kap ki5-tiong sou2 chhiong-moa2--e5 long2 chhut toa7-siaN;
12)	Goan7 chhan5-hng5 kap ki5-tiong sou2-u7--e5 long2 khoai3-lok8;  Hit-si5 chhiu7-na5-lai7 e5 chhiu7-bak8 long2 beh ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN;
13)	In-ui7 I lai5 lah, I lai5 beh sim2-phoaN3 choan5-toe7;  I beh chiau3 kong-gi7 sim2-phoaN3 se3-kai3,  Chiau3 I e5 sin3-sit8 sim2-phoaN3 ban7 peh-siN3.

[97]	Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 ong5; toe7 tioh8 khoai3-lok8;  Cheng3 hai2-su7 tioh8 hoaN-hi2.
2)	Bat8-hun5 kap ou-am3 ti7 I e5 si3-ui5;  Gi7-li2 kap kong-peng5 si7 I po2-cho7 e5 toe7-ki.
3)	He2 kiaN5 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5,  Sio I si3-ui5 e5 tui3-tek8.
4)	I e5 sih-na3 chio3-kng se3-kai3;  Toe7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 tin2-tang7.
5)	Ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, chiu7-si7 choan5-toe7 e5 Chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5,  Chiah e5 soaN siau-iuN5 chhin-chhiuN7 lah8.
6)	Chiah e5 thiN hian2-beng5 I e5 gi7,  Liat8-pang khoaN3-kiN3 I e5 eng5-kng.
7)	Hoan7-na7 hok8-sai3 tiau-khek e5 ngou2-siong7,  Eng7 hu-ke2 e5 sin5 chu7-khoa--e5, long2 tioh8 siu7 kian3-siau3;  Lin2 chiah e5 sin5 ah, long2 tioh8 keng3-pai3 I;
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, in-ui7 Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3,  Sek-an thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 hoaN-hi2,  Iu5-tai7 e5 siaN5 iah8 long2 khoai3-lok8.
9)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Li2 si7 chi3-koaiN5 poaN5-ke3 choan5-toe7;  Li2 si7 chi3-chun, poaN5-ke3 cheng3 sin5-beng5.
10)	ThiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5, lin2 long2 tioh8 oan3-hun7 phaiN2;  I po2-hou7 I seng3 e5 peh-siN3 e5 siN3-mia7;  I chin2-kiu3 in thoat-li7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhiu2.
11)	Kng-beng5 si7 ui7-tioh8 gi7-lang5 lai5 pi7-pan7,  HoaN-hi2 si7 ui7-tioh8 sim cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5 lai5 pi7-pan7.
12)	Gi7-lang5 ah, lin2 tioh8 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 hoaN-hi2;  Ki3-liam7 I e5 seng3-mia5 lai5 o-lo2.

[98]	Chit8 phiN si.
1)	Lin2 tioh8 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiuN3 sin e5 koa;  In-ui7 I bat kiaN5 ki5-biau7 e5 su7;  I e5 chiaN3-chhiu2, kap I seng3 e5 chhiu2-kut, i2-keng ui7 ka-ki7 kiaN5 chin2-kiu3.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 lang5 chai I e5 chin2-kiu3;  Ti7 liat8-pang-lang5 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 hian2-beng5 I e5 kong-gi7.
3)	I ki3-liam7 I tui3 I2-sek-liat8 ke sou2 hoat-chhut e5 chu5-ai3 kap sin3-sit8;  Toe7 e5 si3-kak long2 khoaN3-kiN3 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 chin2-kiu3.
4)	Choan5-toe7 long2 tioh8 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN;  Tioh8 chhut toa7-siaN hoaN-hi2 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 I.
5)	Tioh8 toaN5-khim5 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Tioh8 toaN5-khim5 ho5 si-koa e5 siaN o-lo2 I.
6)	Eng7 ho7-thau5 kap sau3-kak e5 siaN,  Ti7 Kun-ong5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.
7)	Goan7 hai2, kap ki5-tiong sou2 chhiong-moa2--e5, long2 tioh8 chhut toa7-siaN;  Se3-kai3, kap tiam3 ti7 hit tiong-kan--e5, iah8 tioh8 chhut-siaN;
8)	Goan7 toa7-chui2 phah chhiu2-chiuN2,  Goan7 chiah e5 soaN ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.
9)	In-ui7 I lai5 beh sim2-phoaN3 choan5-toe7;  I beh chiau3 kong-gi7 sim2-phoaN3 se3-kai3,  Chiau3 I e5 cheng3-tit8 sim2-phoaN3 liat8-pang.

[99]	Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 ong5, liat8-pang tioh8 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah;  I che7 ti7 ki-lou7-peng, toe7 tioh8 io5-tang7.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Sek-an choe3 toa7;  I poaN5-ke3 ti7 ban7 peh-siN3 e5 teng2-bin7.
3)	In tioh8 o-lo2 Li2 toa7 koh thang kiaN-ui3 e5 mia5;  I si7 chi3-seng3.
4)	Ong5 u7 khui3-lat8, hoaN-hi2 kong-peng5;  Li2 hou7 cheng3-tit8 kian-kou3.  Ti7 Nga2-kok tiong kiaN5 kong-peng5 kap gi7-li2.
5)	Lin2 tioh8 chun-tiong7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3,  Ti7 I kha-tah8-i2 e5 thau5-cheng5 kui7-pai3;  I si7 chi3-seng3.
6)	Ti7 I e5 che3-si-tiong, u7 Mou5-se kap A-lun5,  Ti7 kiu5-kio3 I e5 mia5 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, u7 Sat-bou2-jiN2;  In kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I chiu7 thiaN in.
7)	I ti7 hun5-thiau7 e5 tiong-kan tui3 in kong2-oe7;  In chun-siu2 I kan-cheng3 e5 oe7, kap I sou2 siuN2-su3 in e5 lut8-hoat.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 u7 in3--in;  Li2 sui-jian5 chiau3 in e5 sou2-kiaN5 po3-eng3 in,  Iau2-ku2 Li2 si7 sia3-bian2 in e5 Siong7-te3.
9)	Lin2 tioh8 chun-tiong7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3,  Ti7 I e5 seng3-soaN kui7-pai3;  In-ui7 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 chi3-seng3.

[100]	Kam2-sia7 e5 si.
1)	Choan5-toe7 tioh8 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.
2)	Lin2 tioh8 hoaN-hi2 e5 sim hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  ChhiuN3-koa lai5 kau3 I e5 bin7-cheng5.
3)	Lin2 tioh8 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 Siong7-te3;  Lan2 si7 I chhong3-cho7-e5, lan2 iah8 si7 I e5;  Lan2 si7 I e5 peh-siN3, iah8 si7 I chhau2-tiuN5 e5 iuN5.
4)	Tioh8 eng7 kam2-sia7 jip8 I e5 mng5,  Eng7 o-lo2 jip8 I e5 iN7;  Tioh8 kam2-sia7 I, o-lo2 I e5 mia5.
5)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 ho2;  I e5 chu5-ai3 kau3 eng2-oan2;  I e5 sin3-sit8 kau3 ban7 se3-tai7.

[101]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Goa2 beh chhiuN3 chu5-ai3 kap kong-peng5 e5 koa;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 beh ng3 Li2 chhiuN3 o-lo2 e5 koa.
2)	Goa2 beh eng7 ti3-hui7 kiaN5 ti7 oan5-choan5 e5 lou7;  Li2 beh siaN2-si5 kau3 goa2 chia?  Goa2 beh eng7 oan5-choan5 e5 sim kiaN5 ti7 goa2 e5 ke-lai7.
3)	Sia5-phiah e5 su7, goa2 long2 m7 pai5 ti7 goa2 e5 bak8-cheng5;  Poe7-to7 e5 lang5 sou2 choe3 e5 su7, goa2 chin oan3-hun7;  M7 hou7 i liam5-tioh8 goa2.
4)	Oan-khiau e5 sim tek-khak hou7 i li7-khui goa2;  It-chhe3 e5 phaiN2 goa2 m7-bat i.
5)	Am3-tiong hui2-pong3 i e5 chhu3-piN--e5, goa2 beh biat8 i;  Bak8-chiu-khou toa7 e5, sim kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5, goa7 bo5 iong5-un2 i.
6)	Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu beh khoaN3 kok-lai7 seng5-sit8 e5 lang5, hou7 in kap goa2 saN-kap toa3;  KiaN5 ti7 oan5-choan5 e5 lou7--e5, i beh hok8-sai7 goa2.
7)	KiaN5 khui2-cha3 e5 lang5 boe7-tit-thang toa3 goa2 e5 ke-lai7;  Kong2 peh8-chhat8-oe7 e5 lang5 boe7-tit-thang khia7-tiau5 ti7 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5.
8)	Tak8 cha2-khi2 goa2 beh biat8-bo5 kok-lai7 e5 phaiN2-lang5;  Thang chiong it-chhe3 choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5, tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN5 tu5--khi3.

[102]	Khun3-khou2 e5 lang5, kek8 loan2-jiok8 e5 si5, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 thou3-chhut khou2-cheng5 e5 ki5-to2.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 thiaN goa2 e5 ki5-to2,  Hou7 goa2 kiu5-kio3 e5 siaN thau3 kau3 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
2)	Goa2 ti7 gui5-kip e5 jit8, m7-thang ng Li2 e5 bin7 m7-khoaN3 goa2; kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2;  Goa2 kiu5-kio3 e5 jit8, kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 in3--goa2.
3)	In-ui7 goa2 e5 jit8-chi2 chhin-chhiuN7 he2-hun siau-soaN3,  Goa2 e5 kut siu7 sio, chhin-chhiuN7 he2-tiong e5 chha5.
4)	Goa2 e5 sim siu7-siong, kou-ta5 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2;  Goa2 long2 boe7 kou3--tit chiah8.
5)	In-ui7 goa2 thou2-khui3 e5 siaN,  Goa2 e5 bah khih8 ti7 kut--nih.
6)	Goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 khong3-ia2 e5 the5-ou5-chiau2,  Iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7 e5 am3-kong-chiau2.
7)	Goa2 kui-mi5 bo5 khun3;  Iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 chhu3-teng2 kou-toaN e5 chhek-chiau2-a2.
8)	Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 thong-jit8 siat-tok8 goa2;  Thong3-hun7 goa2 e5 lang5 ki2 goa2 lai5 chiu3-chou2.
9)	Goa2 eng7 he2-hu chun2 png7 chiah8;  Sou2 lim--e5 u7 chham bak8-sai2.
10)	Che si7 in-ui7 Li2 e5 hoat-seng3 toa7 siu7-khi3;  In-ui7 Li2 chiong goa2 ku2-khi2, koh chiong goa2 hiat-loh8.
11)	Goa2 e5 jit8-chi2 chhin-chhiuN7 jit8-iaN2 i2-keng chhia5,  Goa2 iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2 kou-ta5.
12)	Tok8-tok8 Li2 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng2-oan2 ti7-teh;  Li2 hou7 lang5 ki3-liam7 kau3 ban7-tai7.
13)	Li2 beh khi2--lai5 lin5-bin2 Sek-an,  In-ui7 hian7-chai7 si7 kho2-lin5 i e5 si5; tiaN7-tioh8 e5 ki5 i2-keng kau3 lah.
14)	Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 hoaN-hi2 Sek-an e5 chioh8-thau5,  Kho2-lin5 i e5 thou5-hun2.
15)	Liat8-kok chiu7 beh keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5;  Se3-chiuN7 chiah e5 ong5 long2 beh keng3-ui3 Li2 e5 eng5-kng.
16)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2-cho7 Sek-an,  Ti7 I eng5-kng-tiong hian2-hian7.
17)	I aN3-loh8 thiaN song3-hiong lang5 e5 ki5-to2,  Bo5 khoaN3-khin in e5 ki5-to2.
18)	Che beh ui7 au7-tai7 e5 lang5 ki3-chai3,  Chiong-lai5 siu7-cho7 e5 peh-siN3 beh o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
19)	In-ui7 I tui3 I chi3-koaiN5 e5 seng3-sou2 khoaN3--loh8-lai5,  Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 thiN khoaN3 loh8 toe7;
20)	Beh thiaN siu5-hoan7 e5 thou2-khui3;  Beh thau2-pang3 gi2 tiaN7-tioh8 si2 e5 lang5.
21)	Hou7 lang5 ti7 Sek-an thoan5-pou3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5;  Ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 thoan5-pou3 o-lo2 I e5 oe7.
22)	Chiu7-si7 ban7 peh-siN3 kap liat8-kok chu7-chip8 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 si5.
23)	I hou7 goa2 e5 khui3-lat8 poaN3-lou7 soe-lam2;  Hou7 goa2 e5 jit8-chi2 te2-chio2.
24)	Goa2 kong2, Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, m7-thang ti7 goa2 tiong-lian5 tho2 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7;  Li2 e5 ni5-he3 ban7 se3-tai7 bu5-kiong5-chin7.
25)	Li2 khi2-thau5 he7 toe7 e5 toe7-ki;  ThiN iah8 si7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 cho7--e5.
26)	In beh biat8-bo5, tok8-tok8 Li2 ku2-tng5 ti7-teh;  In beh chhin-chhiuN7 saN chiam7-chiam7 ku7;  Li2 beh chiong in koe2-oaN7, chhin-chhiuN7 koe2-oaN7 saN; in chiu7 pian3-oaN7.
27)	Tok8-tok8 Li2 bo5 pian3-oaN7,  Li2 e5 he3-siu7 bo5 kiong5-chin7.
28)	Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 e5 kiaN2-sun beh tng5-tng5 ti7-teh;  In e5 hou7-e3 beh khia7-chai7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.

[103]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 ah, li2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Hoan7-na7 ti7 goa2 lai7-bin7--e5, iah8 tioh8 o-lo2 I e5 seng3-mia5.
2)	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 ah, li2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  M7-thang boe7-ki3-tit I it-chhe3 e5 un-hui7;
3)	I sia3-bian2 li2 long2-chong2 e5 choe7;  I-ho2 li2 long2-chong2 e5 piN7;
4)	I kiu3-siok8 li2 e5 siN3-mia7 thoat-li7 si2-bo5;  Eng7 jin5-ai3 kap chu5-pi choe3 li2 e5 bian2-liu5;
5)	Eng7 ho2-mih8 chiok li2 e5 sim-goan7;  Hou7 li2 hok8-to3 siau3-lian5 chhin-chhiuN7 eng-chiau2.
6)	Ia5-ho5-hoa kiaN5 kong-gi7,  Ui7-tioh8 it-chhe3 siu7 un-khut e5 lang5 sin-oan.
7)	Eng7 I e5 to7-lou7 chi2-si7 Mou5-se,  Eng7 I e5 kiaN5-choe3 chi2-si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 lin5-bin2, u7 un-tian2;  Bo5 khoai3-khoai3 siu7-khi3, koh u7 hong-seng7 e5 chu5-ai3.
9)	I bo5 tng5-tng5 chek-pi7,  Iah8 bo5 eng2-oan2 khng3 siu7-khi3.
10)	I bo5 chiau3 lan2 e5 choe7-koa3 khoan2-thai7 lan2,  Iah8 bo5 chiau3 lan2 e5 choe7-ok po3-eng3 lan2.
11)	In-ui7 thiN li7-khui toe7 hiah--nih koaiN5,  I e5 chu5-ai3 tui3 keng3-ui3 I e5 lang5 iah8 si7 hiah--nih toa7.
12)	Tang li7-khui sai u7 joa7-hng7,  I hou7 lan2 e5 choe7-koa3 li7-khui lan2 iah8 si7 hiah hng7.
13)	Lau7-pe7 chaiN2-iuN7 lin5-bin2 i e5 kiaN2-ji5,  Ia5-ho5-hoa lin5-bin2 keng3-ui3 I e5 lang5 iah8 si7 an2-ni.
14)	In-ui7 I chai lan2 e5 the2-chit,  Siau3-liam7 lan2 si7 thou5-hun2.
15)	Lun7-kau3 lang5, i e5 jit8-chi2 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2,  I e5 heng-ong7 chhin-chhiuN7 soaN--nih e5 hoe.
16)	Keng-ke3 hong chit8-e7 chhe, chiu7 bo5--khi3;  I e5 goan5-ui7 boe7 koh jin7--tit.
17)	Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chu5-ai3 kui ti7 keng3-ui3 I e5 lang5, tui3 eng2-oan2 kau3 eng2-oan2;  I e5 kong-gi7 ia7 kui ti7 kiaN2-kiaN2 sun-sun;
18)	Chiu7-si7 hiah e5 chun-siu2 I e5 iok,  Ki3-liam7 I e5 ka3-si7 lai5 chun-than3 e5 lang5.
19)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 thiN-teng2 siat-lip8 I e5 po2-cho7,  I e5 kok-koan5 koan2-hat ban7-hang7-u7.
20)	Lin2 chiah e5 u7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 thiN-sai3 ah,  ThiaN I e5 siaN, chiaN5 I e5 beng7-leng7 e5,  Long2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
21)	Lin2 chiah e5 choe3 I e5 cheng3 kun-peng, choe3 I e5 chhe-sai3, kiaN5 I sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5,  Long2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
22)	Lin2 it-chhe3 siu7 I chhong3-cho7--e5, ti7 I sou2 koan2-li2 e5 tak8-ui7,  Long2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 ah, li2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[104]	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 ah, li2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 si7 chi3-toa7;  Li2 eng7 chun-eng5 ui-giam5 choe3-saN lai5 chheng7.
2)	Li2 chheng7 kng-beng5 chhin-chhiuN7 goa7-saN;  Thi2-khui thiN chhin-chhiuN7 tiuN3-pak.
3)	I ti7 chui2-tiong an-ti3 I lau5-koh e5 thong-iN5,  Eng7 hun5 choe3 I e5 chhia,  Eng7 hong e5 sit8 lai5 kiaN5;
4)	Eng7 hong choe3 I e5 su3-chia2,  Eng7 iam7-he2 choe3 I e5 chhe-eng7;
5)	Chiong toe7 he7 ti7 i e5 toe7-ki teng2,  Hou7 i eng2-eng2 bo5 io5-choah.
6)	Li2 eng7 chhim-ian chhin-chhiuN7 i-chiuN5 jia-kham3 toe7-bin7;  Chiah e5 chui2 im-ke3 soaN-nia2.
7)	Li2 chit8-e7 hoah, chui2 chiu7 kin2-kin2 chau2;  Li2 e5 lui5 chit8-e7 tan5, chui2 chiu7 kin2-kin2 lau5;
8)	Chheng3 kau3 soaN-thau5, loh8 kau3 soaN-kok,  Kui ti7 Li2 ka7 in tiaN7-tioh8 e5 sou2-chai7.
9)	Li2 tiaN7-tioh8 kai3-han7 hou7 chui2 boe7-oe7 poaN5-ke3,  Bo5 koh to3-tng2-lai5 jia-kham3 toe7-bin7.
10)	Hou7 chui2-choaN5 chheng3-chhut ti7 soaN-kok,  Lau5 ti7 soaN-tiong;
11)	Hou7 soaN--nih e5 chau2-siu3 long2 u7 thang lim,  Ia2-lu5 tit-tioh8 chi2 chhui3-ta.
12)	ThiN-tiong e5 pe-chiau2 hioh ti7 chui2-piN,  Hau2 ti7 chhiu7-ki teng2.
13)	I tui3 I e5 lau5-koh-tiong koan3-ak soaN-nia2,  Tui3 Li2 sou2 choe3 e5 hau7-ko2 toe7 chiu7 chhiong-chiok.
14)	I hou7 chhau2 hoat-siN, hou7 cheng-siN thang chiah8,  Ia7 u7 chhai3-soe choe3 lang5 e5 lou7-eng7,  Hou7 chiah8-mih8 tui3 toe7--nih chhut.
15)	Koh u7 chiu2 hou7 lang5 e5 sim hoaN-hi2,  U7 iu5 lun7-tek8 lang5 e5 bin7,  U7 chiah8-mih8 pou2-iong2 lang5 e5 sim-lat8.
16)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu7 long2 tit-tioh8 chhiong-chiok e5 lun7-tek8;  Chiu7-si7 I sou2 chai Li7-pa-lun3 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7.
17)	Pe-chiau2 choh-siu7 ti7 hit lai7-bin7;  Hoh8 khia7-khi2 ti7 siong5-chhiu7 e5 tiong-kan.
18)	KoaiN5-soaN si7 hou7 ia2-soaN-iuN5 tiam3,  Chioh8-poaN5 si7 sa-hoan siam2-bih e5 sou2-chai7.
19)	I eng7 geh8 lai5 tiaN7-tioh8 si5-choeh;  Jit8-thau5 ia7 chai thang loh8.
20)	Li2 hou7 i am3, chiu7 choe3 mi5--si5;  Hit-si5 chhiu7-na5-lai7 e5 pah-siu3 chiu7 long2 pe5--chhut-lai5.
21)	Sai-a2-thun5 hau2, beh jiau3 mih8-chiah8,  Tui3 Siong7-te3 tho2 in e5 chiah8-mih8.
22)	Jit8-thau5 chit8-e7 chhut, in chiu7 chau2--khi3 bih,  To2 ti7 in e5 tong7-lai7.
23)	Lang5 chhut-khi3 choe3-kang,  Tioh8-boa5 kau3 e5-hng-si5.
24)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 sou2 cho7--e5 chaiN2-iuN7 hiah choe7!  Long2 si7 Li2 eng7 ti3-hui7 cho7-chiaN5--e5;  Pian3-toe7 moa2-moa2 Li2 e5 pu3-u7.
25)	Hia u7 hai2, toa7 koh khoah,  Ki5-tiong u7 sng3-boe7-liau2 e5 tong7-but8,  Toa7-soe3 e5 oah8-mih8 long2 u7.
26)	Ti7-hia u7 chun5 teh kiaN5;  U7 Li2 sou2 chhong3-cho7 e5 toa7-hi5 iu5-lai5 iu5-khi3.
27)	Chiah-e5 long2 teh theng3-hau7 Li2,  Thang chiau3-si5 hou7 in chiah8-mih8.
28)	Li2 hou7 in, in chiu7 khioh--khi2-lai5;  Li2 thi2-khui Li2 e5 chhiu2, in tit-tioh8 ho2-mih8 kau3-pa2.
29)	Li2 ng Li2 e5 bin7, in chiu7 khoa3-lu7;  Li2 chiong in e5 khui3 siu-hoe5, in chiu7 si2-bo5,  Lai5 kui ti7 thou5-hun2.
30)	Li2 hoat-chhut Li2 e5 sin5, in chiu7 siu7 chhong3-cho7;  Li2 hou7 toe7-bin7 oaN7 choe3 sin.
31)	Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng eng2-oan2 ti7-teh;  Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ui7-tioh8 I sou2-cho7--e5 lai5 hoaN-hi2.
32)	I khoaN3 toe7, toe7 chiu7 tin2-tang7;  I bong soaN, soaN chiu7 chhut-ian.
33)	Goa2 beh chit8-si3-lang5 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa gim5-si;  Goa2 iau2 oah8 e5 si5 beh ng3 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2.
34)	Goan7 I liah8 goa2 e5 cheng7-cheng7-siuN7 choe3 hah8-i3;  Goa2 beh in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoaN-hi2.
35)	Goan7 choe7-jin5 tui3 se3-chiuN7 siau-biat8,  Goan7 phaiN2-lang5 long2 bo5--khi3;  Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 ah, tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa; Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[105]	Lin2 tioh8 kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kiu5-kio3 I e5 mia5;  Ti7 ban7 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan po3-iong5 I e5 sou2-choe3.
2)	Tioh8 ng3 I gim5-si, ng3 I chhiuN3-koa o-lo2,  Tam5-lun7 I it-chhe3 ki5-biau7 e5 sou2-kiaN5.
3)	Tioh8 in-ui7 I e5 seng3-mia5 lai5 khoa-khau2;  Chhe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5, sim-lai7 tioh8 hoaN-hi2.
4)	Tioh8 kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap I e5 koan5-leng5;  Siong5-siong5 chhe7-kiN3 I e5 bin7.
5-6)	I e5 lou5-pok8 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 hou7-e3,  I sou2 keng2 Nga2-kok e5 kiaN2-sun ah,  Lin2 tioh8 siau3-liam7 I sou2-choe3 ki5-biau7 e5 su7,  Kap I e5 sin5-jiah, kap I e5 chhui3 phoaN3-toan3 e5 oe7.
7)	I si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lan2 e5 Siong7-te3;  Choan5-toe7 long2 u7 I e5 phoaN3-toan3.
8)	I ki3-liam7 I e5 iok, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2;  I sou2 hoan-hu3 e5 oe7, tit8-kau3 chheng-tai7;
9)	Chiu7-si7 kap A-pek-lah8-han2 sou2 lip8 e5 iok,  Tui3 I2-sat sou2 chiu3 e5 choa7.
10)	I koh chiong chit e5 iok tui3 Nga2-kok tiaN7-tioh8 choe3 lut8-le7;  Tui3 I2-sek-liat8 tiaN7-tioh8 choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 iok.
11)	Kong2, Goa2 beh chiong Ka-lam5 toe7 siuN2-su3 li2,  Choe3 li2 san2-giap8 e5 hun7-giah8.
12)	Tng-si5 in e5 jin5-teng iu2-han7;  Siau3-giah8 chio2-chio2, koh ti7-hia choe3 chhut-goa7.
13)	In tui3 chit-chok8 kiaN5 kau3 hit-chok8,  Tui3 chit-kok kau3 pat8 e5 peh-siN3.
14)	I bo5 iong5-un2 sim2-mih8 lang5 khi-hu7 in,  Ui7-tioh8 in e5 ian5-kou3 khian3-chek chiah e5 kun-ong5;
15)	Kong2, M7-thang hoan7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 siu7 boah-iu5--e5,  Iah8 m7-thang phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 Goa2 e5 sian-ti.
16)	I beng7-leng7 ki-hng kang3-loh8 ti7 hit e5 thou2-toe7;  Chiong sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 bi2-niu5, it-khai3 toan7-choat8.
17)	I ti7 in e5 thau5-cheng5 chhe chit8-lang5 khi3;  Iok-sek siu7-boe7 choe3 lou5-pok8;
18)	Lang5 eng7 kha-khau3 siong i e5 kha,  I siu7 thih-lian7 khun2-pak8;
19)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 chhi3-lian7 i,  Tit8-kau3 I sou2 kong2--e5 eng3-giam7.
20)	Ong5 chhe lang5 ka7 i thau2-khui,  Chiu7-si7 ti7-li2 peh-siN3--e5, ka7 i thau2-pang3;
21)	Siat-lip8 i choe3 ong5-ka e5 chu2,  Koan2-li2 i it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5,
22)	Thang sui5-i3 pak8 i e5 jin5-sin5,  Chiong ti3-hui7 ka3-si7 i e5 tiong2-lo2.
23)	I2-sek-liat8 iah8 kau3 Ai-kip8,  Nga2-kok chhut-goa7 ti7 Ham5 e5 toe7.
24)	Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 i e5 peh-siN3 siN-thoaN3 choe7-choe7;  Hou7 in pi2 tui3-tek8 khah-kiong5.
25)	I pian3-oaN7 tui3-tek8 e5 sim, oan3-hun7 I e5 peh-siN3,  Soa3 eng7 khui2-khiat e5 ke3-bou5 khoan2-thai7 I e5 lou5-pok8.
26)	I chhe I e5 lou5-pok8 Mou5-se,  Kap I sou2 keng2 e5 A-lun5.
27)	In ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 tiong-kan kiaN5 I e5 sin5-jiah,  Ti7 Ham5 e5 toe7 kiaN5 ki5-su7.
28)	I beng7-leng7 ou-am3, chiu7 u7 ou-am3;  In bo5 ui5-keh8 I e5 oe7.
29)	I hou7 in e5 chui2 pian3 huih,  Hou7 in e5 hi5 long2 si2.
30)	Ti7 in e5 thou2-toe7 chhan5-kap-a2 siN choe7-choe7,  Lian5 in e5 ong5 e5 bat8-pang5 iah8 u7.
31)	I chit8-e7 chhut-siaN, hou5-sin5 kui-tin7 pe--lai5,  Koh u7 sat-bu2 ti7 in e5 keng2-lai7 moa2 si3-koe3.
32)	I loh8-phauh8 hou7 in choe3 hou7;  Ti7 in e5 thou2-toe7 kang3-loh8 iam7-he2.
33)	I iah8 phah in e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 kap bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7,  Hui2-hoai7 in keng2-lai7 e5 chhiu7-bak8.
34)	I chit8-e7 chhut-siaN hong5-thiong5 chiu7 lai5,  Chhau2-meh boe7-sng3--tit.
35)	It-chin7 chiah8 in e5 thou2-toe7 e5 chhai3-soe,  Koh chiah8 in chhan5-hng5 sou2 chhut--e5.
36)	I koh phah-si2 in kok-lai7 it-chhe3 e5 toa7-kiaN2,  Chiu7-si7 in khui3-lat8 e5 khi2-thau5.
37)	I chhoa7 in chhut-lai5, toa3 gun5 toa3 kim;  I e5 chi-phai3 tiong, bo5 chit8 e5 loan2-jiok8 e5 lang5.
38)	In chhut--lai5 e5 si5, Ai-kip8 chiu7 hoaN-hi2,  In-ui7 Ai-kip8 bat ui7-tioh8 in lai5 kiaN.
39)	I khi2 hun5 choe3 pou3-phang5,  Mi5--si5 eng7 he2 chio3-kng.
40)	In chit8-e7 kiu5, I chiu7 hou7 ian-chhun pe--lai5,  Koh eng7 thiN e5 piaN2 hou7 in pa2-chiok.
41)	I phah-khui chioh8-poaN5, chui2 chiu7 chheng3-chhut;  Ti7 ta-toe7 chui2 lau5 chhin-chhiuN7 ho5.
42)	In-ui7 I ki3-liam7 I seng3 e5 oe7,  Kap I e5 lou5-pok8 A-pek-lah8-han2.
43)	I chhoa7 I e5 peh-siN3 tai7-iat8 chhut-lai5,  Chhoa7 I keng2 e5 peh-siN3 chhiuN3 hoaN-hi2 e5 koa chhut--lai5.
44)	I chiong liat8-kok e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 in,  In chiu7 seng5-chiap hiah e5 peh-siN3 tioh8-boa5 sou2 tit-tioh8--e5;
45)	Beh hou7 in than3 I e5 lut8-le7,  Siu2 I e5 hoat-tou7.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[106]	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Lin2 tioh8 kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; in-ui7 I si7 ho2;  I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7--teh.
2)	Chi7-chui7 oe7 kong2-khi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 toa7 koan5-leng5?  Chi7-chui7 oe7 piau2-beng5 I it-chhe3 e5 mia5-siaN?
3)	KiN3-na7 chun-siu2 kong-peng5, siong5-siong5 kiaN5 kong-gi7--e5;  Chit-ho7 lang5 chiu7 u7 hok-khi3.  
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 eng7 un-hui7 Khoan2-thai7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3, kiu5 Li2 iah8 eng7 che ki3-liam7 goa2;  Eng7 Li2 e5 kiu3-un lim5-kau3 goa2.
5)	Hou7 goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 keng2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 hok-khi3,  HoaN-hi2 Li2 e5 kok e5 khoai3-lok8,  Kap Li2 e5 san2-giap8 saN-kap eng5-kng.
6)	Goan2 kap goan2 e5 chou2-kong piN5-piN5 hoan7-choe7,  Goan2 chok-giat8, kiaN5 phaiN2.
7)	Goan2 e5 chou2-kong ti7 Ai-kip8 bo5 beng5-pek8 Li2 e5 ki5-su7;  Bo5 ki3-liam7 Li2 hong-seng7 e5 chu5-ai3;  Hoan2-tng2 ti7 hit e5 hai2, chiu7-si7 ti7 Ang5-hai2, kiaN5 poe7-gek8.
8)	Na7-si7 I in-ui7 ka-ki7 e5 mia5 chin2-kiu3 in,  Ui7-tioh8 beh hian2-beng5 I e5 toa7 koan5-leng5.
9)	Koh hoah Ang5-hai2, hai2 chiu7 ta;  I chhoa7 in keng-ke3 chhim e5 sou2-chai7, na2 chhin-chhiuN7 keng-ke3 khong3-ia2.
10)	I kiu3 in thoat-li7 oan3-hun7 in e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2,  Tui3 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2-tiong kiu3-siok8 in.
11)	Chui2 im-bat8 in e5 tui3-tek8;  In chiu7 bo5 lau5 chit8-e5.
12)	Hit-tiap8 in chiah sin3 I e5 oe7;  ChhiuN3-koa o-lo2 I.
13)	In khoai3-khoai3 boe7-ki3-tit I e5 sou2-choe3;  Bo5 theng3-hau7 I e5 chi2-kau3;
14)	Hoan2-tng2 ti7 khong3-ia2 toa7 khi2 tham-chiah8;  Ti7 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7 chhi3 Siong7-te3.
15)	I chiong in sou2 kiu5--e5 hou7--in,  Chong2-si7 hou7 in e5 sin5-hun5 soe-lam2.
16)	In koh ti7 iaN5-tiong oan3-tou3 Mou5-se,  Kap Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 seng3 e5 A-lun5.
17)	Toe7 chiu7 khui, thun Tai7-tan,  Iam2-bat8 A-pi2-lan5 e5 tong2.
18)	U7 he2 ti7 in e5 tong2-tiong hoat-khi2,  U7 he2-iam7 sio-biat8 hiah e5 phaiN2-lang5.
19)	In ti7 Ho5-liat8 cho7 gu5-a2,  Phak-pai3 sou2 chu3 e5 siong7.
20)	An2-ni chiong in e5 eng5-kng  OaN7 choe3 chiah8-chhau2 e5 gu5-a2 siong7.
21)	Boe7-ki3-tit kiu3 in e5 Siong7-te3,  Bat kiaN5 toa7 e5 tai7-chi3 ti7 Ai-kip8--e5;
22)	KiaN5 ki5-su7 ti7 Ham5 e5 toe7,  KiaN5 thang kiaN e5 su7 ti7 Ang5-hai2.
23)	Sou2-i2 I kong2 beh biat8-bo5 in,  Na7 m7-si7 u7 I sou2 keng2 e5 Mou5-se, tng koat-liat8 e5 si5, khia7 I e5 bin7-cheng5,  Ban2-hoe5 I e5 siu7-khi3, kiaN-liau2 I biat8-bo5 in.
24)	In koh khoaN3-khin hit e5 ho2 e5 toe7,  M7-sin3 I e5 oe7.
25)	Ti7 in pou3-piN5-lai7 hoat-chhut oan3-hun7 e5 oe7,  M7-thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN.
26)	Sou2-i2 I tui3 in kiah8-khi2 chhiu2 chiu3-choa7,  Beh hou7 in si2 ti7 khong3-ia2.
27)	Hou7 in e5 hou7-e3 si2 ti7 liat8-kok e5 tiong-kan,  Si3-soaN3 ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7.
28)	In koh kap Pa-lek8-pi2-jiN2 lian5-hap8,  Chiah8 che3-hian3 si2--e5 e5 mih8.
29)	In an2-ni kiaN5, jia2 I e5 siu7-khi3;  Chiu7 u7 un-ek8 liu5-heng5 ti7 in tiong-kan.
30)	Hit-si5 Hui-ni5-hap khi2--lai5, kiaN5 heng5-hoat8;  Un-ek8 chiah soah.
31)	Chit-e5 chiu7 ka7 i sng3-choe3 gi7,  Se3-se3 tai7-tai7, tit8 kau3 eng2-oan2.
32)	In ti7 Bi2-li7-pa e5 chui2, koh hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa siu7-khi3,  Sim7-chi3 Mou5-se ui7-tioh8 in e5 ian5-kou3 ia7 siu7 khui-sun2;
33)	Si7 in-ui7 in ngou2-gek8 I e5 sin5,  Ti3-kau3 Mou5-se kong2-chhut so3-seng3 e5 oe7.
34)	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 in chau5-biat8 hiah e5 peh-siN3;  In bo5 thiaN-than3.
35)	Hoan2-tng2 kap goa7-pang lang5 hun7-chap8,  Oh8 in e5 sou2-choe3;
36)	Hok8-sai7 in e5 ngou2-siong7,  Che si7 chiaN5-choe3 hai7 in e5 oah8-tauh.
37)	Chiong in e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 che3-su7 kui2-sin5,
38)	Lau5 bo5-choe7 e5 lang5 e5 huih, chiu7-si7 in e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 huih,  chiong in che3-su7 Ka-lam5 e5 ngou2-siong7;  Hit e5 toe7 chiu7 hou7 huih phah la5-sam5.
39)	An2-ni in hou7 ka-ki7 e5 sou2-choe3 phah la5-sam5,  Ti7 in e5 sou2-kiaN5 hoan7-tioh8 im5-heng7.
40)	Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 tui3 I e5 peh-siN3 hoat-chhut,  Iam3-ouN3 I e5 san2-giap8.
41)	Chiong in kau-tai3 goa7-pang lang5 e5 chhiu2;  Oan3-hun7 in e5 lang5 chiu7 koan2-hat in.
42)	In e5 tui3-tek8 ia7 ap-che3 in,  In chiu7 khut-hok8 ti7 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2-e7.
43)	I choe7-choe7 pai2 chin2-kiu3 in;  Chong2-si7 in ti7 in e5 ke3-bou5-tiong poe7-gek8 I;  In-ui7 ka-ki7 e5 choe7-ok kang3-choe3 pi-chian7.
44)	Iau2-ku2 I thiaN-kiN3 in ai-kio3 e5 si5, chiu7 the2-thiap in e5 gui5-kip;
45)	Ui7-tioh8 in lai5 ki3-liam7 I e5 iok,  Chiau3 I hong-seng7 e5 chu5-ai3 hoe5-sim tng2-i3.
46)	I ia7 hou7 in ti7 long2-chong2 liah8 in e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5,  Tit-tioh8 lin5-bin2.
47)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 chin2-kiu3 goan2,  Tui3 goa7-pang-tiong chu7-chip8 goan2;  Thang hou7 goan2 chiok-sia7 Li2 e5 seng3-mia5,  Liah8 Li2 e5 siu7 o-lo2 choe3 tai7-iat8.
48)	Tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3,  Tui3 eng2-oan2 kau3 eng2-oan2.  Goan7 cheng3 peh-siN3 long2 kong2,  A-beng7.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

Koan3  V
[107]	Lin2 tioh8 kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 I si7 ho2,  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-eng2 ti7-teh.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kiu3-siok8--e5 tioh8 kong2 che oe7,  Chiu7-si7 I tui3 tui3-tek8 chhiu2-tiong sou2 kiu3-siok8--e5;
3)	Tui3 tak8-kok, tui3 tang tui3 sai, tui3 lam5 tui3 pak,  Sou2 chu7-chip8--e5 long2 tioh8 an2-ni kong2.
4)	In ti7 khong3-ia2 pha-hng e5 lou7 phiau-liu5,  Chhe7 bo5 siaN5 thang khia7-khi2.
5)	Ia7 iau, ia7 chhui3-ta,  In e5 sim-sin5 hun7--khi3.
6)	In chiu7 ti7 khou2-lan7-tiong ai-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  I tui3 in e5 hoan7-lan7-tiong chin2-kiu3 in.
7)	Koh chhoa7 in kiaN5 tit8 e5 lou7,  Hou7 in khi3 kau3 thang khia7-khi2 e5 siaN5.
8)	Ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chu5-ai3 kap I tui3 se3-kan lang5 sou2 kiaN5 e5 ki5-su7,  Goan7 lang5 long2 o-lo2 I.
9)	In-ui7 I hou7 pek-chhiat him-bou7 e5 sim tit-tioh8 ti-chiok;  Hou7 iau-go7 e5 sim tit-tioh8 ho2-mih8 kau3 pa2.
10)	Hiah-e5 che7 ti7 ou-am3 si2-im3-tiong e5 lang5,  Siu7 khun3-khou2 kap thih-lian7 pe2-pak8 e5 lang5;
11)	Si7 in-ui7 in poe7-gek8 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7,  KhoaN3-khin Chi3-koaiN5--e5 e5 chi2-i3.
12)	Sou2-i2 I eng7 lo5-khou2 ka3-koai in e5 sim;  In poah8-to2, bo5 lang5 hu5-chou7.
13)	In chiu7 ti7 khou2-lan7-tiong ai-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  I tui3 in e5 hoan7-lan7-tiong khan-kiu3 in.
14)	I tui3 ou-am3 si2-im3-tiong chhoa7 in chhut--lai5,  Chhoah-tng7 pak8 in e5 soh.
15)	Ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chu5-ai3 kap I tui3 se3-kan lang5 sou2 kiaN5 e5 ki5-su7,  Goan7 lang5 long2 o-lo2 I.
16)	In-ui7 I phah-phoa3 tang5 e5 mng5,  Cham7-tng7 thih e5 mng5-kong5.
17)	Gong7-lang5 in-ui7 in e5 ke3-sit,  Koh in-ui7 in e5 choe7-ok, siu7 khou2-chhou2.
18)	In e5 sim iam3-ouN3 tak8-iuN7 e5 chiah8-mih8,  Chiu7 oa2-kun7 si2 e5 mng5.
19)	In chiu7 ti7 khou2-lan7-tiong ai-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  I tui3 in e5 hoan7-lan7-tiong khan-kiu3 in.
20)	I chhut beng7-leng7 i-ho2 in,  Kiu3 in thoat-li7 si2-bo5.
21)	Ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chu5-ai3, kap I tui3 se3-kan lang5 sou2 kiaN5 e5 ki5-su7,  Goan7 lang5 long2 o-lo2 I.
22)	Iah8 goan7 in hian3 kam2-sia7 e5 che3,  Chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN kong2-khi2 I e5 sou2-choe3.
23)	Che7-chun5 ke3-hai2,  Ti7 toa7-chui2-tiong keng-eng5 su7-giap8--e5,
24)	In khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sou2-choe3,  Kap I ti7 chhim-ian sou2 kiaN5 e5 ki5-su7;
25)	In-ui7 I chit8-e7 beng7-leng7, kong5-hong chiu7 khi2;  Hai2-tiong e5 eng2 chiu7 gia5--khi2-lai5;
26)	In chiuN7 kau3 kiong-chhong, loh8 kau3 hai2-toe2;  In in-ui7 gui5-hiam2, sin5-hun5 chiu7 siau-soaN3.
27)	In tian-tian to2-to2, tang-to2 sai-oai, chhin-chhiuN7 chiu2-chui3 e5 lang5,  In e5 ti3-hui7 bu5-hoat kho2-si.
28)	In chiu7 ti7 khou2-lan7-tiong ai-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  I tui3 in e5 hoan7-lan7-tiong chhoa7 in chhut--lai5.
29)	I hou7 kong5-hong tiaN7,  Hai2-eng2 chiu7 peng5-cheng7.
30)	Hong tiaN7, eng2 cheng7, in chiu7 hoaN-hi2;  I chiu7 chhoa7 in kau3 sou2 ai3 khi3 e5 hai2-khau2.
31)	Ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chu5-ai3 kap I tui3 se3-kan-lang5 sou2 kiaN5 e5 ki5-su7,  Goan7 lang5 long2 o-lo2 I.
32)	Goan7 in ti7 peh-siN3 e5 hoe7-tiong chun I choe3 koaiN5,  Ti7 tiong2-lo2 e5 che7-ui7 o-lo2 I.
33)	I hou7 kang-ho5 piN3-choe3 khong3-ia2,  Hou7 chui2-choaN5 piN3-choe3 ta-so3 e5 toe7.
34)	I hou7 pui5-toe7 piN3 kiam5 e5 toe7,  Long2 si7 in-ui7 khia7-khi2 ti7-hia e5 lang5 e5 choe7-ok.
35)	I hou7 khong3-ia2 piN3-choe3 tham5-khut,  Hou7 ta-toe7 piN3-choe3 chui2-choaN5.
36)	I hou7 iau-go7 e5 lang5 tiam3 ti7-hia,  Hou7 in oe7 khi2-cho7 thang khia7-khi2 e5 siaN5;
37)	Koh cheng3-choh chhan5-hng5, chai phu5-to5,  Tit-tioh8 sou2 chhut e5 thou2-san2.
38)	I koh siuN2-su3 hok-khi3 hou7 in, hou7 in siN-thoaN3 choe7-choe7,  Iah8 hou7 in e5 cheng-siN bo5 kiam2-chio2.
39)	In koh in-ui7 po7-giok8, hoan7-lan7, iu-khou2,  Chiu7 kiam2-chio2 koh pi-ke7.
40)	I hou7 kui3-chok8 siu7 khoaN3-khin,  Hou7 in phiau-liu5 ti7 pha-hng bo5 lou7 e5 sou2-chai7.
41)	Chong2-si7 I ku2-khi2 song3-hiong lang5, hou7 in thoat-li7 khou2-lan7,  Hou7 i e5 ka-chok8 heng-ong7 chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-kun5.
42)	Cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5 beh khoaN3-kiN3 lai5 hoaN-hi2;  It-chhe3 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhui3 beh that-bat8.
43)	KiN3-na7 u7 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 beh koan-sim chiah e5 tai7-chi3,  Iah8 beh siau3-liam7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chu5-ai3.

[108]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si-koa.
1)	Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 e5 sim chu7-chai7;  Goa2 beh gim5-si, goa2 e5 sim-sin5 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2.
2)	Khim5--ah, sek--ah, lin2 tioh8 cheng-sin5 khi2-lai5;  Goa2 pun2-sin beh chin-cha2 cheng-sin5 khi2--lai5.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 beh ti7 ban7 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan kam2-sia7 Li2;  Ti7 liat8-pang e5 tiong-kan chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2.
4)	In-ui7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 khah-toa7 thiN,  Li2 e5 seng5-sit8 kau3 kiong-chhong.
5)	Siong7-te3 ah, goan7 Li2 koaiN5-toa7 poaN5-ke3 chiah e5 thiN;  Goan7 Li2 e5 eng5-kng poaN5-ke3 choan5-toe7.
6)	Kiu5 Li2 thiaN goan2, eng7 chiaN3-chhiu2 khan-kiu3 goan2;  Thang hou7 Li2 sou2 thiaN3 e5 lang5 tit-tioh8 kiu3.
7)	Siong7-te3 i2-keng chi2 I e5 seng3-kiat lai5 kong2, Goa2 beh tai7-iat8;  Goa2 beh pun-khui Si7-kiam3, niu5 Sou3-kat e5 soaN-kok.
8)	Ki-liat8 si7 Goa2-e5; Ma2-na2-se iah8 si7 Goa2-e5;  I2-hoat-lian5 si7 Goa2 e5 thau5-khoe;  Iu5-tai7 si7 Goa2 e5 koan5-peng3.
9)	Mou5-ap beh choe3 Goa2 e5 ek8-phun5;  Goa2 beh hiat goa2 e5 oe5 ti7 I2-tong;  Goa2 beh in-ui7 khah-iaN5 Hui-li7-su7 lai5 toa7-siaN hoah.
10)	Chi7-chui7 oe7 chhoa7 goa2 jip8 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5?  Chi7-chui7 chhoa7 goa2 jip8 I2-tong e5 toe7?
11)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 kiam3 m7-si7 khi3-sak goan2 mah?  Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 bo5 kap goan2 e5 kun-peng saN-kap khi3.
12)	Kiu5 Li2 pang-chan7 goan2, kong-kek tui3-tek8;  In-ui7 lang5 e5 chin2-kiu3 si7 khang-khang.
13)	Goan2 oa2-kho3 Siong7-te3, choe3-chiaN5 toa7 tai7-chi3;  In-ui7 thun2-tah8 goan2 e5 tui3-tek8--e5, chiu7-si7 I.

[109]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si; kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Goa2 sou2 o-lo2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 boh8-tit cheng7-cheng7;
2)	In-ui7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhui3, kap kan-cha3 e5 chhui3, in i2-keng thi2-khui kong-kek goa2;  In eng7 peh8-chhat8 e5 chih8 tui3 goa2 kong2-oe7.
3)	In eng7 oan3-hun7 e5 oe7 pau-ui5 goa2;  Koh bo5 in-toaN lai5 kong-kek goa2.
4)	Goa2 thiaN3--in, in hoan2-tng2 choe3 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8;  Tok8-tok8 goa2 choan-bu7 ki5-to2.
5)	In tui3 goa2 eng7 phaiN2 po3 ho2,  Eng7 oan3-hun7 po3 jin5-ai3.
6)	Goan7 Li2 phai3 chit8 e5 phaiN2-lang5 koan2-hat i,  Phai3 chit8 e5 tui3-tek8 khia7 ti7 i e5 chiaN3-peng5.
7)	I siu7 sim2-phoaN3 e5 si5,  goan7 i chhut-lai5 siu7 teng7-choe7;  Goan7 i e5 ki5-to2 piN3-choe3 choe7-koa3.
8)	Goan7 i e5 jit8-chi2 te2-chio2;  Goan7 pat8-lang5 tit-tioh8 i e5 chit.
9)	Goan7 i e5 kiaN2-ji5 choe3 kou-ji5,  I e5 bou2 choe3 koaN2-hu7.
10)	Goan7 i e5 kiaN2-ji5 si3-koe3 khi3 kiu5-khit;  Tui3 in pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7 chhut-lai5 tho2-chiah8.
11)	Goan7 che3-chu2 eng7 ke3-ti3 chhu2 i it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5;  Goan7 siN-hun7-lang5 chhiuN2 i tioh8-boa3 sou2 tit-tioh8--e5.
12)	Goan7 bo5 lang5 chiap-siok8 si-un hou7 i;  Goan7 bo5 lang5 kho2-lin5 i e5 kou-ji5.
13)	Goan7 i e5 hou7-e3 toan7-choat8,  In e5 mia5-ji7 siu7 chhat-biat8,  bo5 thoan5 ti7 e7-tai7.
14)	Goan7 i e5 chou2-kong e5 choe7-ok hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ki3-tit;  Goan7 i e5 lau7-bu2 e5 che7-koa3 bo5 tit-tioh8 chhat-siau.
15)	Goan7 hiah e5 choe7-ok siong5-siong5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5,  Ti3-kau3 I biat8 in e5 mia5 ti7 se3-kan.
16)	In-ui7 i bo5 siuN7-tioh8 beh kiaN5 lin5-bin2;  Hoan2-tng2 khun2-pek hit e5 song3-hiong khun3-khou2 e5 lang5,  Beh hai7-si2 hiah e5 siong-sim e5 lang5.
17)	I ai3 chiu3-chou2, chiu3-chou2 chiu7 kau3 ti7 i;  I m7-ai3 chiok-hok, chiok-hok chiu7 li7-khui i hng7-hng7.
18)	I eng7 chiu3-chou2 choe3 saN lai5 chheng7;  chiu3-chou2 chiu7 chhin-chhiuN7 chui2 jip8 i e5 pak-lai7,  Chhin-chhiuN7 iu5 jip8 i e5 kut.
19)	Goan7 chit e5 chiu3-chou2 choe3 i chheng7 ti7 sin-khu e5 i-hok8,  Choe3 i siong5-siong5 ha5 e5 io-toa3.
20)	Che chiu7-si7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8, kap eng7 phaiN2-oe7 kong-kek goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 e5 lang5,  Tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hia sou2 siu7 e5 po3-eng3.
21)	Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 in-ui7 Li2 e5 mia5 ho2 khoan2-thai7 goa2;  In-ui7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 chin-ho2, kiu5 Li2 khan-kiu3 goa2.
22)	In-ui7 goa2 song3-hiong, khun3-khou2,  Goa2 e5 lai7-sim siu7-siong.
23)	Goa2 e5 he3-siu7 chhin-chhiuN7 jit8-iaN2 chiam7-chiam7 chhia5;  Goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2-meh siu7 koaN2-chhut.
24)	Goa2 in-ui7 kim3-chiah8, kha-thau5-u sng-nng2;  Goa2 e5 bah siau-san2, bo5 lun7-tek8.
25)	Goa2 siu7 in e5 hui2-pong3;  In khoaN3-kiN3 goa2, chiu7 io5-thau5.
26)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 pang-chan7 goa2;  Chiau3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 chin2-kiu3 goa2;
27)	Hou7 in chai che si7 chhut ti7 Li2 e5 chhiu2;  Si7 Li2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7.
28)	Chhut-chai7 in chiu3-chou2, kiu5 Li2 su3-hok;  In khi2--lai5 e5 si5, beh tu2-tioh8 kian3-siau3,  Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 beh hoaN-hi2.
29)	Goan7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 eng7 leng5-jiok8 choe3-saN chheng7;  Goan7 in eng7 in e5 kian3-siau3 choe3 phau3, moa sin-khu.
30)	Goa2 beh eng7 goa2 e5 chhui3 toa7-toa7 kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Goa2 beh ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan o-lo2 I.
31)	In-ui7 I beh khia7 ti7 song3-hiong lang5 e5 chiaN3-peng5,  Beh kiu3 i thoat-li7 sim2-phoaN3 i e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5.

[110]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 e5 chu2 kong2,  Li2 che7 Goa2 e5 iu7-peng5,  Theng3-hau7 Goa2 hou7 li2 e5 tui3-tek8 choe3 Li2 e5 kha-tah8.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa beh tui3 Sek-an chhun-chhut li2 u7 leng5-lek8 e5 koaiN2;  Li2 tioh8 ti7 li2 tui3-tek8 e5 tiong-kan chiang2-koan5.
3)	Li2 chhut-kun e5 jit8, li2 e5 peh-siN3 beh eng7 seng3-kiat e5 chng-thaN7 choe3 saN, kam-sim hian3 ka-ki7;  Li2 e5 chong3-teng kui-oa2 li2, chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-khi2-si5 sou2 kiat e5 lou7-chui2.
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng chiu3-choa7, tek-khak bo5 the3-hoe2, kong2,  Li2 eng2-oan2 choe3 che3-si,  Chiau3 Bek8-ki-se2-tek e5 pan-liat8.
5)	Ti7 li2 chiaN3-peng5 e5 Chu2,  Tng I siu7-khi3 e5 jit8, beh phah-pai7 liat8-ong5.
6)	I beh ti7 liat8-pang-tiong lai5 sim2-phoaN3,  I beh hou7 sin-si pian3-moa2 tak8 sou2-chai7;  I beh ti7 choe7-choe7 kok phah-phoa3 tui3-tek8 e5 thau5-khak.
7)	I beh lim lou7-piN e5 khoe-chui2;  In-ui7 an2-ni, i beh kiah8-khi2 thau5.

[111]	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Ti7 cheng3-tit8 lang5 e5 hoe7-tiong, kap kong-hoe7 tiong,  Goa2 beh choan-sim kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sou2 choe3 chin-toa7,  Hoan7-na7 hoaN-hi2 I sou2 choe3--e5,  long2 beh chha5-kho2 i.
3)	I sou2 kiaN5--e5 si7 chun-kui3 ui-giam5;  I e5 gi7 eng2-eng2 ti7-teh.
4)	I kiaN5 ki5-su7, hou7 lang5 ki3-liam7;  Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 un-hui7, u7 lin5-bin2.
5)	I siuN2-su3 bi2-niu5 hou7 keng3-ui3 I e5 lang5;  I beh eng2-oan2 ki3-liam7 I e5 iok.
6)	I chiong I toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 sou2-choe3 hian2-beng5 ti7 I e5 peh-siN3;  Chiong liat8-pang e5 giap8 siuN2-su3 in.
7)	I e5 chhiu2 sou2-choe3 si7 seng5-sit8 kong-peng5;  I e5 ka3-si7 long2 si7 khak-sit8.
8)	Si7 eng2 se3-tai7 kian-kou3--e5,  Si7 chiau3 seng5-sit8 cheng3-tit8 siat-lip8--e5.
9)	I ng3 I e5 peh-siN3 si-heng5 kiu3-siok8;  I tiaN7-tioh8 I e5 iok, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2;  I e5 mia5 si7 seng3, thang kiaN-ui3.
10)	Keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 ti3-hui7 e5 kun-pun2;  KiN3-na7 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5-e5, chiah u7 chhang-mia5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5-siaN tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.

[112]	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, toa7 hoaN-hi2 I e5 beng7-leng7--e5,  Chit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
2)	I e5 hou7-e3 ti7 se3-kan tek-khak kiong5-seng7;  Cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5 e5 au7-tai7, tek-khak beh tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.
3)	I e5 ke-lai7 u7 he3-mih8, u7 chiN5-chai5;  I e5 kong-gi7 chun5 kau3 eng2-oan2.
4)	Cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5 ti7 ou-am3 e5 tiong-kan, u7 kng ui7-tioh8 i hoat-hian7;  I u7 un-hui7, u7 lin5-bin2, u7 kong-gi7.
5)	Si-un lai5 chioh lang5--e5, u7 hok-khi3;  I siu7 sim2-phoaN3 e5 si5, beh sou3-beng5 ka-ki7 e5 su7.
6)	I eng2-eng2 bo5 io5-choah;  Gi7-lang5 siu7 ki3-liam7, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.
7)	I m7-kiaN phaiN2 siau-sit;  I e5 sim kian-kou3, oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
8)	I e5 sim chu7-chai7, long2 bo5 kiaN-hiaN5,  Tit8-kau3 i khoaN3-kiN3 i e5 tui3-tek8 siu7 po3-eng3.
9)	I toa7 sia2-si3, i chin2-che3 song3-hiong lang5;  I e5 jin5-gi7 chun5 kau3 eng2-oan2;  I e5 kak tit-tioh8 ku2-khi2, u7 eng5-kng.
10)	PhaiN2-lang5 khoaN3-liau2 boe7-khat-tit,  Tek-khak ka7-ge5 chhiat-chhi2, lai5 siau-biat8;  PhaiN2-lang5 e5 sim-goan7 beh kui ti7 bo5.

[113]	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lou5-pok8 ah, lin2 tioh8 o-lo2,  O-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5.
2)	Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 siu7 o-lo2,  Tui3 chit-si5 kau3 eng2-oan2.
3)	Tui3 jit8-chhut kau3 jit8-loh8 e5 sou2-chai7,  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 si7 eng-kai o-lo2--e5.
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa poaN5-ke3 long2-chong2 e5 kok,  I e5 eng5-kng khah-koaiN5 ti7 chiah e5 thiN.
5)	Chi7-chui7 chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ah?  I che7 ti7 chi3-koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7--e5.
6)	I ka-ki7 khiam-pi,  Koan-khoaN3 thiN-teng2 toe7-e7 e5 tai7-chi3.
7)	I tui3 tin5-ai ku2-khi2 song3-hiong lang5,  Tui3 pun3-so3-tui the5-poat8 khiam3-kheh e5 lang5;
8)	Hou7 i kap kui3-chok8 saN-kap che7,  Chiu7-si7 kap pun2-kok e5 kui3-chok8 saN-kap che7.
9)	I hou7 boe7 seng-iok8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 liau7-li2 ke;  Choe3 choe7-choe7 kiaN2 e5 lau7-bu2 lai5 hoaN-hi2.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[114]	I2-sek-liat8 chhut Ai-kip8.  Nga2-kok-ke li7-khui gian5-gu2 boe7 siong-thong e5 peh-siN3;
2)	Hit-si5 Iu5-tai7 choe3 I e5 seng3-sou2,  I2-sek-liat8 choe3 I e5 pang-kok.
3)	Toa7-hai2 khoaN3-kiN3 chiu7 to5-chau2,  Iok-tan3 ho5 iah8 lau5 to3-tng2.
4)	Toa7-soaN tio5-thiau3 chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-kang2;  Soe3-soaN tio5-thiau3 chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-a2-kiaN2.
5)	Toa7-hai2 ah, li2 ui7 siaN2 tai7-chi3 to5-chau2?  Iok-tan3 ah, li2 ui7 siaN2 tai7-chi3 lau5 to3-tng2?
6)	Toa7-soaN ah, li2 chaiN2-iuN7 tio5-thiau3 chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-kang2?  Soe3-soaN ah, li2 chaiN2-iuN7 tio5-thiau3 chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-a2-kiaN2?
7)	Toe7 ah, li2 kiN3-tioh8 Chu2 e5 bin7,  KiN3-tioh8 Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7, chiu7 tioh8 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.
8)	I hou7 chioh8-poaN5 piN3-choe3 chui2-ti5,  Hou7 teng7-chioh8 piN3-choe3 chui2-choaN5.

[115]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, eng5-kng boh8-tit kui hou7 goan2, boh8-tit kui hou7 goan2,  Tioh8 in-ui7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 kap seng5-sit8, kui ti7 Li2 e5 mia5.
2)	Mih-sai2 tioh8 hou7 goa7-pang-lang5 kong2,  TaN, in e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 toh-loh8?
3)	Chong2-si7 goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 thiN-teng2;  Long2 chiau3 I sou2-ai3--e5 kiaN5 tai7-chi3.
4)	In e5 ngou2-siong7 si7 gun5--e5, kim--e5,  Si7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 sou2 cho7--e5.
5)	In u7 chhui3, iah8 boe7 kong2-oe7;  U7 bak8-chiu, iah8 boe7 khoaN3;
6)	In u7 hi7-khang, iah8 boe7 thiaN;  U7 phiN7-khang, iah8 boe7 phiN7;
7)	In u7 chhiu2, iah8 boe7 theh8;  U7 kha, iah8 boe7 kiaN5;  In iah8 bo5 eng7 in e5 na5-au5 chhut-siaN.
8)	Cho7 in-e5, kho3 in-e5,  Long2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 in.
9)	I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 tioh8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  I si7 in e5 pang-chan7, in e5 tin5-pai5.
10)	A-lun5 e5 ke ah, lin2 tioh8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  I si7 in e5 pang-chan7, in e5 tin5-pai5.
11)	Lin2 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa--e5, tioh8 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  I si7 in e5 pang-chan7, in e5 tin5-pai5.
12)	Ia5-ho5-hoa peng5-si5 siau3-liam7 goan2, I beh su3 hok-khi3;  Beh su3 hok-khi3 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 ke;  Beh su3 hok-khi3 hou7 A-lun5 e5 ke.
13)	KiN3-na7 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5, Bo5-lun7 toa7-soe3, I beh su3 hok-khi3 hou7 in.
14)	Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ke-thiN lin2,  Ke-thiN lin2 kap lin2 e5 kiaN2-sun.
15)	Chhong3-cho7 thiN toe7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  SiuN2-su3 hok-khi3 hou7 lin2.
16)	ThiN si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 thiN,  Toe7 si7 I hou7 se3-kan-lang5--e5.
17)	Si2-lang5 boe7-oe7 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Loh8 kau3 cheng7-cheng7 e5 sou2-chai7--e5, iah8 long2 boe7-oe7.
18)	Chong2-si7 goan2 beh o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Tui3 chit-si5 kau3 eng2-oan2.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[116]	Goa2 thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  In-ui7 I thiaN goa2 e5 siaN, goa2 e5 khun2-kiu5.
2)	I i2-keng aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2;  Sou2-i2 goa2 chit8-si3-lang5 beh kiu5-kio3 I.
3)	Si2-bo5 e5 soh tiN5-tioh8 goa2,  Im-kan e5 thong3-khou2 khiN5-tioh8 goa2;  Goa2 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 iu-khou2.
4)	Goa2 chiu7 kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5, kong2,  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah,  taN kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 un-hui7, u7 kong-gi7;  Goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 u7 chu5-pi.
6)	Ia5-ho5-hoa po2-hou7 gong7-tit8 e5 lang5;  Goa2 kau3 ti7 pi-bi5 e5 toe7-ui7, I chiu7 kiu3 goa2.
7)	Goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 ah, tioh8 kui ti7 li2 an-hioh e5 sou2-chai7,  In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 toa7-un khoan2-thai7 li2.
8)	In-ui7 Li2 kiu3 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 bian2-tit si2-bo5;  Kiu3 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu bian2 lau5 bak8-sai2;  Kiu3 goa2 e5 kha bian2 poah8-to2.
9)	Goa2 beh ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5,  KiaN5 ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7.
10)	Goa2 sin3, sou2-i2 kong2;  Goa2 siu7 kek8-toa7 e5 khun3-khou2;
11)	Goa2 bat tioh8-kip lai5 kong2,  Lang5 long2 si7 hu-ke2.
12)	Ia5-ho5-hoa siuN2-su3 goa2 it-chhe3 e5 toa7-un,  Goa2 beh eng7 sim2-mih8 po3-tap I?
13)	Goa2 beh phang5-khi2 kiu3-un e5 poe, Kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5.
14)	Goa2 beh ti7 I cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5,  Tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sia7 goa2 e5 goan7.
15)	Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3 I seng3 e5 peh-siN3 e5 si2,  Choe3 chin po2-poe3.
16)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 sit8-chai7 si7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8;  Goa2 si7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, si7 Li2 lu2-pi7 e5 kiaN2;  Li2 i2-keng thau2-khui khun2-pak8 goa2 e5 soh.
17)	Goa2 beh eng7 kam2-sia7 e5 che3 hian3 hou7 Li2;  Koh beh kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5.
18)	Goa2 beh ti7 I cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5,  Tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sia7 goa2 e5 goan7.
19)	Ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhu3 e5 iN7-lai7,  Ti7 li2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 tiong-kan;  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[117]	Ban8-kok ah, lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Ban7 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 tioh8 chheng-hou7 I.
2)	In-ui7 I tui3 lan2 toa7 si chu5-ai3;  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 seng5-sit8 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[118]	Lin2 tioh8 kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 I si7 ho2;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
2)	Goan7 I2-sek-liat8 kong2,  I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
3)	Goan7 A-lun5 e5 ke kong2,  I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
4)	Goan7 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5 kong2,  I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
5)	Goa2 ti7 gui5-kip e5 tiong-kan kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 in3 goa2, chiong goa2 he7 ti7 khoan-khoah e5 sou2-chai7.
6)	U7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap goa2 ti7-teh, goa2 chiu7 bo5 kiaN;  Lang5 beh siaN2 hoat-tit goa2 ta-oa5?
7)	Ti7 hiah e5 pang-chan7 goa2--e5 e5 tiong-kan, u7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap goa2 ti7-teh;  Sou2-i2 goa2 beh khoaN3-kiN3 hiah e5 oan3-hun7 goa2 e5 lang5 siu7 po3-eng3.
8)	Oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Pi2 oa2-kho3 lang5 khah-ho2.
9)	Oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Pi2 oa2-kho3 ong5-chhin khah-ho2.
10)	Ban7 peh-siN3 ui5-lui5 goa2;  Goa2 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5, beh chau5-biat8 in.
11)	In ui5--goa2, khun3--goa2;  Goa2 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5, beh chau5-biat8 in.
12)	In chhin-chhiuN7 phang ui5 goa2;  Chhin-chhiuN7 sio chhi3-phe3 e5 he2, siu7 phah-hoa.  Goa2 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 beh chau5-biat8 in.
13)	Li2 chhut-lat8 chhia goa2, beh hou7 goa2 to2;  Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa pang-chan7 goa2.
14)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 e5 khui3-lat8, si7 goa2 e5 si-koa;  I iah8 chiaN5-choe3 chin2-kiu3 goa2 e5.
15)	Ti7 gi7-lang5 e5 pou3-piN5-lai7 u7 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, chin2-kiu3 e5 siaN;  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 si-chhut toa7 koan5-leng5.
16)	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 kiah8-koaiN5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 si-chhut toa7 koan5-leng5.
17)	Goa2 boe7 ti3-kau3 si2, iau2 oe7 oah8-teh;  Soa3 beh po3-iong5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sou2-choe3.
18)	Ia5-ho5-hoa bat giam5-giam5 keng2-kai3 goa2;  Chong2-si7 be7 u7 chiong goa2 kau ti7 si2-bo5.
19)	Tioh8 ka7 goa2 khui gi7 e5 mng5;  Goa2 beh jip8--khi3, kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
20)	Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mng5,  Gi7 e5 lang5 beh jip8--khi3.
21)	Goa2 beh kam2-sia7 Li2, in-ui7 Li2 i2-keng in3 goa2;  Koh chiaN5-choe3 chin2-kiu3 goa2--e5.
22)	Sai-hu7 sou2 khi3-sak e5 chioh8,  I2-keng chiaN5-choe3 chhu3-kak-thau5 e5 chioh8.
23)	Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2-choe3--e5,  Lan2 e5 bak8-chiu khoaN3 i choe3 ki5-koai3.
24)	Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 jit8;  Lan2 ti7 chit-jit8 e5 tiong-kan beh hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8.
25)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, taN kiu5 Li2 chin2-kiu3;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, taN kiu5 Li2 hou7 goan2 hoat-tat8.
26)	Hong7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 lai5--e5, eng-kai tit-tioh8 hok-khi3;  Goan2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 ka7 lin2 chiok-hok.
27)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 Siong7-te3, I e5 kng chio3 goan2;  Tioh8 eng7 soh pak8 che3-su7 e5 cheng-siN kau3 toaN5-kak.
28)	Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 beh kam2-sia7 Li2;  Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 beh chun Li2 choe3 koaiN5.
29)	Lin2 tioh8 kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 I si7 ho2;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.

[119]	Sou2 kiaN5 oan5-choan5, chun-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lut8-hoat e5,  Chit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
2)	Chun-siu2 I kan-cheng3 e5 oe7,  Choan-sim chhe7 I--e5, chit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
3)	In bo5 choe3 put-gi7 e5 su7;  In chun-than3 I e5 to7-lou7.
4)	Li2 bat chiong Li2 ka3-si7 e5 oe7 hoan-hu3 goan2;  Si7 ai3 goan2 un-khun5 chun-siu2.
5)	Goan7 goa2 e5 chhu-hiong3 tiaN7-tioh8,  Lai5 siu2 Li2 e5 lut8-le7.
6)	Goa2 tui3-tiong7 Li2 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7,  Chiu7 put-ti3 kian3-siau3.
7)	Goa2 hak8-sip8 Li2 kong-gi7 e5 phoaN3-toan3,  Chiu7 beh eng7 cheng3-tit8 e5 sim kam2-sia7 Li2.
8)	Goa2 beh siu2 Li2 e5 lut8-le7;  Kiu5 Li2 m7-thang it-chin7 pang3-sak goa2.
9)	Siau3-lian5 lang5 tioh8 eng7 sim2-mih8 lai5 chheng-khi3 i e5 sou2-kiaN5?  Si7 tioh8 chiau3 Li2 e5 oe7 lai5 soe3-ji7 kiaN5.
10)	Goa2 choan-sim chhe7 Li2;  Kiu5 Li2 m7-thang hou7 goa2 be5-lou7 li7-khui Li2 e5 kai3-beng7.
11)	Goa2 chiong Li2 e5 gian5-gu2 khng3 ti7 goa2 e5 sim-lai7,  Bian2-tit goa2 tek-choe7 Li2.
12)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 si7 eng-kai siu7 o-lo2--e5;  Kiu5 Li2 chiong Li2 e5 lut8-le7 ka3-si7 goa2.
13)	Li2 sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 phoaN3-su5,  Goa2 eng7 chhui3-tun5 po3-iong5--i.
14)	Goa2 hoaN-hi2 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 lou7,  Chhin-chhiuN7 hoaN-hi2 it-chhe3 e5 chai5-but8.
15)	Goa2 beh cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 Li2 ka3-si7 e5 oe7,  Iah8 beh chu3-tiong7 Li2 e5 to7-lou7.
16)	Goa2 beh ti7 Li2 e5 lut8-le7-tiong ka-ki7 khoai3-lok8,  Goa2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Li2 e5 oe7.
17)	Kiu5 Li2 eng7 toa7-un khoan2-thai7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, hou7 goa2 tit-tioh8 oah8;  Goa2 chiu7 beh siu2 Li2 e5 oe7.
18)	Kiu5 Li2 khui goa2 e5 bak8-chiu,  Hou7 goa2 khoaN3-chhut Li2 lut8-hoat-tiong e5 ki5-biau7.
19)	Goa2 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 si7 choe3 kia3-kha--e5;  Kiu5 Li2 m7-thang tui3 goa2 un2-bat8 Li2 e5 kai3-beng7.
20)	Goa2 e5 sim piak-lih8,  In-ui7 si5-siong5 chhiat-chhiat him-bou7 Li2 e5 phoaN3-su5.
21)	Li2 chek-pi7 kiau-ngou7 siu7 chiu3-chou2 e5 lang5,  Chiu7-si7 be5-lou7 li7-khui Li2 e5 kai3-beng7 e5 lang5.
22)	Kiu5 Li2 ka7 goa2 tu5--khi3 leng5-jiok8 kap khoaN3-khin,  In-ui7 goa2 siu2 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
23)	Kui3-chok8 che7-teh, lam7-sam2 gi7-lun7 goa2;  Na7-si7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 Li2 e5 lut8-le7.
24)	Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7 si7 goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5,  Si7 goa2 e5 bou5-su7.
25)	Goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 khah8-tiau5 ti7 thou5-hun2,  Kiu5 Li2, chiau3 Li2 e5 oe7, chin2-kiu3 goa2 oah8.
26)	Goa2 kong2-khi2 goa2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7, Li2 in3 goa2;  Kiu5 Li2 chiong Li2 e5 lut8-le7 ka3-si7 goa2.
27)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 beng5-pek8 Li2 ka3-si7 e5 lou7,  Goa2 chiu7 cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 Li2 e5 ki5-su7.
28)	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 in-ui7 iu-khou2 lai5 siau-iuN5;  Kiu5 Li2, chiau3 Li2 e5 oe7, hou7 goa2 iong2-kiaN7.
29)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 li7-khui kan-cha3 e5 lou7,  Chiong Li2 e5 lut8-hoat un-su3 goa2.
30)	Goa2 u7 keng2 sin3-sit8 e5 lou7,  Chiong Li2 e5 phoaN3-su5 he7 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
31)	Goa2 loan5-bou7 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang hou7 goa2 kian3-siau3.
32)	Li2 khui-khoah goa2 e5 sim e5 si5,  Goa2 chiu7 chau2 ti7 Li2 kai3-beng7 e5 lou7.
33)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 chiong Li2 lut8-le7 e5 lou7 chi2-si7 goa2;  Goa2 beh thiat-ti2 chun-siu2.
34)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 ti3-hui7, goa2 chiu7 siu2 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat;  Koh beh choan-sim chip-siu2.
35)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 kiaN5 Li2 kai3-beng7 e5 lou7,  In-ui7 chit e5 lou7 si7 goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5.
36)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 e5 sim ng3 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7,  Bo5 ng3 put-gi7 e5 chiN5-chai5.
37)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu oat8-chau2, bo5 khoaN3 hu-ke2;  Koh hou7 goa2 ti7 Li2 e5 lou7-tiong lai5 oah8.
38)	Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 keng3-ui3 Li2,  Kiu5 Li2 ui7 i kian-kou3 Li2 e5 oe7.
39)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 sou2 kiaN e5 leng5-jiok8 li7-khui goa2;  In-ui7 Li2 e5 phoaN3-su5 si7 ho2.
40)	Goa2 him-bou7 Li2 ka3-si7 e5 oe7;  Kiu5 Li2, ti7 Li2 e5 kong-gi7, hou7 goa2 lai5 oah8.
41)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goan7 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 oe7,  Hou7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3, chiu7-si7 Li2 e5 kiu3-un, lim5-kau3 goa2.
42)	Goa2 chiu7 u7 oe7 thang in3 hit e5 leng5-jiok8 goa2--e5;  In-ui7 goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2 e5 oe7.
43)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 chin-li2 e5 oe7 bo5 it-chin7 li7-khui goa2 e5 chhui3;  In-ui7 goa2 ng3-bang7 Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3.
44)	Goa2 beh siong5-siong5 siu2 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat,  Tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.
45)	Goa2 beh kiaN5 ti7 khoan-khoah e5 sou2-chai7,  In-ui7 goa2 u7 kang2-kiu3 Li2 ka3-si7 e5 oe7.
46)	Goa2 iah8 beh ti7 kun-ong5 e5 bin7-cheng5 kang2-lun7 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7,  Iah8 bo5 ti3-kau3 kian3-siau3.
47)	Goa2 beh ti7 Li2 e5 kai3-beng7-tiong ka-ki7 khoai3-lok8;  Chiah e5 kai3-beng7 peng5-sou3 si7 goa2 sou2 thiaN3-sioh--e5.
48)	Goa2 thiaN3-sioh Li2 e5 kai3-beng7, goa2 beh tui3 i kiah8-khi2 chhiu2;  Li2 e5 lut8-le7 goa2 iah8 beh cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 i.
49)	Kiu5 Li2 ki3-tit tui3 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 sou2 eng3-un2 e5 oe7,  In-ui7 Li2 bat hou7 goa2 u7 ng3-bang7.
50)	Li2 e5 oe7 chiong goa2 kiu3-oah8,  Goa2 ti7 hoan7-lan7-tiong tui3 che tit-tioh8 an-ui3.
51)	Kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 chin7-chai7 bu2-ban7 goa2;  Chong2-si7 goa2 be7-bat phian-li7 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat.
52)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 ki3-liam7 Li2 tui3 cha2 i2-lai5 e5 phoaN3-su5,  Chiu7 ka-ki7 tit-tioh8 an-ui3.
53)	Goa2 in-ui7 khi3-sak Li2 e5 lut8-hoat e5 phaiN2-lang5,  Chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 he2 toh8.
54)	Goa2 ti7 kia3-kha e5 chhu3,  Peng5-si5 eng7 Li2 e5 lut8-le7 choe3 si-koa.
55)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 mi5-kan ki3-liam7 Li2 e5 mia5,  Siu2 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat.
56)	Goa2 tit-tioh8 an2-ni,  Si7 in-ui7 goa2 siu2 Li2 ka3-si7 e5 oe7.
57)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 e5 ki-giap8,  Goa2 bat kong2, Goa2 beh siu2 Li2 e5 oe7.
58)	Goa2 bat choan-sim kiu5 Li2 e5 un,  Goan7 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 oe7 lin5-bin2 goa2.
59)	Goa2 chhim-chhim siuN7 goa2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7,  Chiu7 oat8-tng2 kha ng3 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
60)	Goa2 siu2 Li2 e5 kai3-beng7,  KoaN2-kin2 bo5 ian5-chhian5.
61)	PhaiN2-lang5 e5 soh pak8-tiN5 goa2;  Chong2-si7 goa2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Li2 e5 lut8-hoat.
62)	Goa2 in-ui7 Li2 kong-gi7 e5 phoaN3-toan3,  PoaN3-mi5 beh khi2-lai5 kam2-sia7 Li2.
63)	KiN3-na7 keng3-ui3 Li2, kap siu2 Li2 e5 ka3-si7 e5 lang5,  Goa2 kap in choe3-phoaN7.
64)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 chu5-ai3 pian3-moa2 toe7-bin7;  Kiu5 Li2 chiong Li2 e5 lut8-le7 ka3-si7 goa2.
65)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 bat ho2 khoan2-thai7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8,  Si7 chiau3 Li2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.
66)	Kiu5 Li2 chiong ho2 e5 chhang-mia5 kap ti3-sek, ka3-si7 goa2;  In-ui7 goa2 sin3 Li2 e5 kai3-beng7.
67)	Goa2 be7 siu7-khou2 i2-cheng5, u7 kiaN5 be5-lou7;  Chong2-si7 goa2 taN siu2 Li2 e5 oe7.
68)	Li2 si7 ho2, sou2-kiaN5 iah8 si7 ho2;  Kiu5 Li2 chiong Li2 e5 lut8-le7 ka3-si7 goa2.
69)	Kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 cho7-chok bo5-iaN2 oe7, kong-kek goa2;  Chong2-si7 goa2 beh choan-sim siu2 Li2 e5 ka3-si7.
70)	In e5 sim tun7, chhin-chhiuN7 iu5 pau-bat8;  Chong2-si7 goa2 hoaN-hi2 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat.
71)	Goa2 u7 siu7-khou2, si7 choe3 goa2 e5 li7-ek;  In-ui7 beh hou7 goa2 hak8-sip8 Li2 e5 lut8-le7.
72)	Li2 sou2 kong2 e5 lut8-hoat si7 choe3 goa2 e5 li7-ek;  IaN5-ke3 chheng-ban7 e5 kim-gun5.
73)	Li2 e5 chhiu2 chhong3-cho7 goa2, chhiaN5-ti5 goa2;  Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 ti3-hui7, thang hak8-sip8 Li2 e5 kai3-beng7.
74)	Keng3-ui3 Li2 e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 chiu7 beh hoaN-hi2;  In-ui7 ti7 Li2 e5 oe7, goa2 u7 ng3-bang7.
75)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 chai Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 si7 kong-gi7;  Li2 hou7 goa2 siu7-khou2 si7 tui3 ti7 sin3-sit8.
76)	Kiu5 Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 an-ui3 goa2;  Chiau3 Li2 tui3 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.
77)	Goan7 Li2 e5 chu5-pi lim5-kau3 goa2, hou7 goa2 oah8;  In-ui7 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat si7 goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5.
78)	Goan7 kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 siu7 kian3-siau3, in-ui7 in bo5 li2-iu5 ong2-khut goa2;  Chong2-si7 goa2 beh cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 Li2 e5 ka3-si7.
79)	Goan7 keng3-ui3 Li2 e5 lang5 kui-ng3 goa2;  In chiu7 chai Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
80)	Goan7 goa2 e5 sim oan5-choan5 siu2 Li2 e5 lut8-le7,  Hou7 goa2 put-ti3 kian3-siau3.
81)	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 him-bou7 Li2 e5 kiu3-un kau3 hun7--khi3;  Chong2-si7 ti7 Li2 e5 oe7, goa2 u7 ng3-bang7.
82)	Goa2 in-ui7 ng3-bang7 Li2 e5 oe7, bak8-chiu hoe,  Kong2, Li2 sim2-mih8 si5 beh an-ui3 goa2?
83)	In-ui7 goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 he2-hun-tiong e5 phe5-te7;  Chong2-si7 goa2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Li2 e5 lut8-le7.
84)	Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 e5 jit8-chi2 u7 joa7-choe7 ah?  Li2 beh ti7-si5 sim2-phoaN3 khun2-pek goa2 e5 lang5.
85)	Kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 bo5 than3 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat--e5,  Kut8 ham7-khiN, beh hai7 goa2.
86)	Li2 e5 kai3-beng7 it-chin7 seng5-sit8; in bo5 in-toaN khun2-pek goa2;  Kiu5 Li2 pang-chan7 goa2.
87)	In hiam2-hiam2 biat8-bo5 goa2 ti7 se3-kan;  Chong2-si7 goa2 bo5 pang3-sak Li2 e5 ka3-si7.
88)	Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 hou7 goa2 oah8;  Goa2 chiu7 beh siu2 Li2 e5 chhui3 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
89)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 oe7 an-tiaN7 ti7 thiN--nih,  Tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.
90)	Li2 e5 seng5-sit8 chun5 kau3 ban7-tai7;  Li2 kian3-lip8 toe7, toe7 chiu7 tng5-tng5 ti7--teh.
91)	Chiau3 Li2 e5 teng7-le7, in kau3-taN iau2 ti7--teh;  In-ui7 ban7-mih8 long2 si7 Li2 e5 chhe-eng7.
92)	Goa2 na7 m7-si7 hoaN-hi2 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat,  Chiu7 cha2-cha2 ti7 goa2 e5 khou2-lan7-tiong biat8-bo5 lah.
93)	Goa2 eng2-eng2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Li2 e5 ka3-si7;  In-ui7 Li2 eng7 che hou7 goa2 oah8.
94)	Goa2 si7 Li2-e5, kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2;  In-ui7 goa2 chhe7 Li2 e5 ka3-si7.
95)	PhaiN2-lang5 tng-tan2 goa2, beh biat8-bo5 goa2,  Chong2-si7 goa2 beh kang2-kiu3 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
96)	Goa2 khoaN3 sou2-u7 e5 oan5-choan5, long2 si7 iu2-han7;  Tok8-tok8 Li2 e5 beng7-leng7 kek8-ki5 khui-khoah.
97)	Goa2 thiaN3-sioh Li2 e5 lut8-hoat kau3 chaiN2-iuN7 ah!  Goa2 thong-jit8 cheng7-cheng7 siuN7.
98)	Li2 e5 kai3-beng7 siong5-siong5 kap goa2 ti7--teh,  Hou7 goa2 pi2 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 khah u7 ti3-hui7.
99)	Goa2 pi2 goa2 long2-chong2 e5 sian-siN khah thong-tat8;  In-ui7 goa2 cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
100)	Goa2 pi2 lau7-lang5 khah beng5-pek8,  In-ui7 goa2 siu2 Li2 e5 ka3-si7.
