101)	Goa2 kim3 goa2 e5 kha, it-chhe3 e5 phaiN2-lou7 bo5 kiaN5;  Hou7 goa2 thang siu2 Li2 e5 oe7.
102)	Goa2 bo5 phian-li7 Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3;  In-ui7 Li2 u7 ka3-si7 goa2.
103)	Li2 e5 oe7 ti7 goa2 e5 chiuN7-kiuN kau3 joa7 tiN!  Ti7 goa2 e5 chhui3, pi2 bit8 khah-tiN.
104)	Goa2 tui3 Li2 e5 ka3-si7 tit-tioh8 beng5-pek8;  Sou2-i2 goa2 oan3-hun7 it-chhe3 e5 sia5-lou7.
105)	Li2 e5 oe7 choe3 goa2 kha-cheng5 e5 teng,  Choe3 goa2 lou7-chiuN7 e5 kng.
106)	Li2 kong-gi7 e5 phoaN3-toan3, goa2 bat chiu3-choa7 beh chun-siu2;  Goa2 koat-toan3 an2-ni kiaN5.
107)	Goa2 siu7-khou2 kau3-kek8;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 oe7 hou7 goa2 oah8.
108)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 kam3-lap8 goa2 e5 chhui3 sou2 hoaN-hi2 hian3 e5 o-lo2,  Koh chiong Li2 e5 phoaN3-su5 ka3-si7 goa2.
109)	Goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 siong5-siong5 tu2-tioh8 gui5-hiam2;  Iau2-ku2 goa2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Li2 e5 lut8-hoat.
110)	PhaiN2-lang5 siat lo5-bang7 beh hai7 goa2;  Chong2-si7 goa2 bo5 phian-li7 Li2 e5 ka3-si7.
111)	Goa2 chiong Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 ki-giap8;  In-ui7 che si7 goa2 sim-lai7 sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5.
112)	Goa2 hou7 goa2 e5 sim choan ng3 Li2 e5 lut8-le7;  Eng2-oan2 chun-than3, tit8-kau3 lou7-be2.
113)	Nng7-iuN7 sim e5 lang5 si7 goa2 sou2 thong3-hun7;  Tok8-tok8 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat si7 goa2 sou2 thiaN3-sioh.
114)	Li2 si7 goa2 siam2-bih e5 sou2-chai7, koh si7 goa2 e5 tin5-pai5;  Goa2 ti7 Li2 e5 oe7 u7 ng3-bang7.
115)	Choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5 ah, lin2 tioh8 li7-khui goa2;  Hou7 goa2 thang siu2 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 kai3-beng7.
116)	Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 oe7 hu5-chhi5 goa2, hou7 goa2 oah8;  Iah8 bo5 hou7 goa2 in-ui7 sou2 ng3-bang7--e5 lai5 kian3-siau3.
117)	Kiu5 Li2 hu5-chhi5 goa2, goa2 chiu7 tit-kiu3;  Goa2 beh siong5-siong5 tui3-tiong7 Li2 e5 lut8-le7.
118)	KiN3-na7 kiaN5 chha-lou7, li7-khui Li2 e5 lut8-le7 e5 lang5, Li2 khoaN3-khin in;  In-ui7 in e5 khui2-cha3 si7 hu-ke2.
119)	Se3-kan e5 phaiN2-lang5, Li2 long2 ka7 in tu5--khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 che-tai2;  In-ui7 an2-ni, goa2 thiaN3-sioh Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
120)	Goa2 in-ui7 kiaN-ui3 Li2, goa2 e5 bah chiu7 chhoah;  Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 iah8 hou7 goa2 kiaN-hiaN5.
121)	Goa2 peng2-kong kiaN5-gi7;  Kiu5 Li2 m7-thang chiong goa2 pang3 hou7 ap-che3 goa2 e5 lang5.
122)	Kiu5 Li2 po2-jin7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, thang tit-tioh8 ho2 keng2-gu7;  Boh8-tit hou7 kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 ap-che3 goa2.
123)	Goa2 in-ui7 ng3-bang7 Li2 e5 kiu3-un, kap Li2 kong-gi7 e5 oe7,  Ti3-kau3 bak8-chiu hoe.
124)	Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 khoan2-thai7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8;  Chiong Li2 e5 lut8-le7 ka3-si7 goa2.
125)	Goa2 si7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 ti3-hui7;  Hou7 goa2 oe7 chai Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
126)	Hian7-kim tng si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kiaN5 tai7-chi3 e5 si5;  In-ui7 lang5 hoe3-bo5 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat.
127)	Sou2-i2 goa2 thiaN3-sioh Li2 e5 kai3-beng7,  IaN5-ke3 kim, iah8 iaN5-ke3 ho2-kim.
128)	Sou2-i2 Li2 it-chhe3 e5 ka3-si7, ban7-su7, goa2 long2 liah8-choe3 cheng3-tit8;  Koh goa2 oan3-hun7 it-chhe3 e5 sia5-lou7.
129)	Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7 si7 ki5-biau7;  Sou2-i2 goa2 e5 sim kin2-sin7 chip-siu2.
130)	Li2 e5 oe7 chit8-e7 khui-thiah, chiu7 hoat-chhut kng,  Hou7 gong7-lang5 thong-tat8.
131)	Goa2 khui-chhui3 tit8-tit8 chhoan2;  In-ui7 goa2 chhiat-chhiat him-bou7 Li2 e5 kai3-beng7.
132)	Kiu5 Li2 oat8-tng2 ng3 goa2, lin5-bin2 goa2;  Chhin-chhiuN7 Li2 peng5-siong5 khoan2-thai7 hiah e5 keng3-ai3 Li2 e5 mia5 e5 lang5.
133)	Kiu5 Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 oe7 hou7 goa2 e5 kha-pou7 un2-tang3;  Boh8 iong5-un2 sim2-mih8 choe7-ok koan2-hat goa2.
134)	Kiu5 Li2 kiu3-siok8 goa2, thoat-li7 lang5 e5 ap-che3,  Goa2 chiu7 beh siu2 Li2 e5 ka3-si7.
135)	Goan7 Li2 hou7 Li2 e5 bin7 e5 kng chio3 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8;  Koh chiong Li2 e5 lut8-le7 ka3-si7 goa2.
136)	Goa2 e5 bak8-sai2 chhin-chhiuN7 khoe-chui2 teh lau5;  In-ui7 in bo5 siu2 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat.
137)	Ia5-ho5-hoa, Li2 si7 kong-gi7-e5;  Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 iah8 si7 cheng3-tit8--e5.
138)	Li2 sou2 beng7-leng7 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7, si7 chiau3 kong-gi7,  Kek8-ki5 seng5-sit8.
139)	Goa2 e5 sim jiat8, chhin-chhiuN7 he2 sio-biat8 goa2;  In-ui7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 boe7-ki3-tit Li2 e5 oe7.
140)	Li2 e5 oe7 thoan3-lian7 kau3 chin cheng;  Sou2-i2 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 chin i3-ai3.
141)	Goa2 pi-bi5, hou7 lang5 khoaN3-khin,  Chong2-si7 goa2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Li2 e5 ka3-si7.
142)	Li2 e5 kong-gi7 si7 eng2-oan2 e5 kong-gi7;  Li2 e5 lut8-hoat si7 chin-sit8.
143)	Goa2 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 iu-khou2;  Chong2-si7 Li2 e5 kai3-beng7 si7 goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5.
144)	Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7 eng2-oan2 si7 kong-gi7;  Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 ti3-hui7, goa2 chiu7 oe7 oah8.
145)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 choan-sim kiu5-kio3 Li2, kiu5 Li2 in3 goa2;  Goa2 beh kin2-sin7 siu2 Li2 e5 lut8-le7.
146)	Goa2 tui3 Li2 kiu5-kio3, kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2;  Goa2 chiu7 beh siu2 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
147)	Goa2 than3 thiN be7 kng kiu5-kio3 Li2;  Ti7 Li2 e5 oe7 goa2 u7 ng3-bang7.
148)	Mi5--si5, kiN iau2-be7 chhim, goa2 e5 bak8-chiu i2-keng nih-khui;  In-ui7 beh cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 Li2 e5 oe7.
149)	Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3, thiaN goa2 e5 siaN;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 chiong Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3, hou7 goa2 oa7 oah8.
150)	Koan3-lian7 kiaN5-phaiN2 e5 lang5 pek-oa2 lai5;  In li7-khui Li2 e5 lut8-hoat hng7-hng7.
151)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 si7 kun7-kun7;  Li2 e5 kai3-beng7 long2 si7 chin-sit8.
152)	Goa2 kang2-kiu3 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7, cha2-cha2 i2-keng chai,  Si7 Li2 lip8-tiaN7 kau3 eng2-oan2--e5.
153)	Kiu5 Li2 khoaN3-kou3 goa2 e5 khou2-lan7, lai5 khan-kiu3 goa;  In-ui7 goa2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Li2 e5 lut8-hoat.
154)	Kiu5 Li2 ka7 goa2 sin-oan, kiu3-siok8 goa2;  Chiau3 Li2 e5 oe7 hou7 goa2 oah8.
155)	Kiu3-un li7-khui phaiN2-lang5 hng7-hng7;  In-ui7 in bo5 chhe7 Li2 e5 lut8-le7.
156)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 chu5-pi si7 toa7;  Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 hou7 goa2 oah8.
157)	Khun2-pek goa2 e5, ti2-tek8 goa2 e5, chin-choe7,  Chong2-si7 goa2 bo5 phian-li7 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
158)	Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 kan-ok e5 lang5, chiu7 chin iam3-ouN3;  In-ui7 in bo5 siu2 Li2 e5 oe7.
159)	Li2 khoaN3 goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 thiaN3-sioh Li2 e5 ka3-si7;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 hou7 goa2 oah8.
160)	Li2 e5 oe7 e5 chong2-kun-thau5 si7 chin-sit8;  Li2 it-chhe3 kong-gi7 e5 phoaN3-toan3 si7 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
161)	Kui3-chok8 bo5 in-toaN khun2-pek goa2;  Chong2-si7 goa2 e5 sim kiaN-ui3 Li2 e5 oe7.
162)	Goa2 hoaN-hi2 Li2 e5 oe7,  Chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 tit-tioh8 choe7-choe7 thai5-iaN5 e5 mih8.
163)	Peh8-chhat8-oe7 si7 goa2 sou2 thong3-hun7, sou2 iam3-chian7--e5;  Li2 e5 lut8-hoat si7 goa2 sou2 thiaN3-sioh--e5.
164)	Goa2 in-ui7 Li2 kong-gi7 e5 phoaN3-toan3,  Tak8-jit8 chhit-pai2 o-lo2 Li2.
165)	ThiaN3-sioh Li2 e5 lut8-hoat e5 lang5 u7 toa7 peng5-an,  Bo5 chit8-hang7 oe7 tiN5-poaN3 in e5 kha.
166)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 u7 teh ng3-bang7 Li2 e5 kiu3-un,  U7 kiaN5 Li2 e5 kai3-beng7.
167)	Goa2 e5 sim u7 siu2 Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7,  chiah e5 oe7, goa2 chin7-chai7 i3-ai3.
168)	Goa2 u7 siu2 Li2 e5 ka3-si7, kap Li2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7;  In-ui7 goa2 it-chhe3 sou2 kiaN5--e5, long2 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
169)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goan7 goa2 kiu5-kio3 e5 siaN thau3-kau3 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 oe7, siuN2-su3 goa2 ti3-hui7.
170)	Goan7 goa2 khun2-kiu5 e5 oe7 kau3 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 oe7 khan-kiu3 goa2.
171)	Goan7 goa2 e5 chhui3-tun5 hoat-chhut o-lo2 e5 oe7,  In-ui7 Li2 chiong Li2 e5 lut8-le7 ka3-si7 goa2.
172)	Goan7 goa2 e5 chih8 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2 e5 oe7;  In-ui7 Li2 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7 long2 si7 kong-gi7.
173)	Goan7 Li2 chhun-chhiu2 pang-chan7 goa2;  In-ui7 goa2 u7 keng2 Li2 e5 ka3-si7.
174)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 chhiat-chhiat him-bou7 Li2 e5 kiu3-un;  Li2 e5 lut8-hoat iah8 si7 goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2--e5.
175)	Goan7 goa2 oah8--teh, goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 chiu7 beh o-lo2 Li2;  Goan7 Li2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 pang-chan7 goa2.
176)	Goa2 be5-lou7 chhin-chhiuN7 phah-m7-kiN3 e5 iuN5; kiu5 Li2 chhe7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8;  In-ui7 goa2 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Li2 e5 kai3-beng7.

[120]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si.
1)	Goa2 ti7 gui5-kip-tiong kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  I chiu7 in3 goa2.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 peh8-chhat8 e5 chhui3-tun5,  Kap khui2-cha3 e5 chih8.
3)	Khui2-cha3 e5 chih8 ah, Chu2 beh hou7 li2 sim2-mih8 ah?  Beh eng7 sim2-mih8 ke-thiN hou7 li2 ah?
4)	Chiu7-si7 iong2-beng2 e5 lang5 e5 lai7-chiN3,  Kap lo5-theng5-chha5 e5 jiat8-thoaN3.
5)	Goa2 chin chham2 ah, kia3-kha ti7 Bi2-siat,  Khia7-khi2 ti7 Ki-tat8 hiah e5 pou3-piN5 e5 tiong-kan.
6)	Goa2 kap hiah e5 oan3-hun7 ho5-peng5 e5 lang5,  Ku2-ku2 saN-kap khia7-khi2.
7)	Goa2 ai3 ho5-peng5;  Chong2-si7 goa2 khui-chhui3, in chiu7 beh cheng-chian3.

[121]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si.
1)	Goa2 beh kiah8-bak8 ng3 soaN;  Goa2 e5 pang-chan7 tui3 toh-loh8 lai5?
2)	Goa2 e5 pang-chan7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5;  I si7 chhong3-cho7 thiN toe7 e5.
3)	I bo5 beh hou7 li2 e5 kha io5-choah;  Po2-siu2 Li2-e5 tek-khak bo5 tuh-bin5.
4)	KhoaN3 ah, po2-siu2 I2-sek-liat8 e5, Ia7 bo5 tuh-bin5, ia7 bo5 khun3--khi3.
5)	Po2-siu2 li2--e5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 li2 e5 chiaN3-peng5 choe3 li2 e5 im3-ng2.
6)	Jit8--si5 thai3-iong5 bo5 siong li2,  Mi5--si5 geh8 iah8 boe7 hai7 li2.
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa beh po2-siu2 li2, bian2 siu7 it-chhe3 e5 chai-hai7;  I beh po2-siu2 li2 e5 siN3-mia7.
8)	Li2 chhut, li2 jip8, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh po2-siu2 li2,  Tui3 chit-si5 tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.

[122]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si; Tai7-pit8 sou2 choe3-e5.
1)	Lang5 tui3 goa2 kong2, Lan2 lai5 khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3,  Goa2 chiu7 hoaN-hi2.
2)	Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah,  Goan2 e5 kha khia7 ti7 li2 e5 mng5-lai7.
3)	Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 siu7 khi2-cho7,  Chhin-chhiuN7 lian5-lok8 cheng2-choe5 e5 siaN5.
4)	Chiah e5 chi-phai3, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chi-phai3,  Chiau3 I2-sek-liat8 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 le7,  ChiuN7-khi3 hia beh o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5.
5)	In-ui7 ti7-hia siat-lip8 sim2-phoaN3 e5 po2-cho7,  Chiu7-si7 Tai7-pit8 ke e5 po2-cho7.
6)	Tioh8 thoe3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kiu5 peng5-an;  KiN3-na7 thiaN3 li2 e5 lang5 tek-khak an-lok8.
7)	Goan7 Li2 siaN5-lai7 peng5-an,  Goan7 Li2 e5 kiong-lai7 an-lok8.
8)	In-ui7 goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7 kap tang5-phoaN7 e5 ian5-kou3,  Goa2 beh kong2, Goan7 peng5-an ti7 li2 e5 lai7-bin7.
9)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3 e5 ian5-kou3,  Goa2 beh thoe3 li2 kiu5 hok-khi3.

[123]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si.
1)	Che7 ti7 thiN-teng2 e5 Chu2 ah,  Goa2 kiah8-bak8 ng3 Li2.
2)	KhoaN3 ah, choe3 lou5-pok8--e5 e5 bak8-chiu, chaiN2-iuN7 ng3 chu2-lang5 e5 chhiu2,  Choe3 lu2-pi7--e5 e5 bak8-chiu, chaiN2-iuN7 ng3 chu2-bu2 e5 chhiu2,  Goan2 e5 bak8-chiu iah8 chiau3 an2-ni ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3;  Tit8-tit8 kau3 I lin5-bin2 goan2.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kho2-lin5 goan2, kho2-lin5 goan2;  In-ui7 goan2 hou7 lang5 khoaN3-khin, i2-keng kau3-kek8.
4)	Goan2 e5 sim hou7 hiah e5 la5-eng5 e5 lang5 leng2-chhio3,  Hou7 kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 khoaN3-khin,  I2-keng kau3-kek8.

[124]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si; Tai7-pit8 sou2 choe3.
1)	I2-sek-liat8 taN tioh8 kong2,  Na7 m7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chan7 goan2,
2)	Na7 m7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chan7 goan2,  Ti7 lang5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek goan2,
3)	Ti7 in tui3 goan2 hoat siu7-khi3 e5 si5,  Chiu7 chiong goan2 oah8-oah8 thun--loh8-khi3;
4)	Hit-si5 chiah e5 chui2 tek-khak poaN5-ke3 goan2,  Ho5-chui2 tek-khak im-bat8 goan2.
5)	Hiong-kong5 e5 chui2 tek-khak im-bat8 goan2.
6)	Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa siu7 o-lo2,  In-ui7 I bo5 chiong goan2 choe3 chiah8-mih8, kau hou7 in pou7-chiah8.
7)	Goan2 e5 siN3-mia7 chhin-chhiuN7 chiau2-a2, thoat-li7 liah8-chiau2--e5 e5 lo5-bang7;  Lo5-bang7 phoa3-lih8, goan2 chiu7 thoat-li7.
8)	Goan2 tit-tioh8 pang-chan7, si7 kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5,  I si7 chhong3-cho7 thiN-toe7--e5.

[125]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si.
1)	Oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5  Chhin-chhiuN7 eng2-eng2 khia7-chai7, boe7 io5-choah e5 Sek-an soaN.
2)	Cheng3-soaN pau-ui5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2,  Ia5-ho5-hoa iah8 an2-ni pau-ui5 I e5 peh-siN3;  Tui3 chit-tiap8 kau3 eng2-oan2.
3)	Choe7-ok e5 koan5-peng3 boe7 tiaN7-tiaN7 ti7 gi7-lang5 e5 hun7-giah8;  Bian2-tit gi7-lang5 chhun chhiu2 choe3-phaiN2.
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 ho2 khoan2-thai7 hiah e5 choe3 ho2--e5,  I2-kip8 sim cheng3-tit8 e5 lang5.
5)	Lun7-kau3 hiah e5 oai-chhoah8, kiaN5 i oan-khiau e5 lou7 e5 lang5,  Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak hou7 in kap choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5 tang5-teng2.  Goan7 peng5-an kui ti7 I2-sek-liat8.

[126]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa chhoa7 hiah e5 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3-tng2 lai5 Sek-an;  Hit-si5 lan2 chhin-chhiuN7 bin5-bang7.
2)	Hit-si5 lan2 e5 chhui3 hah-hah-chhio3,  Lan2 e5 chih8 chhut toa7 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN;  Goa7-pang-tiong chiu7 u7 lang5 kong2,  Ia5-ho5-hoa ui7 in kiaN5 toa7-su7.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 ui7 lan2 kiaN5 toa7-su7,  Lan2 chiu7 hoaN-hi2.
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 goan2 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3-tng2,  Chhin-chhiuN7 lam5-hng e5 khoe-chui2 koh lau5.
5)	Lau5 bak8-sai2 ia7 cheng2-chi2--e5,  Beh chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN siu-koah.
6)	Hit e5 lau5 bak8-sai2 toa3 cheng2-chi2 chhut-khi3--e5,  Tek-khak beh toa3 i e5 tiu7-pe2 hoaN-hoaN hi2-hi2 to3--lai5.

[127]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si; Sou2-lo5-bun5 sou2 choe3-e5.
1)	Chhu3-theh8 na7 m7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2-cho7,  Khi2-cho7 i e5 lang5 chiu7 khang-khang tioh8-boa5;  SiaN5-ti5 na7 m7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kou3-siu2,  Chiu7 kou3-siu2 e5 lang5 khang-khang keng2-seng2.
2)	Lin2 cha2-cha2 khi2, oaN3-oaN3 khun3,  Chiah8 lo5-lok8 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 png7, iah8 si7 khang-khang;  Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 thiaN3 e5 lang5, I beh hou7 i ho2-khun3.
3)	KhoaN3 ah, kiaN2-ji5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 siuN2-su3 e5 san2-giap8;  Hoai5-in7 e5 thai, si7 I sou2 hou7 i e5 po3-siuN2.
4)	Siau3-lian5 e5 si5 sou2-siN e5 kiaN2,  Chhin-chhiuN7 iong2-su7 chhiu2-tiong e5 chiN3.
5)	I e5 chiN3-te7 chhiong-moa2 e5 lang5 u7 hok-khi3;  In ti7 siaN5-mng5-khau2 kap tui3-tek8 kong2-oe7,  Tek-khak put-ti3 kian3-siau3.

[128]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si.
1)	KiN3-na7 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kiaN5 ti7 I e5 lou7--e5, Hit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
2)	Li2 beh chiah8 li2 e5 chhiu2 tioh8-boa5 sou2 tit-tioh8--e5,  Li2 beh hiong2-hok, su7-su7 heng-thong.
3)	Li2 e5 bou2 ti7 li2 e5 chhu3 e5 pang5-lai7, chhin-chhiuN7 kiat choe7-choe7 ke2-chi2 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7;  Li2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 ui5-lui5 li2 e5 toh, chhin-chhiuN7 kaN-na2-chai.
4)	KhoaN3 ah, keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5,  Tek-khak beh an2-ni tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa beh tui3 Sek-an su3-hok li2;  Li2 it-seng beh khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 hok-khi3.
6)	Li2 beh khoaN3-kiN3 li2 e5 kiaN2 e5 kiaN2.  Goan7 peng5-an kui ti7 I2-sek-liat8.

[129]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si.
1)	I2-sek-liat8 tioh8 kong2, Tui3 goa2 soe3-han3 e5 si5,  In tauh8-tauh8 khou2-chhou2 goa2.
2)	Tui3 goa2 soe3-han3 e5 si5 in tauh8-tauh8 khou2-chhou2 goa2;  Chong2-si7 in be7-bat khah-iaN5 goa2.
3)	HoaN7-loe5 e5 lang5 loe5 goa2 e5 ka-chiah-phiaN,  Loe5 e5 kau-hun5 thoa chin-tng5.
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 kong-gi7--e5;  I u7 cham7-tng7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 soh.
5)	KiN3-na7 oan3-hun7 Sek-an--e5, Goan7 in tu2-tioh8 kian3-siau3 the3-au7.
6)	Goan7 in chhin-chhiuN7 chhu3-teng2 e5 chhau2,  Be7 toa7-chang5 chiu7 kou-ta5;
7)	Koah-e5 koah bo5 moa2-pe2,  Ha5-e5 ha5 bo5 kui-lam2.
8)	Ke3-lou7 e5 lang5 iah8 bo5 kong2,  Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3 lin2 hok-khi3;  Goan2 hong7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5, ka7 lin2 chiok-hok.

[130]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 tui3 chhim-ian kiu5-kio3 Li2,
2)	Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 thiaN goa2 e5 siaN;  Goan7 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 khun2-kiu5 e5 siaN.
3)	Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 na7 kiu3-kham3 choe7-ok,  Chi7-chui7 khia7-oe7-tiau5?
4)	Chong2-si7 Li2 u7 sia3-bian2 e5 un,  Beh hou7 lang5 keng3-ui3 Li2.
5)	Goa2 theng3-hau7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, goa2 e5 sim-sin5 teh theng3-hau7;  Ti7 I e5 oe7 goa2 u7 ng3-bang7.
6)	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 theng3-hau7 Chu2,  Pi2 chiu2-kiN e5 lang5 theng3-hau7 thiN-kng khah-chhiat,  Pi2 chiu2-kiN e5 lang5 theng3-hau7 thiN-kng khah-chhiat.
7)	I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 tioh8 ng3-bang7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  In-ui7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 chu5-ai3,  Ti7 I u7 hong-seng7 e5 kiu3-siok8.
8)	I tek-khak kiu3-siok8 I2-sek-liat8,  Thoat-li7 i it-chhe3 e5 choe7-ok.

[131]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si; Tai7-pit8 choe3 e5.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 sim bo5 kiau-ngou7, goa2 e5 bak8-thau5 bo5 koaiN5;  Toa7-hang7 e5 su7, kap ki5-biau7 siuN7-boe7-chhut e5,  Goa2 m7-kaN2 kiaN5.
2)	Goa2 chin-chiaN3 hou7 goa2 e5 sim peng5-un2 an-cheng7;  Chhin-chhiuN7 tng7-lin e5 gin2-na2, oa2 ti7 i e5 lau7-bu2,  goa2 e5 sim ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 chhin-chhiuN7 tng7-lin e5 gin2-na2.
3)	I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 tioh8 ng3-bang7 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Tui3 chit-si5 kau3 eng2-oan2.

[132]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Tai7-pit8 sou2 siu7 it-chhe3 e5 khou2-lan7,  Kiu5 Li2 ki3-liam7 i;
2)	I chaiN2-iuN7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu3-choa7,  tui3 Nga2-kok e5 toa7 Koan5-leng5--e5 he7-goan7;
3)	Kong2, Goa2 tek-khak bo5 jip8 goa2 e5 ke e5 pou3-piN5,  Ia7 bo5 chiuN7 goa2 e5 bin5-chhng5;
4)	Goa2 bo5 iong5-un2 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu khun3--khi3,  Ia7 bo5 iong5-un2 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu-phe5 hap8-oa2;
5)	Theng3-hau7 goa2 ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhe7-tioh8 sou2-chai7,  Ui7 Nga2-kok e5 toa7 Koan5-leng5--e5 chhe7-tioh8 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7.
6)	KhoaN3 ah, goan2 thiaN-kiN3 iok-kui7 ti7 I2-hoat-tha;  Goan2 ti7 chhiu7-na5 e5 chhan5 tu2-tioh8 i.
7)	Goan2 beh jip8 I khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7;  Goan2 beh pai3 ti7 I e5 kha-tah8-i2 cheng5.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 khi2-lai5;  Li2 kap Li2 e5 khui3-lat8 e5 iok-kui7 saN-kap jip8 Li2 hioh-khun3 e5 sou2-chai7.
9)	Goan7 Li2 e5 che3-si chheng7 kong-gi7 choe3 saN;  Goan7 Li2 seng3 e5 peh-siN3 chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.
10)	Kiu5 Li2 in-ui7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 e5 ian5-kou3,  Boh8-tit khi3-sak Li2 e5 siu7-boah-iu5--e5.
11)	Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 seng5-sit8 tui3 Tai7-pit8 chiu3-choa7,  Tek-khak bo5 hoan2-hok,  Kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 li2 sou2-siN-e5 che7 ti7 li2 e5 po2-cho7.
12)	Li2 e5 kiaN2 na7 siu2 Goa2 e5 iok,  Kap Goa2 sou2 beh ka3-si7 in e5 hoat-tou7,  In e5 kiaN2-sun beh eng2-oan2 che7 ti7 li2 e5 po2-cho7.
13)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 keng2 Sek-an,  Ai3 eng7 i choe3 pun2-sin khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7;
14)	Kong2, Che si7 Goa2 eng2-oan2 hioh-khun3 e5 sou2-chai7;  Goa2 beh tiam3 ti7-chia,  In-ui7 si7 Goa2 sou2 i3-ai3 e5.
15)	Goa2 beh hou7 i e5 bi2-niu5 hong-seng7,  Goa2 beh eng7 chiah8-mih8 hou7 i e5 song3-hiong-lang5 kau3-giah8.
16)	Goa2 beh hou7 i e5 che3-si chheng7 kiu3-un choe3 saN;  I seng3 e5 peh-siN3 beh chhut toa7 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.
17)	Goa2 beh hou7 Tai7-pit8 e5 kak ti7-hia hoat-siN;  Goa2 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 siu7-boah-iu5--e5 pi7-pan7 kng-teng.
18)	Goa2 beh hou7 i e5 tui3-tek8 chheng7 kian3-siau3 choe3 saN;  Chong2-si7 i e5 bian2-liu5 beh ti7 i e5 thau5-khak-teng2 hoat-chhut kng.

[133]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si; Tai7-pit8 sou2 choe3.
1)	KhoaN3 ah, hiaN-ti7 ho5-ho2 saN-kap khia7-khi2,  Si7 ho5-teng2 e5 ho2, ho5-teng2 e5 an-lok8!
2)	Che thang pi2-pheng7 hit e5 kui3-khi3 e5 iu5 thin5 ti7 thau5-khak-teng2,  Lau5 kau3 chhui3-chhiu,  Chiu7-si7 A-lun5 e5 chhui3-chhiu,  Koh lau5 kau3 i e5 saN-a2-ku.
3)	Ia7 thang pi2-pheng7 Hek-bun5 e5 lou7-chui2,  Loh8 ti7 Sek-an chiah e5 soaN;  In-ui7 ti7-hia Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 tiaN7-tioh8 su3-hok,  Chiu7-si7 eng2-oan2 e5 oah8-mia7.

[134]	ChiuN7 kia7-a2 e5 si.
1)	KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa chiah e5 lou5-pok8, mi5-kan tiam3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhu3-lai7 e5,  Lin2 long2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
2)	Lin2 tioh8 ng3 seng3-sou2 kiah8-khi2 lin2 e5 chhiu2,  O-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
3)	Goan7 chhong3-cho7 thiN toe7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Tui3 Sek-an su3 hok-khi3 hou7 li2.

[135]	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa chiah e5 lou5-pok8, tiam3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3,
2)	Tiam3 ti7 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3 e5 iN7-lai7 e5,  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 I.
3)	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 ho2;  Tioh8 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 I e5 mia5, in-ui7 che si7 chin biau7.
4)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa keng2 Nga2-kok kui I ka-ki7,  Keng2 I2-sek-liat8 choe3 ka-ki7 tek8-piat8 e5 peh-siN3.
5)	Goa2 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 toa7,  Ia7 chai lan2 e5 Chu2 poaN5-ke3 long2-chong2 e5 sin5-beng5.
6)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 thiN-teng2, ti7 toe7-chiuN7, ti7 hai2-tiong, ti7 it-chhe3 e5 chhim-ian,  Long2 chhut-chai7 I e5 i3-su3 lai5 kiaN5.
7)	I hou7 hun5-bu7 tui3 toe7-kek8 chheng3-khi2;  Ui7-tioh8 hou7 chhong3-cho7 sih-na3,  Tui3 I e5 khou3-pang5 tiong toa3 hong chhut-lai5.
8)	I chiong Ai-kip8 lang5 kap cheng-siN thau5-chiuN7-e5,  Long2 ka7 in phah-si2.
9)	Ai-kip8 ah, I kiaN5 sin5-jiah ki5-su7 ti7 li2 e5 tiong-kan,  Ti7 Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 cheng3 jin5-sin5.
10)	I phah-iaN5 choe7-choe7 pang-kok,  Koh thai5-si2 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 ong5;
11)	Chiu7-si7 A-mou5-li7 ong5 Se-hong5,  Kap Pa-san ong5 Gok8,  I2-kip8 Ka-lam5 tak8-kok.
12)	Chiong in e5 toe7 choe3 giap8,  Chiu7-si7 hou7 I e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 choe3 giap8.
13)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 mia5 lau5 kau3 eng2-oan2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 thang ki3-liam7 e5 mia5 lau5 kau3 ban7-tai7.
14)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ka7 I e5 peh-siN3 sin-oan;  Ui7-tioh8 I chiah e5 lou5-pok8 he5-sim tng2-i3.
15)	Goa7-pang e5 ngou2-siong7 si7 gun5--e5 kim--e5,  Si7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 sou2 cho7--e5.
16)	In u7 chhui3, ia7 boe7 kong2-oe7;  U7 bak8-chiu, ia7 boe7 khoaN3;
17)	In u7 hi7-khang, ia7 boe7 thiaN;  Chhui3-lai7 ia7 bo5 chhoan2-khui3.
18)	Cho7-in--e5 kho3-in--e5,  Long2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 in.
19)	I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  A-lun5 e5 ke ah, lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;
20)	Li7-bi7 e5 ke ah, lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lang5 ah, lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
21)	Ia5-ho5-hoa khia7-khi2 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2;  Goan7 I tui3 Sek-an tit-tioh8 o-lo2.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[136]	Lin2 tioh8 kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 I si7 ho2;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
2)	Lin2 tioh8 kam2-sia7 chiah e5 siong7-te3 e5 Siong7-te3;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
3)	Lin2 tioh8 kam2-sia7 ban7-chu2 e5 Chu2;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
4)	Kam2-sia7 hit e5 ka-ki7 kiaN5 toa7 ki5-su7 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
5)	Kam2-sia7 hit e5 eng7 ti3-hui7 chhong3-cho7 thiN e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
6)	Kam2-sia7 hit e5 phou toe7 ti7 chui2 e5 teng2-bin7 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
7)	Kam2-sia7 hit e5 chhong3-cho7 toa7 e5 kng-the2 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
8)	Chiu7-si7 jit8-thau5 lai5 koan2 jit8--si5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh;
9)	Geh8 kap chhiN koan2 mi5--si5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
10)	Kam2-sia7 hit e5 phah-si2 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 toa7-kiaN2 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
11)	Chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 in tiong-kan chhut-lai5 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
12)	Eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2 kap chhun-chhut-lai5 e5 chhiu2-kut;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
13)	Kam2-sia7 hit e5 pun-khui Ang5-hai2 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
14)	Ia7 chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 tui3 hit e5 tiong-kan keng-ke3 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
15)	Chiong Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 kun-peng hiat ti7 Ang5-hai2 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
16)	Kam2-sia7 hit e5 chhoa7 I e5 peh-siN3 kiaN5 ti7 khong3-ia2 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
17)	Kam2-sia7 hit e5 phah-si2 toa7 kun-ong5 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
18)	Thai5-si2 u7 mia5-siaN e5 ong5 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
19)	Thai5-si2 A-mou5-li7 ong5 Se-hong5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
20)	Koh thai5-si2 Pa-san ong5 Gok8;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
21)	Chiong in e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 choe3 giap8;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
22)	Chiu7-si7 siuN2-su3 I e5 lou5-pok8 I2-sek-liat8 choe3 giap8;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
23)	I siau3-liam7 lan2 ti7 pi-bi5 e5 ui7;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
24)	Chin2-kiu3 lan2 thoat-li7 lan2 e5 tui3-tek8;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
25)	I siuN2-su3 bi2-niu5 hou7 kiN3 u7 hiat-khi3 e5;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.
26)	Lin2 tioh8 kam2-sia7 thiN-teng2 e5 Siong7-te3;  In-ui7 I e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh.

[137]	Goan2 bat che7 ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 ho5-piN,  Chit8-e7 siuN7-tioh8 Sek-an, bak8-sai2 chiu7 lau5.
2)	Goan2 chiong goan2 e5 khim5  Tiau3 ti7 hit-ui7 e5 liu2-chhiu7.
3)	In-ui7 ti7-hia liah8-goan2--e5, ai3 goan2 chhiuN3-koa,  ChhiuN2-goan2--e5 ai3 goan2 khoai3-lok8,  Kong2, Lin2 tioh8 ka7 goan2 chhiuN3 chit8 siu2 Sek-an e5 koa.
4)	Goan2 ti7 goa7-pang  Thai2-tho2 oe7 chhiuN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 koa?
5)	Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, goa2 na7 boe7-ki3-tit li2,  Goan7 goa2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 sit-loh8 i e5 pun2-su7.
6)	Goa2 na7 boe7-ki3-tit li2,  Na7 bo5 khoaN3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khah ke3-thau5 ti7 goa2 sou2 te7-it hoaN-hi2 e5,  Goan7 goa2 e5 chih8 liam5 ti7 goa2 e5 chiuN7-kiuN.
7)	Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 si5,  I2-tong lang5 kong2, Thiah-hui2 i, thiah-hui2 i,  Tit8-tit8 thiah kau3 toe7-ki;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 ki3-tit hit-jit8.
8)	Teh-beh siu7 biat8 e5 Pa-pi2-lun5 siaN5 ah,  Po3-eng3 li2 chhin-chhiuN7 li2 khoan2-thai7 goan2 e5,  Hit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.
9)	Liah8 li2 e5 eN-a2, siak ti7 chioh8-poaN5 e5,  Hit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.

[138]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Goa2 beh choan-sim kam2-sia7 Li2,  Ti7 chiah e5 siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2.
2)	Goa2 beh ng3 Li2 e5 seng3-tian7 kui7-pai3,  In-ui7 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 kap seng5-sit8, o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5;  In-ui7 Li2 hou7 Li2 e5 oe7 choe3 toa7, iaN5-ke3 Li2 sou2 u7 e5 mia5.
3)	Goa2 kiu5-kio3 e5 jit8 Li2 chiu7 in3 goa2,  Kou2-bu2 goa2, hou7 goa2 e5 sim u7 khui3-lat8.
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, se3-chiuN7 e5 kun-ong5 long2 beh kam2-sia7 Li2,  In-ui7 in u7 thiaN-kiN3 Li2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.
5)	In beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 kiaN5-choe3,  In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng chin-toa7.
6)	Ia5-ho5-hoa sui-jian5 chin koaiN5, iau2-ku2 khoaN3-kou3 pi-bi5 e5 lang5;  Chong2-si7 I tui3 hng7-hng7 khoaN3-chhut kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5.
7)	Goa2 sui-jian5 kiaN5 ti7 hoan7-lan7-tiong, Li2 beh hou7 goa2 oah8;  Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8 siu7-khi3, Li2 beh chhun-chhiu2 lai5 ti2-tng i,  Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 iah8 beh kiu3 goa2.
8)	Koan-he7 goa2 e5 su7, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chiaN5--i;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 e5 chu5-ai3 eng2-oan2 ti7-teh;  Kiu5 Li2 boh8-tit pang3-sak Li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 cho7--e5.

[139]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 i2-keng kam3-chhat goa2, bat goa2.
2)	Goa2 che7--loh8-khi3, goa2 peh--khi2-lai5, Li2 long2 chai;  Li2 tui3 hng7-hng7 chai goa2 e5 liam7-thau5.
3)	Goa2 kiaN5-lou7, goa2 to2 ti7 bin5-chhng5, Li2 long2 siong5-se3 chai;  Goa2 it-chhe3 sou2-kiaN5--e5, Li2 ia7 chhim-chai.
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7,  Li2 bo5 chit8-ku3 m7-chai.
5)	Li2 ti7 goa2 e5 cheng5-au7 ui5 goa2,  HoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 goa2 e5 teng2-bin7.
6)	Chit khoan2 e5 chai-bat ki5-biau7, goa2 boe7-oe7 chhek-tok8;  Chin-koaiN5, goa2 boe7-oe7 kau3.
7)	Goa2 beh khi3 toh-loh8, siam2-pi7 Li2 e5 sin5?  Goa2 beh chau2-khi3 toh-loh8, siam2-pi7 Li2 e5 bin7?
8)	Goa2 na7 chiuN7 thiN, Li2 ti7-hia;  Goa2 na7 khun3 ti7 im-kan, Li2 iah8 ti7-hia.
9)	Goa2 na7 thi2-khui chheng-cha2 e5 sit8,  Pe kau3 hai2 e5 kek8-thau5 lai5 khia7-khi2;
10)	Chiu7 na7 ti7-hia, Li2 e5 chhiu2 iah8 beh in2-chhoa7 goa2,  Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 iah8 beh khan goa2.
11)	Goa2 na7 kong2, OU-am3 beh jia-kham3 goa2,  Koh si3-ui5 e5 kng beh piN3-choe3 am3-mi5;
12)	Chiu7 ou-am3 iah8 boe7-oe7 jia-kham3 goa2, hou7 Li2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3;  OU-am3 mi5 chhin-chhiuN7 jit8--si5 hoat-kng.  OU-am3 kap kng-beng5, chai7 Li2 khoaN3 long2 si7 chit8-iuN7.
13)	In-ui7 goa2 e5 chong7-hu2, si7 Li2 sou2 chhong3-cho7--e5;  Goa2 ti7 lau7-bu2 e5 pak-tou2-lai7, Li2 u7 pi3-iu7 goa2.
14)	Goa2 beh kam2-sia7 Li2, in-ui7 goa2 siu7-cho7 ki5-biau7 thang kiaN;  Li2 e5 sou2-choe3 ki5-biau7;  Che si7 goa2 e5 sim chhim chai--e5.
15)	Goa2 ti7 am3-tiong siu7-cho7,  Ti7 toe7 e5 chin-toe2 siu7 lian5-lok8,  Hit-si5 goa2 e5 heng5-the2 bo5 un2-moa5 ti7 Li2.
16)	Goa2 be7 chiaN5-heng5 e5 the2-chit,  Li2 e5 bak8-chiu i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3,  Sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 jit8, iau2-be7 u7 chit8-jit8,  Long2 ki3 ti7 Li2 e5 chheh.
17)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 e5 i3-su3 tui3 ti7 goa2, kau3 chiah po2-poe3!  Hit e5 siau3-giah8, kau3 chiah choe7!
18)	Goa2 na7 beh sng3--i, pi2 hai2-soa khah-choe7;  Goa2 khun3 cheng-sin5 e5 si5, iu5-goan5 kap Li2 saN-kap ti7-teh.
19)	Siong7-te3 ah, Li2 tek-khak beh chau5-biat8 phaiN2-lang5;  Sou2-i2 lin2 chiah e5 ai3 hou7 lang5 lau5-huih--e5, tioh8 li7-khui goa2 khi3.
20)	In-ui7 in kong2 phaiN2-oe7, tu2-tak Li2;  Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 iah8 lam7-sam2 chheng Li2 e5 mia5.
21)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, oan3-hun7 Li2--e5, goa2 kiam2 bo5 oan3-hun7 in mah?  Khi2-lai5 kong-kek Li2--e5, goa2 kiam2 bo5 iam3-chian7 in mah?
22)	Goa2 chin7-chai7 oan3-hun7 in, liah8 in choe3 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8.
23)	Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 kam3-chhat goa2, chai goa2 e5 sim-su;  Chhi3-giam7 goa2, chai goa2 e5 i3-su3.
24)	KhoaN3 goa2 u7 sim2-mih8 phaiN2 sou2-kiaN5 bo5,  Chhoa7 goa2 kiaN5 eng2-oah8 e5 lou7.

[140]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si, kau hou7 Gak8-koaN.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 phaiN2-lang5;  Po2-hou7 goa2 thoat-li7 kiong5-ok e5 lang5.
2)	In e5 sim-lai7 tou5-bou5 kan-ok,  Siong5-siong5 chu7-chip8 ai3 kau-chian3.
3)	In hou7 in e5 chih8 lai7 chhin-chhiuN7 choa5;  Chhui3-tun5-e7 u7 tok8-choa5 e5 tok8. [se3-lah8
4)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 po2-siu2 goa2 thoat-li7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhiu2;  Po2-hou7 goa2 thoat-li7 kiong5-ok e5 lang5;  In siuN7 beh chhia hou7 goa2 poah8-to2.
5)	Kiau-ngou7 e5 lang5 ui7 goa2 am3-chiN7 tiuN oah8-tauh kap soh;  In ti7 lou7-piN an lo5-bang7, Siat khoan5-tho3, beh hai7 goa2. [se3-lah8
6)	Goa2 bat tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3;  Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 khun2-kiu5 e5 siaN.
7)	Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, goa2 kiu3-un e5 lat8 ah,  Ti7 kau-chian3 e5 jit8, Li2 jia-chah8 goa2 e5 thau5-khak.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang chiau3 phaiN2-lang5 e5 sou2 ai3;  M7-thang chiaN5 in e5 ke3-bou5, kiaN-liau2 in chu7-ko. [se3-lah8
9)	Lun7-kau3 hiah-e5 ui5-khun3 goa2 e5 lang5 e5 thau5,  Goan7 in chhui3-tun5 e5 kan-ok im-bat8 in ka-ki7;
10)	Goan7 jiat8-jiat8 e5 he2-thoaN3 loh8 ti7 in e5 sin-chiuN7;  Goan7 in siu7 hiat ti7 he2--nih,  Hiat ti7 chhim-khiN-lai7, boe7 koh khi2-lai5.
11)	Kong2 phaiN2-oe7 e5 lang5 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 tek-khak khia7-boe7-tiau5;  Chai-e7 tek-khak tui-jip kiong5-po7 e5 lang5, chiong in taN2-to2.
12)	Goa2 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ui7 khun3-khou2 e5 lang5 sin-oan,  Beh ui7 song3-hiong lang5 pian7-beng5 un-khut.
13)	Gi7-lang5 tek-khak beh kam2-sia7 Li2 e5 mia5;  Cheng3-tit8 lang5 beh khia7-khi2 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.

[141]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 bat kiu5-kio3 Li2;  Kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 lim5-kau3 goa2;  Goa2 kiu5-kio3 Li2 e5 si5,  Goan7 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 siaN.
2)	Goan7 goa2 e5 ki5-to2, chhin-chhiuN7 hiuN, pai5 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  Goan7 goa2 e5 kiah8-khi2 chhiu2, chhin-chhiuN7 e5-hng-si5 e5 che3-su7.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 kou3-siu2 goa2 e5 chhui3;  Pe2-siu2 goa2 chhui3-tun5 e5 mng5.
4)	Kiu5 Li2 bo5 hou7 goa2 e5 sim phian-ng3 sia5-ok,  Ti3-kau3 goa2 kap chok-giat8 e5 lang5 tang5-kiaN5 phaiN2-tai7;  Iah8 bo5 hou7 goa2 chiah8 in e5 ho2-mih8.
5)	Gi7-lang5 phah goa2, goa2 sng3-choe3 jin5-chu5;  I chek-pi7 goa2, goa2 sng3-choe3 thau5-khak-teng2 boah-iu5;  Goa2 e5 thau5-khak bo5 beh oat8-siam2;  Tng in kiaN5-phaiN2 e5 si5, goa2 iu5-goan5 beh ki5-to2.
6)	In e5 sim2-phoaN3-koaN siu7 hiat-loh8 soaN-kham3;  In beh thiaN goa2 e5 oe7, in-ui7 che oe7 si7 tiN.
7)	Goan2 e5 kut-thau5 si3-soaN3 ti7 bong7-piN;  Chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 choh-chhan5, loe5-khui hit e5 thou5.
8)	Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 e5 bak8-chiu ng3 Li2;  Goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2, kiu5 Li2 m7-thang pang3-sak goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 bo5 i-oa2.
9)	Kiu5 Li2 po2-hou7 goa2 thoat-li7 in ui7-tioh8 goa2 tiuN e5 oah8-tauh,  Kap kiaN5-phaiN2 e5 lang5 e5 khoan5-tho3.
10)	Goan7 phaiN2-lang5 ham7-loh8 ti7 in e5 lo5-bang7;  Chong2-si7 goa2 tit-tioh8 thoat-li7.

[142]	Tai7-pit8 ti7 tong7-lai7 e5 si5, choe3 chit e5 ka3-si7 e5 si; iah8 si7 ki5-to2.
1)	Goa2 chhut-siaN au5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Chhut-siaN khun2-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
2)	Goa2 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 thou3-chhut goa2 e5 khou2-cheng5.  Goa2 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 pai5-liat8 goa2 e5 hoan7-lan7.
3)	Goa2 e5 sin5 ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 hun7--khi3 e5 si5, Li2 chai goa2 e5 lou7;  Ti7 goa2 kiaN5 e5 lou7, in ui7-tioh8 goa2 am3-chiN7 tiuN oah8-tauh.
4)	Kiu5 Li2 ng3 goa2 e5 chiaN3-peng5 lai5 khoaN3, in-ui7 bo5 lang5 bat goa2;  Goa2 bo5 te3 thang to5-siam2, iah8 bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kou3 goa2.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 bat tui3 Li2 ai-kiu5;  Goa2 kong2, Li2 si7 goa2 to5-siam2 e5 sou2-chai7,  Ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7, Li2 si7 goa2 e5 ki-giap8.
6)	Kiu5 Li2 aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 kiu5-kio3; in-ui7 goa2 loh8 kau3 kek8-ke7 e5 ui7;  Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 khun2-pek goa2 e5 lang5, in-ui7 in pi2 goa2 khah-kiong5.
7)	Kiu5 Li2 chhoa7 goa2 chhut kaN, goa2 chiu7 thang o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5;  Gi7-lang5 beh ui5 goa2, in-ui7 Li2 eng7 un-tian2 khoan2-thai7 goa2.

[143]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 thiaN goa2 e5 ki5-to2, aN3 hi7-khang thiaN goa2 e5 khun2-kiu5;  Chiau3 Li2 e5 sin3-sit8, chiau3 Li2 e5 kong-gi7, lai5 in3 goa2.
2)	Kiu5 Li2 boh8-tit sim2-mng7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8,  In-ui7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, oah8-teh e5 lang5, bo5 chit8-e5 chheng-choe3-gi7.
3)	Tui3-tek8 khun2-pek goa2,  Chiong goa2 e5 siN3-mia7, phah-to2 ti7 toe7--nih;  Hou7 goa2 tiam3 ti7 ou-am3 e5 sou2-chai7,  chhin-chhiuN7 si2 ku2-ku2 e5 lang5 chit8-iuN7.
4)	Sou2-i2 goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 hun7-khi3;  Goa2 e5 sim ti7 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7 chhiN-chhin3.
5)	Goa2 ki3-tit kou2-cha2 e5 jit8;  Siau3-liam7 Li2 it-chhe3 e5 sou2-kiaN5;  Cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 Li2 e5 chhiu2 e5 sou2-choe3.
6)	Goa2 ng3 Li2 kiah8-khi2 chhiu2,  Goa2 e5 sim him-bou7 Li2, chhin-chhiuN7 khong3-han7 e5 toe7 chit8-iuN7. [se3-lah8
7)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 kin2-kin2 in3 goa2;  Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 hui3-liau2-liau2;  M7-thang tui3 goa2 ng bin7;  Bian2-tit goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 loh8-bong7 e5 lang5.
8)	Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 cha2-khi2-si5 thiaN-kiN3 Li2 chu5-ai3 e5 siaN,  In-ui7 goa2 oa2-kho3 Li2;  Kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 chai eng-kai kiaN5 e5 lou7.  In-ui7 goa2 e5 sim giong2-bong7 Li2.
9)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8;  Goa2 chau2--khi3 bih ti7 Li2 hia.
10)	Li2 si7 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3, kiu5 Li2 ka3-si7 goa2 kiaN5 Li2 e5 chi2-i3;  Li2 e5 sin5 si7 ho2, kiu5 Li2 chhoa7 goa2 ti7 piN5-tit8 e5 toe7.
11)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 ui7-tioh8 Li2 e5 mia5 hou7 goa2 oah8;  Chiau3 Li2 e5 kong-gi7, chhoa7 goa2 chhut hoan7-lan7-tiong.
12)	Chiau3 Li2 e5 chu5-ai3, tu5-khi3 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8,  Chau5-biat8 it-chhe3 khou2-chhou2 goa2 e5 lang5;  In-ui7 goa2 si7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8.

[144]	Tai7-pit8 e5 si.
1)	Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 chioh8-poaN5, si7 eng-kai o-lo2--e5;  I ka3-si7 goa2 e5 chhiu2 oe7 cheng-chian3,  Ka3-si7 goa2 e5 chng2-thau5-a2 oe7 saN-thai5.
2)	I si7 goa2 e5 chu5-ai3, goa2 e5 soaN-che7,  Goa2 e5 koaiN5-tai5, goa2 e5 kiu3-chu2;  Goa2 e5 tin5-pai5, si7 goa2 sou2 oa2-kho3--e5;  I hou7 goa2 e5 peh-siN3 hang5-hok8 ti7 goa2 e5 e7-bin7.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, lang5 si7 sim2-mih8, Li2 keng2-jian5 bat i?  Lang5 e5 kiaN2 si7 sim2-mih8, Li2 keng2-jian5 siau3-liam7 i?
4)	Lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 pun5 chit8 e5 khui3;  I e5 jit8-chi2 chhin-chhiuN7 iaN2 ke3--khi3.
5)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 thiN sui5-loh8, chhin-sin kang3-lim5;  Bong soaN, soaN chiu7 chhut ian.
6)	Kiu5 Li2 hoat-chhut sih-na3, hou7 in si3-soaN3;  Sia7-chhut Li2 e5 chiN3, hou7 in jiau2-loan7.
7)	Li2 tui3 teng2-bin7 chhun-chhiu2 kiu3 goa2;  Kiu3 goa2 chhut toa7-chui2,  Kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa7-pang lang5 e5 chhiu2.
8)	In e5 chhui3 kong2 peh8-chhat8,  In e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 si7 kan-cha3 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2.
9)	Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 beh tui3 Li2 chhiuN3 sin e5 koa;  Eng7 chap8-tiau5-hian5 e5 sek, chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2.
10)	Li2 si7 hit e5 chin2-kiu3 liat8-ong5--e5,  Li2 si7 hit e5 kiu3 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 thoat-li7 hai7-mia7 e5 to--e5.
11)	Kiu5 Li2 chin2-kiu3 goa2, kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa7-pang lang5 e5 chhiu2;  In e5 chhui3 kong2 peh8-chhat8,  In e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 si7 kan-cha3 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2.
12)	Goan2 e5 ta-pou-kiaN2 tng siau3-lian5 e5 si5, chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-a2 toa7-chang5;  Goan2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 chhin-chhiuN7 chhu3-kak e5 chioh8, chiau3 khi2-keng e5 khoan2-sit tiau-tok--e5.
13)	Goan2 e5 chhek-chhng moa2-moa2, oe7 chhut tak8-iuN7 e5 bi2-niu5;  Goan2 e5 iuN5 ti7 soaN-ia2 siN-thoaN3, chiaN5-chheng chiaN5-ban7.
14)	Goan2 e5 gu5 thoa-mih8 moa2-chai7;  Bo5 u7 lang5 jip8-lai5 chhim-chiam3, iah8 bian2 chhut-khi3 cheng-chian3;  Goan2 e5 koe-chhi7, iah8 bo5 u7 thi5-khau3 e5 siaN.
15)	Tu2-tioh8 chit-ho7 keng2-hong2 e5 peh-siN3, u7 hok-khi3;  U7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3, chit-ho7 e5 peh-siN3 u7 hok-khi3.

[145]	Tai7-pit8 o-lo2 e5 si.
1)	Goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 goa2 e5 Ong5 ah, Goa2 beh chun Li2 choe3 koaiN5, goa2 beh eng2-oan2 o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5.
2)	Goa2 beh jit8-jit8 chiok-sia7 Li2;  Iah8 beh eng2-oan2 o-lo2 Li2 e5 mia5.
3)	Ia5-ho5-hoa chi3-toa7, eng-kai siu7 toa7 e5 o-lo2;  I e5 toa7 kau3 boe7 chhek-tok8--tit.
4)	Chit-tai7 beh tui3 hit-tai7 o-lo2 Li2 e5 sou2-choe3;  Iah8 beh po3-iong5 Li2 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 su7.
5)	Goa2 beh cheng7-cheng7 siuN7 Li2 chun-kui3 eng5-kng e5 ui-giam5,  Kap Li2 ki5-biau7 e5 sou2-choe3.
6)	Lang5-lang5 beh kong2-khi2 Li2 thang kiaN e5 su7 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5;  Goa2 iah8 beh po3-iong5 Li2 e5 chi3-toa7.
7)	In beh po3-iong5 Li2 toa7-un e5 ki3-liam7,  Iah8 beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 Li2 e5 kong-gi7.
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 un-hui7, u7 lin5-bin2;  Bo5 khoai3-khoai3 siu7-khi3, toa7-toa7 u7 chu5-ai3.
9)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ho2 khoan2-thai7 ban7-lui7;  I e5 lin5-bin2 ti3-im3 I it-chhe3 sou2 cho7--e5.
10)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 it-chhe3 sou2 cho7--e5 beh kam2-sia7 Li2;  Li2 seng3 e5 peh-siN3 iah8 beh o-lo2 Li2.
11)	In kong2-khi2 Li2 e5 kok e5 eng5-kng;  Tam5-lun7 Li2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5.
12)	Thang hou7 se3-kan-lang5 chai Li2 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 sou2-choe3,  Kap Li2 kok ui-giam5 e5 eng5-kng.
13)	Li2 e5 kok si7 eng2-oan2 e5 kok;  Li2 chip-chiang2 e5 koan5-peng3 kau3 ban7-tai7.
14)	Hoan7-na7 poah8-to2--e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa hu5-chhi5 in;  Hoan7-na7 siu7 ap-che3--e5, hu5 in khi2--lai5.
15)	Ban7-hang7-u7 long2 kiah8-bak8 ng3 Li2,  Li2 chiau3-si5 hou7 in chiah8-mih8.
16)	Li2 khui Li2 e5 chhiu2,  Hou7 u7 oah8-khi3--e5 long2 chiau3 sou2-ai3 pa2-chiok.
17)	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 I it-chhe3 sou2 kiaN5--e5, bo5 m7 kong-gi7,  Ti7 I it-chhe3 sou2 choe3--e5, long2 u7 chu5-ai3.
18)	Hoan7-na7 kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa kap in chhin-kun7,  Chiu7-si7 chhin-kun7 hiah e5 seng5-sit8 kiu5-kio3 I e5.
19)	Keng3-ui3 I e5, I beh chiaN5 in e5 sim sou2 ai3;  Iah8 beh thiaN in e5 kiu5-kio3, lai5 chin2-kiu3 in.
20)	Ia5-ho5-hoa po2-hou7 it-chhe3 thiaN3 I e5 lang5;  Chong2-si7 it-chhe3 choe3-phaiN2 e5 lang5, I beh biat8-bo5 in.
21)	Goa2 e5 chhui3 beh kong2-chhut o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7;  Goan7 kiN3 u7 hiat-khi3--e5, long2 eng2-oan2 o-lo2 I e5 seng3-mia5.

[146]	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Goa2 e5 sim ah, li2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
2)	Goa2 it-seng beh o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Goa2 iau2-oah8 e5 si5, beh chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3.
3)	Lin2 boh8--tit oa2-kho3 kun-ong5, boh8--tit oa2-kho3 se3-kan lang5;  In chit8-tiam2-a2 boe7-oe7 pang-chan7.
4)	I chit8-e7 tng7-khui3, chiu7 kui-thou2;  I sou2 ke3-ek8--e5, ti7 hit-jit8 chiu7 siau-biat8.
5)	U7 Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 choe3 i e5 pang-chan7,  Ng3-bang7 i e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, chit-ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3;
6)	I si7 chhong3-cho7 thiN, toe7, hai2, kap ki5-tiong e5 ban7-mih8;  I po2-siu2 seng5-sit8 kau3 ti7 eng2-oan2;
7)	I ui7-tioh8 siu7 un-khut e5 lang5 sin-oan;  SiuN2-su3 chiah8-mih8 hou7 iau-go7--e5.  Ia5-ho5-hoa thau2-pang3 siu7 koaiN-kaN--e5;
8)	Ia5-ho5-hoa khui chhiN-mi5-lang5 e5 bak8-chiu;  Ia5-ho5-hoa hu5-khi2 siu7 ap-che3 e5 lang5;  Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN3-sioh gi7-lang5;
9)	Ia5-ho5-hoa po2-hou7 chhut-goa7 lang5;  Hu5-chhi5 kou-ji5 koaN2-hu7;  Tok8-tok8 phaiN2-lang5 e5 to7-lou7, hou7 i oan-khiau.
10)	Ia5-ho5-hoa beh choe3 ong5 kau3 eng2-oan2;  Sek-an ah, li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh choe3 ong5 kau3 ban7-tai7.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[147]	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  In-ui7 chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3, si7 chin-ho2 chin-biau7;  O-lo2 si7 hap8-gi5.
2)	Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2-cho7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2;  Chu7-chip8 I2-sek-liat8 tiong siu7 chhian-soa2 e5 lang5;
3)	I i-ho2 siong-sim e5 lang5;  Pau in e5 siong.
4)	I sng3 chhiN-sin5 e5 siau3-giah8;  Sui5-liap8 ka7 i ho7-mia5.
5)	Lan2 e5 Chu2 chi3-toa7, kek8 u7 khui3-lat8;  I e5 ti3-hui7 bu5-kiong5-chin7.
6)	Ia5-ho5-hoa hu5-chhi5 khiam-pi e5 lang5;  Chiong phaiN2-lang5 kang3-ke7 kau3 thou5-kha.
7)	Lin2 tioh8 eng7 kam2-sia7 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhiuN3-koa;  ToaN5-khim5 chhiuN3-koa, o-lo2 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3.
8)	I khi2-hun5 jia-thiN,  Ui7-tioh8 toe7 pi7-pan7 hou7,  Hou7 soaN hoat-chhau2.
9)	I siuN2-su3 chiah8-mih8 hou7 chau2-siu3,  Kap teh-hau2 e5 ou-a-kiaN2.
10)	I bo5 i3-ai3 be2 e5 lat8 toa7,  I bo5 hoaN-hi2 lang5 e5 kha gau5-chau2.
11)	Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 hoaN-hi2 keng3-ui3 I,  Kap ng3-bang7 I chu5-ai3 e5 lang5.
12)	Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ah, li2 tioh8 chheng-hou Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Sek-an ah, li2 tioh8 o-lo2 li2 e5 Siong7-te3.
13)	In-ui7 I kian-kou3 li2 e5 mng5-kong5;  Su3-hok hou7 li2 tiong-kan e5 kiaN2-ji5.
14)	I hou7 li2 e5 keng2-lai7 thai3-peng5;  Eng7 siong7-ho2 e5 beh8 hou7 li2 chiah8-pa2.
15)	I hoat-chhut beng7-leng7 ti7 toe7--nih,  I e5 oe7 pan-heng5 chin-kin2.
16)	I kang3-loh8 seh chhin-chhiuN7 mi5-hoe,  Iah8 loh8-sng chhin-chhiuN7 he2-hu.
17)	I hiat-loh8 phauh8 chit8-te3 chit8-te3;  I hoat-chhut koaN5-chhin3, chi7-chui7 tong3-oe7-tiau5?
18)	I chit8-e7 chhut-leng7, chiah-e5 chiu7 long2 iuN5;  I hou7 hong chhe, chui2 chiu7 lau5.
19)	I chiong I e5 oe7 chi2-si7 Nga2-kok,  Chiong I e5 lut8-le7 kap phoaN3-toan3, chi2-si7 I2-sek-liat8.
20)	I m7-bat an2-ni khoan2-thai7 pat8-kok;  I e5 phoaN3-toan3, in long2 m7-bat.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[148]	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Tui3 thiN-teng2 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 o-lo2 I.
2)	I e5 cheng3 su3-chia2 ah, lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 I.  I e5 cheng3 thian-kun ah, lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 I.
3)	Jit8 kap geh8 ah, lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 I;  Hoat-kng e5 chhiN-sin5 ah, lin2 long2 tioh8 o-lo2 I.
4)	ThiN-teng2 e5 thiN, kap thiN i2-chiuN7 e5 chui2 ah,  Lin2 long2 tioh8 o-lo2 I.
5)	Chiah-e5 long2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5;  In-ui7 I chit8-e7 beng7-leng7, chiu7 long2 siu7 chhong3-cho7.
6)	I chiong chiah-e5 kian3-lip8, kau3 eng2-eng2 oan2-oan2;  I u7 teng7-le7, boe7-oe7 hoe3-bo5.
7)	Tui3 toe7-chiuN7 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  Chiu7-si7 toa7-hi5 kap it-chhe3 e5 chhim-ian;
8)	He2 kap peng-phauh8, seh kap hun5-bu7;  Than3 I e5 oe7 e5 kong5-hong;
9)	Toa7-soaN kap it-chhe3 e5 sio2-soaN;  Kiat ke2-chi2 e5 chhiu7, kap it-chhe3 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7;
10)	Ia2-siu3 kap it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN;  Thang5-thoa7 kap pe-chiau2;
11)	Se3-chiuN7 e5 kun-ong5 kap ban7-bin5;  Kui3-chok8 kap se3-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 sim2-phoaN3-koaN;
12)	Siau3-lian5-lang5 kap chai7-sek-lu2;  Lau7-lang5 kap gin2-na2;
13)	Chiah-e5 long2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5;  In-ui7 chi2-u7 I e5 mia5 siu7 chun choe3 koaiN5;  I e5 eng5-kng poaN5-ke3 thiN toe7.
14)	I heng-khi2 I e5 peh-siN3 e5 kak,  Hou7 I seng3 e5 peh-siN3 long2 o-lo2 I,  Chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, chhin-kun7 Chu2 hit e5 peh-siN3.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[149]	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Tioh8 chhiuN3 sin e5 koa, o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  Ti7 seng3 e5 peh-siN3 e5 hoe7-tiong o-lo2 I.
2)	Goan7 I2-sek-liat8 in-ui7 cho7 i e5 Chu2 lai5 hoaN-hi2;  Goan7 Sek-an e5 peh-siN3 in-ui7 in e5 Ong5 lai5 khoai3-lok8.
3)	Goan7 in thiau3-bu2 o-lo2 I e5 mia5;  Phah-kou2 toaN5-khim5, chhiuN3-koa o-lo2 I.
4)	In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoaN-hi2 I e5 peh-siN3;  I beh eng7 kiu3-un choe3 khiam-pi e5 lang5 e5 chng-thaN7.
5)	Goan7 seng3 e5 peh-siN3 in-ui7 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 eng5-kng lai5 hoaN-hi2;  Goan7 in ti7 bin5-chhng5--nih chhut hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.
6)	Goan7 in e5 chhui3 o-lo2 Siong7-te3 choe3-koaiN5,  Chhiu2 kiah8 siang-bin7 lai7 e5 kiam3;
7)	Thang po3-eng3 goa7-pang,  Heng5-hoat8 liat8-kok;
8)	Eng7 lian7 pak8 in e5 kun-ong5,  Eng7 thih-khau3 lai5 so2 in e5 jin5-sin5;
9)	Beh ti7 in e5 sin-chiuN7 kiaN5 sou2 ki3-chai3 e5 phoaN3-toan3;  I seng3 e5 peh-siN3 long2 u7 chit-ho7 eng5-kng.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[150]	Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  tioh8 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 seng3-sou2 o-lo2 I;  Tioh8 ti7 I koan5-leng5 e5 kiong-chhong o-lo2 I.
2)	Tioh8 in-ui7 I toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 kiaN5-choe3, o-lo2 I;  Chiau3 I bi2-biau7 e5 koaiN5-toa7, o-lo2 I.
3)	Tioh8 pun5 sau3-kak o-lo2 I;  ToaN5-sek toaN5-khim5 o-lo2 I.
4)	Phah-kou2 thiau3-bu2 o-lo2 I;  Eng7 si-hian5 e5 gak8-khi3 kap pun5-siau o-lo2 I.
5)	Eng7 siaN-toa7 e5 la5-poah8 o-lo2 I;  Eng7 im-koaiN5 e5 la5-poah8 o-lo2 I.
6)	Hoan7-na7 u7 chhoan2-khui3--e5, long2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  Lin2 tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
